
α.1.1 UMmonomansuonk Isaiah wunnaumonuh Amoz, ne nag* papaume Judah kah Jerusalem, pâmontog Uzziah, Jotham, Ahaz, kah Hezekiah Judae ketass8tamwog.
E.1.1 The vision of Isaiah the son of Amoz, which he saw concerning Judah and Jerusalem in the days of Uzziah, Jotham, Ahaz, and Hezekiah, kings of Judah.

α.1.2 N8tam8k woi kesukquog, & kuhkeitash woi ohke: newutche Jehovah ket8hkau, nummahche sohkomm8s8wam, kah nukkésukeh mukkiésog, kah nag nutcheketunkquog.
E.1.2 Hear, O heavens, and give ear, O earth: for the LORD hath spoken, I have nourished and brought up children, and they have rebelled against me.

α.1.3 Ox waheau[m]eh wadtihéunitcheh wuhhog, kah asse wahteoh wussontimomuh ne ahhut assamukqut: qut Israel matta wahteóou, nummissinninneumog matta natwontam8[o]g.
E.1.3 The ox knoweth his owner, and the ass his master's crib: but Israel doth not know, my people doth not consider.

α.1.4 Yea matcheseáe wutohtimóin, missinninnúog neg nayeutogig matcheseongash, 8skannémune8h matchesécheg: mukki[ó]g neg ánusséhuácheg, nag ohquanumáog Jehovah, nag m8m8sqhe[á]og 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, musquánittamunat, nag qushkée amaéog.
E.1.4 Ah sinful nation, a people laden with iniquity, a seed of evildoers, children that are corrupters: they have forsaken the LORD, they have provoked the Holy One of Israel unto anger, they are gone away backward.

α.1.5 Toh$waj wonk woh tattogkomitteaog? pish nano kutassaemw8: mamusse muppuhkuk mahchimom8, kah mamússe metah sauu[X]um8m8.
E.1.5 Why should ye be stricken any more? ye will revolt more and more: the whole head is sick, and the whole heart faint.

α.1.6 Wutch agwusseet, wehque muppuhkukqut, na wanne menuhkano, qut annehikanash, kah woskissinn8ongash, kah ánue kehkechésuongash, matta yanémun8ash, asuh weesquabi[n]i[nn]8ash, asuh matta wutogkunnum8unash nashpe pummee.
E.1.6 From the sole of the foot even unto the head there is no soundness in it; but wounds, and bruises, and putrifying sores: they have not been closed, neither bound up, neither mollified with ointment.

α.1.7 Kutohk8 touushin, kutotanáoash chikoht[á]ash n8taut, kutohke, penuwohteáog ummatchteauuneau ut anaquabeóg kah ne touushin, onatuh sohkomuk nashpe penuwohteáog.
E.1.7 Your country is desolate, your cities are burned with fire: your land, strangers devour it in your presence, and it is desolate, as overthrown by strangers.

α.1.8 Kah Zione wuttaunin nukkonau onatuh wetuomémesut ut seenominneohtekonit, onatuh kohkouémuk ut cucumbere tanohketeaonganit, onatuh wéenuhkausik keitotan.
E.1.8 And the daughter of Zion is left as a cottage in a vineyard, as a lodge in a garden of cucumbers, as a besieged city.

α.1.9 Kuttumma Jehovah ayeuhteáanit sequnnumunkqueog peásin sequnittuonk, woh keáneyeu8mun Sodom, kah woh kutogqueneunkqussimun Gomorrah.
E.1.9 Except the LORD of hosts had left unto us a very small remnant, we should have been as Sodom, and we should have been like unto Gomorrah.

α.1.10 N8tam8k wuttinn8wâonk Jehovah, kenaau Sodome nanawunnuaenúog, kukkeitam8k wuttinnaumatuonk kut$Jehovahumun, woi Gomorrahe missinninnúog.
E.1.10 Hear the word of the LORD, ye rulers of Sodom; give ear unto the law of our God, ye people of Gomorrah.

α.1.11 Ne teag wutch mataáneum kussephammayeuongan8, n8wau Jehovah? nunnumwohtóh ramse chikohtáe mag8ongash, kah 8weesum8 wunogque puppinashimwog, kah matta nuttapeneam8 8sqheongan8 oxinog, asuh lambsog, asuh namposhimwe goatsog.
E.1.11 To what purpose is the multitude of your sacrifices unto me? saith the LORD: I am full of the burnt offerings of rams, and the fat of fed beasts; and I delight not in the blood of bullocks, or of lambs, or of he goats.

α.1.12 Peyôog kenógqussinneaóut ut anaquabeh, [h]owan yeu wunnat8tamuhkon ut kenutcheganit, tattashkukomuneat, nutchippinneutungash.
E.1.12 When ye come to appear before me, who hath required this at your hand, to tread my courts?

α.1.13 Padtauúhteogk wonk tahn8che mag8ongash, incense ne nehchanumukquodt ut nuhhogkat, wuske nepâuzsaog, kah sabbathaash, moáe wehkomonát nutjishontamun, ne matcheseonk, ne moáe miya[é]onk.
E.1.13 Bring no more vain oblations; incense is an abomination unto me; the new moons and sabbaths, the calling of assemblies, I cannot away with; it is iniquity, even the solemn meeting.

α.1.14 K8ske kenepâuzs8m8óog, kah kukkuhquttum8we mishadtupp8ongan8oash, nukketeahogkou nish wutjishontamunash: nish n8tamêhikqunash, nussauunum nish nutchequnehtamunat.
E.1.14 Your new moons and your appointed feasts my soul hateth: they are a trouble unto me; I am weary to bear them.

α.1.15 Kah sepagenumog kenutch[e]gan8oash, pish nutadtahtóh nuskesukquash wutch kuhhogkaout, nux, ayimog monatash peantam8ongash, matta pish nunn8tam8h, kenutchegan8out numwohte[á]u wusqueheongash. 
E.1.15 And when ye spread forth your hands, I will hide mine eyes from you: yea, when ye make many prayers, I will not hear: your hands are full of blood.

α.1.16 Kutchessumók, pahkheuk kuhhogkóog, amaunum8k kum̃atcheseongan8oash wutch anaquabeh, netahshe matchesek,
E.1.16 Wash you, make you clean; put away the evil of your doings from before mine eyes; cease to do evil;

α.1.17 Kodnetuhtau8k wunnésen, natinneham8k wussittumóonk, aninnumok noh sonkqutchahwhut, wussumok touwies, ken8tamwa[n]sheuk sekousq.
E.1.17 Learn to do well; seek judgment, relieve the oppressed, judge the fatherless, plead for the widow.

α.1.18 Yeuyeu peyunk, kah moáe ennóm[á]iyeuhteadtuh, n8wau Lord; t[ô]hkonogque k[u]m̃atcheseongan8ash onatuhheyeu8 skarletut, nish pish ogque wompiyeuash k8nit: tôhkonogque nish unnemusqui crimson, nish pish onatuhyeu8ash w8lut.
E.1.18 Come now, and let us reason together, saith the LORD: though your sins be as scarlet, they shall be as white as snow; though they be red like crimson, they shall be as wool.

α.1.19 Unnantamóg kah n8swehtamóg, pish kummeechum8 ohkée wunnummeechum.
E.1.19 If ye be willing and obedient, ye shall eat the good of the land:

α.1.20 Qut sekeneamóg, kah cheketamóg, pish kummohtuppaémo nashpe togkodt[e]g: newutche wutt8n Jehovah ket8hkontamun.
E.1.20 But if ye refuse and rebel, ye shall be devoured with the sword: for the mouth of the LORD hath spoken it.

α.1.21 Uttôh en pâbuhtantam8e keitotan nanwun8dsquaáesuenúin? ne numwohtop wussittumóonk, sampweusseonk ne ayeum8, qut yeuyeu nushehteaenúog.
E.1.21 How is the faithful city become an harlot! it was full of judgment; righteousness lodged in it; but now murderers.

α.1.22 Kus$silverum p[e]htóou, k8winum kenuksheau nippe.
E.1.22 Thy silver is become dross, thy wine mixed with water:

α.1.23 Kussontimomog cheketamwog, kah weechayemá[h]etticheh kumm8towa[é]nuog, nishnoh pasuk womantam mag8ongash; kah asuhkom kemunkquatungash: nag matta wussumauóog touwiesoh, kah wuttinniyeuonk sekousq matta uppeyógk8uneau.
E.1.23 Thy princes are rebellious, and companions of thieves: every one loveth gifts, and followeth after rewards: they judge not the fatherless, neither doth the cause of the widow come unto them.

α.1.24 Newaj n8wadt Lord, Jehovah ayeuhteaanit, noh masugkenuk ut Israel, yâ nunnunkeh nuhhog wutch yeu ay8kausitcheg, kah nutann8tau nummatwomog.
E.1.24 Therefore saith the LORD, the LORD of hosts, the mighty One of Israel, Ah, I will ease me of mine adversaries, and avenge me of mine enemies:

α.1.25 Kah nukquinnuppinnum nunnutcheg en kuhhogkat, kah nuppannuppe pahketeoh kuppehtom, kah nutamaúnum wame kuttinnum.
E.1.25 And I will turn my hand upon thee, and purely purge away thy dross, and take away all thy tin:

α.1.26 Kah kenompenumoush k8sittumwaéneumwog neáne negonne, kah ken8snaéneumog neáne waj kutchissik: ompetak pish kuttéhenit, sampweusseáe keitotan, pabahtanumwe keitotan.
E.1.26 And I will restore thy judges as at the first, and thy counsellors as at the beginning: afterward thou shalt be called, The city of righteousness, the faithful city.

α.1.27 Zion pish pohquohwhuttauun, nashpe wussittumóonk, kah n[e]g ne adt quinnuppecheg, nashpe sampweusséonk.
E.1.27 Zion shall be redeemed with judgment, and her converts with righteousness.

α.1.28 Kah pagwanoungan8 panneseaénûog, kah matcheseaenúog pish moeyeu88: kah nág ohquanumoncheg Jehovah pish mohtuppaéog.
E.1.28 And the destruction of the transgressors and of the sinners shall be together, and they that forsake the LORD shall be consumed.

α.1.29 Newutche nag pish akodchuog n8timisseash nish kodtantogish, kah pish kukquequenauánumumw8, newutche tanohketeaongash nish pepenamogish.
E.1.29 For they shall be ashamed of the oaks which ye have desired, and ye shall be confounded for the gardens that ye have chosen.

α.1.30 Newutche pish kutogqueneunkqussum8 n8timisseit noh 8neepóg pánshunk, kah onatuh tanohketeáonk ne mat napén8g
E.1.30 For ye shall be as an oak whose leaf fadeth, and as a garden that hath no water.

α.1.31 Káh manuhkésitcheg pish onatuhyeu8og hashabput, kah noh ayik, onatuh chikinn[a]sit, kah nag pish neeswe moeu chikossuog, kah wanne pish howan wutontáhwoh.
E.1.31 And the strong shall be as tow, and the maker of it as a spark, and they shall both burn together, and none shall quench them.

α.2.1 WUttinn8waonk ne Isayah wunnaumonuh Amoz nag*, papaume Judah kah Jerusalem.
E.2.1 The word that Isaiah the son of Amoz saw concerning Judah and Jerusalem.

α.2.2 Kah pish n$nih majish kesukodtash, wek Jehovah 8wadcheum, ne pish menehketeauun ut koduhkô[á]e wadchukontu, kah pish anue tahshinausu onk wadchuash, kah wame wutohtimóineash uppeyaont[á]muneau.
E.2.2 And it shall come to pass in the last days, that the mountain of the LORD's house shall be established in the top of the mountains, and shall be exalted above the hills; and all nations shall flow unto it.

α.2.3 Kah monaog missinninn[u]og pish moncheog[;] kah n8waog, peyunk, kuhkuhquehtuh 8wadcheum Jehovah, en wekit um-Manitt8moh Jakob, kah noh pish nuppomushamun ummayut: newutche Zion wutch sohham ennaumatuonk, kah wuttinn8waonk Jehovah wutch Jerusalem.
E.2.3 And many people shall go and say, Come ye, and let us go up to the mountain of the LORD, to the house of the God of Jacob; and he will teach us of his ways, and we will walk in his paths: for out of Zion shall go forth the law, and the word of the LORD from Jerusalem.

α.2.4 Kah noh pish wussittum ut kenugke wutohtim[o]inneat, kah pish áushkomau mónaoh missinninnuh: kah nag pish plowshearehteáog wuttogkodtegan8óash, kah pish tisaskwheganéhteáog ukqunuhtugquash: wutohtimóin matta pish ayeuuhkonit[t]ue tohshinnumauóou togkodteg wutohtimóiñeuh, kah matta pish wonk netuhtauóog ayeuwuttuonk.
E.2.4 And he shall judge among the nations, and shall rebuke many people: and they shall beat their swords into plowshares, and their spears into pruninghooks: nation shall not lift up sword against nation, neither shall they learn war any more.

α.2.5 Woi wek Jakob, peyunk, kah pomushadtuh 8wequaiyeumut Jehovah.
E.2.5 O house of Jacob, come ye, and let us walk in the light of the LORD.

α.2.6 Newaj nukkonadt kummissinninneumog, wek Jakob: newutche tapauwaméog wutch wutchepwoiyeu, kah ogquonnetuog Philistiansut, kah tapheaog wuhhogkauh nashpe wunneechan8oh penuwohteáog.
E.2.6 Therefore thou hast forsaken thy people the house of Jacob, because they be replenished from the east, and are soothsayers like the Philistines, and they please themselves in the children of strangers.

α.2.7 Kah nag wutohkou numwohteau silver kah gold, kah matta wohkukquoshininn8 wunnompakounn8ash; wonk wutohkeeu wunnumwábeneau horsesoh, kah matta wohkukquos[n]in8 wut-chariotsumash.
E.2.7 Their land also is full of silver and gold, neither is there any end of their treasures; their land is also full of horses, neither is there any end of their chariots:

α.2.8 Kah wonk wutohkéim8 wunnumwábeneau nunneukontunkanog, wowussittumwog néhenwonche wunnutchegane anakausuongan8oash, ne nehenwonche wuttinwhunnitche8 kestoum8uk.
E.2.8 Their land also is full of idols; they worship the work of their own hands, that which their own fingers have made:

α.2.9 Kah noh peississit, nauwáeu, kah noh masugkenuk hohppáheau wuhhogkuh, newutche ahquontamauúhkon.
E.2.9 And the mean man boweth down, and the great man humbleth himself: therefore forgive them not.

α.2.10 Petutteah qussukquanit, kah puttogqush ut puppissiyeuut wutche qushaonk Jehovah, kah wutche wussohsumóe maumuttanussuonk.
E.2.10 Enter into the rock, and hide thee in the dust, for fear of the LORD, and for the glory of his majesty.

α.2.11 Ukqunuhqunneunkqussuonk wosketomp pish hohpóm8, kah uppehtuánum8ongan8 missinninnúog pish nauwa[é]m[X], kah Jehovah nussu pish misheh[e]au ne kesukok.
E.2.11 The lofty looks of man shall be humbled, and the haughtiness of men shall be bowed down, and the LORD alone shall be exalted in that day.

α.2.12 Newutche ukkesukodtum Jehovah ayeuhteáanit, pish nuhkuhkauau nish$noh howane noh pahtuánumit, kah noh pohtuanumwinneunkqussit, kah nish$noh pasuk noh tahshinit, kah noh pish tiuhquon[a]heuh.
E.2.12 For the day of the LORD of hosts shall be upon every one that is proud and lofty, and upon every one that is lifted up; and he shall be brought low:

α.2.13 Kah ut wame Lebanone Cedaro[h], nish quanunkquokish kah tohshiná[unk]ish, kah ut wame Bashanne n8time[s]éash.
E.2.13 And upon all the cedars of Lebanon, that are high and lifted up, and upon all the oaks of Bashan,

α.2.14 Kah ut wame qu[n]u[h]qui wadchuuhkontu, kah ut wame wadchuuhkontu nish tahshinaúsikish.
E.2.14 And upon all the high mountains, and upon all the hills that are lifted up,

α.2.15 Kah ut nish$noh qunuhqui tower, kah ut nish$noh pummeneutausue pummeneútunk.
E.2.15 And upon every high tower, and upon every fenced wall,

α.2.16 Kah ut wame Tarshish-kuht8nogquehtu, kah ut wame tapeneunkquotte nunneukontu[n]kanéhtu.
E.2.16 And upon all the ships of Tarshish, and upon all pleasant pictures.

α.2.17 Kah uppehtuanumwunneunkqussuonk wosketomp pish nauwaemo, kah tiuhquonkqutteau: kah Jehovah nussu pish tahshinau ne kesukok.
E.2.17 And the loftiness of man shall be bowed down, and the haughtiness of men shall be made low: and the LORD alone shall be exalted in that day.

α.2.18 Kah nunneukontunkoh papuhquáne matcheheau.
E.2.18 And the idols he shall utterly abolish.

α.2.19 Kah nag pish petutteáog qussukquanónogqut, kah puhpohkohteaiyeuut, newutch qusháonk Jehovah, kah newutch sussohsum8ongane maumutta[n]suonk, noh omohkit unkquanumwe nunnukshadtunk ohke.
E.2.19 And they shall go into the holes of the rocks, and into the caves of the earth, for fear of the LORD, and for the glory of his majesty, when he ariseth to shake terribly the earth.

α.2.20 Ne kesukok wosketomp pish amaúhteau wussilvere nunneukontunkoh, kah uk-golde nunneukontunkoh, neh ayimáhetticheh nish$noh pasuk nehenwonche wowussumónat, en molsut, kah en mattabashquásit.
E.2.20 In that day a man shall cast his idols of silver, and his idols of gold, which they made each one for himself to worship, to the moles and to the bats;

α.2.21 Petukonat passipskodtut, kah woskeche passipskodtut, wutche qusháonk Lord, kah wutche wussohsumóemaumuttá[u]suonk omohkeit wutunkquánume nunnukshadtauunat ohke
E.2.21 To go into the clefts of the rocks, and into the tops of the ragged rocks, for fear of the LORD, and for the glory of his majesty, when he ariseth to shake terribly the earth.

α.2.22 Ahqueteau8k wutch wosketompaut, noh wunnasháonk ohtag wutchanit newutche, uttoh ut ogquanumon?
E.2.22 Cease ye from man, whose breath is in his nostrils: for wherein is he to be accounted of ?

α.3.1 NEwutche kusseh, Lord, Lord ayeuhteáanit amaunum wutch Jerusalem, kah wutch Judah, ompatissun8 kah anwohhou, mamusse petukqunnegane ompatissun8onk, kah mámusse nippee ompatissun8onk
E.3.1 For, behold, the Lord, the LORD of hosts, doth take away from Jerusalem and from Judah the stay and the staff, the whole stay of bread, and the whole stay of water.

α.3.2 Menuhkésuénin, kah ayeuteaénin, wussittumwaénin, kah quoshodtumwaènin, kah waantamwen kah kehchisog.
E.3.2 The mighty man, and the man of war, the judge, and the prophet, and the prudent, and the ancient,

α.3.3 Napanna adtahshinchagkussitcheg kah quohtiánumukqussuénin, kah ken8suaénin, nehtóanakausuénin, kah wowúnonuhk8waénin.
E.3.3 The captain of fifty, and the honourable man, and the counsellor, and the cunning artificer, and the eloquent orator.

α.3.4 Kah nussontimôhteam mukkiésog, kah peissesog pish wunnánauwunóuh.
E.3.4 And I will give children to be their princes, and babes shall rule over them.

α.3.5 Kah missinninnúog nish$noh pasuk, pish sonkqutchahwhuttuog, kah, nishnoh pasuk nashpe weetatteamungoh: mukkies pish ayeuuhkonittue pehchuánumwe ussehtauau kehchisoh, kah meshananumukqussit ayeuuhkonittue quohtianumukqussinitcheh.
E.3.5 And the people shall be oppressed, every one by another, and every one by his neighbour: the child shall behave himself proudly against the ancient, and the base against the honourable.

α.3.6 Wosketomp tohqunont wematoh, wutch wekit 8shoh, n8wadt, k8htogk8in, nanawi[n]yean, kah yeu matchehteoonk ohtaj agw[é] kenutcheganit.
E.3.6 When a man shall take hold of his brother of the house of his father, saying, Thou hast clothing, be thou our ruler, and let this ruin be under thy hand:

α.3.7 Ne kesukok noh pish chadchekeyeuau, n8wau, matta neetskehuwáenu8: newutche ut nekit matta petukquanegan8 asuh hogk8unun8: ahque nanawunnumw[á]heh ut missinninnútu.
E.3.7 In that day shall he swear, saying, I will not be an healer; for in my house is neither bread nor clothing: make me not a ruler of the people.

α.3.8 Newutche Jerusalem paguatauun, kah Judah penusheau, newutche weenaneu, kah wutusseongan8oash wutayeuuhkonukquanash Jehovah, m8m8squeteauunat wussohsum8e wuskesukquash.
E.3.8 For Jerusalem is ruined, and Judah is fallen: because their tongue and their doings are against the LORD, to provoke the eyes of his glory.

α.3.9 Ne[-]anompamukqussimuk ne 8wauwaónukquneau, kah nag ogque wahteauwáhuwaog ummatcheseongan8 Sodom, matta wutadtahtau8uneau: pish onkapunnaoh ukketeahogkôun8oh, newutche matonkquottauáog wuhhogkauh.
E.3.9 The shew of their countenance doth witness against them; and they declare their sin as Sodom, they hide it not. Woe unto their soul! for they have rewarded evil unto themselves.

α.3.10 Unnok sampwesecheg, nag pish 8niyeuwontamuneau: newutche nag pish meechwog wutanakausuongane meechummuonganóash.
E.3.10 Say ye to the righteous, that it shall be well with him: for they shall eat the fruit of their doings.

α.3.11 Pish onkapunáog matcheetowog, pish ummatchiyeuôntamun: newutche wunnutchegane onkquatunk pish aninnumau[ó]n.
E.3.11 Woe unto the wicked! it shall be ill with him: for the reward of his hands shall be given him.

α.3.12 Papaume nummissinninneumog, mukkiog neh wussonkqutchahwhóuh, kah mittamwussissog nanawunóuh, woi nummissinninneumog, neg sogkompagunukquéaneg kuppanneáhikquog, kah nag paguatoog kuppomushaongane mayash.
E.3.12 As for my people, children are their oppressors, and women rule over them. O my people, they which lead thee cause thee to err, and destroy the way of thy paths.

α.3.13 Jehovah neepau ukken8tamunat, kah neepau 8sumónat missinninnúh.
E.3.13 The LORD standeth up to plead, and standeth to judge the people.

α.3.14 Jehovah pish uppas8oh wussittum8onganit ummissinninneum8e ke[h]chisumoh, kah wussontimom8[ó]h: newutche kummahchepumw8 weenominneohteuk, sequttahhamauáonk matcheku, ut kekuóut.
E.3.14 The LORD will enter into judgment with the ancients of his people, and the princes thereof: for ye have eaten up the vineyard; the spoil of the poor is in your houses.

α.3.15 Toh kuttin nauwuttamumw8, kussukquéhtahwhônaóont nummissinninneumog, kah togguhhamunat wuskesuk8oash matchekuog, n8wau Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaanit.
E.3.15 What mean ye that ye beat my people to pieces, and grind the faces of the poor? saith the Lord GOD of hosts.

α.3.16 Nano Jehovah n8wau, newutche Sione wuttauneunk, pehtuánumóog, kah sekoushquáusháog, kah nanwun8dsquaeskesukquáog, pomushaog, kah wowunnomâusháog pomusháhettit, kah papónshittáusháog.
E.3.16 Moreover the LORD saith, Because the daughters of Zion are haughty, and walk with stretched forth necks and wanton eyes, walking and mincing as they go, and making a tinkling with their feet:

α.3.17 Newaj Lord pish tádteadt mukkeontupaonk ut kodto[n]tupont wuttaunoh Zion; kah Jehovah pish poshkinum ukkôsuonganú8ash.
E.3.17 Therefore the LORD will smite with a scab the crown of the head of the daughters of Zion, and the LORD will discover their secret parts.

α.3.18 Ne kesukok Lord pish amaunum wunn8whôsue wanegukish ut wusseetut, kah ukkaulsum8ash, kah woweeyôwe wunn8whosuongash onatuh nahnepâush[á]dtaut.
E.3.18 In that day the Lord will take away the bravery of their tinkling ornaments about their feet, and their cauls, and their round tires like the moon,

α.3.19 Chainsash, kah kehtippittenápeash, kah mufflersash,
E.3.19 The chains, and the bracelets, and the mufflers,

α.3.20 Bonnetsash, kah muhkontee wunnuhwhosuongash, kah assuhquabeash, kah tabletsash, kah soggussohhouunash,
E.3.20 The bonnets, and the ornaments of the legs, and the headbands, and the tablets, and the earrings,

α.3.21 Pehtehhennitchabheash, kah mutchâne hogqunnu[m]aongash.
E.3.21 The rings, and nose jewels,

α.3.22 Os8ogk8unaongash kah m8[na]kinash, kah wimplsash, kah 8wutchippussum8e auwohteaongash,
E.3.22 The changeable suits of apparel, and the mantles, and the wimples, and the crisping pins,

α.3.23 Pepenauutchitchunkquongash, kah wunne hashabponak, kah h8dsash, kah onkquequohh8unash.
E.3.23 The glasses, and the fine linen, and the hoods, and the vails.

α.3.24 Kah pish n$nih, nompe ne weetemungquok, pish annimmungquot: kah nompe puttukquobpus, nehneksh[á]eu, kah nompe wanoht[ó]e muhpuhkuk, mukukkontupáonk; kah nompe mohpanôganit ahhohtag man8t[i]ónak puttukquobpissinneat, kah chikkossuonk nompe wunnetuonganit.
E.3.24 And it shall come to pass, that instead of sweet smell there shall be stink; and instead of a girdle a rent; and instead of well set hair baldness; and instead of a stomacher a girding of sackcloth; and burning instead of beauty.

α.3.25 K8wosketompomog pish penusháog nashpe togkodteg, kah kummenuhkesuene[ú]mog ut ayeuwuttineat.
E.3.25 Thy men shall fall by the sword, and thy mighty in the war.

α.3.26 Kah 8squontamash pish neuantam8m8ash, kah noh nâsiit, pish appu ohkeit.
E.3.26 And her gates shall lament and mourn; and she being desolate shall sit upon the ground.

α.4.1 KAh ne kesukok nesausuk tahsuog mittamwussissog pish togqunáog pasuk8 wosketompuh, n8waog, nummeechimun nehenwonche nuppetukqunneganun, kah nuth[o]gkumun nehenwonche nuthogk8onganun: webe k8wesuonk uss8wésitteaongunan, nutamaunumunnanónut nukkekómitteaonganun.
E.4.1 And in that day seven women shall take hold of one man, saying, We will eat our own bread, and wear our own apparel: only let us be called by thy name, to take away our reproach.

α.4.2 Ne kesukok, 8tuhqunnum Jehovah pish pahkeneunkquot, kah sohsum8eyeu8, kah ummeechummúonk ohke pish wunnegen kah tapeneunkquot, wutche yeug Israelitsog pohquohhogig.
E.4.2 In that day shall the branch of the LORD be beautiful and glorious, and the fruit of the earth shall be excellent and comely for them that are escaped of Israel.

α.4.3 Kah pish n$nih noh ashqunit ut Zion, kah noh ashqunit ut Jerusalem, pish hennau wunneetupanatamwen, nishnoh pasuk noh wâsukuhwhôsit kenugke neg pâmontogig ut Jerusalem
E.4.3 And it shall come to pass, that he that is left in Zion, and he that remaineth in Jerusalem, shall be called holy, even every one that is written among the living in Jerusalem:

α.4.4 Lord amâpadtunk wunnishkeneunkquodt8m8 Zione wuttauneunk, kah pahketeunk Jerusaleme wusqueheonk, wutch ne nôeu, nashpe wussittum8e nashauanit, kah nashpe nashqunnae nashauanit.
E.4.4 When the Lord shall have washed away the filth of the daughters of Zion, and shall have purged the blood of Jerusalem from the midst thereof by the spirit of judgment, and by the spirit of burning.

α.4.5 Kah Jehovah pish kesteau ut nishnoh ayeuonganit ut wadchuut Zion, kah ut umm[ó]eonganéhtu, matokqs kah pukut kesukodáe, kah wôhsum8e n8n8náe n8teau nukkonáeu, newutche ut wame sohsum8onganit pish onk8wôhkussú8nú8.
E.4.5 And the LORD will create upon every dwelling place of mount Zion, and upon her assemblies, a cloud and smoke by day, and the shining of a flaming fire by night: for upon all the glory shall be a defence.

α.4.6 Kah na pish tabernakle, wutch wutonka[u]óhtóm8 wutch kesukodáe kussittaut, kah wutche spuhh8aé ayeuonk, kah wutch abohquos mehshittahshik kah sokanon.
E.4.6 And there shall be a tabernacle for a shadow in the day time from the heat, and for a place of refuge, and for a covert from storm and from rain.

α.5.1 YEuyeu nukket8homau wâmonog, an8homáonk, papaume n8womonog, papaume 8weenominneohteuk: n8womónog 8weenominneohtekoneu ahche mishummeechummúe wadchuut.
E.5.1 Now will I sing to my wellbeloved a song of my beloved touching his vineyard. My wellbeloved hath a vineyard in a very fruitful hill:

α.5.2 Kah uppummeneutauun, kah mukkinnum nish qussukquanash, kah wutohtekontamuneash pepenamwe weenomwussippagwash, kah ayim towér ut nashaue, kah wonk ne wuttittannehteauun wine-presse: kah ukkenompadtamun woh paudtau[ó]m8t weenominneash, kah tannegen touohkomukque weenominneash.
E.5.2 And he fenced it, and gathered out the stones thereof, and planted it with the choicest vine, and built a tower in the midst of it, and also made a winepress therein: and he looked that it should bring forth grapes, and it brought forth wild grapes.

α.5.3 Kah yeuyeu, woi kenaau wadohkeógish Jerusalem, kah Judae wosketompaog, wussittum8k k8wehquetumauonumw8, nashaue nen kah n8weenominneohteuk?
E.5.3 And now, O inhabitants of Jerusalem, and men of Judah, judge, I pray you, betwixt me and my vineyard.

α.5.4 Toh woh wonk uñehteauun n8weenominneohteuk, ne matta á[h]teau8? tohwutch, ashkauwompadtamon woh paudtauóm8 weenominneash, paudtauóm8uk tauohkomukque weenominneash.
E.5.4 What could have been done more to my vineyard, that I have not done in it? wherefore, when I looked that it should bring forth grapes, brought it forth wild grapes?

α.5.5 Kah yeuyeu éhha, kuttinnonuneau uttoh a[h]teáu n8weenominneohteuk: nutamaunum ne pumme[n]eutunk, kah pish mahchipun; kah nussukqunnum ne pummeneutunk kah pish tahtashkuhkomun
E.5.5 And now go to; I will tell you what I will do to my vineyard: I will take away the hedge thereof, and it shall be eaten up; and break down the wall thereof, and it shall be trodden down:

α.5.6 Kah pish n8wôhshwushittea[n]un, kah matta pish wunnehteauun, asuh wônuhkontam8un, qut na pish wutut neekineau kôussog kah asinnekôussog: kah wonk nutann8tam matokqs woh matta missippano sokanunk.
E.5.6 And I will lay it waste: it shall not be pruned, nor digged; but there shall come up briers and thorns: I will also command the clouds that they rain no rain upon it.

α.5.7 Newutche 8weenominneohteuk Jehovah ayeu[t]eaanit, ne wek Israel, kah Judae wosketompoh ne wuttapeneam8e ohketeaonk: kah askauwompattam wussittumóonk, qut kusseh s[o]nkqutcha[w]huttuonk, sampweseonk qut kusseh mauonk.
E.5.7 For the vineyard of the LORD of hosts is the house of Israel, and the men of Judah his pleasant plant: and he looked for judgment, but behold oppression; for righteousness, but behold a cry.

α.5.8 Onkapunáhettich neg ahasuhkauunukeg wetuómash, kah ahasuhkauunukeg ohteuhkonash, noh pajeh matta ayeuonga[n]in8g, onk woh nag nussiyeuog ut nôeu ohkeit.
E.5.8 Woe unto them that join house to house, that lay field to field, till there be no place, that they may be placed alone in the midst of the earth!

α.5.9 Ut nuhtauogut n8wau Jehovah ayeuhteanit, wunnamuhkut monatash wetuómash pish touushin, mogkiyeuash, kah wowunnegenash matta ayéin.
E.5.9 In mine ears said the LORD of hosts, Of a truth many houses shall be desolate, even great and fair, without inhabitant.

α.5.10 Nux, piukque akerseu8 weenominneohteuk, pish wutchegen pasuk bath, kah homere wuskannem pish wutchegen ephah.
E.5.10 Yea, ten acres of vineyard shall yield one bath, and the seed of an homer shall yield an ephah.

α.5.11 Onkapunáhettich neg nompoáe o[X]ohkécheg, onk woh nag asuhkomwog onkup, nag wunnagwutteanumuneau nô pajeh wunnonk88k, nô pajeh wine kussopposikqhettit.
E.5.11 Woe unto them that rise up early in the morning, that they may follow strong drink; that continue until night, till wine inflame them!

α.5.12 Kah harp, kah viol, kah tabret, kah puhpegq, kah wine wutohtauuneau ut mishadtupp8onganit, qut nag matta wutt8antamóog wutanakausuonk Lord, kah matta natwontamóog wunnetchegane anakausuonk
E.5.12 And the harp, and the viol, the tabret, and pipe, and wine, are in their feasts: but they regard not the work of the LORD, neither consider the operation of his hands.

α.5.13 Newaj missináhettit nummissinninneumog, newutche matta 8wahteauonganéog: kah ukquttiánumweneum8uh paskonontamwoh, kah ummuttaán8m8uh nunnassuoh nashpe kûhkuht8[n]8onk.
E.5.13 Therefore my people are gone into captivity, because they have no knowledge: and their honourable men are famished, and their multitude dried up with thirst.

α.5.14 Newaj chepiohkomuk mishe kishkeheont wuhhogkuh, kah mishe wôshwunnum wutt8n, wanne quttuhham8e: kah wussohsum8ongan8 kah umm[u]ttaán8ongan8, kah 8nauwámeongan8, kah noh mashkouá[n]atog, pish na wuttin w8ms[i]u.
E.5.14 Therefore hell hath enlarged herself, and opened her mouth without measure: and their glory, and their multitude, and their pomp, and he that rejoiceth, shall descend into it.

α.5.15 Kah peississitcheg pish tiohquonkhéaog, kah masukenuk pish hohpáheau, k[á]h wuskesuk8oash pehtuánumóog pish hohpóm8ash.
E.5.15 And the mean man shall be brought down, and the mighty man shall be humbled, and the eyes of the lofty shall be humbled:

α.5.16 Qut Jehovah ayeuhteaanit pish misheheau ut wussittum8onganit, kah wunneetupanatamwe God pish wunneetupanatamwe ogquanumau ut sampweusseonganit.
E.5.16 But the LORD of hosts shall be exalted in judgment, and God that is holy shall be sanctified in righteousness.

α.5.17 Neit lambsog pish unnadtupp8og ne áhhunnadtupwéhettit, kah wuttouwashinneume wutayeuongan[ó]ash pen8wohteáog pish wuttit meetsinneau.
E.5.17 Then shall the lambs feed after their manner, and the waste places of the fat ones shall strangers eat.

α.5.18 Onkapunáhettich neg wádto[ntn]uk[e]g panneseonk nashpe tahn8che pemeneohtanash, kah matcheseonk onatuh nashp[é] carte pemeneohtanit.
E.5.18 Woe unto them that draw iniquity with cords of vanity, and sin as it were with a cart rope:

α.5.19 Neg án8wacheg, kenuppe usseitch, kenupanakausitch, onk woh naumunán: kah ukeen8s8wáonk 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, pas8tsh[a]úm8utch, kah peyaum8utch, onk woh n8wahteauuna[n].
E.5.19 That say, Let him make speed, and hasten his work, that we may see it: and let the counsel of the Holy One of Israel draw nigh and come, that we may know it!

α.5.20 Onkapunâhettich nag an8wacheg papaume machuk, ne wunnegen, kah wanegik ne matchet, neg nompatunkig pohkenái wutch wequai, kah wequai wutch pohkenái, neg nompatunkig weesogkon wutch weekon, kah weekon wutch weesogkon.
E.5.20 Woe unto them that call evil good, and good evil; that put darkness for light, and light for darkness; that put bitter for sweet, and sweet for bitter!

α.5.21 Onkapunáhettich nag waantogig ut nehenwonche wuskesuk8óut, kah napwóncheg ut nehenwonche anaquabhettit.
E.5.21 Woe unto them that are wise in their own eyes, and prudent in their own sight!

α.5.22 Onkapun[á]hettich neg manuhke wuttattogig wine, kah menuhk[é]suenuog kenukkeaumunat onkup.
E.5.22 Woe unto them that are mighty to drink wine, and men of strength to mingle strong drink:

α.5.23 Neg sampweogquanumoncheg matcheet8oh wutche onkquatunk, kah amaunumauoncheg wussampweusseongan8 sampwesécheg.
E.5.23 Which justify the wicked for reward, and take away the righteousness of the righteous from him!

α.5.24 Newaj onatuh n8teau mahchukkissuk sequekepunneg, kah n8n8uneau mahchukki[ss]um wussadteámuneash, ne ne 8wadchabuk8 pish anit, kah wunnet8nunk pish o[g]que us[h]pém8 puppissiyeuut, newutche pogketamwog wuttinnaumatuonk Jehovah ayeuhteáanit, kah jishantamwog wuttinn8wáonk 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
E.5.24 Therefore as the fire devoureth the stubble, and the flame consumeth the chaff, so their root shall be as rottenness, and their blossom shall go up as dust: because they have cast away the law of the LORD of hosts, and despised the word of the Holy One of Israel.

α.5.25 Newaj ummusquantam8onk Jehovah ayeuuhkonittue nashqunneau en ummissininneumut, kah mahche ayeuuhkonittue summagunúmauau wunnutcheg, na[h] wuttogkomuh: kah wadchuash nunnukshaash, kah nupp8e wuhhogkáuh nehnehkohkou[X]uh ut nôeu toumaogqu[e]htu: wutch wame yeu, ummusquanittam8onk matta ámaémun8, qut wunnutcheg ashpumme summagunum. 
E.5.25 Therefore is the anger of the LORD kindled against his people, and he hath stretched forth his hand against them, and hath smitten them: and the hills did tremble, and their carcases were torn in the midst of the streets. For all this his anger is not turned away, but his hand is stretched out still.

α.5.26 Kah noh pish tahshinum ensigne wutch nôadtit wutohtimóneat, kah pish ukkehke[m]womuh, wutch wehqshik ohke, kah kusseh, nag pish kenuppe kenupsháe peyaog.
E.5.26 And he will lift up an ensign to the nations from far, and will hiss unto them from the end of the earth: and, behold, they shall come with speed swiftly:

α.5.27 Matta howan pish sauunnum8, asuh togkussittassun8 ut nah kenugke: wanne pish howan ukkogkou[ó]quoh, asuh koueu, kah matta pish mussuk[q]unádtikame puttukquobpus ompenum8un, kah mattógquonápeash matta pish poshkishán8ash.
E.5.27 None shall be weary nor stumble among them; none shall slumber nor sleep; neither shall the girdle of their loins be loosed, nor the latchet of their shoes be broken:

α.5.28 Ukkouhquodt8oash kenag, kah wame wutahtompeyeumoh wutonkqunosuoh, wuthorsese 8kossum8oh pish ogquanumukqussuoh qussukquanit, kah 8wheelum8 ogqueneunkqusseum8 pemsquahut.
E.5.28 Whose arrows are sharp, and all their bows bent, their horses' hoofs shall be counted like flint, and their wheels like a whirlwind:

α.5.29 OOwadtauatonkqussuongan8 pish tatuppeyeu8 qunnonouut, nag pish ogquont8aog wuske qunnonouut: nux, nag pish mishont8waog, & togqunumwog sequttahhamukeh, kah pish 8wohque moncha[u]ouh, kah wanne howan pish uppohquohwhunuh.
E.5.29 Their roaring shall be like a lion, they shall roar like young lions: yea, they shall roar, and lay hold of the prey, and shall carry it away safe, and none shall deliver it.

α.5.30 Kah ne kesukok nah pish ummishont8waounouh, onatuh mashont8wom8uk keitoh: kah howan monunneog ohke, kusseh pohkenai kah unkquanumoonk, kah wequáei pohkenahteauun ut ukkesukquehteaum8ouh.
E.5.30 And in that day they shall roar against them like the roaring of the sea: and if one look unto the land, behold darkness and sorrow, and the light is darkened in the heavens thereof.

α.6.1 NE kodtum8k ketass8t Uzziah napuk, wonk nunnauomp Lord quenappu appuonganit, qunuhque kah tahshinau: kah ne asukunkqut numwohteau templeut.
E.6.1 In the year that king Uzziah died I saw also the LORD sitting upon a throne, high and lifted up, and his train filled the temple.

α.6.2 Wa[a]be neepoog seraphimsog, nish$noh pasuk nequtta tahshe nuppohwhunau, nashpe nees8oh onkquequohhou, nashpe nees8oh onkhum wusseetash, kah nashpe nees8oh pt8wu.
E.6.2 Above it stood the seraphims: each one had six wings; with twain he covered his face, and with twain he covered his feet, and with twain he did fly.

α.6.3 Kah pasuk mishont8wohtauau onkatogeh, kah n8wau wunneetupantam, wunneetupantam, wunneetupantam Jehovah ayeuhteaanit, mamusse ohke numwohteau wussohsumoonk.
E.6.3 And one cried unto another, and said, Holy, holy, holy, is the LORD of hosts: the whole earth is full of his glory.

α.6.4 Kah squontame nepattunkquongash o[n]tahtaash nahspe 8wadtauatonkqussuonk noh mashont8adt, & wetuomut numwohta pukut
E.6.4 And the posts of the door moved at the voice of him that cried, and the house was filled with smoke.

α.6.5 Neit nussip nutonkapunam, newutche nuttammetahwhit, newutche nen nishkeneungwe mussissitt8ne wosketomp kah nuttai nashaue nishkeneungque mussissitt8ne missinninnuog: newutche nuskesukquash naau ketass8t, Jehovah ayeuteaanit.
E.6.5 Then said I, Woe is me! for I am undone; because I am a man of unclean lips, and I dwell in the midst of a people of unclean lips: for mine eyes have seen the King, the LORD of hosts.

α.6.6 Neit pasuk Seraphim unnunau nuhhogkat, n8tae mohkus ohteau wunnutcheganit ne nemunuk nashpe tongs wutch Altarut.
E.6.6 Then flew one of the seraphims unto me, having a live coal in his hand, which he had taken with the tongs from off the altar:

α.6.7 Kah mussikquomwahtou nutt8n, kah n8wau, kusseh, yeu mussuhkom8m8 kussisset8nash, kah kummatcheseonk amaunumun; kah kuppanneseonk pahketeauun.
E.6.7 And he laid it upon my mouth, and said, Lo, this hath touched thy lips; and thine iniquity is taken away, and thy sin purged.

α.6.8 Wonk nunn8tam 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Lord, n8wau, howan woh negont8waeh, kah howan woh moncheaunshikqueog? neit nussip, nen yeu, ann8neh.
E.6.8 Also I heard the voice of the Lord, saying, Whom shall I send, and who will go for us? Then said I, Here am I; send me.

α.6.9 Kah n8wau, monchish, us yeug missinninnuog, wunnamuhkut n8tam8k, qut wohtam8hteogk: kah wunnamuhkut naum8k, qut wahteau8hteogk.
E.6.9 And he said, Go, and tell this people, Hear ye indeed, but understand not; and see ye indeed, but perceive not.

α.6.10 Wunogquehteaha yeug missinninnuog, kah tuhkequtteauush  wuhtauog8oash, kah yanunush wuskesuk8oash: ishkont nag wutch naumwog wuskesuk8out, kah n8tamwog wutch wuhtauog8oash, kah wohtamwog wutch wuttahhou, kah woh quinnuppeog kah neetskeheaog.
E.6.10 Make the heart of this people fat, and make their ears heavy, and shut their eyes; lest they see with their eyes, and hear with their ears, and understand with their heart, and convert, and be healed.

α.6.11 Neit nussip, Lord, toh utt8che? kah namp8ham, nô pajeh keitotanash mohtupp[a]em8ug, ne toh ut wanne wutohkenat, kah weetuomash wanne wosketompaun8it, kah ohke tóuushinée touushinit.
E.6.11 Then said I, Lord, how long? And he answered, Until the cities be wasted without inhabitant, and the houses without man, and the land be utterly desolate,

α.6.12 Kah Jehovah amaunont missinninnuh en nôadtit, kah na mishe nukkodtum8onganu8uk ut nashaue ohkeit.
E.6.12 And the LORD have removed men far away, and there be a great forsaking in the midst of the land.

α.6.13 Qut onch pish piogque chippag ohteau, kah pish quinnuppem8, kah pish ogque meechin Tyluhtugqut, kah onatuh n8times ashkunkquamuuk mahchippogkok: netatuppe wunneetupanatamwe wuskannem ne pish wutashkunkquamuonk.
E.6.13 But yet in it shall be a tenth, and it shall return, and shall be eaten: as a teil tree, and as an oak, whose substance is in them, when they cast their leaves: so the holy seed shall be the substance thereof.

α.7.1 KAh nniyeup pamontog Ahaz wunnaumonuh Jotham, wunnaumonuh Uzziah Judae ketass8t, Rezin Syriae ketass8t, kah Pekah wunnaumonuh Remaliah Israelle ketass8t, kuhkuhqueog nogque en Jerusalem, wutayeuuhkontamunaoont, qut wunn8numuneau sohkomunat.
E.7.1 And it came to pass in the days of Ahaz the son of Jotham, the son of Uzziah, king of Judah, that Rezin the king of Syria, and Pekah the son of Remaliah, king of Israel, went up toward Jerusalem to war against it, but could not prevail against it.

α.7.2 Kah unnon wek David, n8wo[u], Siria wet8womau Ephraimoh, kah wuttah ontohteau, kah wuttahhou ummissinninneumoh, onatuh touohkomukque mehtugquash mamontanuhtog waban.
E.7.2 And it was told the house of David, saying, Syria is confederate with Ephraim. And his heart was moved, and the heart of his people, as the trees of the wood are moved with the wind.

α.7.3 Neit Jehovah unnau Isaiáhoh, sohhash yeuyeu nogkushkauonat Ahaz, ken, kah Shearjashub, kenaumon, wutchehtanniyeu kuhkuhqueeu nippessepagwe Conduit$ut, kehchemayog fullerse wutohteakonit.
E.7.3 Then said the LORD unto Isaiah, Go forth now to meet Ahaz, thou, and Shearjashub thy son, at the end of the conduit of the upper pool in the highway of the fuller's field;

α.7.4 Kah us; nunnikqusish, kah chequnapsh: wabes[e]hkon asuh wabesuitteahuhkon newutche neesukqunnom8ugish yeush pukuttae pohquttaash, newutche ummishe musquantam8onk Rezin weeche Siria, kah wunnaumonuh Remaliah.
E.7.4 And say unto him, Take heed, and be quiet; fear not, neither be fainthearted for the two tails of these smoking firebrands, for the fierce anger of Rezin with Syria, and of the son of Remaliah.

α.7.5 Newutche Syria, Ephraim Kah wunnaumonuh Remaliah, matche ken8nittuog ayeuuhkonittue ken, n8waog,
E.7.5 Because Syria, Ephraim, and the son of Remaliah, have taken evil counsel against thee, saying,

α.7.6 Ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquehtauontuh Judah, kah n8chumwehteadtuh, kah naut ayimontuh to[u]wutchahtham8onk, kah ketass8t ponontuh nashaue, wunnaumonuh Tabeal.
E.7.6 Let us go up against Judah, and vex it, and let us make a breach therein for us, and set a king in the midst of it, even the son of Tabeal:

α.7.7 Kah yeu wussin Lord Jehovah, matta pish menuhkohtano, kah matta pish nnano,
E.7.7 Thus saith the Lord GOD, It shall not stand, neither shall it come to pass.

α.7.8 Newutche uppuhkuk Syria, ne Damascus, kah uppuhkuk Damascus noh Rezin, kah wuttúhshit nequtta tahshinchage kodtum8it kah napanna, Ephraim pish sohquttahwhau, matta ummissinninnu8uneat.
E.7.8 For the head of Syria is Damascus, and the head of Damascus is Rezin; and within threescore and five years shall Ephraim be broken, that it be not a people.

α.7.9 Kah uppuhkuk Ephraim, ne Samaria, kah uppuhkuk Samaria, noh wunnaumonuh Remaliah: matta wunnamptam8óg wunnamuhkut matta pish kummenuhkappe[u]mw8.
E.7.9 And the head of Ephraim is Samaria, and the head of Samaria is Remaliah's son. If ye will not believe, surely ye shall not be established.

α.7.10 Nano wonk Jehovah ken8nau Ahazoh n8wau,
E.7.10 Moreover the LORD spake again unto Ahaz, saying,

α.7.11 Wehquetumau Jehovah kuhkinneasuonk wutche ken; wehquetush asuh ut m8n[ó]iyeuut, asuh qunuhqueé ut wóhqut.
E.7.11 Ask thee a sign of the LORD thy God; ask it either in the depth, or in the height above.

α.7.12 Qut Ahaz n8wau, matta n8wehquetum8, kah matta nukqutchheau Jehovah.
E.7.12 But Ahaz said, I will not ask, neither will I tempt the LORD.

α.7.13 Kah n8wau, n8tam8k yeuyeu, woi wek David; sun peásin ken kussauunonat wosketompaog, qut wonk kussauunnumw8 num-Manitt8m?
E.7.13 And he said, Hear ye now, O house of David; Is it a small thing for you to weary men, but will ye weary my God also?

α.7.14 Newaj Lord nehenwonche nagum aninnumunkqueóg kuhkinneasuonk: Kusseh, penomp pish wompequoou, kah neechau wunnaumoniinneuh, & pish wuttissowenuh Immanuel.
E.7.14 Therefore the Lord himself shall give you a sign; Behold, a virgin shall conceive, and bear a son, and shall call his name Immanuel.

α.7.15 Butter kah hony pish peech, onk woh wahteou sekeneamunat machuk, kah pepenamunat wanegik.
E.7.15 Butter and honey shall he eat, that he may know to refuse the evil, and choose the good.

α.7.16 Newutche asquam mukkies wahteou sekeneamunat machuk, kah pepenamunat wanegik, ohke ne jishantaman, pish ohquanumau naneeswe ukketass8tamómuh.
E.7.16 For before the child shall know to refuse the evil, and choose the good, the land that thou abhorrest shall be forsaken of both her kings.

α.7.17 Jehovah pish kuppaudtunk, kah ut kummissinninneumut, kah ut k8sh weekit, kesukodtash nish asq paómun8gish, wutch na kesukok Ephraim chabeit wutch Judah; noh Assyriae ketass8t.
E.7.17 The LORD shall bring upon thee, and upon thy people, and upon thy father's house, days that have not come, from the day that Ephraim departed from Judah; even the king of Assyria.

α.7.18 Kah pish nnih, ne kesukok Jehovah pish quekqsumau 8cháussoh, noh aongkoue Egypte sepuésut, kah Bee noh Assyriae ohkeit.
E.7.18 And it shall come to pass in that day, that the LORD shall hiss for the fly that is in the uttermost part of the rivers of Egypt, and for the bee that is in the land of Assyria.

α.7.19 Kah nag pish peyaog, kah wame pish appuog ut touushinne 8nôuhkóiyeuut, kah en hassinn[ê]kómukqut, kah ut wame assinn[e]kôussehtu, kah ut wame chipishinneuhtugquehtu.
E.7.19 And they shall come, and shall rest all of them in the desolate valleys, and in the holes of the rocks, and upon all thorns, and upon all bushes.

α.7.20 Ne$nan kesukok, Lord pish chequodtweyaheau nashpe chequodtweyáheg, n[e]h onkquattauoncheh nashpe neg ogkomut apitcheg, nashpe Assyriae ketass8t, muppuhkuk kah wusseete wishagkinash: kah pish wonk mohtupanum weeshitt8unash.
E.7.20 In the same day shall the Lord shave with a razor that is hired, namely, by them beyond the river, by the king of Assyria, the head, and the hair of the feet: and it shall also consume the beard.

α.7.21 Kah pish nnih ne kesukok, wosketomp pish wadch[a]nau wuske cowishinneoh, kah nes8oh sheepsoh.
E.7.21 And it shall come to pass in that day, that a man shall nourish a young cow, and two sheep;

α.7.22 Kah pish nnih, newutche madtaaneuk sogkodtunk ne adtahshipagsehettit, pish meech butter; newutche butter kah hony, nishnoh pasuk pish ummeechin noh sequnit ut ohkeit.
E.7.22 And it shall come to pass, for the abundance of milk that they shall give he shall eat butter: for butter and honey shall every one eat that is left in the land.

α.7.23 Kah pish nnih ne kesukok, nishnoh ayeuonk, uttoh adt nequt muttannonganogok weenomwussippagwash anôadtik silvere nequt muttannonganogkodtash, ne pish kôussu8 kah asinnekôussu8.
E.7.23 And it shall come to pass in that day, that every place shall be, where there were a thousand vines at a thousand silverlings, it shall even be for briers and thorns.

α.7.24 Nashpe kôuhquodtash kah ahtompeh wosketompaog na pish wuttit peyoneau, newutche wame ohke pish kôussu8, kah asinnekôussu8.
E.7.24 With arrows and with bows shall men come thither; because all the land shall become briers and thorns.

α.7.25 Kah wame wadchuash nish pish kodhamukish nashpe mattock, na matta pish peyomun8 qushaonk k[ó]ussog kah asinnekóussog: qut ne pish sohwhun[ó]naóont oxinog, kah wuttattashkuhkomunaóont papeississitcheg neetasuog.
E.7.25 And on all hills that shall be digged with the mattock, there shall not come thither the fear of briers and thorns: but it shall be for the sending forth of oxen, and for the treading of lesser cattle.

α.8.1 NAno, Jehovah nuttinuk, neemunush mishe tuttuppagenausu, kah ne wussukwhush nashpe wosketompae pen, papaume Maher-shal$al$hash-baz.
E.8.1 Moreover the LORD said unto me, Take thee a great roll, and write in it with a man's pen concerning Mahershalalhashbaz.

α.8.2 Kah nunneemunnumom pabuhtanumwe wauwaénuog mehquontamunat, Uriah sephausuen kah Zechariah wunnaumonuh Jeberechiah.
E.8.2 And I took unto me faithful witnesses to record, Uriah the priest, and Zechariah the son of Jeberechiah.

α.8.3 Kah nuppas8sukauomp mittamwossisse quoshodtumwáen, kah wompequoou, kah neechau wunnaumonuh: neit Jehovah nuttinuk, uss8wes Maher-shal-al-hash-baz.
E.8.3 And I went unto the prophetess; and she conceived, and bare a son. Then said the LORD to me, Call his name Mahershalalhashbaz.

α.8.4 Newutche mukkies asquam wahteau8gkup n8wónat, n8sh kah nokas, Damascusse weenauwetuongash, kah Samariae sequttahamóonk, pish amaunau ut anaquabit Assyriae ketass8t.
E.8.4 For before the child shall have knowledge to cry, My father, and my mother, the riches of Damascus and the spoil of Samaria shall be taken away before the king of Assyria.

α.8.5 Jehovah wonk nukken8nuk n8wau,
E.8.5 The LORD spake also unto me again, saying,

α.8.6 Newutche yeug missinninnúog sekeneamwog Shiloahe nippeash, nish mánunnutch[uo]gish, kah weekontamwog ut Rezin, kah wunnaumonat Remaliah:
E.8.6 Forasmuch as this people refuseth the waters of Shiloah that go softly, and rejoice in Rezin and Remaliah's son;

α.8.7 
E.8.7 Now therefore, behold, the Lord bringeth up upon them the waters of the river, strong and many, even the king of Assyria, and all his glory: and he shall come up over all his channels, and go over all his banks:

α.8.8 Kah noh pish paumushau Judah, noh pish anúpadto, kah pish anúchuan, pish sokkoshkittuk8, kah nean sep[á]ginont wunnuppuhwhunash, pish numwohteau ne koshkag kutohke, woi Immanuel.
E.8.8 And he shall pass through Judah; he shall overflow and go over, he shall reach even to the neck; and the stretching out of his wings shall fill the breadth of thy land, O Immanuel.

α.8.9 Miyán8k kuhhogkaóog, woi kenaau missinninnúog, kah pish kussukqutteawhuteamw8, kah n8tam8k, wame kenaau nôohtáe wutohtimóneash, puttukquobpissegk, kah pish kussukqutteawhutteamw8, puttukquobpissegk, kah pish kussukqutteawhutteamw8.
E.8.9 Associate yourselves, O ye people, and ye shall be broken in pieces; and give ear, all ye of far countries: gird yourselves, and ye shall be broken in pieces; gird yourselves, and ye shall be broken in pieces.

α.8.10 Moáe ken8nittegk, kah pish matteagwunninno: n8wagk kutt8wonk, kah matta menuhkotano: newutche God k8weetomukqun.
E.8.10 Take counsel together, and it shall come to nought; speak the word, and it shall not stand: for God is with us.

α.8.11 Newutche Lord yeu nuttin ken8nukqun, nashpe menuhki menutcheg, kah nukkuhk8tomunk matta woh nuppomushóunat ummayeuóut yeug missinninnúog, n8wau,
E.8.11 For the LORD spake thus to me with a strong hand, and instructed me that I should not walk in the way of this people, saying,

α.8.12 N8wáhteogk, weetuódtuonk en wame nag, n[e]h pish ánoncheh yeuh missinninnuh, weetu[u]ódtuonk: kah ahque quihtam8k nag qushaongan8, asuh wabesehteogk.
E.8.12 Say ye not, A confederacy, to all them to whom this people shall say, A confederacy; neither fear ye their fear, nor be afraid.

α.8.13 Wunneetupanatamwe ogquanumok Jehovah ayeuteaanit nagum, kah noh qush8k, k[a]h noh wabesu[óm]8k.
E.8.13 Sanctify the LORD of hosts himself; and let him be your fear, and let him be your dread.

α.8.14 Kah noh pish Sanctuarih88, togkussittass[im]8e qussuk, kah chamsquassunóe hassun, en naneeswe Israelle wekuóo[n]t: wutch appeh, kah sinnukkeg wutch neg wadóhkitcheg Jerusalem.
E.8.14 And he shall be for a sanctuary; but for a stone of stumbling and for a rock of offence to both the houses of Israel, for a gin and for a snare to the inhabitants of Jerusalem.

α.8.15 Kah monaog na ut kenugke pish togkussittassunwog, kah kepshaog, kah pish sohqussunwog, kah pish puttahhamwog, kah pish togqunóog.
E.8.15 And many among them shall stumble, and fall, and be broken, and be snared, and be taken.

α.8.16 Weesquabenuash wauwaonk, sealoh naumatuonk ut kenugke nunnetuhtauw[á]en[e]umut.
E.8.16 Bind up the testimony, seal the law among my disciples.

α.8.17 Kah nuppah Lord, noh padtogguhhuk wuskesuk wutch Jakob, kah nutaskauwompam[,]
E.8.17 And I will wait upon the LORD, that hideth his face from the house of Jacob, and I will look for him.

α.8.18 Kusseh, nen kah mukkiog neh Jehovah anummiitcheh, nukkehkinneásuonganeumun, kah nummonchanatam8onganeumun ut Israelut: wutch Jehovah ayeuteaanit, noh ayit wadchuut Zion.
E.8.18 Behold, I and the children whom the LORD hath given me are for signs and for wonders in Israel from the LORD of hosts, which dwelleth in mount Zion.

α.8.19 Kah nag unnukqueog, natinneah8k neg wámatchinahshaóngan[ú]mitcheg, kah mamontamáog, neg peant8wácheg, kah tadtumwácheg: sunnummatta woh missinninnuog natinnewhauóog um-Manitt8m8oh? wutch pomontamunutcheh en neh napunutcheh?
E.8.19 And when they shall say unto you, Seek unto them that have familiar spirits, and unto wizards that peep, and that mutter: should not a people seek unto their God? for the living to the dead?

α.8.20 En naumatuonganit, kah en wauwaonganit: matta n8wahetteg neaunak yeu kutt8wonk, yeu, newutche matta wequaiyeumu.
E.8.20 To the law and to the testimony: if they speak not according to this word, it is because there is no light in them.

α.8.21 Kah nag pish auwakonche kah kodtupp8e uppannupushoneau: kah pish nnih, nag kodtupwehettit, nag pish m8m8skumáog wuhhogkauh, kah matanumaog ukketass8tam8m8oh, kah um$Manitt8m8oh kah pish ushpuhquaéog.
E.8.21 And they shall pass through it, hardly bestead and hungry: and it shall come to pass, that when they shall be hungry, they shall fret themselves, and curse their king and their God, and look upward.

α.8.22 Kah nag pish monunneamwog ohke, kah kusseh wuttamehpunáonk, kah pohkenái, pogkenum[ó]e wuttamehpunáonk, kah nag pish n8hkauôog en pohkenahtu.
E.8.22 And they shall look unto the earth; and behold trouble and darkness, dimness of anguish; and they shall be driven to darkness.

α.9.1 QUt onch, pohkennumóonk matta pish neanéinn8, wunn8wadtaméhpunadt, negonne ogguhse onkapunadtunk Zebulone ohke, kah Naphtalie ohke, kah ompetak, wutúhque onkquanu[m]wéheuh, ut kehtahhanne mayit, ogkomut Jordan, ut wutohtimóinne Galile.
E.9.1 Nevertheless the dimness shall not be such as was in her vexation, when at the first he lightly afflicted the land of Zebulun and the land of Naphtali, and afterward did more grievously afflict her by the way of the sea, beyond Jordan, in Galilee of the nations.

α.9.2 Missinninnúog neg pomushácheg pohkenahtu naumwog mishe wequai: neg wadohkitcheg nupp8ongane onkauohtáe ohkeit, neh 8wôhsumauoh.
E.9.2 The people that walked in darkness have seen a great light: they that dwell in the land of the shadow of death, upon them hath the light shined.

α.9.3 Kummuttaanteóh wutohtimóneas, kah matta nano mishehteaou wekontamóonk: weekontamwog ut anaquabean, neaunak kepenumwe weekontamóonk, kah neáhhenn8weekontamwéhettit wosketompaog, chachabenumohetticheh sequttahhamóonk.
E.9.3 Thou hast multiplied the nation, and not increased the joy: they joy before thee according to the joy in harvest, and as men rejoice when they divide the spoil.

α.9.4 Newutche kussohqutahham 8wéassue yoakumoh, kah wuttippomóne anwohhou: wussonkqutchóh8wae pogkommunk, neane ut Midiane kesukodtut.
E.9.4 For thou hast broken the yoke of his burden, and the staff of his shoulder, the rod of his oppressor, as in the day of Midian.

α.9.5 Newutche nishnoh wutayeuwuttuonk ayeuhteaen, ne wodtauatonkquodt, kah hogk8unash unuhkónash ut wusqueheonganit, qut yeu pish nashpe chikkósuonk, kah n8tae wuttuhqunash.
E.9.5 For every battle of the warrior is with confused noise, and garments rolled in blood; but this shall be with burning and fuel of fire.

α.9.6 Newutche ut kuhhogkanónut mukkies neetu, ut en kuhhogkanónut Wunnaumoniin magun, kah nanaánittuonk pish ohteau ut wuttukeit: kah pish ussowesu Monchanu nukqussuaen Ken8s8waénin, Manuhkésit God, Machemapit Wut8shimau, Wunohteáe Sontim.
E.9.6 For unto us a child is born, unto us a son is given: and the government shall be upon his shoulder: and his name shall be called Wonderful, Counsellor, The mighty God, The everlasting Father, The Prince of Peace.

α.9.7 Kah matta pish wohkukquoshininno nano missáe wunnanawunnum[o]onk, kah wunohteáonk, ut wutâppuonganit David, kah ut wutass8tam8onganit, wunohtauunat, kah menehkheonat, nashpe wussittumóonk kah s[á]mpweseonk, yeu$wutch onk yean micheme: wus$zealum Lord ayeuhtea[a]nit yeu pish wutussen. 
E.9.7 Of the increase of his government and peace there shall be no end, upon the throne of David, and upon his kingdom, to order it, and to establish it with judgment and with justice from henceforth even for ever. The zeal of the LORD of hosts will perform this.

α.9.8 Lord negonshhuau kutt8onk en Jakobut, kah upp[a]gs8kqun Israel.
E.9.8 The Lord sent a word into Jacob, and it hath lighted upon Israel.

α.9.9 Kah wame missinninnúog pish wahteauog, Ephraim kah wadohkitcheg Samaria, neg pi[t]uánumóe kah menehketeaháe an8wacheg.
E.9.9 And all the people shall know, even Ephraim and the inhabitant of Samaria, that say in the pride and stoutness of heart,

α.9.10 Briksash penushaash, qut pish n8weekitteahtómun wunnáguttahham8e qussukquanash: Sycomorúhtugquash tummehthamunash, qut pish nutôs8wunnununnánonash en cedaruhtugqut.
E.9.10 The bricks are fallen down, but we will build with hewn stones: the sycomores are cut down, but we will change them into cedars.

α.9.11 Newaj Jehovah pish ayeuuhkonittue wunoht[a]uou ummatwomoh Rezinoh, kah weech8hamau ummatwomoh.
E.9.11 Therefore the LORD shall set up the adversaries of Rezin against him, and join his enemies together;

α.9.12 Syriansog negonáeu, kah Philistiansog wuttát, kah nag mahchipp8og Israeloh nashpe woshwohtáe mutt8n: newutche yeu waame, ummusquanittam8onk matta am[a]émun8, qut wunnutcheg ashpumme su[n]maguna[u]sh.
E.9.12 The Syrians before, and the Philistines behind; and they shall devour Israel with open mouth. For all this his anger is not turned away, but his hand is stretched out still.

α.9.13 Ne[u]utche missinninnuog matta quinnuppeog en néh togkomukquehetticheh, kah matta natinneahwho8og Jehovah ayeuhteaanit.
E.9.13 For the people turneth not unto him that smiteth them, neither do they seek the LORD of hosts.

α.9.14 Newaj Jehovah tummehthog wutch Israelut muhpuhkuk, kah wussukqun, wuhtuk puppishashquash ut pasuk kesukodtut.
E.9.14 Therefore the LORD will cut off from Israel head and tail, branch and rush, in one day.

α.9.15 Kohchisu8it, kah quohtianumukqussit, noh muppuhkuk88; kah quoshodtumwaen noh kohk8tomwehteadt pann8waongash, noh wussukqu[n]eiyeu.
E.9.15 The ancient and honourable, he is the head; and the prophet that teacheth lies, he is the tail.

α.9.16 Newutche sampshano[n]cheg yeuh missinninnuh uppanneseaheouh, kah neg neh sagkompagunukqhetticheh paguanuoh.
E.9.16 For the leaders of this people cause them to err; and they that are led of them are destroyed.

α.9.17 Newaj matta Lord woh weekontamuonunk wuskeneuh, asuh matta pish monanumôou touwyesoh, kah sekousquoh, newutche nish$noh p[a]suk eiantogkei, kah matcheseaenin, kah nish$noh mutt8n as8tueyeum8: newutche yeu wame, matta ummusquanittam8onk qushkemun8, qut ash s[um]ogohteau wunnutcheg.
E.9.17 Therefore the LORD shall have no joy in their young men, neither shall have mercy on their fatherless and widows: for every one is an hypocrite and an evildoer, and every mouth speaketh folly. For all this his anger is not turned away, but his hand is stretched out still.

α.9.18 Newutche matcheseonk ogque chikohteau n8taut: pish mahchukiswau kôussoh kah assinnekôussoh, kah pish nashqunneau touo[h]komukque kuppahtu, kah neg pish ogque waabpem8uk pukuttau.
E.9.18 For wickedness burneth as the fire: it shall devour the briers and thorns, and shall kindle in the thickets of the forest, and they shall mount up like the lifting up of smoke.

α.9.19 Nashpe ummusquanittam8onk Jehovah ayeuteaunit ohke pohkenai kah pish missinninnuog ogqunneunkqussuog ne woh chogkohtag: wanne pish howan kushpaoou weematuh.
E.9.19 Through the wrath of the LORD of hosts is the land darkened, and the people shall be as the fuel of the fire: no man shall spare his brother.

α.9.20 Kah pish wuttinnohkounit wutch neemp8au kah pish onch kodtupp8, k[a]h pish menadchipp8, kah matta pish tap[e]p8og, nag pish meechwog nish$noh pasuk wuhpitteanue weyaus.
E.9.20 And he shall snatch on the right hand, and be hungry; and he shall eat on the left hand, and they shall not be satisfied: they shall eat every man the flesh of his own arm:

α.9.21 M[e]nasseh, Ephraimoh, kah Ephraim Manassehoh: kah nag na moeu pish ayeuuhkon[á]og Judahoh.
E.9.21 Manasseh, Ephraim; and Ephraim, Manasseh: and they together shall be against Judah. For all this his anger is not turned away, but his hand is stretched out still.


α.9.22 Newutche yeu$wutch wame, ummusquantam8onk matta qushkemun8h, qut ash sumogohteau wunnutcheg.

α.10.1 MIssi wutonkapunnaongan8 kohk8wachég mat sampweusseae naumatuongash: kah wosukuhh8keg ûhquanum8ongash, nash kohkinnum8hettichish.
E.10.1 Woe unto them that decree unrighteous decrees, and that write grievousness which they have prescribed;

α.10.2 Qushkeheonao[u]t quenahukqutcheg wutch wussittum8onganit, kah ama[u]numauonat wussampwohtoongan8 wutch machekitcheg: onk woh sekousquoh tohquomáog: onk woh nag mukk8ki[n]ó[o]g touwiêsoh.
E.10.2 To turn aside the needy from judgment, and to take away the right from the poor of my people, that widows may be their prey, and that they may rob the fatherless!

α.10.3 Kah toh woh kutussemw8 natauwahuwae kesukok, kah pagu[a]nuonk peyont wutch n8adtut? howan pish kutushphouonomw8 wutch kuttannumunkqunnaout? kah uttoh pish kénukkodtumunneau kussohsumoongan8?
E.10.3 And what will ye do in the day of visitation, and in the desolation which shall come from far? to whom will ye flee for help? and where will ye leave your glory?

α.10.4 M[e]hcheu nen, nag pish n[à]uwaehtauaog kuppishagkinnuw[h]enuh, kah nag pish penushaog agwu nohshitcheg: yeu nashpu wame, asquam qushkemun8 ummusqu[an]tam8onk qut askq wuñutcheg sussumohogteau.
E.10.4 Without me they shall bow down under the prisoners, and they shall fall under the slain. For all this his anger is not turned away, but his hand is stretched out still.

α.10.5 Woi wut-Assyrian nummusquantam8e sasamatuhh8waontug, kah ne anwohhou ut wunnutchegan8wout, ne nummusquanittam8onk.
E.10.5 O Assyrian, the rod of mine anger, and the staff in their hand is mine indignation.

α.10.6 Nutann8noog ayuuhkontamunat eiantukeiyeue wutohtimoin, kah ayeuuhkononat missinninnuog n[e]g musquanumogig nuttinninnumau meechummuonk nemunnumunat sequehtahhamukish, kah nemunnumunat wutohqu[a]muwaongan8, kah tahtasku[h]kauonaoont onatuh matehchuogkok tau8maogwash.
E.10.6 I will send him against an hypocritical nation, and against the people of my wrath will I give him a charge, to take the spoil, and to take the prey, and to tread them down like the mire of the streets.

α.10.7 Qut matta ne ukkodsei[n], onk wuttah maata ne wuttenamam8un: qut ne wuttahh8wout, paguanonat, kah koshksumunat wutohtimoneash matta ogguhsinash.
E.10.7 Howbeit he meaneth not so, neither doth his heart think so; but it is in his heart to destroy and cut off nations not a few.

α.10.8 Newutche n8w[a]u sunnummatta nussontimomog pannuppe kehtass8tam8og?
E.10.8 For he saith, Are not my princes altogether kings?

α.10.9 Suñummatta Calmo, neane Carchemish? Sunnummatta Hamath neane Arphad? sunnummatta Samaria neane Damaskus?
E.10.9 Is not Calno as Carchemish? is not Hamath as Arpad? is not Samaria as Damascus?

α.10.10 Neane nunnutcheg namehteau nunneukontungane kehtass8tam8ongash; kah neg unnunneukontunkanog anue mishanumukqussuog, onk neg wadchiitcheg Jerusalem kah Samaria
E.10.10 As my hand hath found the kingdoms of the idols, and whose graven images did excel them of Jerusalem and of Samaria;

α.10.11 Neane nea[n]teau Samaria kah neh wuttinneu[x]o[h]tunkanoh, Sunnummatta ne nan woh nuttinteauouun Jerusalem, kah wuttinneukontunkanoh? 
E.10.11 Shall I not, as I have done unto Samaria and her idols, so do to Jerusalem and her idols?

α.10.12 Newajeh pish n$nahk, ne Lord pogkojteunk wame wutanakausuonk ut wadchuut Sion, kah ut Jerusalem, nussasamatuhham ummeechummuonk máhshetahh8wae ketass8t ut Assyria, kah wussohsumóe quonohquttauwompuonk.
E.10.12 Wherefore it shall come to pass, that when the Lord hath performed his whole work upon mount Zion and on Jerusalem, I will punish the fruit of the stout heart of the king of Assyria, and the glory of his high looks.

α.10.13 Newutche n8wau, nashpe nunnutchegane menuhkesuonk yeu nutussen, kah nashpe n8waantamóonk, newutche nutompuwussuénúh: kah nutontahtoh ukkuhkinonkanóash missinninnuog, kah nummukk8kinóog wunnompak8unóash, kah nuttinnuhkauóog neg noh wadohkitcheg, onatuh menuhkesuenuut.
E.10.13 For he saith, By the strength of my hand I have done it, and by my wisdom; for I am prudent: and I have removed the bounds of the people, and have robbed their treasures, and I have put down the inhabitants like a valiant man:

α.10.14 Kah nunnutcheg mehqunum 8weenauwetuongan8ash misinninnuog, neáne wadchishadt: & neáne mohmounuk wôanash, uttiyeush sequnumukish, nuttinne mohmóunumun wame ohke, kah wanne howan wutt8we wuttauóuunash, asuh wôhshinum8 wutt8n, asuh sesék8.
E.10.14 And my hand hath found as a nest the riches of the people: and as one gathereth eggs that are left, have I gathered all the earth; and there was none that moved the wing, or opened the mouth, or peeped.

α.10.15 Sun togkunk woh waenomau wuhhogkuh ayuuhkononat neh kauhunkquahukqutche: asuh poksunkquonk sun woh mishehheau wuhhogkuh ayeuuhkonau neh mâmamóntinukqutcheh? neáne sauobpunk nehenwonche mâmamo[n]tshont ayeuuhkonónát ashpunukqutcheh, asuh neàne anwohhou nehenwonche ushpéit, neane matta mahtugk88uk. 
E.10.15 Shall the axe boast itself against him that heweth therewith? or shall the saw magnify itself against him that shaketh it? as if the rod should shake itself against them that lift it up, or as if the staff should lift up itself, as if it were no wood.

α.10.16 Newajeh Lord, um-Manitt8m8uh kehche8shaog, pish ununau ônauwussinutcheh, ut kenugke waonogqutcheg, kah ut agwe wussohsum8onganit, pish pasqunnánum ch[i]kohsumóo[n]k, neane n8tae chiko[k]sum8ongánit.
E.10.16 Therefore shall the Lord, the Lord of hosts, send among his fat ones leanness; and under his glory he shall kindle a burning like the burning of a fire.

α.10.17 Kah 8wequa8m Israel ne pish n8to8, kah 8neetupanatam8moh noh n8n8uneau: kah pish nashqutteau, kah mahchekuswau wutásinnekôsumoh, kah ukkôussumoh ut pasuk kesukodtut.
E.10.17 And the light of Israel shall be for a fire, and his Holy One for a flame: and it shall burn and devour his thorns and his briers in one day;

α.10.18 Kah pish mahchikussum wuttouohkomukque sohsumóonk, kah ummissegane ohteuk, naneeswe keteahogkou kah muhhog: kah nag pish ogqueneungqussuog noh kôunuk muttô[a]gk, sauwunuk.
E.10.18 And shall consume the glory of his forest, and of his fruitful field, both soul and body: and they shall be as when a standard-bearer fainteth.

α.10.19 Kah sequeneádtunkish wuttouohkomukque mehtugquash pish ogguhsinash, onk woh mukkies 8sukuhhumunash.
E.10.19 And the rest of the trees of his forest shall be few, that a child may write them.

α.10.20 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, neg sequttahwhutcheg Israel, kah neg wadchiitcheg Jakob wekit neg pohquohhukeg, matta pish wonk wutompattussun8unah noh togkomo[n]t, qut pish ompatussen Jehovah, 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, wunnamuhkutée.
E.10.20 And it shall come to pass in that day, that the remnant of Israel, and such as are escaped of the house of Jacob, shall no more again stay upon him that smote them; but shall stay upon the LORD, the Holy One of Israel, in truth.

α.10.21 Neg sequttahwhutcheg pish qushkeog, sequttahhamauutcheh Jakob, en masugkenuk Manit.
E.10.21 The remnant shall return, even the remnant of Jacob, unto the mighty God.

α.10.22 Newutche tókonogque kummissinninneumog Israel wutteas8unneáont ketahhane nagu[n]tuut, neg aguhsikeg pish qushkeog: mahchekonaéonk noh káhtimit, pish tomogkeu ut sampweusseonganit.
E.10.22 For though thy people Israel be as the sand of the sea, yet a remnant of them shall return: the consumption decreed shall overflow with righteousness.

α.10.23 Newutche Lord wut-Jehovanum8oh ayeuteaog, pish ayeuau mahchekonae onkoh, noh kahtimit ut nashaue wame ohkeit.
E.10.23 For the Lord GOD of hosts shall make a consumption, even determined, in the midst of all the land.

α.10.24 Newutche yeu wussin Lord God ayeuwutteaunit, woi nummissinninneumog wadohkéogish Sion, ahque wabesuón8k wut-Assyrian: noh pish kuttogkomuk pogkomunk, kah pish kutayeuuhkonittue tahshinumunk wutanwohhou, ne asehetteup Egyptianéog.
E.10.24 Therefore thus saith the Lord GOD of hosts, O my people that dwellest in Zion, be not afraid of the Assyrian: he shall smite thee with a rod, and shall lift up his staff against thee, after the manner of Egypt.

α.10.25 Newutche ogguhsese sepe, kah unkque m8squanetam8onk pish ahquohteau kah nummusquanittam8onk ut uppaguanuongan8óut.
E.10.25 For yet a very little while, and the indignation shall cease, and mine anger in their destruction.

α.10.26 Kah Jehovah ayeuteaunit pish 8wogkauunumauoh sasamatahwhuttuonk netatupe paguanáonk Midian, kishke Orebe qussukquanit: kah onatuh ne ônohtagkup uppogkomunk woskeche kehtahanit, ne pish wuttinne tahshinumun neanheomp wut-Egyptianeh.
E.10.26 And the LORD of hosts shall stir up a scourge for him according to the slaughter of Midian at the rock of Oreb: and as his rod was upon the sea, so shall he lift it up after the manner of Egypt.

α.10.27 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, 8wéanun pish amaunumun wutch kuttugkeet, kah weyoakumoh wutch kussittipukanit, kah yoak pish matcheheau newutche sesequnáonk.
E.10.27 And it shall come to pass in that day, that his burden shall be taken away from off thy shoulder, and his yoke from off thy neck, and the yoke shall be destroyed because of the anointing.

α.10.28 Noh peyau Ajath, noh pahmohkom Migron, ut Michmash na upponamun ukkenúm8ongash.
E.10.28 He is come to Aiath, he is passed to Migron; at Michmash he hath laid up his carriages:

α.10.29 Qushkodteáog ósukongkanit, nag kaueneau Geba, Ramah wabesu, uk-Gibeahum Saul wussem8.
E.10.29 They are gone over the passage: they have taken up their lodging at Geba; Ramah is afraid; Gibeah of Saul is fled.

α.10.30 Mishont8ash, woi wuttaunoh Gallim: n8tamwah Laish, woi kuttamunge Anathoth.
E.10.30 Lift up thy voice, O daughter of Gallim: cause it to be heard unto Laish, O poor Anathoth.

α.10.31 Madmenah ontsum, wadohkitcheg Gebim moèog wussemuneát.
E.10.31 Madmenah is removed; the inhabitants of Gebim gather themselves to flee.

α.10.32 Ashpume pish appu ut Nob ne kesukok: pish ayeuuhkonittue tattauunkauau wunnutcheg 8wadcheum wuttaunoh Zion; Jerusaleme wadchu.
E.10.32 As yet shall he remain at Nob that day: he shall shake his hand against the mount of the daughter of Zion, the hill of Jerusalem.

α.10.33 Kusseh; Lord, Jehovah ayeuteaanit pish tumehtham wuttuhqunash nashpe wabesuonk, kah quaquonunkquokish pish kouwehthamunash, kah pahtuánumweenunkqussit pish hohpaheau.
E.10.33 Behold, the Lord, the LORD of hosts, shall lop the bough with terror: and the high ones of stature shall be hewn down, and the haughty shall be humbled.

α.10.34 Kah noh pish tumehtham touohkomukque kókuppagish, nashpe m8uhshog, kah Lebanon pish penushau wutch masukkenuk.
E.10.34 And he shall cut down the thickets of the forest with iron, and Lebanon shall fall by a mighty one.

α.11.1 KAh sauobpunk pish wutchegen 8wepunkquamut Jesse, kah Wuttuhk pish wutchegen 8wadchabukqut.
E.11.1 And there shall come forth a rod out of the stem of Jesse, and a Branch shall grow out of his roots:

α.11.2 Kah wunnashauanitt8moh Jehovah pish wutapehtunkquoh, wa[a]ntamóe kah wohwohtamóe nashauanit, kuhquttue kah menuhkesue nashauanit, wahteóe nashauanit, kah qushónat Jehovah.
E.11.2 And the spirit of the LORD shall rest upon him, the spirit of wisdom and understanding, the spirit of counsel and might, the spirit of knowledge and of the fear of the LORD;

α.11.3 Kah pish wutayimunkquoh kogkinne wohtamu[m] ut quoshonat Jehovah, kah noh matta pish unne wussittum8 neaunak wuskesukque naum8onk, asuh áushkomuóou neane wohtog wutch wehtauogkut.
E.11.3 And shall make him of quick understanding in the fear of the LORD: and he shall not judge after the sight of his eyes, neither reprove after the hearing of his ears:

α.11.4 Qut nashpe sampweusseonk pish wussumau matchekuoh, kah pish áushkomuau nashpe sampwagk, wutche manunnissitcheg ut ohkeit: kah noh pish togkodtam ohke nashpe wutt8n8e pogkomunk, kah nashpe wussissitt8n8e nashauonk pish nushau matchet8oh.
E.11.4 But with righteousness shall he judge the poor, and reprove with equity for the meek of the earth: and he shall smite the earth: with the rod of his mouth, and with the breath of his lips shall he slay the wicked.

α.11.5 Kah sampweusseonk ne pish uppetukquobpis ut wusseganit: kah pabahtanumukqussuonk ne pish uppetukquobpis ut wutt8unussit.
E.11.5 And righteousness shall be the girdle of his loins, and faithfulness the girdle of his reins.

α.11.6 Kah wonk mukquoshom pish weetomau lamboh, kah leopard pish sepsinn8wehtauau kidsoh, kah kalfsoh, kah qunnonouwem, kah wanogqunutcheh moeu, kah mukkies pish wussagkompanoh
E.11.6 The wolf also shall dwell with the lamb, and the leopard shall lie down with the kid; and the calf and the young lion and the fatling together; and a little child shall lead them.

α.11.7 Kah cow kah mosk pish weetatup8tuog, wunnechan8oh pish neesinwoh, kah qunnonou pish meech sékupoghegash onatuh ox.
E.11.7 And the cow and the bear shall feed; their young ones shall lie down together: and the lion shall eat straw like the ox.

α.11.8 Kah n8n8e mukkies pish tannuppompu 8wonogqut asp, kah 8chininnáe mukkies pish pethennum wunnutcheg sesegq 8wonogqut.
E.11.8 And the sucking child shall play on the hole of the asp, and the weaned child shall put his hand on the cockatrice' den.

α.11.9 Matta nag pish woskehuwau8og asuh pagwahteau8og ut wame n8neetupanatamwe wadcheumut: newutche ohke pish numwohteau wahheáonk Jehovah, onatuh nippe nuhkokkog keihtoh.
E.11.9 They shall not hurt nor destroy in all my holy mountain: for the earth shall be full of the knowledge of the LORD, as the waters cover the sea.

α.11.10 Kah ne kesukok na pish 8wadchabuk Jesse ne pish nepatag wutch muttaagk kônunumauont missinninneuh; nehhoh Gentils pish wunnatinneahwhoh, kah wutanwôhsin8onk pish sohsum88.
E.11.10 And in that day there shall be a root of Jesse, which shall stand for an ensign of the people; to it shall the Gentiles seek: and his rest shall be glorious.

α.11.11 Kah pish nnih ne kesukok, Lord pish wunnutcheg nahohtoeu ne ponumun, uppohquohwhunonat asquttawhutcheh ummissinninneumoh wutch Assyria, kah wutch Egypt, kah wutch Pathros, kah wutch Cush, kah wutch Elam, kah wutch Shinar, kah wutch Hamath, kah wutch kehtahhanne aquidnehtu.
E.11.11 And it shall come to pass in that day, that the Lord shall set his hand again the second time to recover the remnant of his people, which shall be left, from Assyria, and from Egypt, and from Pathros, and from Cush, and from Elam, and from Shinar, and from Hamath, and from the islands of the sea.

α.11.12 Kah noh pish wunnashau muttaagk kohkinnunnumunutcheh wutche wutohtimoneash, kah pish miyanau Israelle pagkenitcheg, kah pish miyanau Judahe nanwisinitcheh, wutch yaue p8chag muttaohke.
E.11.12 And he shall set up an ensign for the nations, and shall assemble the outcasts of Israel, and gather together the dispersed of Judah from the four corners of the earth.

α.11.13 Wutiskauanittuonk Ephraim pish amaem8, kah ummatwomoh Judah pish tummehtahwhoog, Ephraim matta pish iskauonoou Judahoh, kah Judah matta pish m8m8sqheoou Ephraimoh.
E.11.13 The envy also of Ephraim shall depart, and the adversaries of Judah shall be cut off: Ephraim shall not envy Judah, and Judah shall not vex Ephraim.

α.11.14 Qut nag pish ushpuhh8waog, ut wuttugkeout Philistinsog, nogque en wutcheksuiyeu, nag pish matcheheaog neg wadohkitcheg wutchepwoieu moaeu nag pish ponamwog wunnutchegan8 ut Edom kah Moab: kah wunneechanoh Ammon pish wunn8swehtauouh.
E.11.14 But they shall fly upon the shoulders of the Philistines toward the west; they shall spoil them of the east together: they shall lay their hand upon Edom and Moab; and the children of Ammon shall obey them.

α.11.15 Kah Jehovah pish papuhquanne paguanau ketahanne Egyptiane meenan, kah nashpe ummishetahshinneumoh pish tattauohteau wunnutcheg waabe sepuut, kah pish wuttogkodtamun ut nesausuk tahshe po[m]utchuanit, kah pish qushkodteaheau missinninnuh nobohteaouut.
E.11.15 And the LORD shall utterly destroy the tongue of the Egyptian sea; and with his mighty wind shall he shake his hand over the river, and shall smite it in the seven streams, and make men go over dryshod.

α.11.16 Kah ne pish nanwe ummayou asquttahwhutcheh ummissinninneumoh, nég asquttawhutcheg wutch Assyria, neanagkup wutch Israel ne kesukok waj sohhog ohkeit Egypt.
E.11.16 And there shall be an highway for the remnant of his people, which shall be left, from Assyria; like as it was to Israel in the day that he came up out of the land of Egypt.

α.12.1 KAh nekesukok pish kussim, woi Jehovah, k8waeenomush: tohkonogque kummusquanuminneah, kummusquantam8onk qushkem8, kah kuttapheh.
E.12.1 And in that day thou shalt say, O LORD, I will praise thee: though thou wast angry with me, thine anger is turned away, and thou comfortedst me.

α.12.2 Kusseh God noh n8wadchanitteaonk: nuppabuhtanum, kah matta n8wabesuh, newutche Lord Jehovah noh nummenuhkesuonk, kah nukket8homaonk, noh wonk n8wadchanitteaonkanin.
E.12.2 Behold, God is my salvation; I will trust, and not be afraid: for the LORD JEHOVAH is my strength and my song; he also is become my salvation.

α.12.3 Newutche wekontamoe pish k8thuppam8 wutch wadchanittuae wuttahhamonganit.
E.12.3 Therefore with joy shall ye draw water out of the wells of salvation.

α.12.4 Kah ne kesukok pish kussimw8 wowussumok Jehovah, wehquetumok 8wesuonk, wahteauwahuwagk wutusseongash ut kenugke missinninnutu, missohham8k 8weesuonk mishehteauun.
E.12.4 And in that day shall ye say, Praise the LORD, call upon his name, declare his doings among the people, make mention that his name is exalted.

α.12.5 Ket8hamok Jehovah newutche noh usseu waunnegukish, yeu wahteauun ut wame ohkeit.
E.12.5 Sing unto the LORD; for he hath done excellent things: this is known in all the earth.

α.12.6 Wuttauate[u]kqussek, kah mishont8wagk ken wadohkean Zion, newutche masugkenuk 8neetupanatam8moh Israel ut kenashomut.
E.12.6 Cry out and shout, thou inhabitant of Zion: for great is the Holy One of Israel in the midst of thee.

α.13.1 OOWeanun Babilon, ne Isaiah wunnaumonuh Amoz nagkup.
E.13.1 The burden of Babylon, which Isaiah the son of Amoz did see.

α.13.2 Tahshinum8k muttaagk ut kussòhkôiyeuut, mishont8wanumok, tattauwunnumok kenutcheg onk petutteaog wuttusquontam8out puhponkompoog.
E.13.2 Lift ye up a banner upon the high mountain, exalt the voice unto them, shake the hand, that they may go into the gates of the nobles.

α.13.3 Nuttaann8nomp n8neetupanatam8mog: kah n8wehomomp nummenuhkeseumog, wutche nummusquanittam8onk, neg weekontogeg ut nukqununkqussuonganit
E.13.3 I have commanded my sanctified ones, I have also called my mighty ones for mine anger, even them that rejoice in my highness.

α.13.4 OOwadtauatonkqussuongan8 monacheg ut wadchuuhkontu, ogqunneunkqussu[o]g mutta[a]nukeg missinninnuog wogkouee wuttauatonkqussuonganu8 wutohtim[ô]unne tass8tam8ongash miyaé[m]8ash: Jehovah ay[e]uteaunit 8sukkomp[a]nh mattompagwe ayeuteuh.
E.13.4 The noise of a multitude in the mountains, like as of a great people; a tumultuous noise of the kingdoms of nations gathered together: the LORD of hosts mustereth the host of the battle.

α.13.5 Nag 8mwog nôadtit wutohtimóneat, wutch weekqshik kesuk, noh Jehovah, kah ummusquantamwe auwohteaongash, pagwohtauunat mamusse ohke.
E.13.5 They come from a far country, from the end of heaven, even the LORD, and the weapons of his indignation, to destroy the whole land.

α.13.6 Mau8k, newutche ukkesukkodtum Jehovah paswohteau: pish ogque peyau pagwanuonganit wutch wame manuhkesitteáut.
E.13.6 Howl ye; for the day of the LORD is at hand; it shall come as a destruction from the Almighty.

α.13.7 Newutche wame menutchegash pish sauunum8m8ash, kah nishnoh wosketomp wuttah pish mohtupohteau.
E.13.7 Therefore shall all hands be faint, and every man's heart shall melt:

α.13.8 Kah nag pish wabesuog: onkquommom8ongash kah unkquanum8ongash pish wuttohqunóuh; nag pish unúhquommom8og mittamwossis neechadt, nag pish chepsh[á]ettuog, wuskesuk8oash pish onatuh n8hn8unag.
E.13.8 And they shall be afraid: pangs and sorrows shall take hold of them; they shall be in pain as a woman that travaileth: they shall be amazed one at another; their faces shall be as flames.

α.13.9 Kusseh ukkesukodtum Jehovah peyom8, onkuppunohteáe naneeswe nashpe unkque musquanittam8onk kah mishe musquantam8onk, touwishinneat ohke, kah noh pish paguanau ummatcheseaéneumoh na$wutch.
