E.13.9 Behold, the day of the LORD cometh, cruel both with wrath and fierce anger, to lay the land desolate: and he shall destroy the sinners thereof out of it.

α.13.10 Newutche kesukque anogqsog kah chippanogqussog matta pish wóhsumóog: nepauz pish pogkenum sohhog, kah nanepâushadt matta pish 8wequai wohsum8mun8.
E.13.10 For the stars of heaven and the constellations thereof shall not give their light: the sun shall be darkened in his going forth, and the moon shall not cause her light to shine.

α.13.11 Kah pish nussasamatahham muttaok, wutche uppaneseongan8, kah matchetoog wutch ummatcheseongan8oash: kah uppehtuánúmweenungqussuongan8 pehtuánum8og, n8wohkuhquôshitteauwahtauun: kah nutti[u]hquonkqutteoh uppehtuánumwenunkqussuongan8 uhqueneunkqussitcheg.
E.13.11 And I will punish the world for their evil, and the wicked for their iniquity; and I will cause the arrogancy of the proud to cease, and will lay low the haughtiness of the terrible.

α.13.12 Kah wosketomp nutanue mish[ô]adteh onk ne wanegik gold: nux wosketomp onk ne Ophire golde wedge.
E.13.12 I will make a man more precious than fine gold; even a man than the golden wedge of Ophir.

α.13.13 Newutche nuttattauwohteam kesukquash, kah o[h]ke pish ontohteau wutch wutayeuonganit, ut ummusquanittam8onganit Jehovah ayeuteaunit, kah ne kesukok uhque musquantog.
E.13.13 Therefore I will shake the heavens, and the earth shall remove out of her place, in the wrath of the LORD of hosts, and in the day of his fierce anger.

α.13.14 Kah pish tatuppeyeu8 key8hkauut ayomp, kah ontauh sheeput, ne matta howan wadchanunkeh, nishnoh pasuk qushkeu en nehenwonche missinninneumut, kah pish spuhh8waog nishnoh pasuk en nehenwonche wutohket.
E.13.14 And it shall be as the chased roe, and as a sheep that no man taketh up: they shall every man turn to his own people, and flee every one into his own land.

α.13.15 Nishnoh pasuk noh namhit pish asishahtahwh[á]u: kah nishnoh pasuk noh weetomont pish penushau nashpe togkodteg.
E.13.15 Every one that is found shall be thrust through; and every one that is joined unto them shall fall by the sword.

α.13.16 Kah wonk ummukkieseum8uh pish sukquóhkônunk an[a]quabhettit, week8oash pish mukkinumwó[n]tamunash, kah ummittamwuss8oh pish chekehéonunneoh.
E.13.16 Their children also shall be dashed to pieces before their eyes; their houses shall be spoiled, and their wives ravished.

α.13.17 Kusseh, n8wogkouun Medsog ayeuuhkonittue n[a]goh, neg matta pish tohhe[n]tup anatam8gig silver: kah wonk gold matta wuttapeneam8uneau.
E.13.17 Behold, I will stir up the Medes against them, which shall not regard silver; and as for gold, they shall not delight in it.

α.13.18 Wutahtompeyeuoh pish sukquehtahwaog 8skeneum8uh, kah nag pish matta kitteamonteanumau8og ummeechu[m̃]uonk ôontomuk: wuskesuk88ash matta pish wohquanumauôog mukkiesoh.
E.13.18 Their bows also shall dash the young men to pieces; and they shall have no pity on the fruit of the womb; their eyes shall not spare children.

α.13.19 Kah Babylon wussohsum8wongan8oash ass8tam8onganog, 8neetuonk Caldeansog, ummissugken8ongan8 pish onatuh God kepuhteadt Sodom kah Gomorrah.
E.13.19 And Babylon, the glory of kingdoms, the beauty of the Chaldees' excellency, shall be as when God overthrew Sodom and Gomorrah.

α.13.20 Matta pish wonk wutohkein, asuh matta pish ayéin wutch pometuonganit onk ye[á]n pometuonganit: kah Arabian matta pish na 8weekéin, kah nanawesheepsaenuog matta pish na ponam8uneau wekuòash.
E.13.20 It shall never be inhabited, neither shall it be dwelt in from generation to generation: neither shall the Arabian pitch tent there; neither shall the shepherds make their fold there.

α.13.21 Qut touohkomukque puppinashimwog na pish wusseepsineau, kah wekuoash pish wunn[á]numw[à]pine u[t] [n]ishkeneunkque ow[à]asineg, kah k8k8khôsog na pish 8tohkineau, kah Satyrsog ka pish wuttit pumukoneau
E.13.21 But wild beasts of the desert shall lie there; and their houses shall be full of doleful creatures; and owls shall dwell there, and satyrs shall dance there.

α.13.22 Kah munnohhanne puppinashimwog pish 8n8og ut mahchikomukque wekuout, kah Dragonsog ut 8nekomuk8out: kah wutaquompiyeum pas8che peyaum8, kah ukkesukodtum8oash matta pish sepohtan8ash.
E.13.22 And the wild beasts of the islands shall cry in their desolate houses, and dragons in their pleasant palaces: and her time is near to come, and her days shall not be prolonged.

α.14.1 NEwutche Jehovah pish monanumau Jakoboh kah ohnch pish pepenauau Israeloh, kah pish upponuh nehenwonche wutohkeyeu[o]ut: kah pen8wot pish weetomuk: kah pish menuhkappuog wekit Jakob.
E.14.1 For the LORD will have mercy on Jacob, and will yet choose Israel, and set them in their own land: and the strangers shall be joined with them, and they shall cleave to the house of Jacob.

α.14.2 Kah missinninnuog pish nag wuneemunnouh, kah uppas8ouh ut wutayeuongan8out, kah wek Israel nag pish 8tohtauonganinnéauh ut wutohkit Jehovah wutche wuttinneumuonk, kah mittamwossisse wuttinneumineunk, kah pish ummissi[n]uhkonauh nag neh masinohteacheg: kah pish nanawunaog neh woskhikqhettipoh.
E.14.2 And the people shall take them, and bring them to their place: and the house of Israel shall possess them in the land of the LORD for servants and handmaids: and they shall take them captives, whose captives they were; and they shall rule over their oppressors.

α.14.3 Kah pish n$nih, ne kesukok Jehovah anwosumwahikquean wutch kutungquanumwinneat, kah wutch k8wabesuonganit, kah wutch siogke missinnainneat ut$toh adt wuttinneumuhkonuninumukup.
E.14.3 And it shall come to pass in the day that the LORD shall give thee rest from thy sorrow, and from thy fear, and from the hard bondage wherein thou wast made to serve,

α.14.4 Neit pish kussim yeu woweenuhwh[á]muae kutt8wonk ayeuuhkonittue Babylone ketass8t: uttoh in woskehuwaenin wôhkuhquosinin?
E.14.4 That thou shalt take up this proverb against the king of Babylon, and say, How hath the oppressor ceased! the golden city ceased!

α.14.5 Jehovah pohquetahham wutánwohh8un8 matchet8og, kah uppiuhquttumwe anwoh8un8 nananuwach[e]g.
E.14.5 The LORD hath broken the staff of the wicked, and the sceptre of the rulers.

α.14.6 Noh musquantamwe togkomont missinninnuh nagwutteauhshine, moh musquantamwe nanawunuk wutohtimoneash, noh woskeheau, kah matta howan wuttamehh[u]waunuh.
E.14.6 He who smote the people in wrath with a continual stroke, he that ruled the nations in anger, is persecuted, and none hindereth.

α.14.7 Mamusse ohke anwohsin, kah chequnohteau: nag pohqua8homaog
E.14.7 The whole earth is at rest, and is quiet: they break forth into singing.

α.14.8 Nux qunonuhquaog kummuskauanatam8[ó]nukquog, Lebannonne chikupog n8waog, nadteuh pagkenumuk, matta kouuhkukquaenin ayeuuhkonittue nukkuhkuhquéhtunk8un.
E.14.8 Yea, the fir trees rejoice at thee, and the cedars of Lebanon, saying, Since thou art laid down, no feller is come up against us.

α.14.9 Chepiohkomuk wutch agwe ontohteau wutche ken, kenogskunkqunat peyôa[n], wogkouineau n[á]pinitche wutche ken, wame puppunkompóog muttaohkit, wutomohkinuh wutch wutappuonganehtu, wame wutohtimóinne ketass8tamwog.
E.14.9 Hell from beneath is moved for thee to meet thee at thy coming: it stirreth up the dead for thee, even all the chief ones of the earth; it hath raised up from their thrones all the kings of the nations.

α.14.10 Wame nag pish ket8kaog, kah kuttukquog, ken wonk sun ken8chumwes netatupe nenawun? ken k[ù]ttatuppinneunkqusseumumun?
E.14.10 All they shall speak and say unto thee, Art thou also become weak as we? art thou become like unto us?

α.14.11 K8nadchéseum paudtauun weenohkeit, kah k8wadtauatonkqussue wanont8wagk: 8hqua[ó]g sepakéog ut kutagwéiyeumut, kah 8hquaog kenuhkuhkunk.
E.14.11 Thy pomp is brought down to the grave, and the noise of thy viols: the worm is spread under thee, and the worms cover thee.

α.14.12 Uttoh kuttinne penushon wutch kesukqut, woi Lucifer, wunnaumonuh mohtompan? uttoh kittin tummehtawhuttean en ohkeit, ken n8chumwehteauop wutohtimóneash?
E.14.12 How art thou fallen from heaven, O Lucifer, son of the morning! how art thou cut down to the ground, which didst weaken the nations!

α.14.13 Newutche kussip ut kuttahhut, nukkuhkuhquem en kesukqut, pish nuttahshinum nutappuonk anue wutannogqusseumut God: kah wonk nukquenáp mukkinneáe wadchuut nannumiy[ê]u.
E.14.13 For thou hast said in thine heart, I will ascend into heaven, I will exalt my throne above the stars of God: I will sit also upon the mount of the congregation, in the sides of the north:

α.14.14 Nukkuhkuhquem anue ne sohkunkquok mahtókqs, pish ne[a]nenunkqus noh anue quanunkquapit.
E.14.14 I will ascend above the heights of the clouds; I will be like the most High.

α.14.15 Qut pish ken8t[n]init en chepiohkomukqut, ut sussippôe psahtheganit. 
E.14.15 Yet thou shalt be brought down to hell, to the sides of the pit.

α.14.16 Neg nogqueáneg pish kuppapásinunk kah kenatwánumuk, n8waog, sun yeuoh wosketomp noh nunkshadtauwahtunkup ohke, noh nánukkishadtunkup ketass8tam8ongash?
E.14.16 They that see thee shall narrowly look upon thee, and consider thee, saying, Is this the man that made the earth to tremble, that did shake kingdoms;

α.14.17 Noh áyikup muttaok onatuh touohkomuk, kah pagwatunkup wutotanash? noh matta wohshinumauonk wek8 ukkupshagki[n]omuh?
E.14.17 That made the world as a wilderness, and destroyed the cities thereof; that opened not the house of his prisoners?

α.14.18 Wame wutohtimóinne wuttahs8timwog, nag wame sohsumohteásinwog, nishnoh pasuk nehenwonceh wekit.
E.14.18 All the kings of the nations, even all of them, lie in glory, every one in his own house.

α.14.19 Qut ken kussohwhôhkonit wutch weenohkeit, onatuh nishkeungque wuttuhqunit, kah onatuh wuthogk8un8oash neg na[h]shitcheg, papashpetahwhut togkodteg, neg w8mussitcheg psahthegane qussukquanéhtu, ontuh nupp8e muhhog tahtashkuhka[ú]ut ut musseetut.
E.14.19 But thou art cast out of thy grave like an abominable branch, and as the raiment of those that are slain, thrust through with a sword, that go down to the stones of the pit; as a carcase trodden under feet.

α.14.20 Matta pish nag k8weechayeumôog posekinitteóg, newutche kuppagquadtoh kutohke, kah nushonat kummissinninnúmog; 8skannémunnu matchet8g matta pish w[a]eenódtum8un.
E.14.20 Thou shalt not be joined with them in burial, because thou hast destroyed thy land, and slain thy people: the seed of evildoers shall never be renowned.

α.14.21 Quoshauwehtau wunneechanoh shehteaénuh wutche ummatcheseongan88ash 8sh8oh, nag woh matta wutomohkéinnaout, kah matta wutohta8unaóut ohke, kah matta numwohtau8unat wuskesukqut muttaok 8tanash.
E.14.21 Prepare slaughter for his children for the iniquity of their fathers; that they do not rise, nor possess the land, nor fill the face of the world with cities.

α.14.22 Newutche nag ayeuuhkonittue n8waabehtauóog, n8wau Jehovah ayeuteaunit: kah pish nuttummetahham wutch Babylon, wesuonk, wunnaumoniin, kah 8w[á]dtunkquassin, n8wau Jehovah.
E.14.22 For I will rise up against them, saith the LORD of hosts, and cut off from Babylon the name, and remnant, and son, and nephew, saith the LORD.

α.14.23 Kah wonk n8ta[h]tauonga[n]éhheon Bittern, kah nippissepagwash, kah nutchekhamun nashpe paguanue chekhikunk, n8wau Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
E.14.23 I will also make it a possession for the bittern, and pools of water: and I will sweep it with the besom of destruction, saith the LORD of hosts.

α.14.24 Jehovah ayeuteaunit chadchekeyeuau, n8wau, wunnamuhkut, neanantamup, ne pish n$nih,, kah ne pakodtantamup, ne pish unne menehketeauun.
E.14.24 The LORD of hosts hath sworn, saying, Surely as I have thought, so shall it come to pass; and as I have purposed, so shall it stand:

α.14.25 Nuppokshan wut-Assyrian ut nutohkit, kah ut n8wadchumehtu nuttahtashkuhkau ut agwe nusseetut, neit pish weyoakum8oh âmaehtunkquog, kah 8weanun pish amaem8 wutch wuttugkeit.
E.14.25 That I will break the Assyrian in my land, and upon my mountains tread him under foot: then shall his yoke depart from off them, and his burden depart from off their shoulders.

α.14.26 Yeu pogkodtantam[ó]onk ne pakodtantamuk ut mamusse ohkeit, kah yeu menutcheg ne samogkinumuk en wame wutohtimóneat.
E.14.26 This is the purpose that is purposed upon the whole earth: and this is the hand that is stretched out upon all the nations.

α.14.27 Newutche Jehovah ayeuhteaanit uppogkodtanatamun, kah howan woh uppanshadta[u]wahtauun? kah wunnutcheg summagohteau, & howan woh ukqushkinnumun?
E.14.27 For the LORD of hosts hath purposed, and who shall disannul it? and his hand is stretched out, and who shall turn it back?

α.14.28 Ne kodtum8k ketass8t Ahaz napuk, yeu wéanunúo8p.
E.14.28 In the year that king Ahaz died was this burden.

α.14.29 Ahque muskouantash ken mamusse Palestina, newutche uppogkomunk noh togkomukqueóp pokshau: newutche wutch 8wadchaubukqut ask8k pish 8tsohhamu[n] sesekq, kah ummechummuonk pish n8tae pt8wée ask8k.
E.14.29 Rejoice not thou, whole Palestina, because the rod of him that smote thee is broken: for out of the serpent's root shall come forth a cockatrice, and his fruit shall be a fiery flying serpent.

α.14.30 Kah ummohtommegitteomoh noh machekit pish meetsuoh, kah quenauhikquit pish wunniyeue sepsin[,] kah nunnehto k8wadchabuk nashpe mashshagquot, kah noh pish nushau sequttahhamaúúnumukeh.
E.14.30 And the firstborn of the poor shall feed, and the needy shall lie down in safety: and I will kill thy root with famine, and he shall slay thy remnant.

α.14.31 OO[n]sh, woi squont, maush, woi keitotan, ken mamusse Palestina kussukqunit, newutche pukuttau pish 8m88 naunummiyeu, kah wanne pish nussiyeoh ut ukkuhquttumoe aquompiyeumut.
E.14.31 Howl, O gate; cry, O city; thou, whole Palestina, art dissolved: for there shall come from the north a smoke, and none shall be alone in his appointed times.

α.14.32 Neit toh pish unneu namp8hamauau wutann8teamweneum8uh wutohtimmoneunk? Jehovah ummenuhkehteauun Zion, kah ummissinninnúme matchekeumoh, pish uppanuhtantamunin.
E.14.32 What shall one then answer the messengers of the nation? That the LORD hath founded Zion, and the poor of his people shall trust in it.

α.15.1 OWeanun Moab: newutche nukonáeu Ar ut Moab mohtupohsin, kah chequnapheau, newutche nukonàeu Kir ut Moab moh[tu]pohsin, kah chequnapheau.
E.15.1 The burden of Moab. Because in the night Ar of Moab is laid waste, and brought to silence; because in the night Kir of Moab is laid waste, and brought to silence;

α.15.2 Kuhkuhquéi en Bajith kah en Dibon, qunuhqui ayeuonganéhtu, mauunat: Moab pish 8nowontam Nabo, kah Medeba: wame uppuhkukquash pish mukukkiyeuash, kah nishnoh weeshitt8n tummuhs[ô]su.
E.15.2 He is gone up to Bajith, and to Dibon, the high places, to weep: Moab shall howl over Nebo, and over Medeba: on all their heads shall be baldness, and every beard cut off.

α.15.3 Ut wutaumaogk8out, pish puttukquobpissuwontamog man8tionak: ut woskechekomukquehtu kah ut wutaumaogk8out, nish$noh pasuk pish 8n8, m8cheke mauun.
E.15.3 In their streets they shall gird themselves with sackcloth: on the tops of their houses, and in their streets, every one shall howl, weeping abundantly.

α.15.4 Kah Heshbon pish mau kah Elealeh 8wadtauatonkqussuonk pish n8tamun weehque Jahaz, newaj ukkenauwamee matwomoh pish mishont8wauh, uppomantamoonk pish uhquanittamhik.
E.15.4 And Heshbon shall cry, and Elealeh: their voice shall be heard even unto Jahaz: therefore the armed soldiers of Moab shall cry out; his life shall be grievous unto him.

α.15.5 Nuttah pish mishont8wau wutche Moab, 8sem8moh pish usishauh Zoar, nashwe kodtumohkog kouwashinem; newutche adt kutóhkoag Luhith[.] nashpe mauonk pish kuhkuhqueog, newutche ut Haronaimme mayut, na pish wutch waapem8 paguanue mauonk.
E.15.5 My heart shall cry out for Moab; his fugitives shall flee unto Zoar, an heifer of three years old: for by the mounting up of Luhith with weeping shall they go it up; for in the way of Horonaim they shall raise up a cry of destruction.

α.15.6 Newutche Nimrimme nippeash pish touwushinneash: newutche moskehtuash ohp8htaash, askoshquosh wanne ohtan8ash, wanne ashkoshqun8.
E.15.6 For the waters of Nimrim shall be desolate: for the hay is withered away, the grass faileth, there is no green thing.

α.15.7 Newutche madtauneuk ne ohtauwehettit, kah ne wadchanumohettit, pish ummonchadtauunneau, en anumussikkuppeyeue sepuwussut.
E.15.7 Therefore the abundance they have gotten, and that which they have laid up, shall they carry away to the brook of the willows.

α.15.8 Newutche wuttauatonkqussuonk quinnuppem8 en wame wussissippoiyeumut Moab: 8n8onk weehque Eglaim kah 8n8onk weque wussissippoiyeumut Be[o]r$Elim.
E.15.8 For the cry is gone round about the borders of Moab; the howling thereof unto Eglaim, and the howling thereof unto Beerelim.

α.15.9 Newutche wunnuppeimash Dimon pish numwohteau musqueheonk, newutche nukk8tne pas8 ut Dimon qunn8n8óh quentunkqutch noh pohquohhogkup wutch Moab, kah neg asquttahwhutcheg ut ohkeit.
E.15.9 For the waters of Dimon shall be full of blood: for I will bring more upon Dimon, lions upon him that escapeth of Moab, and upon the remnant of the land.

α.16.1 NEgonshhuagk lamb en noh nanawunuk ohke, wutch Sela wehque touohkomukqut, wehque 8wadchumut wuttaunoh Zion.
E.16.1 Send ye the lamb to the ruler of the land from Sela to the wilderness, unto the mount of the daughter of Zion.

α.16.2 Newutche pish n$nih, onatuh kogkeish[á]e psukses: ne pish wuttattúppeyeuwunneau wuttaunoh Moab, ut Arnone t8skeonganit.
E.16.2 For it shall be, that, as a wandering bird cast out of the nest, so the daughters of Moab shall be at the fords of Arnon.

α.16.3 Kogkáhquttegk, ussek wussittum8onk, ogquehteaush kutonkauohtom nohkog, ut noeu pohshequaut, puttogquehtog neg sohwohteamukeg, ahque wa[n]shan8k noh nánwushadt.
E.16.3 Take counsel, execute judgment; make thy shadow as the night in the midst of the noonday; hide the outcasts; bewray not him that wandereth.

α.16.4 Neg pakenogeg wutch ontogkit weetomukqush Moab, ken wunnenéhuwaéneush wutch wuskesukqut woskhuadt, newutche mukk8kinnuwaenúh wohkuhquosinwoh, matchehuwaenin áhquappu, woskehuw[à]enuog mahchekussuog wutch ohkeit.
E.16.4 Let mine outcasts dwell with thee, Moab; be thou a covert to them from the face of the spoiler: for the extortioner is at an end, the spoiler ceaseth, the oppressors are consumed out of the land.

α.16.5 Kah monaneteáe appeuonk pish menehketeauun; kah pish ukquenappin ut wunnamuhkuteyeu8ut, ut wut-tabernaklumut David, wussittum kah natinneham wussittumóonk kah kenuppeteau sampweusseonk.
E.16.5 And in mercy shall the throne be established: and he shall sit upon it in truth in the tabernacle of David, judging, and seeking judgment, and hasting righteousness.

α.16.6 Nunn8tamumu[n] uppehtuanumôonk Moab (noh mishe pittuánum8) ukqunuhqunneunkqussuonk, kah uppehtuánumóonk, kah ummusquantamóonk: qut uppann8waongash matta pish ne nano.
E.16.6 We have heard of the pride of Moab; he is very proud: even of his haughtiness, and his pride, and his wrath: but his lies shall not be so.

α.16.7 Newaj pish Moab 8n8wonont Moaboh, nishnoh pasuk pish 8n8, wutch ukquenohtag8mash Kir-hareseth, pish kummaum8 wunnamuhkut togkomóog.
E.16.7 Therefore shall Moab howl for Moab, every one shall howl: for the foundations of Kirhareseth shall ye mourn; surely they are stricken.

α.16.8 Newutche Heshbone ohteuhkonash kôhkutt[a]ash, 8wenomassippog Sibmah, wussontim8m8oh penuwohteaog pokshadtóog negonneyeugish wutohkehte[a]ongash, peyaog wehque Jazer, nanwushaog pannuppe touohkomuk, wuttuhqunash summagnunumunash, qushkodteaog keitoh.
E.16.8 For the fields of Heshbon languish, and the vine of Sibmah: the lords of the heathen have broken down the principal plants thereof, they are come even unto Jazer, they wandered through the wilderness: her branches are stretched out, they are gone over the sea.

α.16.9 Newutche nummauwétam nashpe Jazere mauonk, 8wenomussippog Sibmah, kutogquechipanash nussippeguash, woi Heshbon, kah Elealeth: newutche mishontowaonk wutche sequ[a]nnáe kummeechum8mash, kah wutche kukkepenum8onk penusheau.
E.16.9 Therefore I will bewail with the weeping of Jazer the vine of Sibmah: I will water thee with my tears, O Heshbon, and Elealeh: for the shouting for thy summer fruits and for thy harvest is fallen.

α.16.10 Kah wekontamóonk amaunumun, kah muskouantam8onk wutch mishummeechume ohteuhkonit, kah ut weenominneohtekontu, na matta pish ket8hammaonganunn8, kah matta pish mishont8waonganunn8: tahtashkuhkomwenuog pish matta tahtashkuhkom8og wine ut wine$pressut, n8wohkuhquoshitteop ummishont8waonk.
E.16.10 And gladness is taken away, and joy out of the plentiful field; and in the vineyards there shall be no singing, neither shall there be shouting: the treaders shall tread out no wine in their presses; I have made their vintage shouting to cease.

α.16.11 Newutche nunnogkus pish wunnont8wanshau Moaboh onatuh Harp: kah nuttinnomiyeum Kirha[r]esh.
E.16.11 Wherefore my bowels shall sound like an harp for Moab, and mine inward parts for Kirharesh.

α.16.12 Kah pish nnih, naumuk Moab sauwunum ut qunuhque ayeuonganit, neit pish peyau ut wus$Sanctuareumut peantamunat: qut matta pish sohkohseu.
E.16.12 And it shall come to pass, when it is seen that Moab is weary on the high place, that he shall come to his sanctuary to pray; but he shall not prevail.

α.16.13 Yeu kutt8onk ne an8wop Jehovah papaume Moab, nádteuh na ahquompak.
E.16.13 This is the word that the LORD hath spoken concerning Moab since that time.

α.16.14 Qut yeuyeu Jehovah ukket8kontamun, n8wau, ash nanshwu kodtumun8gkup, onatuh ukkodtum8ut wahwuttinninneumuk, kah wuss[ô]hsum8onk Moab pish pogkodchimau, nashpe mamusse neg mataanukeg: kah neg asquttahwhutcheg pish ogguhsesuog kah n8chumwesuog.
E.16.14 But now the LORD hath spoken, saying, Within three years, as the years of an hireling, and the glory of Moab shall be contemned, with all that great multitude; and the remnant shall be very small and feeble.

α.17.1 OWeanun Damascus, kusseh, Damascus amaunôi wutch wut8tanau[n]neat, kah pish webe weep8toou,
E.17.1 The burden of Damascus. Behold, Damascus is taken away from being a city, and it shall be a ruinous heap.

α.17.2 Ukkeitotanash Aroer ahquontamunash, nish pish wutch puppinashimwog, neg pish sepsukeg, kah matta pish howan 8wabesuwaheuh.
E.17.2 The cities of Aroer are forsaken: they shall be for flocks, which shall lie down, and none shall make them afraid.

α.17.3 Wonkônous wonk pish wohkukquoshin wutch Ephraimut, kah ass8tamoonk wutch Damaskus, kah Syriae sequttahwhutceg: nag pish tatuppeyeu8og wussohsum8ongan8out wunnaumonuh Israel, n8wau Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
E.17.3 The fortress also shall cease from Ephraim, and the kingdom from Damascus, and the remnant of Syria: they shall be as the glory of the children of Israel, saith the LORD of hosts.

α.17.4 Kah ne kesukok pish nnih, wussohsumóonk Jakob pish woss[à]ppeteáuun, kah 8weeyauseé wees pish ônauwuss[é]um8.
E.17.4 And in that day it shall come to pass, that the glory of Jacob shall be made thin, and the fatness of his flesh shall wax lean.

α.17.5 Kah pish yáneyéu8 kepenumwaenúut kepenuk weatchiminneash, kah kepenuk missunkquaminash wutch wuhputteit, kah pish yaneyeu8 noh kepenuk missunkquaminnash ut Rephaimme 8n[ó]uhkôi.
E.17.5 And it shall be as when the harvestman gathereth the corn, and reapeth the ears with his arm; and it shall be as he that gathereth ears in the valley of Rephaim.

α.17.6 Qut onch pish mukupashquae weenominneash na$ut sequnumunash: onatuh né[u]emonteamuk olivuhtug, neesinash asuh nishwinásh berrisash ut wanashquonk: yauunash asuh napanna onkouee mishummeechummue wuttuhqunash, wussin Lord um-Manitt8moh Israel.
E.17.6 Yet gleaning grapes shall be left in it, as the shaking of an olive tree, two or three berries in the top of the uppermost bough, four or five in the outmost fruitful branches thereof, saith the LORD God of Israel.

α.17.7 Ne kesukok wosketomp pish monunnea[n]au neh kezhukqutcheh, kah wuskesukquash pish k[e]nompamau 8neetupanatam8m[ó]h Israel.
E.17.7 At that day shall a man look to his Maker, and his eyes shall have respect to the Holy One of Israel.

α.17.8 Kah matta pish monunneauôou Altarsash wunnutchegane anakaus[ú]onk, kah matta pish kenompattam8 ne wuttinwhunnutcheash kezteunkupash, asuh kuppahtu, asuh nunneukontunkanog.
E.17.8 And he shall not look to the altars, the work of his hands, neither shall respect that which his fingers have made, either the groves, or the images.

α.17.9 Ne kesukok ummenuhke 8tanash pish tatuppeyeu8ash ahquontam8e wuttuhkq, kah wanaskkunkquame wuttuhq, ne sequenum[o]hettit, newutche wunnaumonuh Israel: kah na pish tauwushin.
E.17.9 In that day shall his strong cities be as a forsaken bough, and an uppermost branch, which they left because of the children of Israel: and there shall be desolation.

α.17.10 Newutche k8wanánum k8wadchanuae Manit, kah matta kummehqutonam8 kumme[n]uhkesue qussukquanum, newaj pish ohkehteaan wunneohkehteaongash, & pish kutohteuhkon penowe ontsohkodtoongash.
E.17.10 Because thou hast forgotten the God of thy salvation, and hast not been mindful of the rock of thy strength, therefore shalt thou plant pleasant plants, and shalt set it with strange slips:

α.17.11 Ne kesukok pish kenetuwohto kutohketeaonk, kah mohtompanáeu pish kenekitteáuun k8skannem: qut kepenumoonk pish numwunkquae ut unkquanu[mo]e kesukodtut mat anno[ó]sue unkquanumwi[t].
E.17.11 In the day shalt thou make thy plant to grow, and in the morning shalt thou make thy seed to flourish: but the harvest shall be a heap in the day of grief and of desperate sorrow.

α.17.12 Missi wut[o]nkapunnaongan8 monacheg missinninnuog, ogque wadtauatonkqussuog kehtah, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kah wutohtimoinne munnumuhkeonk onatuh manumuhkem8uk menuhkee nippeash.
E.17.12 Woe to the multitude of many people, which make a noise like the noise of the seas; and to the rushing of nations, that make a rushing like the rushing of mighty waters!

α.17.13 Wutohtimoinash pish munumuhkem8ash, onatuh manumuhkem8ut monatash nippeash: qut God pish nah wutaushkomuh, kah nag pish nóadtit spuhh8waog, kah pish wunnaumatuhkauóog onatuh ut wuss[a]dtreamunne wadchuut ut anaquabit waban, kah onatuhyeu8 tatuppequashunk ut anaquabit pemsquoh.
E.17.13 The nations shall rush like the rushing of many waters: but God shall rebuke them, and they shall flee far off, and shall be chased as the chaff of the mountains before the wind, and like a rolling thing before the whirlwind.

α.17.14 Kah kusseh, wunnonk88k wuttamehpunáonk kah asquam mamohtompan8gkup, matta ohtan8, né wutchippiyeum8 neg waskhikqueagig, kah wuttittanohtôadtuongan8 neg mag8kqunukqueagig.
E.17.14 And behold at eveningtide trouble; and before the morning he is not. This is the portion of them that spoil us, and the lot of them that rob us.

α.18.1 MIssi wutonkapunnaongan8 ne ohke wunnuppawhunne onkauuhtohhup, ne ogkomut Ethiopiáe sepuut.
E.18.1 Woe to the land shadowing with wings, which is beyond the rivers of Ethiopia:

α.18.2 Neg ann8noncheg ann8naénuh en ketahhanniyeu, ut misa[ssi]que kuht8nogquash ut wosketupam: n8waog, monchek kenupshae ann8nutcheg en naswae kah pissagkinnumwe wutohimoneat, en uhqueneunkque missinninnúut wutch wadj kutchissik yeu pajeh,; kuhkohhamwe kah tahtashkuhkôsue wutohtimoineat, noh wutohke sepu[á]sh matchehteauunash. 
E.18.2 That sendeth ambassadors by the sea, even in vessels of bulrushes upon the waters, saying, Go, ye swift messengers, to a nation scattered and peeled, to a people terrible from their beginning hitherto; a nation meted out and trodden down, whose land the rivers have spoiled!

α.18.3 Wame kenaau wadohkeógish muttaohket, kah wadohkitcheg ohkeit, naum8k, tahshinuk muttôag ut wadchutu, puhpequohtunk monopupeg, n8tok.
E.18.3 All ye inhabitants of the world, and dwellers on the earth, see ye, when he lifteth up an ensign on the mountains; and when he bloweth a trumpet, hear ye.

α.18.4 Newutche ne nuttukqunah Jehovah, nutanwôhsin, kah nunnatwontam ut n[ú]tayeuonganit, onatuh pohkôntag wunnepogquehtu, kah onatuh matokqse neechippog k[ô]soppittag kepenum8onk.
E.18.4 For so the LORD said unto me, I will take my rest, and I will consider in my dwelling place like a clear heat upon herbs, and like a cloud of dew in the heat of harvest.

α.18.5 Newutche asquam kakepenumómukup[,] wunn[e]ht8nunk pakodcheyeu88k, kah seane wenom kesan8htag tanohketeaonganit, pish wunnaneeswe tummussumunash wuttuhqunesash nashpe mukk8kussauwae h8ksash, kah amaunumunash, kah kouwehthamunash wuttuhqunash.
E.18.5 For afore the harvest, when the bud is perfect, and the sour grape is ripening in the flower, he shall both cut off the sprigs with pruning hooks, and take away and cut down the branches.

α.18.6 Nish pish moae nukkodtumunash wutche wadchue puppinshasog, kah ohkee puppinashimwut, kah puppinshasog pish wussequannussinuneau, kah wame ohkee puppinashimwog pish uppopónamineau.
E.18.6 They shall be left together unto the fowls of the mountains, and to the beasts of the earth: and the fowls shall summer upon them, and all the beasts of the earth shall winter upon them.

α.18.7 Ne ahquompak mag8onk pish paudtauun Jehovah ayeuteaunit, wutch nasw[á]yeue kah pissagkinnumwe missinninnuut, wutch unkqueneúnkqué missinninnúog wutch waj kûtchissik yeu pajeh, kuhkohhum8e wutohtimoin kah tahtashkuhkôsue ut musseetut, noh wutohke sepúash máchtteómuk, wehque wutayeuonganit Jehovah áyeuhteaunit, wadchuut Zion.
E.18.7 In that time shall the present be brought unto the LORD of hosts of a people scattered and peeled, and from a people terrible from their beginning hitherto; a nation meted out and trodden under foot, whose land the rivers have spoiled, to the place of the name of the LORD of hosts, the mount Zion.

α.19.1 OOWeanun Egypt, kusseh, Lord naiyeumuk kenupshae matokqs, kah pish peyaum8 Egypt, kah Egyptie nuuneukontúnkanog pish ontappúog ut anaquabit, kah wuttah Egypt pish mohtupohteau ut nôeu. 
E.19.1 The burden of Egypt. Behold, the LORD rideth upon a swift cloud, and shall come into Egypt: and the idols of Egypt shall be moved at his presence, and the heart of Egypt shall melt in the midst of it.

α.19.2 Kah Egyptiansog nummekonitteh Egyptiansog, kah nag nishnoh pasuk pish ayeuuhkonau wematoh; kah nishnoh pasuk ayeuuhkonittue weetatteamungoh, otan ayeuuhkonnittue otan, kah ass8tamóonk ayeuuhkonittue ass8tamóonk.
E.19.2 And I will set the Egyptians against the Egyptians: and they shall fight every one against his brother, and every one against his neighbour; city against city, and kingdom against kingdom.

α.19.3 Kah wunnashauonguh Egypt pish sauunumwoh ut nashauwe, kah pish nuppaguan ukkogkáhquttuongan8, kah nag pish natinnewhaog enineuhkontungoh, & mamontomoh kah pauwaoh, kah kôsukquomoh.
E.19.3 And the spirit of Egypt shall fail in the midst thereof; and I will destroy the counsel thereof: and they shall seek to the idols, and to the charmers, and to them that have familiar spirits, and to the wizards.

α.19.4 Kah nukkuppoh Egyptiansog en wunnutcheganit unkapinohteae sontimoh, kah chenauausu ketass8t pish nah wunnanawunuh, n8wau Lord, Jehvoah ayeuhteaunit.
E.19.4 And the Egyptians will I give over into the hand of a cruel lord; and a fierce king shall rule over them, saith the Lord, the LORD of hosts.

α.19.5 Kah nippe pish mahtsheau wutch ketahhanit, kah seip pish mahchim8 kah nunohteau.
E.19.5 And the waters shall fail from the sea, and the river shall be wasted and dried up.

α.19.6 Kah pish quinnuppechu[i]numwog seip en nôadtut, kah pummeneutonkane sepuash pish mohchiyeuash kah nunohtaash: wekinashquash, kah uppeanashkonog pish upp8taash.
E.19.6 And they shall turn the rivers far away; and the brooks of defence shall be emptied and dried up: the reeds and flags shall wither.

α.19.7 Wussukhum8e wekinashquash ut kishke sepuwussit, ut kutt8n8out sepuwussash, kah nishnoh teag ohteuhkon ut kishke sepuwussit pish uhp8taash, kah t8hanash, kah matta wonk ohtan8ash.
E.19.7 The paper reeds by the brooks, by the mouth of the brooks, and every thing sown by the brooks, shall wither, be driven away, and be no more.

α.19.8 Káh wonk n8tamogquaenuog pish mauog, kah neg wame omácheg sepuwussehtu pish mauog, kah nag sepagkenoncheg quomphunkoh ut nippekontu pish mahchimóog.
E.19.8 The fishers also shall mourn, and all they that cast angle into the brooks shall lament, and they that spread nets upon the waters shall languish.

α.19.9 Kah wonk neg anakausitcheg ut wunne hashabput, kah neg quompho[n]kônehteácheg, pish wohwohkukquianumóog,
E.19.9 Moreover they that work in fine flax, and they that weave networks, shall be confounded.

α.19.10 Kah nag pish pohquetahhamauóog uppogkodtantam8ongan8oash, wame neg ayigeg pahsohthegash kah nuppesash wutche nomohsog.
E.19.10 And they shall be broken in the purposes thereof, all that make sluices and ponds for fish.

α.19.11 Wunnamuhkut Zoane sontimóog as8tuog, kogahquttuonk 8waantamwe Pharo kogagqutteam8moh, puppinashimweyeu8: toh woh kuttin unnomw8 Pharoh, nen wunnau[m]onuh waantog, wunnaumonuh kehchiyeue ket[à]ss8tamwog?
E.19.11 Surely the princes of Zoan are fools, the counsel of the wise counsellors of Pharaoh is become brutish: how say ye unto Pharaoh, I am the son of the wise, the son of ancient kings?

α.19.12 Uttoh nag wutapinneau? uttiyeug waantamwog, kah nag yeuyeu unnukqush, kah wahteauhettich uttoh Jehovah ayeuhteaanit en pogkodtantog ut Egypt.
E.19.12 Where are they? where are thy wise men? and let them tell thee now, and let them know what the LORD of hosts hath purposed upon Egypt.

α.19.13 Zoane sontimóog as8tuog, Nophe sontimóog neg as8kekomóog, nag wonk panne[n]osheaog Egyptiansog, neg k[ô]namunoncheh ut wuchipán8ongan8out.
E.19.13 The princes of Zoan are become fools, the princes of Noph are deceived; they have also seduced Egypt, even they that are the stay of the tribes thereof.

α.19.14 Jehovah kenukunau wonke nashauonguh ut nôe, kah panneseaheáog Egyptiansoh nishnoh pasuk wutanakausuonganit, onatuh kogkeussippamwenin kehkepshont ut ummenadtam8onganit.
E.19.14 The LORD hath mingled a perverse spirit in the midst thereof: and they have caused Egypt to err in every work thereof, as a drunken man staggereth in his vomit.

α.19.15 Kah matta pish na anakausuonganinno wutch Egipt, ne muhpuhkuk asuh wussukqun, wuttuhkq asuh rush woh wutussen.
E.19.15 Neither shall there be any work for Egypt, which the head or tail, branch or rush, may do.

α.19.16 Ne kesukok Egypt pish ogqueneunkqussu mittamwossissut, kah pish wabesu, kah nag pish wabesuog newutch wuttattauwunnumóonk wunnutcheg Jehovah, ayeuteaanit, neh ogkomáe tattauwunnumauumpoh.
E.19.16 In that day shall Egypt be like unto women: and it shall be afraid and fear because of the shaking of the hand of the LORD of hosts, which he shaketh over it.

α.19.17 Kah Judae ohke pish ukquohquaquênauwanum8onganin en Egypt, nishnoh pasuk ne weogqutuk noh pish wabesu, wutche ukken8n8waonk Jehovah ayeuteaunit neh ayeuuhkonittue pakodtantog,
E.19.17 And the land of Judah shall be a terror unto Egypt, every one that maketh mention thereof shall be afraid in himself, because of the counsel of the LORD of hosts, which he hath determined against it.

α.19.18 Ne kesukok napanna tahshinash keitotanash, ut ohkit Egypt, unnont8waog Canaane unnont8w[à]onk, kah chadchekeimau Jehovah ayeuhteaanit, pasuk pish hennau, pagwanue keitotan.
E.19.18 In that day shall five cities in the land of Egypt speak the language of Canaan, and swear to the LORD of hosts; one shall be called, The city of destruction.

α.19.19 Ne kesukok na pish Altareu8 en Jehovahut ut nôeu Egypte ohkeit, kah pogkomuhquonk sussippôeu en Lord$ut.
E.19.19 In that day shall there be an altar to the LORD in the midst of the land of Egypt, and a pillar at the border thereof to the LORD.

α.19.20 Kah ne pish kuhkinneasuonganu8, kah wauwaonganu8 en Jehovah ayeute[à]anit ut ohkeit Egypt, newutche neg pish mauunitteauaog Jehovah wutche woskhuwacheg, kah noh pish ann8nau wadchanuwaenu[h], kah missugken, kah noh pish uppohquohwhunoh.
E.19.20 And it shall be for a sign and for a witness unto the LORD of hosts in the land of Egypt: for they shall cry unto the LORD because of the oppressors, and he shall send them a saviour, and a great one, and he shall deliver them.

α.19.21 Kah Jehovah pish waheau ut Egypt, kah Egyptiansog pish wahheaog Jehovah ne kesukok, kah pish sephausuog, kah mag8og, nux pish nag quoshauwaog quoshauwaonk en Jehovahut, kah pish wutusseneau.
E.19.21 And the LORD shall be known to Egypt, and the Egyptians shall know the LORD in that day, and shall do sacrifice and oblation; yea, they shall vow a vow unto the LORD, and perform it.

α.19.22 Kah Jehovah pish togkodtam Egypt, pish wuttogkodtamun, kah wunnetskehteauun: kah nag pish qushkeog en Jehovahut, kah noh pish nupweshanau, kah pish wunnetskeheuh.
E.19.22 And the LORD shall smite Egypt: he shall smite and heal it: and they shall return even to the LORD, and he shall be intreated of them, and shall heal them.

α.19.23 Ne kesukok na pish wunne may wutch Egypt en Assyria, kah wut-Assyrian pish petutteau Egypt, kah wut-Egy[g]tian en Assyria, kah Egyptiansog pish wuttinneumuhkauóog Assyriansoh.
E.19.23 In that day shall there be a highway out of Egypt to Assyria, and the Assyrian shall come into Egypt, and the Egyptian into Assyria, and the Egyptians shall serve with the Assyrians.

α.19.24 Ne kesukok, Israel noh pish nash8it weeche Egypt, kah weeche Assyria, wunanitteaonk ut nashaue ohkeit.
E.19.24 In that day shall Israel be the third with Egypt and with Assyria, even a blessing in the midst of the land:

α.19.25 Jehovah ayeuteaunit neh pish wunánumuh, n8wadt, Wunnánumunaj Egypt nummissinninneumog, kah Assyria nunnutchegane anakausuonk, kah Israel nutohtóonk.
E.19.25 Whom the LORD of hosts shall bless, saying, Blessed be Egypt my people, and Assyria the work of my hands, and Israel mine inheritance.

α.20.1 NE kôdtum8k Tartan paont Ashdod (Sargon Assyriae ketass8t ann8nont) kah mátomppagwuhkontog Ashdod, kah sohkog.
E.20.1 In the year that Tartan came unto Ashdod, (when Sargon the king of Assyria sent him,) and fought against Ashdod, and took it;

α.20.2 Kah ne na[n] ahquompi Jehovah ket8kau Isaiahoh wunnaumonuh Amoz, n8wau, Monchish ompanish man8tionak wutch kusseganit, kah kodokkussináish, kah ne wutussenáh, pòsqushau, kah mamóhchishkussitteau.
E.20.2 At the same time spake the LORD by Isaiah the son of Amoz, saying, Go and loose the sackcloth from off thy loins, and put off thy shoe from thy foot. And he did so, walking naked and barefoot.

α.20.3 Kah Jehovah n8wop, neane nuttinneum Isaiah posqushadt, kah mamóhchishkussitteadt nishwe kodtumwae wutche kuhkinneasuonk kah monchanatam8onk ut Egypt, kah ut Ethiopia.
E.20.3 And the LORD said, Like as my servant Isaiah hath walked naked and barefoot three years for a sign and wonder upon Egypt and upon Ethiopia;

α.20.4 Ne pish wuttinne Assyriae ketass8t missinóhko[uh] Egyptiansoh kah Ethiopiansoh, wuskênúh kah kutchisoh, poskissue kah mamohchishkussittaeu, kah poskitteáeu wutakodchinat Egypt.
E.20.4 So shall the king of Assyria lead away the Egyptians prisoners, and the Ethiopians captives, young and old, naked and barefoot, even with their buttocks uncovered, to the shame of Egypt.

α.20.5 Kah nag pish wabesuonóuh kah akodchuwóunóuh Ethiopia, annóonáhetticheh, kah Egypt wussohsum8ongan8uh.
E.20.5 And they shall be afraid and ashamed of Ethiopia their expectation, and of Egypt their glory.

α.20.6 Kah neg wadohkitcheg yeu ohkeit pish n8waog ne kesukok, kusseh, ne n$nih annoósuontamog uttoh asph8aogkup wutch nontummóadtuonk, pohquohwhunnittinneat wutch Assyriae ketass8t: kah uttoh woh kuttin pohquohhamunan?
E.20.6 And the inhabitant of this isle shall say in that day, Behold, such is our expectation, whither we flee for help to be delivered from the king of Assyria: and how shall we escape?

α.21.1 OWeanan ketahhanue touohkomuk: onatuh sowanishinne pemsquoh paumshadt, ne ne 8m88 touohkomuk, wutch u[n]kqunneunkquotte ohkeit.
E.21.1 The burden of the desert of the sea. As whirlwinds in the south pass through; so it cometh from the desert, from a terrible land.

α.21.2 Uhqunneunkquotte unnaumanissuonk n8wahteauwahit: wunass8muwaénin wanass8muwae unnéhhuau, kah matchehuwaénin matchehuau, kuhkuhquish, woi Elam: weenussumwehtok, woi Media; wame ummishanóm8ongan8 n8wohkukquoshitteauun.
E.21.2 A grievous vision is declared unto me; the treacherous dealer dealeth treacherously, and the spoiler spoileth. Go up, O Elam: besiege, O Media; all the sighing thereof have I made to cease.

α.21.3 Newaj nusséganit numwohteau onkquomom8onk, onkquomom8ongsh nuttohqunuk, onatuh wutonkquomom8onk mittumwussis neechadt, nunnauwáeep n8tamon, kah nutchepshomp naumon.
E.21.3 Therefore are my loins filled with pain: pangs have taken hold upon me, as the pangs of a woman that travaileth: I was bowed down at the hearing of it; I was dismayed at the seeing of it.

α.21.4 Nuttah nunnuksheau, wabesuonk n8w[a]buwunuk: n8wekontam8e nuhkon8m, ukquinnuppinnumun en 8wabesuontamunut.
E.21.4 My heart panted, fearfulness affrighted me: the night of my pleasure hath he turned into fear unto me.

α.21.5 Quashauwehtam8k table, askuhwekontam8k askuhwete[à]e$komukqut, meetsek kah wuttattam8k: omohkek sontim[ó]og, sussequnnumok ogqunneg.
E.21.5 Prepare the table, watch in the watchtower, eat, drink: arise, ye princes, and anoint the shield.

α.21.6 Newutche yeu nuttugqunah Lord, monchish askuhwheteaénin wunnash, wahteauwahuwaj uttoh [án] nag*.
E.21.6 For thus hath the LORD said unto me, Go, set a watchman, let him declare what he seeth.

α.21.7 Kah naum chariot, kah neesuog horsesoh nay8mukqutcheg, assese chariot, kah kamelse chariot; kah menuhke ahchuwussittámup.
E.21.7 And he saw a chariot with a couple of horsemen, a chariot of asses, and a chariot of camels; and he hearkened diligently with much heed:

α.21.8 Kah mishont8wop, qunnónou: nussontimom nunnagwutteae neepoh ut askuhwheteáe komukqut: kesukodtáe, kah askuhwhekonat n8nashit wowompannu.
E.21.8 And he cried, A lion: My lord, I stand continually upon the watchtower in the daytime, and I am set in my ward whole nights:

α.21.9 Kah kusseh, yeu ut peyom8 wosketompàe chariot, nes8og horsesoh nay8mukqutcheg, kah namp8ham kah n8wau, Babylon penushau, penushau, kah wame ummanitt8mue nunnukontunkanouh, uppohquttahwhoh en ohkeit. 
E.21.9 And, behold, here cometh a chariot of men, with a couple of horsemen. And he answered and said, Babylon is fallen, is fallen; and all the graven images of her gods he hath broken unto the ground.

α.21.10 Woi nuppogham8onk, kah ahhuttanuppoghamuk weatchiminneash, ne n8tamauogkup Lord ayeuteaanit, um$Manitt8moh Israel, k8wahteauwáhununeau.
E.21.10 O my threshing, and the corn of my floor: that which I have heard of the LORD of hosts, the God of Israel, have I declared unto you.

α.21.11 OOweanun Dumah: n8wehkomuk wutch Seir, askuhwheteaènin toh utt8che tipukod? askuhwheteaénin toh utt8che tipukod?
E.21.11 The burden of Dumah. He calleth to me out of Seir, Watchman, what of the night? Watchman, what of the night?

α.21.12 Askuhwheteaénin n8wau, mohtompan peyaum8, kah wonk nuhkon: kod nat8tomwehteáog, nat8tomwehteagk: qushkek, peyunk.
E.21.12 The watchman said, The morning cometh, and also the night: if ye will enquire, enquire ye: return, come.

α.21.13 OOweanun Arabia. Ut Arabiae touohkomukqut ne pish kukkouéneau, woi Dedanimáe chippan8e pomushaog.
E.21.13 The burden upon Arabia. In the forest in Arabia shall ye lodge, O ye travelling companies of Dedanim.

α.21.14 Wadohkitcheg Tema paudtauáog nippe noh kuhkutt8nutche, koshkomme assamáog petukqunneg neh wusseemunutcheh.
E.21.14 The inhabitants of the land of Tema brought water to him that was thirsty, they prevented with their bread him that fled.

α.21.15 Newutche nag wussemóog wutch tohkodteganehtu, wutch kodtunnum8e togkodteg[a]nit, wutch wonkinnónat ohtomp, wutch unkqunneungane mattompagwut.
E.21.15 For they fled from the swords, from the drawn sword, and from the bent bow, and from the grievousness of war.

α.21.16 Newutche yeu nuttugqunat Jehovah, ash nánukqut kodtumun8gkup, neaunag ne ukkodtum8m noh ann8nit, neit wame wussohsumóonk K[e]dar pish penusheau.
E.21.16 For thus hath the LORD said unto me, Within a year, according to the years of an hireling, and all the glory of Kedar shall fail:

α.21.17 Kah neg ashqushoncheg ne adtass8hettit pepummuwaenuog, ummissugkeneumoh wunnaumonuh Kedar, pish ogqusheáog, newutche Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel wussin.
E.21.17 And the residue of the number of archers, the mighty men of the children of Kedar, shall be diminished: for the LORD God of Israel hath spoken it.

α.22.1 OOWeanun monoma[u]sue 8nouhkoi, tohkutushpunam mamusse kuhquhqueog woskeche kommukquehtu.
E.22.1 The burden of the valley of vision. What aileth thee now, that thou art wholly gone up to the housetops?

α.22.2 K[é]n nomwabetunkquean wogkouongash, menumuhquáeu keitotan, wekontamwae otan, nushae k8wosketompomog, matta nushóog nashpe togkodteg, asuh matta nupp8[o]g ut ayeuwuttinneat.
E.22.2 Thou that art full of stirs, a tumultuous city, joyous city: thy slain men are not slain with the sword, nor dead in battle.

α.22.3 Wame nanawunnuácheg moáeu wussem8og, k[è]nepunukquog pepummuwaénúh, wame neg námteauunumukeg nehnesippissuog, neg nôadtit wadt8k[au]utcheg.
E.22.3 All thy rulers are fled together, they are bound by the archers: all that are found in thee are bound together, which have fled from far.

α.22.4 Newaj n8wi, p8nampameh, pish n8weesogkohpûs, ahchue taphehkon, wutche matcheheaongan8 wuttaun8oh nummissinninnúmog.
E.22.4 Therefore said I, Look away from me; I will weep bitterly, labour not to comfort me, because of the spoiling of the daughter of my people.

α.22.5 Newutche ne wuttamehpunáe kesukod, kah tahtashkuhkôadtin, kah unkque wuttaméhpunon nashpe Lord Jehovah ayeuteaunit, ut monomo[n]sue 8nouhkóiyeuut, n8kuhkonat wonkôn8sinash, kah mauongash nogque wadchuuhk[ó]ntu.
E.22.5 For it is a day of trouble, and of treading down, and of perplexity by the Lord GOD of hosts in the valley of vision, breaking down the walls, and of crying to the mountains.

α.22.6 Kah Elam kenunnum petan, nashpe wosketompae chariotsash, kah horsesoh nayeumukqutcheg, kah Kir poshkinumun ogqunneg.
E.22.6 And Elam bare the quiver with chariots of men and horsemen, and Kir uncovered the shield.

α.22.7 Kah pish n$nih, k8ne 8nouuhkóiyeumash pish nanumwohteau ch[e]riotsash, kah horsesoh nayeumukqutcheg, pish sepunnego[n]éhteaog en nogque squontam[é]htu.
E.22.7 And it shall come to pass, that thy choicest valleys shall be full of chariots, and the horsemen shall set themselves in array at the gate.

α.22.8 Kah miskom upputtaguhwheg Judah, kah ne kesukok, kummónunneamup ukkenauwameonk touohkomukque komukqut.
E.22.8 And he discovered the covering of Judah, and thou didst look in that day to the armour of the house of the forest.

α.22.9 Kah wonk kenaumumw8 pohquiyeue ukkeitotan David, nish monatash, kah kummohmóunumumw8 w8muhkôáge nippesse nippeash.
E.22.9 Ye have seen also the breaches of the city of David, that they are many: and ye gathered together the waters of the lower pool.

α.22.10 Kah kutogketamumw8 Jerusalem wetuomash, kah ken8kahteamw8 wetuomash menehketeauunat ummánsk.
E.22.10 And ye have numbered the houses of Jerusalem, and the houses have ye broken down to fortify the wall.

α.22.11 Kah wonk kutayimumw8 pasahtheg ut nashaue neese ummanskut, wutche nukkone nuppisse nuppe: qut matta kummonunnéan[ô]mw8 noh ne kezteunk, kah matta k8t8anumw8 noh kahkenauwehteunkup noadt.
E.22.11 Ye made also a ditch between the two walls for the water of the old pool: but ye have not looked unto the maker thereof, neither had respect unto him that fashioned it long ago.

α.22.12 Kah ne kesukok Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaunit k8wehkomukqun en mauunat, kah neuantamunat, kah mupukkontupónat, kah puttukquobpissineat man8tionak.
E.22.12 And in that day did the Lord GOD of hosts call to weeping, and to mourning, and to baldness, and to girding with sackcloth:

α.22.13 Kah kusseh weekontamóonk, kah muskouantamoonk, nushaonk oxenóg, kah shepsog, meechuonk weyaus, kah wuttattamoonk wine meetsitteuh kah wuttattamutt[u]h, newutche saup pish kenupmun.
E.22.13 And behold joy and gladness, slaying oxen, and killing sheep, eating flesh, and drinking wine: let us eat and drink; for to morrow we shall die.

α.22.14 Kah wahteauwahuwonáh ut nehtauogkut, nashpe Jehovah ayeute[a]anit, wunnamuhkut yeu matcheseonk matta pish pahketeauun ut kuhhogkaóut, nô pajeh kenuppunnaôont, n8wau Lord Jehovah ayeuhteaunit.
E.22.14 And it was revealed in mine ears by the LORD of hosts, Surely this iniquity shall not be purged from you till ye die, saith the Lord GOD of hosts.

α.22.15 Yeu wussin Lord Jehovah ayuhteaunit, monchish, aush noh nompak8 wadchanuk, noh Shebna, noh piohquttuk wetu, n8wash.
E.22.15 Thus saith the Lord GOD of hosts, Go, get thee unto this treasurer, even unto Shebna, which is over the house, and say,

α.22.16 Teagus kutahto yeu$ut? kah teaguas kutahto na$ut? waj 8neeteáan weenohke yeu$ut: noh weenohkéhkauont wuhhogkuh qunuhqu: kah waneúhquttamauont wuhhogkuh wetu ut qussukquanit?
E.22.16 What hast thou here? and whom hast thou here, that thou hast hewed thee out a sepulchre here, as he that heweth him out a sepulchre on high, and that graveth an habitation for himself in a rock?

α.22.17 Kusseh Jehovah pish kummishe missinóhkônittue monchanuk, kah pish wunnamuhkut kupputtaguhhuk.
E.22.17 Behold, the LORD will carry thee away with a mighty captivity, and will surely cover thee.

α.22.18 Noh pish wunnamuhkut chekee k8wahwaapuhkunk onatuh pompasukonganit, en mishékishku wutohtimóneat, na pish kuttit nuppuneau: kah na pish kuttit sohsumoe chariotsash akodjteauunat kussontimom wek.
E.22.18 He will surely violently turn and toss thee like a ball into a large country: there shalt thou die, and there the chariots of thy glory shall be the shame of thy lord's house.

α.22.19 Kah push kutáma8koush wutch kutayeuonganit, kah wutch k8niyeuonganit pish ken8kinuk.
E.22.19 And I will drive thee from thy station, and from thy state shall he pull thee down.

α.22.20 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, pish n8wehkom nuttinneum Eliakim wunnaumonuh Hilkiah.
E.22.20 And it shall come to pass in that day, that I will call my servant Eliakim the son of Hilkiah:

α.22.21 Kah pish nuthogqueh kuppetashqusháonk, kah nummenuhkeh wutch kupputtukquobissu, kah nupponam kena[n]ánuwaonk ut wunnutcheganit, kah noh pish 8sh8oh wadohkitcheg Jerusalem, & en wekit Judah.
E.22.21 And I will clothe him with thy robe, and strengthen him with thy girdle, and I will commit thy government into his hand: and he shall be a father to the inhabitants of Jerusalem, and to the house of Judah.

α.22.22 Kah David weke pohquoshadtikunk, nukquenohtauun wuttugkit: ne pish wuttin wôshinnumun, kah matta pish howan kupham8un, kah noh pish ukkuphamun, kah matta pish howan uppohqu[à]num8un.
E.22.22 And the key of the house of David will I lay upon his shoulder; so he shall open, and none shall shut; and he shall shut, and none shall open.

α.22.23 Kah nukkishpun onatuh kenontukqueg ut wunnamuhkutée ayeuonganit, kah noh pish sohsumóe appuonk 8shoh wekit.
E.22.23 And I will fasten him as a nail in a sure place; and he shall be for a glorious throne to his father's house.

α.22.24 Kah nag pish 8waôhshanóuh wame 8shoh week8e sohsumóonk, wutontseon, kah wutontsétuonk, wame papeasike wishquash wutch wuttattamóe wishquadt, pajeh wame kehchéshquadt.
E.22.24 And they shall hang upon him all the glory of his father's house, the offspring and the issue, all vessels of small quantity, from the vessels of cups, even to all the vessels of flagons.

α.22.25 Ne kesukok, n8wau Jehovah ayeuhteaunit, kenontukquontunk ne manuhkehteamuk ut wunnamuhkutée ayeuonganit, pish ontahtauun, kah pish tummes[s]umun, kah penusheau; kah weanun ne na quenohtagkup ish tummussumun, newutche Jehovah ukkutt8kontámun.
E.22.25 In that day, saith the LORD of hosts, shall the nail that is fastened in the sure place be removed, and be cut down, and fall; and the burden that was upon it shall be cut off: for the LORD hath spoken it.

α.23.1 OOWeanun Tyre. OOn8k kenaau Tarshishe kuht8nogquog, newutche mahchim8, newaj matta wetuwomun8g, wanne petutteau[n]: wutch Chittimme ohkeit nag wahteauwahuoneau.
E.23.1 The burden of Tyre. Howl, ye ships of Tarshish; for it is laid waste, so that there is no house, no entering in: from the land of Chittim it is revealed to them.

α.23.2 Chequnappek wadohkeógish munóhhanéhtu, ken, Zidone anaqushaenuog neg quoshkodteacheg keitoh, ken[a]mwamechumuhkonukquog.
E.23.2 Be still, ye inhabitants of the isle; thou whom the merchants of Zidon, that pass over the sea, have replenished.

α.23.3 Kah nashpe mishe nippeash, wusk[a]nnem Sihor, sepue kepenumóonk ne wutteashegen8m, kah noh wutohtim[o]inne ahhut kodtauwompa[simu]k.
E.23.3 And by great waters the seed of Sihor, the harvest of the river, is her revenue; and she is a mart of nations.

α.23.4 Akodchish, woi Zidon, newutche keitoh ket8hkau, ummenuhkesuonk keitoh, n8wau, matta nukkodta[u]wekhe[ó]h, asuh nunneechóh, asuh matta n8nadchan8 wuskenuog, asuh matta n8wadchan8 nunksquaog.
E.23.4 Be thou ashamed, O Zidon: for the sea hath spoken, even the strength of the sea, saying, I travail not, nor bring forth children, neither do I nourish up young men, nor bring up virgins.

α.23.5 Onatuh neantunkquok papaume Egypt, ne pish wuttin unkque onkquomominneau n8tamwahettit papaume Tyre.
E.23.5 As at the report concerning Egypt, so shall they be sorely pained at the report of Tyre.

α.23.6 Qushkodteagk Tarshish 8n8k kenaau wadohkeógish munohhanit.
E.23.6 Pass ye over to Tarshish; howl, ye inhabitants of the isle.

α.23.7 Sun yeu k8wekontamwe otaneau, na wunnukkoneayeu8onk wutch n8adt? nehenwonche wussetash pish noadtit uss8unuk pen8wohteauneat.
E.23.7 Is this your joyous city, whose antiquity is of ancient days? her own feet shall carry her afar off to sojourn.

α.23.8 Howan yeu nemunuk kogahquttaonk ayeuuhkonittue Tyre, chetuhquabinnuwae keitotan, wutanaqushaenúmoh sontimaúooh, ukkodtauwompasuéneumoh neg quttiánumukqussuog ut ohkeit?
E.23.8 Who hath taken this counsel against Tyre, the crowning city, whose merchants are princes, whose traffickers are the honourable of the earth?

α.23.9 Jehovah ayeuteaunit uppogkodtantamun nishketeauunat wame pehtuánumwe sohsumóonk, kah jishónumwaheonaóont wame quohtianumukqussitcheg ohkeit.
E.23.9 The LORD of hosts hath purposed it, to stain the pride of all glory, and to bring into contempt all the honourable of the earth.

α.23.10 Papannupohkash kutohke onatuh sepuut, woi wuttaunoh Tarshish: matta na wonk menuhkesuonganunn8.
E.23.10 Pass through thy land as a river, O daughter of Tarshish: there is no more strength.

α.23.11 Summ[a]gunum wunnutcheg woskeche kehtahhanit, nunnukshadto ass8tam8ongash, Jehovah ann8team8 ayeuuhkonittue anaqusháe otan, paguatauunat ummenehtekomukquash.
E.23.11 He stretched out his hand over the sea, he shook the kingdoms: the LORD hath given a commandment against the merchant city, to destroy the strong holds thereof.

α.23.12 Kah n8wau, neketeashe wekontamun, woi ken mukk8kinae penomp, wuttaunoh Zidon, omkish qushkodteash en Chittim, na$ut wonk matt apish wonk k8tanwôsinn8onganéin.
E.23.12 And he said, Thou shalt no more rejoice, O thou oppressed virgin, daughter of Zidon: arise, pass over to Chittim; there also shalt thou have no rest.

α.23.13 Kusseh, wutohkeeu Caldeansog yeug missinninnuog matta appupaneg noh pajeh Assyriansog quenohtae ponamwog wutche nag wadohkitcheg touohkomuk: nag wunohtóog ukqunuhque kommuk88ash, nag tahshinnumwog ummishe kommuk88ash, kah uppaguatauun.
E.23.13 Behold the land of the Chaldeans; this people was not, till the Assyrian founded it for them that dwell in the wilderness: they set up the towers thereof, they raised up the palaces thereof; and he brought it to ruin.

α.23.14 OOn8k kenaau Tarshishe kuht8[n]ogquog, newutche kummenuhkesuognan8 mohtupa[sh]in.
E.23.14 Howl, ye ships of Tarshish: for your strength is laid waste.

α.23.15 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, Tyre pish wanantamun nesausuk tahshinchage kodtumwae, neaunak ukkesukodtumash pasuk ketass8t, mahtshunk nesausuk tahshinchage kodtum8, Tyre pish ogk8humau kogkeeusqua[u]t.
E.23.15 And it shall come to pass in that day, that Tyre shall be forgotten seventy years, according to the days of one king: after the end of seventy years shall Tyre sing as an harlot.

α.23.16 Nemunush harp papaumwushash otanat, ken kogkeeusquau wananumunumuk, wunont8ash, m8cheke, unn8humush onk woh kummehquanumit.
E.23.16 Take an harp, go about the city, thou harlot that hast been forgotten; make sweet melody, sing many songs, that thou mayest be remembered.

α.23.17 Kah pish n$nih, mahtshunk nesausuk tahshinchage kodtumm8, Jehovah pish nátauwahto Tyre, kah noh pish quinnuppu ponampóadtinneat, kah pish nanwun8dsquáôsu en wame ass8tam8onganehtu muttaohket, ut woskeche ohkeit.
E.23.17 And it shall come to pass after the end of seventy years, that the LORD will visit Tyre, and she shall turn to her hire, and shall commit fornication with all the kingdoms of the world upon the face of the earth.

α.23.18 Kah nish kodtauwompasitcheh, kah ne ponampauut pish wunnetupanatamweyeu8 Jehovahut: ne matta pish nompak8unehtaun asuh wadchanum8un, newutche ukkodtauwompasuonk pish wutche nag apitcheg anaquabit Jehovah, tapupwunneat, kah sephogk8unon.
E.23.18 And her merchandise and her hire shall be holiness to the LORD: it shall not be treasured nor laid up; for her merchandise shall be for them that dwell before the LORD, to eat sufficiently, and for durable clothing.

α.24.1 KUsseh, Jehovah wussequnnumun ohke kah ummohtupáshitteauun, kah 8nim[usk]inumun, kah seahwau neh ne wadohkinitcheh.
E.24.1 Behold, the LORD maketh the earth empty, and maketh it waste, and turneth it upside down, and scattereth abroad the inhabitants thereof.

α.24.2 Kah pish n$nih, ne anihettit missinninnuog, ne wuttinninneau sephausuaenuog, nea[in]it wuttinneumin, ne wuttinniin wussontimomun, neaniit nunksquoh, ne wuttinniin wussonksquomoh, neaniit adtôadt ne wuttinniin noh maguk, neaniit nagohkouaenin ne wuttinniin noh nogo[h]kouónit, ne aniit noh neemunuk onts[a]uohteaonk ne wuttinniin noh maguk ontsouohteaonk.
E.24.2 And it shall be, as with the people, so with the priest; as with the servant, so with his master; as with the maid, so with her mistress; as with the buyer, so with the seller; as with the lender, so with the borrower; as with the taker of usury, so with the giver of usury to him.

α.24.3 Ohke pish papuhquanne sequnnumun kah papuhquanne matcheteauun, newutche Jehovah wussin yeu kutt8onk. 
E.24.3 The land shall be utterly emptied, and utterly spoiled: for the LORD hath spoken this word.

α.24.4 Ohke maum8, kah mohtsheau, muttaok mahchum8, kah mahchum8, pahtuánumwee[n]unkqussitcheg ohkeit mahchum8og.
E.24.4 The earth mourneth and fadeth away, the world languisheth and fadeth away, the haughty people of the earth do languish.

α.24.5 Kah wonk ohke nishketeauun ut agwe neg wadohkitcheg, newutche panneussehtauáog naumatuonguh, ôs8wunnumwog kuhk8waonk, pohquenumwog m[à]chemohtag wunn8waonk.
E.24.5 The earth also is defiled under the inhabitants thereof; because they have transgressed the laws, changed the ordinance, broken the everlasting covenant.

α.24.6 Newaj matánittuonk paguodtunk ohke, kah neg na apitcheg touwiyeuog, newaj wadohkitcheg ohkeit chikohsuog, kah ogguhsuog sequhkussuog.
E.24.6 Therefore hath the curse devoured the earth, and they that dwell therein are desolate: therefore the inhabitants of the earth are burned, and few men left.

α.24.7 Wuske wine mau, weenomwussippog mahchum8, wame pôanittamwutteahoncheg mishanom8og.
E.24.7 The new wine mourneth, the vine languisheth, all the merryhearted do sigh.

α.24.8 Tabretse wunont8waonk ahquohteau, 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 neg wekontogig wohkukquoshin, harpe wekontamóonk ahquohteau.
E.24.8 The mirth of tabrets ceaseth, the noise of them that rejoice endeth, the joy of the harp ceaseth.

α.24.9 Nag matta pish unn8hamae wuttattamwog wine, onkuppe pish 8wesogkonhúkquneau neg wadtattogig.
E.24.9 They shall not drink wine with a song; strong drink shall be bitter to them that drink it.

α.24.10 Nanwohteae otan pokshadtauun, nish noh wetu kuppuhhôsu, onk woh mo howae wosketomp petutteóou.
E.24.10 The city of confusion is broken down: every house is shut up, that no man may come in.

α.24.11 Wuttohposuog wine ut maikontu, wame wekontamóonk pohkenashin, 8wekontamóonk ohke mohtsheau.
E.24.11 There is a crying for wine in the streets; all joy is darkened, the mirth of the land is gone.

α.24.12 Ut otanat touushin nukkodtumun, kah ussquont togkodtamun paguanuonk.
E.24.12 In the city is left desolation, and the gate is smitten with destruction.

α.24.13 Yeu n$nagk ut noeu ohkeit, ut kenugke missinninnútu, na pish neaneyeu8 nenemonteamuk oliveuhtug, kah mukkuposquae weenominneash mohtouwunneamuk.
E.24.13 When thus it shall be in the midst of the land among the people, there shall be as the shaking of an olive tree, and as the gleaning grapes when the vintage is done.

α.24.14 Nag pish mishont8waog, pish unn8homa[o]g newutche ukquttianumukqussuonk Jehovah, nag pish mishont8waog wutch kehtahhannit.
E.24.14 They shall lift up their voice, they shall sing for the majesty of the LORD, they shall cry aloud from the sea.

α.24.15 Newutche sohsum8wón8k Jehovah ut n8taut, 8wesuonk Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel ut ketahhanne munnahanash.
E.24.15 Wherefore glorify ye the LORD in the fires, even the name of the LORD God of Israel in the isles of the sea.

α.24.16 Wutch aongkauohkomuk n8tamumun ket8homàongash, sohsum8ón8k sampweusseaen, qut nussip, nutônauwussuonk, nutônauwussuonk, missi nutonkapunnaonk: wunass8muwaenuog wunass8muwaog, nux wunass8muwaenuog ahche wunass8muwaog.
E.24.16 From the uttermost part of the earth have we heard songs, even glory to the righteous. But I said, My leanness, my leanness, woe unto me! the treacherous dealers have dealt treacherously; yea, the treacherous dealers have dealt very treacherously.

α.24.17 Wabesuonk, kah pahsahtheg, kah ahpeh kenuhkuhkongquog, woi w[a]dohkeógish ohkeit.
E.24.17 Fear, and the pit, and the snare, are upon thee, O inhabitant of the earth.

α.24.18 Kah pish n$nih, noh waseemwuhteog wadtauatonkqussue wabesuonk, pish petshau psahtheganit, kah noh sohhog wutch noeu psahtheganit, pish puttahwhôu: newutche kenogkanégash wutch waabe wôhshwohtaash, kah ohkee quenohtagish nunnukshaash.
E.24.18 And it shall come to pass, that he who fleeth from the noise of the fear shall fall into the pit; and he that cometh up out of the midst of the pit shall be taken in the snare: for the windows from on high are open, and the foundations of the earth do shake.

α.24.19 Ohke papuhquanne poksheau, ohke papaquanne naswáshin, ohke m8cheke ontohteau.
E.24.19 The earth is utterly broken down, the earth is clean dissolved, the earth is moved exceedingly.

α.24.20 Ohke pish kekepsheau onatuh kogkeissippamwén, kah pish ogque ontaht[à]uun wetuómut, kah uppanneusseonk pish wuttuhkékhúkqun, kah pish penusheau, kah matta wonk omohkemun8[-]
E.24.20 The earth shall reel to and fro like a drunkard, and shall be removed like a cottage; and the transgression thereof shall be heavy upon it; and it shall fall, and not rise again.

α.24.21 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, Jehovah pish sasamatahwhau wutayeuwehtóm8uh quanunkqussitcheg, neg quanukquapicheg, kah ohkee ketass8tamwog, wosketohke.
E.24.21 And it shall come to pass in that day, that the LORD shall punish the host of the high ones that are on high, and the kings of the earth upon the earth.

α.24.22 Kah nag pish miyaéog onatuh kopshagkinatcheg moéhettit ut psahtheganit, kah pish kuppuhwhóog ut kuppishshagkinnittuonganit, kah mahtshik monatash kesukquash pish natauwaheóop.
E.24.22 And they shall be gathered together, as prisoners are gathered in the pit, and shall be shut up in the prison, and after many days shall they be visited.

α.24.23 Neit nahnepauhshadt pish mishakodcheheau, kah nepâuz akodchu, Jehovah ayeuteaunit tahs8tam8it ut Zion kah ut Jerusalem, kah ut anaquabenit ukkehchiyeumoh, sohsumóe.
E.24.23 Then the moon shall be confounded, and the sun ashamed, when the LORD of hosts shall reign in mount Zion, and in Jerusalem, and before his ancients gloriously.

α.25.1 WOi Jehovah, ken num-Manitt8m, kummishhesh, n8woweenodtum k8wesuonk, newutche kummonchanatamwe ussem, kenukkone kogohk8waongash pabuhtanumukqussuonk, kah wunnamuhkutéyeuuk.
E.25.1 O Lord, thou art my God; I will exalt thee, I will praise thy name; for thou hast done wonderful things; thy counsels of old are faithfulness and truth.

α.25.2 Newutche kenumwonkwâhteoh keitotan, k8weepótóhteam pummeneutaúsue otan: wanne kutotanáhtu ut papeáhetti penuwohteaog, matta pish wonk ayim8un.
E.25.2 For thou hast made of a city an heap; of a defenced city a ruin: a palace of strangers to be no city; it shall never be built.

α.25.3 Newaj pish menuhkesue missinninnuog sohsum8ónukquean, unkqueneunkque wutohtimonne keitotan pish k8wabesuonuk.
E.25.3 Therefore shall the strong people glorify thee, the city of the terrible nations shall fear thee.

α.25.4 Newutche ken ummenuhkesuonk machéku, ummenuhkesuonk quenauhikquit, ut ukquehquenauánumwinneat, ushpuhh8waonk wuch mishe tahshinit, onkauohteau wutche kussitteau, upp8tómuwaonk uhqunneunkqussitcheg moshtashuhkontamwéhhettiche pummeneutunk.
E.25.4 For thou hast been a strength to the poor, a strength to the needy in his distress, a refuge from the storm, a shadow from the heat, when the blast of the terrible ones is as a storm against the wall.

α.25.5 Pish kuppeéhteoh 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 penuwohteaog, onatuh kussittea[u] ut nunnobohteaoúut, kussitteau nashpe mahtohqse onkauohteau: 8tukqunn8 uhqunneunkqussitcheg pish n8kinnumun.
E.25.5 Thou shalt bring down the noise of strangers, as the heat in a dry place; even the heat with the shadow of a cloud: the branch of the terrible ones shall be brought low.

α.25.6 Kah yeuut wadchuut Jehovah ayeuteaunit pish weesée mishadtupweheau wame missinninnúh, sekqskausháe wine mishadtup8onk, wâónogqutcheg numwohteau ween sekqskaushae wine, wunnehteausu.
E.25.6 And in this mountain shall the LORD of hosts make unto all people a feast of fat things, a feast of wines on the lees, of fat things full of marrow, of wines on the lees well refined.

α.25.7 Kah yeuut wadchuut, pish paguanau woskechee onkwheg, onkwhut wame missinninnúog, kah puttogwheg sepáginaúsik wame wutohtim[ô]neat.
E.25.7 And he will destroy in this mountain the face of the covering cast over all people, and the vail that is spread over all nations.

α.25.8 Pish sohkôsue misheáskóu nupp8onk, kah Lord Jehovah pish jishkham wussippwegwash wutch wame muskesukqut, kah auskomaonk ummissinninnúmoh pish wutamaunumun wutch ohkeit: newutche Jehovah ukkutt8kontamun.
E.25.8 He will swallow up death in victory; and the Lord GOD will wipe away tears from off all faces; and the rebuke of his people shall he take away from off all the earth: for the LORD hath spoken it.

α.25.9 Kah pish unn8won ne kesukok, kusseh, yeuoh kum-Manitt8mun, nuppáhtsuwóunóun, kah noh pish k8wadchanukqun, yeuoh Jehovah, nuppáhtsuwóunnóun, n8wekontamumun, kah nummuskouantamumun ut 8wadchnuonganit.
E.25.9 And it shall be said in that day, Lo, this is our God; we have waited for him, and he will save us: this is the LORD; we have waited for him, we will be glad and rejoice in his salvation.

α.25.10 Newutche yeu$ut wadchuut wunnutcheg, Jehovah pish anwohshin, kah Moab pish tahtashkuhkauaû ut wutagwiyeumut, onatuh sekuppogheg tahtashkuhkomuk wutche anadtuppúhkout.
E.25.10 For in this mountain shall the hand of the LORD rest, and Moab shall be trodden down under him, even as straw is trodden down for the dunghill.

α.25.11 Kah pish sepagunum wunnutchegash ut wunnashom8wóut, onatuh noh pâmôs8wit sepagunuk wunnutcheash en pamôs8wénat, kah tiahquonkheau pehtuánum8m8uh moeu, nashwunnutchegane sequttahham8ongash.
E.25.11 And he shall spread forth his hands in the midst of them, as he that swimmeth spreadeth forth his hands to swim: and he shall bring down their pride together with the spoils of their hands.

α.25.12 Kah negonohtog kuppummeneutausue umma[n]shk pish wunn8kinnumun, tiuhquonkshin, ohkeit uppaudtauun, puppissiyeuut.
E.25.12 And the fortress of the high fort of thy walls shall he bring down, lay low, and bring to the ground, even to the dust.

α.26.1 NE kesukok, yeu unn8homaonk pish unn8hamon ut ohkeit Judah, nutohtomu menuhki keitotan, God pish kuhquttum wadchanittuonk wutche pummeneutungash kah ummaushkàsh.
E.26.1 In that day shall this song be sung in the land of Judah; We have a strong city; salvation will God appoint for walls and bulwarks.

α.26.2 W[ô]hshinum8k ushquontamash, onk woh sampweusseae wutohtimóin, noh nanawehteunk wanamuhkutéye[u]uk uppetukon.
E.26.2 Open ye the gates, that the righteous nation which keepeth the truth may enter in.

α.26.3 Ken pish kenanaweh ut pannuppee wunohteaonganit, noh ompatussum8wónukquean wuttah, newutche kuppabahtanumuk
E.26.3 Thou wilt keep him in perfect peace, whose mind is stayed on thee: because he trusteth in thee.

α.26.4 Pabahtanumok Jehovah micheme, newutche ut Lord Jehovahut noh michemohtáe menuhkesuonk
E.26.4 Trust ye in the LORD for ever: for in the LORD JEHOVAH is everlasting strength:

α.26.5 Newutche n8kinau neh quanunkquiinitcheh, quanunkquok otan, wutti[ú]hquonkqutteauun, wuttiuhquonkqutteauun pajeh ohkeit, uppuppissiyeúhkon.
E.26.5 For he bringeth down them that dwell on high; the lofty city, he layeth it low; he layeth it low, even to the ground; he bringeth it even to the dust.

α.26.6 Musset pish wuttashkuhkomun, matcheku wusseet, wutôntañehtuongash quenahukquit.
E.26.6 The foot shall tread it down, even the feet of the poor, and the steps of the needy.

α.26.7 Ummay sampweusseaen ne samp8hássuonk: ken anue samp8hassean, kukqutompagh8toh ummay sampweusseaen.
E.26.7 The way of the just is uprightness: thou, most upright, dost weigh the path of the just.

α.26.8 Nux ut k8sittum8e mayut, woi Jehovah, kuppahtsuwóunumun: ukkodtantam8onk nukketeahogkôunun ut k8wesuonganit, kah kummequanumitteanat.
E.26.8 Yea, in the way of thy judgments, O LORD, have we waited for thee; the desire of our soul is to thy name, and to the remembrance of thee.

α.26.9 Nashpe nukketeahogkou kukkodtanumush nuhkonáeu, nux nashpe nunnashaonk nuttinnómiyeumut, nompoáe kenatinneáwhush, newutche k8sittum8ongash ohtag ohkeit, wadohkitcheg muttaohkit pish net[u]htauog sampweusseonk.
E.26.9 With my soul have I desired thee in the night; yea, with my spirit within me will I seek thee early: for when thy judgments are in the earth, the inhabitants of the world will learn righteousness.

α.26.10 Nahtinit kitteamonteanittuonk matchetóog, matta pish netuhtóou sampweusseonk, ut sampweusseae ohkeit pish panne unnehuau, kah matta pish naum8 ukquehtianumáonk Jehovah.
E.26.10 Let favour be shewed to the wicked, yet will he not learn righteousness: in the land of uprightness will he deal unjustly, and will not behold the majesty of the LORD.

α.26.11 Jehovah kenutcheg tahshinnuman, nag matta pish naum8og: qut pish wunnaumuneau: kah pish akodchuog wutche wutishkau[é]naongan8 kummissinninnumoh, nux wunn8tom8 kummatwomog pish nah ummahchukkiswôh.
E.26.11 LORD, when thy hand is lifted up, they will not see: but they shall see, and be ashamed for their envy at the people; yea, the fire of thine enemies shall devour them.

α.26.12 Jehovah, pish kukkuhquttumaiimun wunohteaonk, newutche ken wonk kuttinanakausuwánshimun wame nutanakausuwonganonash.
E.26.12 LORD, thou wilt ordain peace for us: for thou also hast wrought all our works in us.

α.26.13 Woi Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, onkatogig sontimòog chabissitcheg onk ken nanawunukqunnónuppanneg, qut nashpe ken webe nummishamumun k8wesuonk.
E.26.13 O LORD our God, other lords beside thee have had dominion over us: but by thee only will we make mention of thy name.

α.26.14 Nag nupp8k, matta pish pomantam8og: nag wohkukquossinwog, matta pish omohkeog, newaj natauwáhheadt, kah kuppaguanóog, kah k8wa[n]teauwahto wame mehquanumaongan8.
E.26.14 They are dead, they shall not live; they are deceased, they shall not rise: therefore hast thou visited and destroyed them, and made all their memory to perish.

α.26.15 Nano kummishteóh wutohtimoin, woi Jehovah, nano kumishteóh wutohtimóin, kussohsumwahit: noadtit kuttinontahtauun, en wame ongkouohkomukqut.
E.26.15 Thou hast increased the nation, O LORD, thou hast increased the nation: thou art glorified: thou hadst removed it far unto all the ends of the earth.

α.26.16 Jehovah, wadtamehpunáhettit, kenatauwahikquog, sokanumwog peantamóonk, kussasamatahh8waonk nohkugkonkqhettit.
E.26.16 LORD, in trouble have they visited thee, they poured out a prayer when thy chastening was upon them.

α.26.17 Onatuh póseu mittamwossis pas8sukog adt woh neechadt, onkquommamwit, kah môe onkquommamwit, ne nuttinniinnean ut anaquabean, woi Jehovah.
E.26.17 Like as a woman with child, that draweth near the time of her delivery, is in pain, and crieth out in her pangs; so have we been in thy sight, O LORD.

α.26.18 Nuppôosimun, nutonkquomomumun, nunneechámun onatuh wuttin, matta nutussûmun pohquawhunnittuonk ut ohkeit, asuh matta wadohkitcheg muttaohkit penusha8og.
E.26.18 We have been with child, we have been in pain, we have as it were brought forth wind; we have not wrought any deliverance in the earth; neither have the inhabitants of the world fallen.

α.26.19 Kenupp8mog pish pomantamwog, nashpe nunnupp8e muhhog nag pish omohkeog: t8kek kah ket8hamunk kenaau wadohkeógish p[ù]ppissiyeuut: newutche keneechippogkum tatuppeyeu8 herbse neechippogkut, kah ohke pish sohwóhteau nupp8oh.
E.26.19 Thy dead men shall live, together with my dead body shall they arise. Awake and sing, ye that dwell in dust: for thy dew is as the dew of herbs, and the earth shall cast out the dead.

α.26.20 Peyunk nummissinninnúmog, petutteash ut kutchambersumut, kah y[â]nitteanumush quinnuppu, puttogquish onatuh ogguhse, noh pajeh paumushaum8uk musquanittuonk
E.26.20 Come, my people, enter thou into thy chambers, and shut thy doors about thee: hide thyself as it were for a little moment, until the indignation be overpast.

α.26.21 Newutche kusseh, Jehovah wutch sohham wutáyeuonganit sasamatahwhonat wadohkitcheg ohkeit wutch ummatcheseongan8, ohke wonk pish wóhshwem8 8sqheonk, kah matta pish wonk onkwhóou nohtauwutcheh.
E.26.21 For, behold, the LORD cometh out of his place to punish the inhabitants of the earth for their iniquity: the earth also shall disclose her blood, and shall no more cover her slain.

α.27.1 NE kesukok Jehovah nashpe kehkechiyeue & missi & menuhki wutogkodteg pish sasamatahwhau Leviathanoh pannupshae ask8k, nux Leviathan noh pepemsque ask8k kah pish nushau dragonoh ut kehtahhanit.
E.27.1 In that day the LORD with his sore and great and strong sword shall punish leviathan the piercing serpent, even leviathan that crooked serpent; and he shall slay the dragon that is in the sea.

α.27.2 Ne kesukok ket8hamok, musqui wine weenominneohteuk.
E.27.2 In that day sing ye unto her, A vineyard of red wine.

α.27.3 Nen Jehovah nanawehteauun, nutogqutchippadtauun nishnoh utt8che: ishkont howan ummatchteauun, nunnanawehteauun nukkonaeu, kah kesukodaeu.
E.27.3 I the LORD do keep it; I will water it every moment: lest any hurt it, I will keep it night and day.

α.27.4 Mishe musquantam8onk matta nutapehtunk8un: howan woh ayeuuhkonittue ponumunkque kôussoh kah hasinnekôussoh? neg woh nuppannupwushonunk, woh nummoáeu chikoswoog.
E.27.4 Fury is not in me: who would set the briers and thorns against me in battle? I would go through them, I would burn them together.

α.27.5 Asuh menuhkinitch nummenuhkesuonk, onk woh n8nohkonuk, kah noh pish n8nohkonuk.
E.27.5 Or let him take hold of my strength, that he may make peace with me; and he shall make peace with me.

α.27.6 Neg ontsécheg wutch Jakobut pish 8wadchabukeheuh: Israel pish péshauau, kah wunéht8nuhquamú8, kah pish numwohtou woskeche muttaohkit nashpe meechummuonk.
E.27.6 He shall cause them that come of Jacob to take root: Israel shall blossom and bud, and fill the face of the world with fruit.

α.27.7 Sun noh togkomau, neane togkomont neg togkomoncheg? sun nushau, neaunag nushaongan8 neh náshoncheh?
E.27.7 Hath he smitten him, as he smote those that smote him? or is he slain according to the slaughter of them that are slain by him?

α.27.8 Quttuhwhosue sontipohshunk, neit kukkeket8hkonau, kuppahwau ummishetashineum ne kesukok wadchepwashik
E.27.8 In measure, when it shooteth forth, thou wilt debate with it: he stayeth his rough wind in the day of the east wind.

α.27.9 Newutche yeu nashpe, ummatcheseonk Jakob pish pahketeaun8, kah yeu wame ne meechummuonk amaunumunat ummatcheseonk: wame altare qussukquanash agqueteunk chalke qussukquanash, nish soquttahhamukish, kogkompagish kah nunneukontunkanog matta pish nepadta[n]8ash.
E.27.9 By this therefore shall the iniquity of Jacob be purged; and this is all the fruit to take away his sin; when he maketh all the stones of the altar as chalkstones that are beaten in sunder, the groves and images shall not stand up.

α.27.10 Qut onch pummeneutausue keitotan pish touwashin, kah ayeuonk nukkodtumun, kah nukkodtumun netatuppe touohkomukqut, na pish wuttut natupwun calf, na pish wussepsinin, kah matcheteau nish wuttuhqunash.
E.27.10 Yet the defenced city shall be desolate, and the habitation forsaken, and left like a wilderness: there shall the calf feed, and there shall he lie down, and consume the branches thereof.

α.27.11 Wuttuhqunash muss8pohtag pish pokshaash: mittamwossissog peyaog, kah chikohsoog, newutche nag matta wohtam8e missinninnuog, newaje ne kezheump matta pish ummonanumoh, kah noh nah kakenauwaheomp matta pish ukkitteamonteanumoh
E.27.11 When the boughs thereof are withered, they shall be broken off: the women come, and set them on fire: for it is a people of no understanding: therefore he that made them will not have mercy on them, and he that formed them will shew them no favour.

α.27.12 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok Jehovah pish kummoncheahukon wutch sepue posséhteanit pajeh Egipte kussitchuwanit, kah pish kenu[h]aseu mukkinnitteamw8, woi kenaau wunnaumonuh Israel.
E.27.12 And it shall come to pass in that day, that the LORD shall beat off from the channel of the river unto the stream of Egypt, and ye shall be gathered one by one, O ye children of Israel.

α.27.13 Kah pish n$nih ne kesukok, mishe monopu[h]peg pish puhpequohtauun, kah nag pish peyaog, pakodche onkuppunacheg, ut ohkeit Assyria, kah pagkenitcheg ut ohkeit Egipt, kah pish wowussumaog Jehovah, ut wunneetupanatamwe wadchuut, ut Jerusalem.
E.27.13 And it shall come to pass in that day, that the great trumpet shall be blown, and they shall come which were ready to perish in the land of Assyria, and the outcasts in the land of Egypt, and shall worship the LORD in the holy mount at Jerusalem.

α.28.1 MIssi wutonkapunaonk chetuhquabee pechuanumoonk, ukkogkeisippamwaeneumoh Ephraim, noh wussohsumoe wunnetuonk, ne pauuhshauae uppeshau, nish ohtagish 8nogk8e 8nauuhkoiyeue uppuhkuhqut neg sohkunkqutcheg wine.
E.28.1 Woe to the crown of pride, to the drunkards of Ephraim, whose glorious beauty is a fading flower, which are on the head of the fat valleys of them that are overcome with wine!

α.28.2 Kusseh Jehovah ohto how[a] menuhkes[u] kah missugken noh, neaneyeu8g nashqutne mussegan, & pagwohte[á]e nashquttin, onatuh mishe nippeash tômogkok, pish uppenuhkon en ohkeit, nashpe wunnutcheg.
E.28.2 Behold, the Lord hath a mighty and strong one, which as a tempest of hail and a destroying storm, as a flood of mighty waters overflowing, shall cast down to the earth with the hand.
