α.28.3 Petuanumwe chetuhqu[á]b, ukkogkeissippam8moh Ephraim pish tahtashkuhkauoog ut agwe musseetut.
E.28.3 The crown of pride, the drunkards of Ephraim, shall be trodden under feet:

α.28.4 Sohsumoe 8netuonk ne ohtag wunnogque 8nouhkoi uppuhkukqut, ne pish pôuhshauwae uppeshau, kah onatuh kenuppegane meechumuonk, ash achuwan8gkup, ne noh kahkinneog, nag*, ash pampohtag wunnutcheganit, mahchipwun
E.28.4 And the glorious beauty, which is on the head of the fat valley, shall be a fading flower, and as the hasty fruit before the summer; which when he that looketh upon it seeth, while it is yet in his hand he eateth it up.

α.28.5 Ne kesukok Jehovah ayeuteaunit, noh wussohsumoe chetuhquabeyeu, kah 8neetue kenadtukquabpeyeu ashqushonitcheh ummissinninneumoh.
E.28.5 In that day shall the LORD of hosts be for a crown of glory, and for a diadem of beauty, unto the residue of his people,

α.28.6 Kah nasháuanittoe 8sittum8onk noh apit wussittum8onganit, kah ummenuhkesuongan8 nag quoshkinukeg ayeuwuttuonk ut ushquontamut.
E.28.6 And for a spirit of judgment to him that sitteth in judgment, and for strength to them that turn the battle to the gate.

α.28.7 Qut nag wonk panneusseog nashpe wine kah nashpe onkuppe, matta appeog mâyut sephausuen kah quoshodtumwaen panneusseog nashpe unkuppe, nag misseashk8wonukquog wine: nag matta appeog mayut nashpe onkuppe, panneseae monomansuog, togkussittahsunwog wâsittumohettit.
E.28.7 But they also have erred through wine, and through strong drink are out of the way; the priest and the prophet have erred through strong drink, they are swallowed up of wine, they are out of the way through strong drink; they err in vision, they stumble in judgment.

α.28.8 Newutche wame tablesash numwohteau munnadtumoonk kah nishkeneunkquok, newaj wanne ayeuonk pahkan8.
E.28.8 For all tables are full of vomit and filthiness, so that there is no place clean.

α.28.9 Howane woh kohk8tomauont wahteauonk, howane woh kohk8tomauont wahteauonk, howane woh wahtamwaheont kuh[k]8tomwehteaonk? neg 8chininnahitcheg wutch sogkodtunkanit, kah pashkunaog wutch mohpanôganit[.]
E.28.9 Whom shall he teach knowledge? and whom shall he make to understand doctrine? them that are weaned from the milk, and drawn from the breasts.

α.28.10 Newutche kuhk8tomwehteaonk pish ahôsuhkaueyeu8 kuhk8tomwehteaonk, kuhk8tomwehteaonk ahôsuhkaueyeu8 kuhk8tomweheteaonk, kuhkuhheg ahósuhkaueyeu8 kuhkuhheg, kuhkuhheg ahos[ú]hkaueyeu8 kuhkuhheg, yeuut ogguhse, kah naut wonk ogguhse.
E.28.10 For precept must be upon precept, precept upon precept; line upon line, line upon line; here a little, and there a little:

α.28.11 Newutche nashpe nahnogkiae mississitt8nash, kah pen8wont8waonk pish wuttinnont8wanumauon yeuh missinninnuh
E.28.11 For with stammering lips and another tongue will he speak to this people.

α.28.12 Neh anoncheh, yeu anwohsinn8onk ne [á]dt anwosumoh neg sauunukeg, kah yeu ne taphettuonk, qut onch mat n8tam8og.
E.28.12 To whom he said, This is the rest wherewith ye may cause the weary to rest; and this is the refreshing: yet they would not hear.

α.28.13 Qut wuttinnowaonk Jehovah appehtunkquog kuhk8tomwehteaonk ahôsuhkaueyeu8 kuhk8tomwehteaonk, kuhk8tomwehteaonk [a]hosuhkaueyeu8 kuhk8tomwehteaonk; kuhkuhheg ahôsuhkaueyeuo kuhkuhheg, kuhkuhheg ahôsuhkaueyeu8 kuhkuhheg, yeu ogguhse naut wonk ogguhse, onk woh moncheog kah woh ant8[h]shaog, kah pohksunwog, kah puttahwhoog, kah tohqunóog.
E.28.13 But the word of the LORD was unto them precept upon precept, precept upon precept; line upon line, line upon line; here a little, and there a little; that they might go, and fall backward, and be broken, and snared, and taken.

α.28.14 Newutche n8tam8k wuttinnowaonk Jehovah, pahtuanumweogish nanauwunogish missinninnuog neg apitcheg Jerusalem.
E.28.14 Wherefore hear the word of the LORD, ye scornful men, that rule this people which is in Jerusalem.

α.28.15 Newutche kussimw8, n8n8womun nupp8onk, kah n8n8womun chepiohkomuk, aneupae sasamatahwhuttuonk paumushaum8uk, matta pish nuppeyógk8unan: néwutche nutushpohhouwaonganéhteamun pann8waongash, kah agwe as8kekodteam8onganit nupputogquemun.
E.28.15 Because ye have said, We have made a covenant with death, and with hell are we at agreement; when the overflowing scourge shall pass through, it shall not come unto us: for we have made lies our refuge, and under falsehood have we hid ourselves:

α.28.16 Newajeh yeu n8wadt Lord Jehovah, kusseh, nupponamun ut Sion wutche quenohtag, qussuk, qutchehteoe qussuk, mishoadtue nahshine qussuk, papane quenohtag, noh wanamptog matta kenupshau8.
E.28.16 Therefore thus saith the Lord GOD, Behold, I lay in Zion for a foundation a stone, a tried stone, a precious corner stone, a sure foundation: he that believeth shall not make haste.

α.28.17 Kah wonk wussittum8onk nupponamun kuhkuheganit, kah sampweusseonk qutompagh8teganit: kah mussegon pish chekham pann8wae ushpuhh8waongash, kah nippeash pish nehtippadt8 adtahtoe ayeuonk,
E.28.17 Judgment also will I lay to the line, and righteousness to the plummet: and the hail shall sweep away the refuge of lies, and the waters shall overflow the hiding place.

α.28.18 Kah k8n8waongan8 nupp8onk pish mo teagwunnehte[á]uun, kah n8n8waongan8 chepiohkomuk matta pish neepadtano: aneupae sasamatahwhuttuonk pannupwushaum8uk, neit pish kenashpe tashkuhkonteaneau.
E.28.18 And your covenant with death shall be disannulled, and your agreement with hell shall not stand; when the overflowing scourge shall pass through, then ye shall be trodden down by it.

α.28.19 Wutch aquompeyeue sohham8m8uk, pish kuttohqunukquneau; newutche mohmohtompanae pish paumusháum8, kesukodaeu kah nukonaeu, kah pish m8sqhettuwonganu8, webe wohtamunat unnehtunkquot.
E.28.19 From the time that it goeth forth it shall take you: for morning by morning shall it pass over, by day and by night: and it shall be a vexation only to understand the report.

α.28.20 Newutche appin tiohqui wosketomp matta woh wuttit sesekein, kah hogk8onk penompagod, matta woh uppapadtukqussun8un.
E.28.20 For the bed is shorter than that a man can stretch himself on it: and the covering narrower than that he can wrap himself in it.

α.28.21 Newutche Jehovah pish omohku, ne asip ut wadchuut Perazim, pish musquantam ne asip ut Gibeone 8no[ú]hkoiye[ú]ut, onk woh wutussenat wutanakausuonk, penowe wutanakausuonk, onk woh kezteau wutusseonk, penowe wutusseonk.
E.28.21 For the LORD shall rise up as in mount Perazim, he shall be wroth as in the valley of Gibeon, that he may do his work, his strange work; and bring to pass his act, his strange act.

α.28.22 Newutche ahque momonehtásuenuek ishkont kukkinnepsuongan8oash menehketeausuash; newutch nunn8tam wutch Lord Jehovah ayeuteaunit, mohchekonnaeonk kehtimau ut woskeche mamusse ohkeit.
E.28.22 Now therefore be ye not mockers, lest your bands be made strong: for I have heard from the Lord GOD of hosts a consumption, even determined upon the whole earth.

α.28.23 Kuhkeitiek, kah n8tam8k n8wadtauatonkqussuonk, kuhkihtam8k, kah n8tam8k nukkutt8wonk.
E.28.23 Give ye ear, and hear my voice; hearken, and hear my speech.

α.28.24 Sun anaskhomwen anaskham nehteage ohteuhkonat? sun wohshinum kah pohquenum puhquohkomukquash ut wutohteakonit?
E.28.24 Doth the plowman plow all day to sow? doth he open and break the clods of his ground?

α.28.25 M8sitte[u]nk woskeche, sunnummatta seahham8 fitches[à]sh, kah seahhamm8 cummin kah ohkehteau wanegukish wheatash kah kuhquttumwe barly, kah rye ut wutayeaongan8out.
E.28.25 When he hath made plain the face thereof, doth he not cast abroad the fitches, and scatter the cummin, and cast in the principal wheat and the appointed barley and the rie in their place?

α.28.26 Newutche um-Manitt8moh ukkuhk8tomau nehtôe usseonk, kah ukkuhk8tomauuh.
E.28.26 For his God doth instruct him to discretion, and doth teach him.

α.28.27 Newutche fitchesash matta poggohhomwauhtugque poggohhamunash, asuh matta carte-wheel quinnuppenum8un woskeche cummin, qut fitchesash poggohhamunash nashpe anwohhou, kah cummin nashpe souobpunk.
E.28.27 For the fitches are not threshed with a threshing instrument, neither is a cart wheel turned about upon the cummin; but the fitches are beaten out with a staff, and the cummin with a rod.

α.28.28 Petukqunnegane weatchiminneash s8quttahhamunash, newutche matta kod nagwutteae uppogham8un, asuh matta pohquetahhamun nashpe uk-carte-wheelum, asuh matta sohquttahham8 nashpe nayeumukqutcheg horsesoh.
E.28.28 Bread corn is bruised; because he will not ever be threshing it, nor break it with the wheel of his cart, nor bruise it with his horsemen.

α.28.29 Yeu wonk 8m88 wutch Lord ayéuteaunit, noh monchanatamwe koguhtimut, kah waussinit.
E.28.29 This also cometh forth from the LORD of hosts, which is wonderful in counsel, and excellent in working.

α.29.1 MIssi wutonkapunaonk Ariel, A[a]iel, keitotan ne David ayeup k8tnehteau8k kodtum8, nehtauhettich sephausuongash.
E.29.1 Woe to Ariel, to Ariel, the city where David dwelt! add ye year to year; let them kill sacrifices.

α.29.2 Qut onch nukquehquenauánumweh Ariel, kah na pish nupp8anum8onk kah neuantam8onk, kah pish nuttatupontamun Ariel.
E.29.2 Yet I will distress Ariel, and there shall be heaviness and sorrow: and it shall be unto me as Ariel.

α.29.3 Kah pish ayeuuhkonittue k8wéenu tupuksinn8wonsh, kah k8weenussumwehtoush nashpe wadchu, kutayeuuhkonittue waápenumoush ummanshkash.
E.29.3 And I will camp against thee round about, and will lay siege against thee with a mount, and I will raise forts against thee.

α.29.4 Pish ken8kinit, kah pish kukket8hkon wutch ohkeit, kah kukkutt8wongash tiuhquonkod wutch puppissiyeuut: kah k8wadtauatonkqussuonk pish tatuppeyeu8 noh apehtunkqut matche nashauonk wutch ohkeit: kah kukkutt8onk keemompeum8 wutch puppissiyeuut.
E.29.4 And thou shalt be brought down, and shalt speak out of the ground, and thy speech shall be low out of the dust, and thy voice shall be, as of one that hath a familiar spirit, out of the ground, and thy speech shall whisper out of the dust.

α.29.5 Nano, mataanukeg kuppen8wohteomogish pish ogqueneunkqussuog sohque puppissiyeuut, & kutunkqueneunkqusseume monacheg, pish tatupeyeu8og wussadteanumit, ne pamshunk, nux pish kenuppeyeu8, teanuk.
E.29.5 Moreover the multitude of thy strangers shall be like small dust, and the multitude of the terrible ones shall be as chaff that passeth away: yea, it shall be at an instant suddenly.

α.29.6 Jehovah ayeuteaunit pish kenatauwahik nashpé padtohquohhan, kah nashpe quequanash, kah mishont8waongash, nashpe nashquttin kah mishetahshin, kah n8n8nae mahchukkissuwae n8teau.
E.29.6 Thou shalt be visited of the LORD of hosts with thunder, and with earthquake, and great noise, with storm and tempest, and the flame of devouring fire.

α.29.7 Kah mataanukish wutohtimoneash ayeuuhkontam8m8ukish Ariel, wame neg ayeuuhkononcheg, kah wutauwohteaongash, kah quehquenauanumwutcheg, pish tatuppeyeu8og nukkonae monománsue nukquom8onk
E.29.7 And the multitude of all the nations that fight against Ariel, even all that fight against her and her munition, and that distress her, shall be as a dream of a night vision.

α.29.8 Pish tatuppeyeu8, kodtupwen ánukquonk, kah kusseh meetsu, qut t8hku, kah ukketeahogkôunoh mahtussuoh, asuh onatuh kûhkuht8n8wenin ánukquonk kah kusseh wuttattam, qut t8hku, kah kusse, sauunum, kah ukketeahogkôunoh kodtantamoh: ne pish wutti[nnii]neau mataáneukish wutohtimóneash ayeuuhkontogig Zion.
E.29.8 It shall even be as when an hungry man dreameth, and, behold, he eateth; but he awaketh, and his soul is empty: or as when a thirsty man dreameth, and, behold, he drinketh; but he awaketh, and, behold, he is faint, and his soul hath appetite: so shall the multitude of all the nations be, that fight against mount Zion.

α.29.9 Chequnappek kah monchanatam8k, mishont8wak kah mau8k, nag kogkeussippam8og qut matta nashpe wine, kekepshaog, qut matta nashpe onkuppe.
E.29.9 Stay yourselves, and wonder; cry ye out, and cry: they are drunken, but not with wine; they stagger, but not with strong drink.

α.29.10 Newutch Jehovah kussokanumunk8 kussukkouéyeue nashaonguh, yáununum kuskesuk8óash: quoshodtumwaenuog, kah kenanawunnaeneum8og, nauwacheg upputtogúhwhoh.
E.29.10 For the LORD hath poured out upon you the spirit of deep sleep, and hath closed your eyes: the prophets and your rulers, the seers hath he covered.

α.29.11 Kah ummonomansuongan8 wame kuttatuppeyunkquneau sukkúhkehteoeu b8ke kutt8wongash; ne wosketompaog wuttinnumauóneau, neh nohtontauunutcheh, n8waog, yeu ogketash k8wehquetumoush, kah n8wau, n8nanum newutch sukkuhkehteausu.
E.29.11 And the vision of all is become unto you as the words of a book that is sealed, which men deliver to one that is learned, saying, Read this, I pray thee: and he saith, I cannot; for it is sealed:

α.29.12 Kah b8k aninnumauon noh matta nohtantau8k, n8wau, yeu ogketash k8wehquetumoush, kah n8wau, matta nunnetuhtauouun.
E.29.12 And the book is delivered to him that is not learned, saying, Read this, I pray thee: and he saith, I am not learned.

α.29.13 Newaj Jehovah n8wadt, newutche yeug missinninnuog nuppas8sukkongquog nashpe wutt8n8, kah nashpe wussissitt8n8[a]sh nukquehtianumukquog, qut noadtit in nutontuhtongquog wuttahh8woash, kah nukqushhúk8ongan8 kuhk8tomoadtin, nashpe wosketompae kogohk8waongash.
E.29.13 Wherefore the Lord said, Forasmuch as this people draw near me with their mouth, and with their lips do honour me, but have removed their heart far from me, and their fear toward me is taught by the precept of men:

α.29.14 Newutche kusseh nukkutchittôusha[m] ussenat monchanatamwe usseonk ut kenugke yeug missinninnuog, monchanatamwe anakausuonk, kah monchanatam8onk: newutche 8waantam8ongan8 waantamwog pish wutahquohtauun, kah 8wohwohtam8ongan8 wunnupwom8oh pish adtahtauóneau.
E.29.14 Therefore, behold, I will proceed to do a marvellous work among this people, even a marvellous work and a wonder: for the wisdom of their wise men shall perish, and the understanding of their prudent men shall be hid.

α.29.15 Missi wutonkapunnaongan8 neg m8nôi natinneáhogig adtahtauunat ukkogáhqutteam8onk Jehovah, kah wutanakausuongan8oash pohkenaiash, kah n8waog, howan kenogkumun? kah howan k8wahikumun?
E.29.15 Woe unto them that seek deep to hide their counsel from the LORD, and their works are in the dark, and they say, Who seeth us? and who knoweth us?

α.29.16 Wunnamuhkut kukqushkohteáshitteaongan8, pish tatupontamun ahk8hqutteae[nin] umman8nskumut: newutche sun woh anakausuonk n8wom8 noh kezteungkup, matta nukkezhik8? asuh ne teag ne weekitteamuk, sun woh unnau neh weekitteanepoh, matta wohwohtam8?
E.29.16 Surely your turning of things upside down shall be esteemed as the potter's clay: for shall the work say of him that made it, He made me not? or shall the thing framed say of him that framed it, He had no understanding?

α.29.17 Sunnummatta majish ogguhsese, kah Lebanon pish quinnuppenumun en mishummeechumue ohteakonit, kah misummeechume ohteuk pish ogquontamun touohkomuk?
E.29.17 Is it not yet a very little while, and Lebanon shall be turned into a fruitful field, and the fruitful field shall be esteemed as a forest?

α.29.18 Kah ne kesukok kogkopsau pish n8tam b8ke kutt8wongash: kah pogkinnumwe muskesukquash pish naum8m8ash wutch pogkenum8onganit kah pohkenaiyeuut,
E.29.18 And in that day shall the deaf hear the words of the book, and the eyes of the blind shall see out of obscurity, and out of darkness.

α.29.19 Manunnissuog wonk pish pishkonteauog 8wekontam8ongan8 ut Jehovahut, kah matchekuog ut kenugke missinninnuog, pish weekontam8oneau 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
E.29.19 The meek also shall increase their joy in the LORD, and the poor among men shall rejoice in the Holy One of Israel.

α.29.20 Newutche unkqunneunkqussit mattohhentuppéheau, kah mamanauwontamwenin mohtupáeu, kah wame neg askuhwhontogeg matcheseonk tummehtahwhoog.
E.29.20 For the terrible one is brought to nought, and the scorner is consumed, and all that watch for iniquity are cut off:

α.29.21 Neg ayeuoncheg wosketomp matcheseaenuunneat wutche kutt8onk, kah upponamauónaoont noh áuskôadt ut usquontamut, kah wutamaunónaoont sampweusseaenuh wutche monteag.
E.29.21 That make a man an offender for a word, and lay a snare for him that reproveth in the gate, and turn aside the just for a thing of nought.

α.29.22 Newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah noh pohquohwhunomp Abrahamoh, papaume week Jakob, J[o]kob pish yeuyeu matta akodchu, asuh matta yeuyeu wuskesuk womukushànó.
E.29.22 Therefore thus saith the LORD, who redeemed Abraham, concerning the house of Jacob, Jacob shall not now be ashamed, neither shall his face now wax pale.

α.29.23 Qut nauont wunneechanoh nunnutchegáne anakausuonk ut wunnashomut, nag pish wunneetupanatamwahtoog n8wesuonk, kah pish wunnetupanatamwaheaog 8neetupanatam8moh Jakob, kah pish wabesuonaog um-Manitt8moh Israel.
E.29.23 But when he seeth his children, the work of mine hands, in the midst of him, they shall sanctify my name, and sanctify the Holy One of Jacob, and shall fear the God of Israel.

α.29.24 Nag wonk pannesitcheg ut nashauonganit pish wohwohtamwog, kah nag m8m8sk8wacheg, pish nehtuhtóog kogohk8wáonk.
E.29.24 They also that erred in spirit shall come to understanding, and they that murmured shall learn doctrine.

α.30.1 MIssi wutonkapunnaongan8 cheketamwe mukkiesog, n8wau Jehovah, neemunnumwog kogohquttuonk, qut matta nashpe nen, kah neg ágqutcheg onkwhonk, qut matta nashpe nunnashauanitt8moh: onk woh k8tnehteauog matcheséonk en matcheseonganit.
E.30.1 Woe to the rebellious children, saith the LORD, that take counsel, but not of me; and that cover with a covering, but not of my spirit, that they may add sin to sin:

α.30.2 Neg pomushacheg womsinneat en Egypt (kah matta kogáhqutteog ut nutt8nut) ummenuhkehheonaóont wuhhogkauh nashpe ummenuhkesuonk Pharoh, kah pabuhtantamunat wutonkouohtom Egypt.
E.30.2 That walk to go down into Egypt, and have not asked at my mouth; to strengthen themselves in the strength of Pharaoh, and to trust in the shadow of Egypt!

α.30.3 Newutche ummenuhkesuonk Pharoh ne pish k8takodchuwonkaninneau, kah pabahtanumonat onkouòhtom Egypt ne pish kenaswaiyeuongan8.
E.30.3 Therefore shall the strength of Pharaoh be your shame, and the trust in the shadow of Egypt your confusion.

α.30.4 Newutche wussontimósimoh apinitcheh Zoan, kah wutann8naéneumoh peyaog Hanes.
E.30.4 For his princes were at Zoan, and his ambassadors came to Hanes.

α.30.5 Nag wame akodchuheóog missinninnuog neg matta aninnumauunkig, asuh waneheunkig, kah wadchiyeumu[k]eg qut akodchu[h]éoog kah ukkekontuwaheouh.
E.30.5 They were all ashamed of a people that could not profit them, nor be an help nor profit, but a shame, and also a reproach.

α.30.6 OOweanunn8 sowanie puppinashimwog en wuttamehpunáe kah unkquanumóe, ohkeit uttoh wagk wuske kah nukkone qunnonou, viper, kah n8tae pummunáe ask8k: nag pish kenunnumwog 8weenauwetuongan8, ut uhpegwann8óo[u]t wuske assesog, kah wunnompako[ú]unn8oash 8nuhquiyeum8out camelsog, en missinninnúut ne woh mo wanenehikquéhhettegeh.
E.30.6 The burden of the beasts of the south: into the land of trouble and anguish, from whence come the young and old lion, the viper and fiery flying serpent, they will carry their riches upon the shoulders of young asses, and their treasures upon the bunches of camels, to a people that shall not profit them.

α.30.7 Newutche Egyptiansog pish tahn8che aninnôsuog, kah en wanne wanegik, newaj yeu papaume mishont8wi, nag ummenuhkesuongan8 ne chequnappuonk.
E.30.7 For the Egyptians shall help in vain, and to no purpose: therefore have I cried concerning this, Their strength is to sit still.

α.30.8 Yeuyeu monchish wussukwhush ut tableut, ut anaquabhettit, kah wussukwhush ut b8kut, onk woh ne chékeyeu88 micheme kah micheme.
E.30.8 Now go, write it before them in a table, and note it in a book, that it may be for the time to come for ever and ever:

α.30.9 Yeug cheketam8e missinninnúog, pann8wae mukkiesog, mukkiesog neg matta k[o]hkeihtam8gig wuttinnaumatuonk Jehovah.
E.30.9 That this is a rebellious people, lying children, children that will not hear the law of the LORD:

α.30.10 Neg anoncheg namunutche ahque naum8k, quoshódtumwaénúh, ahque sampwe quosh[ó]dtamwiinneau: ussinnan mam8sagish, as8kekodteam8e quoshodtumaiiñean.
E.30.10 Which say to the seers, See not; and to the prophets, Prophesy not unto us right things, speak unto us smooth things, prophesy deceits:

α.30.11 Amayek wutch mayut, pohchagk wutch mayut: 8neetupanatam8moh Israel wohkukquosun ut anaquabeog.
E.30.11 Get you out of the way, turn aside out of the path, cause the Holy One of Israel to cease from before us.

α.30.12 Newaj yeu n8wadt 8neetupanatam8moh Israel; newutche yeu kutjishantamuneau kutt8onk, kah kuppabahtantamumw8 mukk8kinnuwaonk, kah wounkkag, kah ne kutompadtussinuneau.
E.30.12 Wherefore thus saith the Holy One of Israel, Because ye despise this word, and trust in oppression and perverseness, and stay thereon:

α.30.13 Newaj pish yeu matcheseonk tatuppeyeu88k n8kompskishunk, p8tôem8uk qunuhque qussukquaneutunk, noh uppokshaonk koshkomme teanuk peyaum8.
E.30.13 Therefore this iniquity shall be to you as a breach ready to fall, swelling out in a high wall, whose breaking cometh suddenly at an instant.

α.30.14 Kah noh pish wuttinne sokqshadtauun sokqshadtomuk ahkuhqutteaenin 8wisq, ne sohquetahhamuk, matta pish ukkishpadtam8un; newaje pish mat namehteauomuk, ne adt sohqueta[hh]amuk, kodchuhkisq, nemequomunat n8teau wutch n8teau ahhohtag, asuh quomphamunat nippe wutch passohtheganit.
E.30.14 And he shall break it as the breaking of the potters' vessel that is broken in pieces; he shall not spare: so that there shall not be found in the bursting of it a sherd to take fire from the hearth, or to take water withal out of the pit.

α.30.15 Newutche yeu n8wau Lord Jehovah, 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, qushkémuk kah anwôsinimuk pish k8wadchanitteamw8, manunnissimuk kah wutt8anatamuk, ne pish kummenuhkesuongan8, kah kussekenamumw8.
E.30.15 For thus saith the Lord GOD, the Holy One of Israel; In returning and rest shall ye be saved; in quietness and in confidence shall be your strength: and ye would not.

α.30.16 Qut kussimw8, matta, newutch pish n8semun nashpe horsesog, ne$waj pish wussemwe[y]óg: kah naiyeumutteamun kakenupshoncheg, newaj neg n8swuttahukqueógig pish kogkenupwusháog.
E.30.16 But ye said, No; for we will flee upon horses; therefore shall ye flee: and, We will ride upon the swift; therefore shall they that pursue you be swift.

α.30.17 Muttanonganogkussuog pish wussem8og, pasuk wabuwonont, kah napannatahsuog wabuwunáhettit, pish k8semw8 nô pajeh keánewunneaóont beakon koduhkôagk, kah onatuh muttaagk ut wadchuut.
E.30.17 One thousand shall flee at the rebuke of one; at the rebuke of five shall ye flee: till ye be left as a beacon upon the top of a mountain, and as an ensign on an hill.

α.30.18 Newaj Jehovah pahtussit, onk woh kukkitteamonteanumukou, kah newaj mishehit, onk woh kummonánumukou: newutche Jehovah noh wussittumóe Manit. Wunanumunach neg wame pahtussuonóncheg.
E.30.18 And therefore will the LORD wait, that he may be gracious unto you, and therefore will he be exalted, that he may have mercy upon you: for the LORD is a God of judgment: blessed are all they that wait for him.

α.30.19 Newutche missinninnuog pish ayeuog ut Zion, ut Jerusalem: pish matta wonkkummâou, noh pish ahche kukkitteamonteanumuk, ut k8wadtauatonkqussue mauonganit, n8tog neit kenamp8hamunk.
E.30.19 For the people shall dwell in Zion at Jerusalem: thou shalt weep no more: he will be very gracious unto thee at the voice of thy cry; when he shall hear it, he will answer thee.

α.30.20 Kah tohkônogque Lord kittiñumunkquneau onkquommom8e petukqunneg, kah wuttammepunnae nippe, qut onch kukkuhk8tomwehteaeneumog matta pish wonk ontasháog en p8chekeheganit, qut kuskesukquash pish nâau kukkuhk8tomwehteaeneumoh.
E.30.20 And though the Lord give you the bread of adversity, and the water of affliction, yet shall not thy teachers be removed into a corner any more, but thine eyes shall see thy teachers:

α.30.21 Kah kehtauogash pish ken8tam8m8 kutt8onk en kuppusquanit, n8wau, yeu may, ne pomushagk, quinnuppéog en kuttinohk[ô]unit, kah quinnuppeóg en menadcheani.
E.30.21 And thine ears shall hear a word behind thee, saying, This is the way, walk ye in it, when ye turn to the right hand, and when ye turn to the left.

α.30.22 Kah pish wonk kenishketeomw8 wuthogk8ongan8 silvere kittinneukontunkán8, kah wuthogk8unash kussabossume golde unneukontunkanog: nag pish kutogque pogkenóog qushinausue kodchuhkonákinit, pish kuttittamun amaish.
E.30.22 Ye shall defile also the covering of thy graven images of silver, and the ornament of thy molten images of gold: thou shalt cast them away as a menstruous cloth; thou shalt say unto it, Get thee hence.

α.30.23 Neit pish kittinnumunk sokanon ut k8skannemuneat, ne woh ahketeáan, kah petukqununk nashpe ne teashegik wutch ohkeit, kah ne pish wunogk8m8 kah monat: ne kesukok kenetasumog pish nadtupp8og en mummiske tanadtupp8onganit.
E.30.23 Then shall he give the rain of thy seed, that thou shalt sow the ground withal; and bread of the increase of the earth, and it shall be fat and plenteous: in that day shall thy cattle feed in large pastures.

α.30.24 Kah wonk oxinog, kah wuske assesog ne anaskohhogeg ohke, pish mukk8tanéhteamwog weatchimineash, ne seahamoe pahketeamukup nashpe shovel kah paanonteg.
E.30.24 The oxen likewise and the young asses that ear the ground shall eat clean provender, which hath been winnowed with the shovel and with the fan.

α.30.25 Kah nishnoh ut kussohkôi, kah qunuhqui wadchuut na pish sepu8 kah kussehtan nippeyeu8, ut pagwanittue kesukodtut, qunuhkquikommukquash panshunk.
E.30.25 And there shall be upon every high mountain, and upon every high hill, rivers and streams of waters in the day of the great slaughter, when the towers fall.

α.30.26 Nano, 8wôhsumóonk nanepaushadt pish tatuppeyeu8 nepâuzsae pumôsum8onganit, kah 8wôsumóonk nepâuz pish nesausuk tahshit tahshin; onatuh nesausuk tahshit kesukquae wôhsum8onk, ne kesukog Jehovah waashpunont uppokshaonganóoash ummissinninneumoh, kah neetskehteunk n8chumwehtahwaeu annehtahwaonganooash.
E.30.26 Moreover the light of the moon shall be as the light of the sun, and the light of the sun shall be sevenfold, as the light of seven days, in the day that the LORD bindeth up the breach of his people, and healeth the stroke of their wound.

α.30.27 Kusseh, 8wesuonk Jehovah n8adtit 8m88, nashquneau nashpe ummusquanittam8onk, kah ne weanun tuhkequan, wussissitt8nit numwohteau nukque musquanittam8onk, kah wenan tatuppeyeu8 mahchekuss8wae n8taut.
E.30.27 Behold, the name of the LORD cometh from far, burning with his anger, and the burden thereof is heavy: his lips are full of indignation, and his tongue as a devouring fire:

α.30.28 Kah wunnashauonk ánuwutchuwane kussehtanup, pish ohqussinin nôeu mussittipukonit, nohnohkinnumunat wutohtimoneash, nashpe tahn8chee nanahkineg: kah na pish bridle ut wutompekon8wout missinninnuog, panneseáheont.
E.30.28 And his breath, as an overflowing stream, shall reach to the midst of the neck, to sift the nations with the sieve of vanity: and there shall be a bridle in the jaws of the people, causing them to err.

α.30.29 Pish kutahtomw8 unn8homaonk nukkonáeu, wunneetupanatamwe moéonk nanawehteomuk, kah wekontamwáeteaháonk, onatuh noh p[a]ont nashpe puhpekq ut 8wadchumut Jehovah ummissugken8moh Israel.
E.30.29 Ye shall have a song, as in the night when a holy solemnity is kept; and gladness of heart, as when one goeth with a pipe to come into the mountain of the LORD, to the mighty One of Israel.

α.30.30 Kah Jehovah wunn8tamwáheuh wussohsumóe wadtauatonqussuonk, kah pish nahtitteau, 8pittene kutshaumun nashpe wutuhquanittamwe musquanittam8onk, kah nashpe n8n8nae mahchekussuáe n8teau, nashpe seaham8e mishehtash, kah missegan.
E.30.30 And the LORD shall cause his glorious voice to be heard, and shall shew the lighting down of his arm, with the indignation of his anger, and with the flame of a devouring fire, with scattering, and tempest, and hailstones.

α.30.31 Newutche nashpe 8wadtauagonkqussuonk Jehovah wut-Assyrian quttaúwetáhwóu, togkomit nashpe pogkomunk.
E.30.31 For through the voice of the LORD shall the Assyrian be beaten down, which smote with a rod.

α.30.32 Kah nishnoh ut ayeuonganit uttôh adt menuhki anwohhou pish pamshunk, ne Jehovah pish ponamauont, ne pish nashpe tabretsash kah harpsash, kah nunnuksháe ayeuwuttuonganehtu, pish ne nashpe ayeukontamun.
E.30.32 And in every place where the grounded staff shall pass, which the LORD shall lay upon him, it shall be with tabrets and harps: and in battles of shaking will he fight with it.

α.30.33 Newutch Tophet kukkuhquttumunah nôadt, nux quagquoshwehtamauun ketass8t, umm8unonteauun, kah kishki: ne noh ohtag n8tau kah monatash wuttuhqunash wunnashauonk Jehovah wunnashqunánumun, ogqueneunkqut brimstone kussitchuwanut.
E.30.33 For Tophet is ordained of old; yea, for the king it is prepared; he hath made it deep and large: the pile thereof is fire and much wood; the breath of the LORD, like a stream of brimstone, doth kindle it.

α.31.1 MIssi wutonkapunnaongan8 neg wômussitcheg en Egypt wuch aninnumoadtuonk, kah ompatissinwog horsesoh, kah pabuhtantamwog chariotsash, newutche monaash, kah nayeumukqunutcheh horsesoh, newutche ahche menuhkesuoh: qut matta mouninneauou8og 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, asuh matta natinnewhau[ó]og Jehovah.
E.31.1 Woe to them that go down to Egypt for help; and stay on horses, and trust in chariots, because they are many; and in horsemen, because they are very strong; but they look not unto the Holy One of Israel, neither seek the LORD!

α.31.2 Qut onch waantam, kah pish paudto machuk, kah matta pish ontattó8 ukkutt8ongash, qut pish waabéhtauau matcheseaenúe weetu, kah ayeuuhkonittue wutannosuongan8 neg asécheg matcheseonk.
E.31.2 Yet he also is wise, and will bring evil, and will not call back his words: but will arise against the house of the evildoers, and against the help of them that work iniquity.

α.31.3 Qut Egyptiansog wosketomp8og, & matta Mani[t]tt88og, & wut-horsesum8oh weyausu8oh, kah matta nashauanitt88og: Jehovah summagunuk wunnutch, naneese noh aninnausit pish penushau, kah noh aninnumauut pish penushau, kah nag wamu pish moeu penusháog.
E.31.3 Now the Egyptians are men, and not God; and their horses flesh, and not spirit. When the LORD shall stretch out his hand, both he that helpeth shall fall, and he that is holpen shall fall down, and they all shall fail together.

α.31.4 Newutch[è] yeu nuttugqun Jehovah: onatuh qunnonou, kah qunnonuwem, mishont8wae tohq[u]nont ne tohqunoncheh, monanutcheh nanaushipsaen[ù]h ayeuuhkonittue wehquetuog nah wutch, matta wabesu wutch 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8, asuh matta mishanehheaout wuhogkuh wutche nag monacheg: netatuppe Lord ayeuhteaunit pish n8keu wutáyeuwehteaunsh[ô]nat wadchu Zion, kah wutche 8wadcheum.
E.31.4 For thus hath the LORD spoken unto me, Like as the lion and the young lion roaring on his prey, when a multitude of shepherds is called forth against him, he will not be afraid of their voice, nor abase himself for the noise of them: so shall the LORD of hosts come down to fight for mount Zion, and for the hill thereof.

α.31.5 Onatuh psuksesuk pâmunáhettit, netatuppe Jehovah ayeuhteaunit pish wadchanau Jerusalem, kah wadchanuwae pish uppohquohwhuttauun, kah quoshkodteadt pish 8wadchanumun.
E.31.5 As birds flying, so will the LORD of hosts defend Jerusalem; defending also he will deliver it; and passing over he will preserve it.

α.31.6 Qushkek noh en, neh wunneechanoh Israel menuhke amaehtauoncheh.
E.31.6 Turn ye unto him from whom the children of Israel have deeply revolted.

α.31.7 Newutche ne kesukok nishnoh pasuk mittamwossis pish pogkenau silvere wuttinneukontunkoh, kah wosketomp golde wuttinneukontunkoh; neh nehenwonche kenutchegash kezheumpuh wutche matcheseonk.
E.31.7 For in that day every man shall cast away his idols of silver, and his idols of gold, which your own hands have made unto you for a sin.

α.31.8 Neit wut$Assyrian pish penushau nashpe wuttogkodteg, matta menuhkesu[é]nin: kah wuttogkodteg matta kuttamunge wosketomp, pish ummahtupanukqun: qut noh pish wussemo wutch togkodteganit, kah 8skeneumoh pish papuhquojhéonineuh.
E.31.8 Then shall the Assyrian fall with the sword, not of a mighty man; and the sword, not of a mean man, shall devour him: but he shall flee from the sword, and his young men shall be discomfited.

α.31.9 Kah wabesue pish qushkodteau en 8manskut, kah wussontimósimoh pish qusháog mataag k[ó]unumunutcheh, wussin Jehovah, noh wunn8tom ohtag ut Sion, kah ahhut sabasósit ut Jerusalem.
E.31.9 And he shall pass over to his strong hold for fear, and his princes shall be afraid of the ensign, saith the LORD, whose fire is in Zion, and his furnace in Jerusalem.

α.32.1 KUsseh, ketass8t pish sampweusseáe nanauwunnuau, kah sontimosog pish wussittumoe nanauwunnuáog.
E.32.1 Behold, a king shall reign in righteousness, and princes shall rule in judgment.

α.32.2 Kah wosketomp pish tatuppeyeu8 asompamukque ayeuonganit wutche wabanit kah unkwhonk wutch mishehtash, onatuh sepue nippeash ut [n]abohteaiyeuut, onatuh mishikqussukquane onkauohteau, ut sauunnumoe ohkeit.
E.32.2 And a man shall be as an hiding place from the wind, and a covert from the tempest; as rivers of water in a dry place, as the shadow of a great rock in a weary land.

α.32.3 Kah wuskesuk88ash neg nagig matta pish pogkenum8mun8ash, kah wuhtauogk8oash neg n8togig, pish kuhkeihtamwog.
E.32.3 And the eyes of them that see shall not be dim, and the ears of them that hear shall hearken.

α.32.4 Wuttah wonk kákinne musquantog posh wohtam8m8 wahteóonk, nohnogkiáe meenan, pakodche pish wunának8waog.
E.32.4 The heart also of the rash shall understand knowledge, and the tongue of the stammerers shall be ready to speak plainly.

α.32.5 Nishkeneunkqussuenin matta pish wonk hennau chippinin, kah kasenussit matta pish hennou mag8énin.
E.32.5 The vile person shall be no more called liberal, nor the churl said to be bountiful.

α.32.6 Newutche nishkeneunkqussuaénin unn8wau nishkeneunkquokish, kah wuttah ussémo matcheseonk eiantukiyeue ussenat, kah ayeuuhkônitt8e unnónát Jehovah, mohchiéhheonat ukketeahogkounoh noh kódtupwit, kah wohkuhquohsumwaheau kohkutt8nutcheh 8tattam8onk.
E.32.6 For the vile person will speak villany, and his heart will work iniquity, to practise hypocrisy, and to utter error against the LORD, to make empty the soul of the hungry, and he will cause the drink of the thirsty to fail.

α.32.7 Wutauwohteaongash wonk noh kasenussit matchi[t]ash: natwontam matche natwontam8ongash, paguanonat matchekuwog nashpe pann8wae kutt8wongash, quenahikqutcheg sampweyéhettit[.]
E.32.7 The instruments also of the churl are evil: he deviseth wicked devices to destroy the poor with lying words, even when the needy speaketh right.

α.32.8 Qut wunnenéhuwaénin natwontam wunnenehuae teaguassinish kah nashpe wunnenehuwae teaguassinish pish neep[o]u.
E.32.8 But the liberal deviseth liberal things; and by liberal things shall he stand.

α.32.9 Nepo8k kenaau mittamwossisog sasegeneamogish: n8tam8k n8wadtauatonkqussuonk mattohhentupontamwe wuttauninneunk, kuhkeihtam8k nukkutt8wonk.
E.32.9 Rise up, ye women that are at ease; hear my voice, ye careless daughters; give ear unto my speech.

α.32.10 M8chetikquinne, & kodtum8ash pish k8tamehpunomw8, kenaau mat toh$hen tupantam8e mittamwossissog: newutche wenominneash pish mat nekininn8ash, matta pish mauunneaun.
E.32.10 Many days and years shall ye be troubled, ye careless women: for the vintage shall fail, the gathering shall not come.

α.32.11 Nunnukshunk kenau sasegenamwe mittamwossissog, wuttamanátam8k kenaau mattohhentupanatam8ogish, mukk8keg, kah poskishegk, puttukquobpissuontam8k man8tionak ut kussegon8out.
E.32.11 Tremble, ye women that are at ease; be troubled, ye careless ones: strip you, and make you bare, and gird sackcloth upon your loins.

α.32.12 Nag pish mauog wutch sogkodtunkash, wutch wunne ohteuhkonash, wutch mishummeechume weenomwussippog.
E.32.12 They shall lament for the teats, for the pleasant fields, for the fruitful vine.

α.32.13 Ut wutohk8out nummissinninnumog pish 8tch sonkinneau asinnekoussog, kah koussog, nux nish$noh ut wekontamwe wetuomut, ut wekontamwe otanat.
E.32.13 Upon the land of my people shall come up thorns and briers; yea, upon all the houses of joy in the joyous city:

α.32.14 Newutche mishikkomukquash pish ahquontamunash, keitotanae monacheg pish nukkonnoog, ummanshkash kah qunuhk8komukquash, nish pish asampamukquotash micheme, 8wekontam8ongan8 touohkomukque assessog, flokse tanadtupp8onk.
E.32.14 Because the palaces shall be forsaken; the multitude of the city shall be left; the forts and towers shall be for dens for ever, a joy of wild asses, a pasture of flocks;

α.32.15 Nô pajeh nashauanit sokenumonteaog wutch wohqut, kah touohkomuk mishummeechumme ohteukonu8k, kah mishummeechume ohteuk ogquontamuk touohkomuk.
E.32.15 Until the spirit be poured upon us from on high, and the wilderness be a fruitful field, and the fruitful field be counted for a forest.

α.32.16 Neit wussittumoonk pish ayeum8 touohkomuk, kah sampweusseonk ohtaut mishummeechumue ohteuhkonit.
E.32.16 Then judgment shall dwell in the wilderness, and righteousness remain in the fruitful field.

α.32.17 Kah sampweusseae anakausuonk ne pish wunohteaonk: kah sampweusseae usseonk ne manunnissuonk kah pahkontam8onk micheme.
E.32.17 And the work of righteousness shall be peace; and the effect of righteousness quietness and assurance for ever.

α.32.18 Kah nummissinninnumog pish ayeuog wunohteae ayeuonganit, kah menuhki ayeuonganehtu, kah wunohteae anwohsinwe ayeuonganehtu.
E.32.18 And my people shall dwell in a peaceable habitation, and in sure dwellings, and in quiet resting places;

α.32.19 Missegog, n8kit ut touohkomuk, kah keitotan pish tiohqunkquodt, tiuhquonkque ayeuonganit.
E.32.19 When it shall hail, coming down on the forest; and the city shall be low in a low place.

α.32.20 Wunnanumittegk ohketeaogish kiṣhke wame nippeit, na en sohh8kouogish wussét8ash oxinog kah assesog.
E.32.20 Blessed are ye that sow beside all waters, that send forth thither the feet of the ox and the ass.

α.33.1 MIssi kutonkapunaonk woskhuwaan, kah matta k8woskhitteop, kah as8kekodteam8e ussean kah nag matta kutas8kekomuk8panneg: chequnapean wutch k8woskhuwaonganit pish ken k8woskhit, chequnapean wunassumuwae usseonganit nag pish k8nassum8e unnehikquog.
E.33.1 Woe to thee that spoilest, and thou wast not spoiled; and dealest treacherously, and they dealt not treacherously with thee! when thou shalt cease to spoil, thou shalt be spoiled; and when thou shalt make an end to deal treacherously, they shall deal treacherously with thee.

α.33.2 Woi Jehovah, kitteamonteanuminnean, kuppahtsuonumunonup: ken nag uhpittenhettich nish$noh mohtompan, kah wonk n8wadchanitteaonganun wuttamehpunamuk.
E.33.2 O LORD, be gracious unto us; we have waited for thee: be thou their arm every morning, our salvation also in the time of trouble.

α.33.3 Wogkouee wadtauatongqussimuk missinninnuog wussem8og: tahshinadt kuhhog, wutohtimoneash seahhamunapash.
E.33.3 At the noise of the tumult the people fled; at the lifting up of thyself the nations were scattered.

α.33.4 Kah kussequttahhamoonk pish mohmounumun onatuh mohmounuk m8p: onatuh quaqueshontae popomshaonk, ne pish wuttinne quogqueeu tahtashkuhkauon.
E.33.4 And your spoil shall be gathered like the gathering of the caterpiller: as the running to and fro of locusts shall he run upon them.

α.33.5 Jehovah misheheau, newutche qunuhqui ayeu, numwohtau Zion wussittumoonk kah sampweusseonk,
E.33.5 The LORD is exalted; for he dwelleth on high: he hath filled Zion with judgment and righteousness.

α.33.6 Kah waantamoonk kah wahteoon pish ne ummenuhkesuonk kutahquompiyeum, kah wadchanuae menuhkesuonk, qushaonk Jehovah ne wunnompakou.
E.33.6 And wisdom and knowledge shall be the stability of thy times, and strength of salvation: the fear of the LORD is his treasure.

α.33.7 Kusseh, ummenuhkeseum8uh nag pish poquadchit ut móoh: wunohteae ann8nitcheg pish weesogohposuog.
E.33.7 Behold, their valiant ones shall cry without: the ambassadors of peace shall weep bitterly.

α.33.8 Taumaogquash yaunegenash: pomushaenin ahqshau: noh pohqunum wunn8waonk, noh jishontam keitotanash: mattohhentupanumau8 howae wosketompoh.
E.33.8 The highways lie waste, the wayfaring man ceaseth: he hath broken the covenant, he hath despised the cities, he regardeth no man.

α.33.9 Ohke maueem8, kah ahp8teau, Lebanon akodchu, kah tummetahwhau: Sharon ogqueneunkqussu touohkomukqut, kah Baashan; kah Carmel ne[n]emonteáog ummeechummuóngan8.
E.33.9 The earth mourneth and languisheth: Lebanon is ashamed and hewn down: Sharon is like a wilderness; and Bashan and Carmel shake off their fruits.

α.33.10 Yeuyeu nutomohkem n8wau Jehovah, yeuyeu nummishhit, yeuyeu nuttahshin nuhhog.
E.33.10 Now will I rise, saith the LORD; now will I be exalted; now will I lift up myself.

α.33.11 Pish k8wompequomw8 wussadteamunash, pish keneechamw8 séque kepenunk: kenashaongan8 onatuh n8tau, pish kummahtsikquneau.
E.33.11 Ye shall conceive chaff, ye shall bring forth stubble: your breath, as fire, shall devour you.

α.33.12 Kah missinninnuog pish ogqueneunkqussuog chokkoswut lime, onatuh tummehtahwhaeu asinnekôussog pish chikoswóog ut n8taut.
E.33.12 And the people shall be as the burnings of lime: as thorns cut up shall they be burned in the fire.

α.33.13 N8tam8k kenaau nôappéogish uttoh asée, kah kenaau paswoppéogish, wahteau8k nummenuhkesuonk.
E.33.13 Hear, ye that are far off, what I have done; and, ye that are near, acknowledge my might.

α.33.14 Zione matcheseanuog wabesuog, wabesuonk nuhkuhkongquog eiantogkeiog, howan ut kenugke nuhhogkanonut pish ayit mahchukkissuwaeu n8taut? howan ut kenugke nuhhogkanonut pish ayit micheme chikohsuonganit?
E.33.14 The sinners in Zion are afraid; fearfulness hath surprised the hypocrites. Who among us shall dwell with the devouring fire? who among us shall dwell with everlasting burnings?

α.33.15 Noh sampweusseae pomushadt, k[à]h sampwe án8wadt, noh sekeneog woskehuwae anuhamoadtúongash: seahog wunnutchegash wutch kogkôunumunat kemunkquodtunk, noh kobhog wuhtauogash wutch n8tamunat musqueheonk, kah yanunuk wuskesukquash wutch naumunat machuk.
E.33.15 He that walketh righteously, and speaketh uprightly; he that despiseth the gain of oppressions, that shaketh his hands from holding of bribes, that stoppeth his ears from hearing of blood, and shutteth his eyes from seeing evil;

α.33.16 Noh pish qunuhqui ayeu, wutushphouaongane ayeuonk, ne ukqussukquanonkônous, petukqununk pish aninnumauau, wunnippe pish papaneyéu8.
E.33.16 He shall dwell on high: his place of defence shall be the munitions of rocks: bread shall be given him; his waters shall be sure.

α.33.17 Kuskesukquash pish naau ketass8toh ut wunnetuonganit: nag pish kuhkinneamwog ohke ne n[ó]ohtag.
E.33.17 Thine eyes shall see the king in his beauty: they shall behold the land that is very far off.

α.33.18 Kuttah pish natwontam unkqueneunkquok, uttiyeuoh Scribe? uttiyeuoh attumunumwenin? uttiyeuoh agketog qununkqui kommukquash.
E.33.18 Thine heart shall meditate terror. Where is the scribe? where is the receiver? where is he that counted the towers?

α.33.19 Matta pish kenauoh nashquetue missinninnuog, siohkont8wae missinninnuog neg woh mo wohtauoacheg: nahnagkiae menan ne woh mo wohtam8an.
E.33.19 Thou shalt not see a fierce people, a people of a deeper speech than thou canst perceive; of a stammering tongue, that thou canst not understand.

α.33.20 Kukinneam8k Zion moeongane nukkeitotat: kuskesukquash pish naum8m8ash Jerusalem manunne ayeuonk, Tabernakle ne matta pish n8kinum8muk, matta pasuk nepattuhquonk pish ontahto8un micheme, kah matta pasuk uppemunneat pish pokshan8.
E.33.20 Look upon Zion, the city of our solemnities: thine eyes shall see Jerusalem a quiet habitation, a tabernacle that shall not be taken down; not one of the stakes thereof shall ever be removed, neither shall any of the cords thereof be broken.

α.33.21 Qut na$ut sohsumoe Jehovah noh pish kuttatupanumoun mishekishkae kah kussitchuwane sepue ayeuonk: ne matta pish aomun8g wuttuhhongane kuht8nog, kah matta pish wunnegane kuht8nog paumushomun8.
E.33.21 But there the glorious LORD will be unto us a place of broad rivers and streams; wherein shall go no galley with oars, neither shall gallant ship pass thereby.

α.33.22 Newutche Lord noh k8sittumwaeneumun, Jehovah noh naumatuonk ayimunkqueog, Jehovah nukkehtass8tamomun, noh pish k8wadchanukqun.
E.33.22 For the LORD is our judge, the LORD is our lawgiver, the LORD is our king; he will save us.

α.33.23 Kukkishpinegash ompinimunash, matta wunne menehkheauog wussepogkonganuhtugk8oh, n8nanumoog sépagkinnumun sepagheg: neit mishe tohqunumwe sequttahhamoonk chachaubenumun n8chumwesitcheg nemunnumwog tohqunnumoonk.
E.33.23 Thy tacklings are loosed; they could not well strengthen their mast, they could not spread the sail: then is the prey of a great spoil divided; the lame take the prey.

α.33.24 Kah noh wadôhkit matta pish n8woou nummahchinam: missinninnuog neg na wadohkitcheg, pish ahquontamauóog ummatcheseonganooash.
E.33.24 And the inhabitant shall not say, I am sick: the people that dwell therein shall be forgiven their iniquity.

α.34.1 PAhs8tshagk, kenaau wutohtimóneash n8tamunat, kah kuhkeitam8k kenaau missinninnuog, ohke n8taj, kah wame ne naohtag, muttaok, kah wame ne waj sohham8m8uk.
E.34.1 Come near, ye nations, to hear; and hearken, ye people: let the earth hear, and all that is therein; the world, and all things that come forth of it.

α.34.2 Newutche ummishe musquanitteaonk Jehovah ohteau ut wame wutohtimóneat, kah wutôskoméhheaonk ut wame ukkenauwameongan8oont: noh uppápaquane pagwanoh, nah upponuh paguanaonganit,
E.34.2 For the indignation of the LORD is upon all nations, and his fury upon all their armies: he hath utterly destroyed them, he hath delivered them to the slaughter.

α.34.3 Kah wonk pagwatauutcheh pish sohwhôokonuh, kah wuttann8wongan8 pish wutch sohham8m8 wunnupwe hogkaóont, kah wadchuash pish mohtupohtaash nashpe 8sqheongan8.
E.34.3 Their slain also shall be cast out, and their stink shall come up out of their carcases, and the mountains shall be melted with their blood.

α.34.4 Kah wame kesukque kenauwameonk pish ompéog, kah kesukquash pish ogque tuttuppaginausuash ahtunk wussukwhosimuk, kah wame ukkenawameonk pish ogque penushaog weenómwussippog pá[n]shunk, kah onatuh panshunk wutch figsuhtugqut.
E.34.4 And all the host of heaven shall be dissolved, and the heavens shall be rolled together as a scroll: and all their host shall fall down, as the leaf falleth off from the vine, and as a falling fig from the fig tree.

α.34.5 Newutche nuttogkodteg kutchissittauun ut kesukqut, kusseh, pish 8núhkuhkongquneau Idumea, kah ut nummatánumáe missinninnuut, en wussittum8onganit.
E.34.5 For my sword shall be bathed in heaven: behold, it shall come down upon Idumea, and upon the people of my curse, to judgment.

α.34.6 Wuttogkodteg Jehovah numwohteau musqueheonk; ne wu[u]nogquehteauun nashpe wanogqinnu8k, kah nashpe lambse kah goatse 8squeheonk, nas[k]pe ramse wutt8unnusse wees: newutche Jehovah ayim sephausuonk: ut Bozrah kah miṣhe paguanittuonk ut Idumea ohkeit.
E.34.6 The sword of the LORD is filled with blood, it is made fat with fatness, and with the blood of lambs and goats, with the fat of the kidneys of rams: for the LORD hath a sacrifice in Bozrah, and a great slaughter in the land of Idumea.

α.34.7 Kah nequttu[un] pish 8weeche w8mseumoh, & oxinog weeche bulsog, & wutohkeu pish wuttadtippáh naṣhpe musqueheonk: kah uppuppissiyeum8 pish weesteauun naṣhpe wees.
E.34.7 And the unicorns shall come down with them, and the bullocks with the bulls; and their land shall be soaked with blood, and their dust made fat with fatness.

α.34.8 Newutche ne Jehovah wutann8tauwae kesukodtum: kah onkquatongane kodtum8ash wutche Zione penuanittuonk.
E.34.8 For it is the day of the LORD's vengeance, and the year of recompences for the controversy of Zion.

α.34.9 Kah nish kussehtannuppeash pish quinnuppenumunash en pittu$ut, kah uppuppissiyeum en brimstonut kah ne ohke pish chikohtae pitteu8.
E.34.9 And the streams thereof shall be turned into pitch, and the dust thereof into brimstone, and the land thereof shall become burning pitch.

α.34.10 Matta pish ontham8un nukonae kah kesukodae, ne pukuttau pish micheme ushpem8: wutch pometuonganit onk yean pometu[o]nganit pish mohtuppashin, matta pish howan uppamuhkom8un micheme.
E.34.10 It shall not be quenched night nor day; the smoke thereof shall go up for ever: from generation to generation it shall lie waste; none shall pass through it for ever and ever.

α.34.11 Qut kuttis kah bittern pish wutohta[n]unneau, kah wonk k8k8khos, kah konkont pish 8tohkin, kah pish naswaiyeue pemunneohtane ukkuhkhamun kah mahchiyeue qussukquanash. 
E.34.11 But the cormorant and the bittern shall possess it; the owl also and the raven shall dwell in it: and he shall stretch out upon it the line of confusion, and the stones of emptiness.

α.34.12 Pish wekomaog wussontimosum8oh en ass8tam8onganit, qut matta howane pish na wutappeinneau, kah wame wussontimos[u]m8oh pish monteag wunnuoh.
E.34.12 They shall call the nobles thereof to the kingdom, but none shall be there, and all her princes shall be nothing.

α.34.13 Kah asinnekoussoh pish sontuoh ut ummishekommukquehtu; netlesash kah koussog ut 8wonkôn8sinn8wout, & ne pish wutayeuongan8 Dragonsog, kah ummoeayeuongan8 k8k8khausog.
E.34.13 And thorns shall come up in her palaces, nettles and brambles in the fortresses thereof: and it shall be an habitation of dragons, and a court for owls.

α.34.14 Touohkomukque wonk puppinashimwog pish nogkishkouaog munnahhanne puppinashimwog; kah satyr pish wehkomau weecheheioh: kah weewes na pish wuttit anwósinin, kah pish namehteou anwosinoe ayeuonk.
E.34.14 The wild beasts of the desert shall also meet with the wild beasts of the island, and the satyr shall cry to his fellow; the screech owl also shall rest there, and find for herself a place of rest.

α.34.15 Mishe k8k8khaus ná pish wuttit wadchishahkon, kah pish ahtinahsin, kah pwohkuhhoeyau, kah miayeu ut agwu wutonkouohtomut: na wonk pish ut vultursog miaeog nish$noh pasuk weeche wutishquoshomoh.
E.34.15 There shall the great owl make her nest, and lay, and hatch, and gather under her shadow: there shall the vultures also be gathered, every one with her mate.

α.34.16 Natinneakontam8k ut upb8kum Lord, kah ogketam8k: wanne pasuk yeush pish mat teagwuninno, wanne pasuk pish quenauhik8 wutishquoshomoh: newutche nut8n wutann8hteamun, & wunnashauanitt8moh ummukinoh.
E.34.16 Seek ye out of the book of the LORD, and read: no one of these shall fail, none shall want her mate: for my mouth it hath commanded, and his spirit it hath gathered them.

α.34.17 Kah wuttit tanohtóadtuwanshuh, kah wunnutcheg pemuneat wunnashpe chachabinuh: nag pish ummichemohtauuneau, wutch pometuonganit onk yaan pometuonganit na pish wuttaiinneau.
E.34.17 And he hath cast the lot for them, and his hand hath divided it unto them by line: they shall possess it for ever, from generation to generation shall they dwell therein.

α.35.1 TOuohkomuk kah touwushinne ayeuonk pish nah 8wekontam8onuh, kah touohkomuk pish muskouantam, kah peṣhauau onatuh rose.
E.35.1 The wilderness and the solitary place shall be glad for them; and the desert shall rejoice, and blossom as the rose.

α.35.2 Pish m8cheke peṣhauau, kah pish wekontamwe kah ket8hamáe muskouantam: wussohsumoonk Lebanon pish unninnuma[u]on, 8neetuonk Carmel kah Sharon: nag pish naumwog wussohsumóonk Jehovah, kah 8neetuonk kum[-]Manitt8mun.
E.35.2 It shall blossom abundantly, and rejoice even with joy and singing: the glory of Lebanon shall be given unto it, the excellency of Carmel and Sharon, they shall see the glory of the LORD, and the excellency of our God.

α.35.3 Menehketeo8k n8chumwe menutchegash, kah menuhkesuweheuk n8chumwe mukkuttukquog.
E.35.3 Strengthen ye the weak hands, and confirm the feeble knees.

α.35.4 Unnók nag wabesuwutte[à]honcheg, menuhkesek, ahque wabesek, kusseh, kum-Manitt8mw8 pish ann8tauwae peyau Manit nashpe onkquatunk, noh pish peyau k8wadchanukqunnaout.
E.35.4 Say to them that are of a fearful heart, Be strong, fear not: behold, your God will come with vengeance, even God with a recompence; he will come and save you.

α.35.5 Neit wuskesuk88ash pogkenukeg pish wohshwem8[à]sh, kah kohkobsahtauogash pish pohquaémoash.
E.35.5 Then the eyes of the blind shall be opened, and the ears of the deaf shall be unstopped.

α.35.6 Neit pish n8chumwesuenin ogque quequeshau áyompaut, kah mo kakutt8e meenan pish ketohomom8: newutche nippe pish sonkhetchuan wutch touohkomuk, kah kussitchúanash ut touohkomuk.
E.35.6 Then shall the lame man leap as an hart, and the tongue of the dumb sing: for in the wilderness shall waters break out, and streams in the desert.

α.35.7 Kah kôhkohteadtáe ohke pish nuppissú8, & kúhkuht8n8e ohke ne pish nippeae tohkekomu8, ut dragone ayeuonganit, uttoh nish$noh pasuk sepsuk, na pish mosketú8 wekinashquash, kah rushes[á]sh.
E.35.7 And the parched ground shall become a pool, and the thirsty land springs of water: in the habitation of dragons, where each lay, shall be grass with reeds and rushes.

α.35.8 Kah toumaog na pish ohteau, kah may, kah ne pish hettamun wunneetupanatamwe may, nishkeneunkqussit matta pish uppaumukkomm8un, qut ne pish yeug wutche, papaumusháenuog, tohkônogque ass8khettit, matta pish pehchumma8og.
E.35.8 And an highway shall be there, and a way, and it shall be called The way of holiness; the unclean shall not pass over it; but it shall be for those: the wayfaring men, though fools, shall not err therein.

α.35.9 Na matta pish qunnón8wunn8, kah wanne m8wheyausae puppinashim na pish ukkuhkuhquein, matta pish na$ut nameheaun: qut manouhwhutcheg na pish uppomushoneau.
E.35.9 No lion shall be there, nor any ravenous beast shall go up thereon, it shall not be found there; but the redeemed shall walk there:

α.35.10 Kah manouwhoncheh Jehovah pish qushkeog, kah pish peyaog Sion nashpe ket8hom[á]ongash, kah machemohtag wekontamoonk ut uppuhkuk8óut, nag pish attumunumwog mskauantamoonk kah wekontamoonk, kah unkquanumoonk kah mishânom8onk pish pt8sheau.
E.35.10 And the ransomed of the LORD shall return, and come to Zion with songs and everlasting joy upon their heads: they shall obtain joy and gladness, and sorrow and sighing shall flee away.

α.36.1 KAh n$nih nabo weyáue kodtom8m Hezekiah ketass8t, Sennacherib Assyriae ketass8t ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquehtauau wame pummeneutaúsue keitotanash Judah, kah nish wussohkomunash.
E.36.1 Now it came to pass in the fourteenth year of king Hezekiah, that Sennacherib king of Assyria came up against all the defenced cities of Judah, and took them.

α.36.2 Kah Assyriae ketass8t ann8nau Rabshekah wutch Lachish en Jerusalem, en Hezekiah ketass8t[im]wut, weeche miṣhe kenauwameoh: kah ne[é]pau kishke kohkuhquóhtag ohtopaṣhitteunk, ut mayut wutohteuhkonit pôanek8énin.
E.36.2 And the king of Assyria sent Rabshakeh from Lachish to Jerusalem unto king Hezekiah with a great army. And he stood by the conduit of the upper pool in the highway of the fuller's field.

α.36.3 Eliakim wunnaumonuh Hilkiah noh en sohham, noh piahquttuk weetu, kah Shebna noh Scribe, kah Joash wunnaumonuh Asaph mehquontamwahuwaénin.
E.36.3 Then came forth unto him Eliakim, Hilkiah's son, which was over the house, and Shebna the scribe, and Joah, Asaph's son, the recorder.

α.36.4 Kah Rabshakeh nah wuttinuh, yeuyeu unnók Hezekiah, yeu wussin miṣhe ketass8t, Assyriae ketass8t, chaugua yeu teagwe yeu wutt8anatam8onk ne pabahtantaman?
E.36.4 And Rabshakeh said unto them, Say ye now to Hezekiah, Thus saith the great king, the king of Assyria, What confidence is this wherein thou trustest?

α.36.5 Nussim (kussim, qut webe tahn8che kutt8wongash) nutóhto kog[à]hquttuonk, kah menuhkesuonk en ayeuuhkonat: qut h[o]wan kuppabahtanum, waj chek[é]htauwéan?
E.36.5 I say, sayest thou, (but they are but vain words) I have counsel and strength for war: now on whom dost thou trust, that thou rebellest against me?

α.36.6 Kusseh, kuppabahtantam pohquiyeue k8wékinasque anwohhou, ut Egypt, ne howan ompatussum8óntog, woh ummiskouwutchinun: ne wuttátupéyeuwunneau Pharaoh Egypte ketass8t, wame neh pabahtanumukqutcheh.
E.36.6 Lo, thou trustest in the staff of this broken reed, on Egypt; whereon if a man lean, it will go into his hand, and pierce it: so is Pharaoh king of Egypt to all that trust in him.

α.36.7 Qut ussean, nuppabahtanumómun Jehovah num-Manitt8mun[?] sun noh matta, ukqunúhqui ayeuongash, kah wut-altarumash Hezekiah wunneemunumunapash, kah unnóp Judahoh kah Jerusalemoh, pish k8wowussummuwómw8 ut anaquohtag yeu Altar?
E.36.7 But if thou say to me, We trust in the LORD our God: is it not he, whose high places and whose altars Hezekiah hath taken away, and said to Judah and to Jerusalem, Ye shall worship before this altar?

α.36.8 Newutche yeuyeu mag8k kenohtohsuongash, k8wehquetumoush, en nussontimômut Assyriae ketass8t, kah kuttinninnumoush neese muttañonganogkussuog horsesog, tapenuman wutch k8weech8humukqunnaóut neh ná8mahetticheh.
E.36.8 Now therefore give pledges, I pray thee, to my master the king of Assyria, and I will give thee two thousand horses, if thou be able on thy part to set riders upon them.

α.36.9 Tohwutch neit quinuppequaéhtauadt pasuk peississit mugquomp nussontimom wuttinneumoh, kah pabahtánumadt Egypt wutch chariotsash kah nay8mukqutcheg horsesoh?
E.36.9 How then wilt thou turn away the face of one captain of the least of my master's servants, and put thy trust on Egypt for chariots and for horsemen?

α.36.10 Kah yeuyeu nen ayeuuhkonittue nukkuhkuhquéhtamun yeu ohke matta wusseinat Jehovah, pagwatauunat? Jehovah nuttinuk, ayeuuhkonittue kuhkuhquéhtash yeu ohke, kah pagwataush.
E.36.10 And am I now come up without the LORD against this land to destroy it? the LORD said unto me, Go up against this land, and destroy it.

α.36.11 Neit Eliaim kah Shebna, kah Joah unnaog Rábshakehoh, unnont8wanumau k8wehquetumoush kittinneumog Syraie unnont8waonk, newutche n8wohtamunan: kah ahque unnont8wanumaiinnean Jewse unnont8waonk, ut wehtauogk8wout missinninnuog neg apitcheg pummeneutonganit,
E.36.11 Then said Eliakim and Shebna and Joah unto Rabshakeh, Speak, I pray thee, unto thy servants in the Syrian language; for we understand it: and speak not to us in the Jews' language, in the ears of the people that are on the wall.

α.36.12 Qut Rabshakeh n8wau, sun nussontimom nutann8nukqus en kussontimomut, kah en kuhhogkat, unneat yeush kutt8wongash? sunnummatta nuttin ánn8nuk8h wosketompahtu neg apitcheg pummeneutonganit, onk woh meechuog nehenwonche umm8yu, kah wuttattamwog wunnuneyeu, weeche kenauu?
E.36.12 But Rabshakeh said, Hath my master sent me to thy master and to thee to speak these words? hath he not sent me to the men that sit upon the wall, that they may eat their own dung, and drink their own piss with you?

α.36.13 Neit Rabshakeh neepáu, kah mishont8wau, nashpe Jewse unnont8waonk, kah n8wau, n8tám8k ukkutt8wongash mishe ketass8t, Assyriae ketass8t.
E.36.13 Then Rabshakeh stood, and cried with a loud voice in the Jews' language, and said, Hear ye the words of the great king, the king of Assyria.

α.36.14 Yeu wussin ketass8t, ahque Hezechiah as8kekomuk8k, newutche matta pish tapenum8 kuppohquohwhunukqunnaoout.
E.36.14 Thus saith the king, Let not Hezekiah deceive you: for he shall not be able to deliver you.

α.36.15 Asuh ahque Hezechiah pabahtantamwahik8k Jehovah$ut, n8wonat, Jehovah pish wunamuhkut kuppohquohwhunukqun, yeu keitotan matta pish mag8un, en wunnutcheganit Assyriae ketass8t.
E.36.15 Neither let Hezekiah make you trust in the LORD, saying, The LORD will surely deliver us: this city shall not be delivered into the hand of the king of Assyria.

α.36.16 Kuhkehtauuhteok Hezechiah, newutche yeu wussin Assyriae ketass8t, wunn8waonk ayimaiek nashpe mag8onk, kah sohham8k en nuhhogkat: kah meech8k nish$noh pasuk nehenwonche, 8wenomwussippog, kah nehenwonche, figsehtug, kah wuttattam8k nish$noh pasuk ohtopashitteae nippeash.
E.36.16 Hearken not to Hezekiah: for thus saith the king of Assyria, Make an agreement with me by a present, and come out to me: and eat ye every one of his vine, and every one of his fig tree, and drink ye every one the waters of his own cistern;

α.36.17 Noh pajeh nuppéyonat, kah keneemunumunnaoout en ohket tatuppeyeu8uk nehenwonche kutohkeyeuout: weatchiminee ohke, kah wine ohke petukqunneganee kah weenominneohtekonee ohke.
E.36.17 Until I come and take you away to a land like your own land, a land of corn and wine, a land of bread and vineyards.

α.36.18 Nupweshanukquehteok Hezechiah unn8wadt, Jehovah pish kuppohquohwhunukqun: sun howae wutohtimounneae Manittuog pohquohwúttoog wutohtu wutch wunnutcheganit Assyriae ketass8t?
E.36.18 Beware lest Hezekiah persuade you, saying, the LORD will deliver us. Hath any of the gods of the nations delivered his land out of the hand of the king of Assyria?

α.36.19 Uttiyeug Hamathe kah Arpade Manitt8og? uttiyeug Sepharvaim8e M[à]nitt8og? kah sun nag pohquohwhunoog Samaria wutch nunnutcheganit?
E.36.19 Where are the gods of Hamath and Arphad? where are the gods of Sepharvaim? and have they delivered Samaria out of my hand?

α.36.20 Howanig neg ut kénugke wame yeug wutohtimoinne Manitt8og, neg pohquohwhuttunkeg wutohtu wutch nunnutcheganit, waj woh Jehovah pohquohwuttunk Jerusalem wutch nunnutcheganit?
E.36.20 Who are they among all the gods of these lands, that have delivered their land out of my hand, that the LORD should deliver Jerusalem out of my hand?

α.36.21 Qut nag chequnappuog, kah matta wunnamp8hamauouh pasuk kutt8onk, newutche ketáss8t wutann8teám8onk, ne an8womuk namp8hamauuhteok,
E.36.21 But they held their peace, and answered him not a word: for the king's commandment was, saying, Answer him not.

α.36.22 Neit Eliakim wunnaumonuh Hilkiah, noh piahquttuk wetu, kah Shebna noh Scribe kah Joah wunnaumonuh Asaph mehquontamwayeuaenin, peyaunáog Hezechiahoh, sokqshadtauwehettit wuthogk8un8oash, kah nah wuttinnonaoash ukkutt8wongash Rabshakeh.
E.36.22 Then came Eliakim, the son of Hilkiah, that was over the household, and Shebna the scribe, and Joah, the son of Asaph, the recorder, to Hezekiah with their clothes rent, and told him the words of Rabshakeh.

α.37.1 KAh n$nihyeup Hezechiah ketass8t yeu n8tog nehnekshadto wuthogk8unash kah man8tionak hogk8, kah petutteau wekit Jéhovah.
E.37.1 And it came to pass, when king Hezekiah heard it, that he rent his clothes, and covered himself with sackcloth, and went into the house of the LORD.

α.37.2 Kah ann8nau Eliakim noh nanauwunuk weetu, Shebna noh Scribe & Sepausuenue Eldersog, agqhettit man8tionak, en Esayah quoshodtumwaenuut wunnaumonuh Amoz.
E.37.2 And he sent Eliakim, who was over the household, and Shebna the scribe, and the elders of the priests covered with sackcloth, unto Isaiah the prophet the son of Amoz.

α.37.3 Kag nág wuttinouh, yeu wussin Hezechiah, yeu kesukok wuttamehpunae kesukod, kah auskomae, kah Blasphemae, newutche mukkiog kodtauweetuog, kah matta menuhkesuonganun8h neechonat.
E.37.3 And they said unto him, Thus saith Hezekiah, This day is a day of trouble, and of rebuke, and of blasphemy: for the children are come to the birth, and there is not strength to bring forth.

α.37.4 Pagwodcheh woh Jehovah n8tam ukkutt8wongash Rabshakeh, neh Assyriae ketàss8t, wussontimomoh an8nukqut kehkomonat pomantamwae God, kah pish auskontam kutt8wongash nish Lord kum$Manitt8m n8togish: newutche tahshinush kuppeantam8onk, wutche sequttahwhutcheg ne apitcheg.
E.37.4 It may be the LORD thy God will hear the words of Rabshakeh, whom the king of Assyria his master hath sent to reproach the living God, and will reprove the words which the LORD thy God hath heard: wherefore lift up thy prayer for the remnant that is left.

α.37.5 Neit wuttinneumoh ketass8t Hezechiah peyaonaog Isaiahoh.
E.37.5 So the servants of king Hezekiah came to Isaiah.

α.37.6 Kah Isaiah nah wuttinuh, yeu woh kittinnoneau kussontimom8h, yeu wussin Jehovah, wabesuontam8hkon kutt8ongash nish n8tamanish, nish nashpe wuttinneumoh Assyriae ketass8t nupblasphemónukquog.
E.37.6 And Isaiah said unto them, Thus shall ye say unto your master, Thus saith the LORD, Be not afraid of the words that thou hast heard, wherewith the servants of the king of Assyria have blasphemed me.

α.37.7 Kusseh, nupponamau nashauongoh, kah noh pish n8tam unnussittunkquôt, kah pish qushkeu en nehenwonche wutohkit, kah nuppunushah nashpe togkodteg ut nehenwonche wutohkit.
E.37.7 Behold, I will send a blast upon him, and he shall hear a rumour, and return to his own land; and I will cause him to fall by the sword in his own land.

α.37.8 Neit Rabshakeh qushkeu, kah namehheau Assyriae ketass8toh, ayeuuhkontamunat Libnah: newutche n8tamup, moncheai wutch Lachish.
E.37.8 So Rabshakeh returned, and found the king of Assyria warring against Libnah: for he had heard that he was departed from Lachish.

α.37.9 Kah n8tamup papaume Tirhakah Ethiopiae ketass8t, noh sohham kutayeuuhkonukqunat: kah n8tog, ann8nau ann8náenuh en Hezechiahut n8wonat.
E.37.9 And he heard say concerning Tirhakah king of Ethiopia, He is come forth to make war with thee. And when he heard it, he sent messengers to Hezekiah, saying,

α.37.10 Yeu woh kuttinnoneau Hezechiah Judae ketass8t, n8wagk, kum-Manitt8m noh pabahtanumadt as8kukkomuk8hkon, n8wonat Jerusalem matta pish mag8un en wunnutchegani Assyriae ketass8t.
E.37.10 Thus shall ye speak to Hezekiah king of Judah, saying, Let not thy God, in whom thou trustest, deceive thee, saying, Jerusalem shall not be given into the hand of the king of Assyria.

α.37.11 Kusseh, ken8tamup Assyriae ketass8tamwog, ne anteauhettit wame wutohtimoineash, papuhquanne pagwanonaoont, kah ken sun woh kuppohquohwhunit?
E.37.11 Behold, thou hast heard what the kings of Assyria have done to all lands by destroying them utterly; and shalt thou be delivered?

α.37.12 Wutohtimoune Manitt8og, sun nah uppohquohwhunouh, neh n8shog mahche pagwanahetticheh, ut Gozanut, kah Haranut, kah Rezephut, kah wunneechanoh Eden neg apitcheg Telassar?
E.37.12 Have the gods of the nations delivered them which my fathers have destroyed, as Gozan, and Haran, and Rezeph, and the children of Eden which were in Telassar?

α.37.13 Uttiyeuoh Hamathe ketass8t, Arphade ketass8t, kah Sepharvaimme otanae ketass8t, Henah kah Ivah?
E.37.13 Where is the king of Hamath, and the king of Arphad, and the king of the city of Sepharvaim, Hena, and Ivah?

α.37.14 Kah Hezechiah attumunum wussukwhonk, wutch wunnutcheganit ann8naenin kah wutogketamun: kah Hezechiah kuhkuhqueu en wekit Jehovah, kah wussepaginumun ut anaquabit Jehovah.
E.37.14 And Hezekiah received the letter from the hand of the messengers, and read it: and Hezekiah went up unto the house of the LORD, and spread it before the LORD.

α.37.15 Kah Hezechiah peantamauau Jehovahoh, n8wau,
E.37.15 And Hezekiah prayed unto the LORD, saying,

α.37.16 Woi Jehvoah ayeuteaunit, um-Manitt8moh Israel, ken ayean nashauwe Cherubimsut, ken um-Manitt8m8uh, ken webe, wame ass8tam8ongash ut ohkeit, ken kukkesteoh kesuk kah ohke.
E.37.16 O LORD of hosts, God of Israel, that dwellest between the cherubims, thou art the God, even thou alone, of all the kingdoms of the earth: thou hast made heaven and earth.

α.37.17 Ahch8sitash, woi Jehovah, kah n8tash wôhshinush kuskesukquash woi Jehovah, kah naish, kah n8tash wame ukkutt8wongash Senacherib, nish an8teamwutcheh kehkomonat pomantamwae God.
E.37.17 Incline thine ear, O LORD, and hear; open thine eyes, O LORD, and see: and hear all the words of Sennacherib, which hath sent to reproach the living God.

α.37.18 Wunnamuhkut woi Jehovah, Assyriae ketass8tamwog, pagwodteoog wame wutohtimoneash, kah wutohtuoash.
E.37.18 Of a truth, LORD, the kings of Assyria have laid waste all the nations, and their countries,

α.37.19 Kah unnohteaog um[$]Manitt8m8uh en n8taut: newutche nag matta Manitt88og, qut wosketompae wunnutchegane anakausuongash, mehtug káh qussuk: newaj nah pagwanont.
E.37.19 And have cast their gods into the fire: for they were no gods, but the work of men's hands, wood and stone: therefore they have destroyed them.

α.37.20 Newutche yeuyeu, woi Jehovah num-Manitt8mun, wadchaninneau wutch wunnutcheganit onk woh wame ass8tam8ongash muttaohket, wahteauog, ken Jehovah, ken webe.
E.37.20 Now therefore, O LORD our God, save us from his hand, that all the kingdoms of the earth may know that thou art the LORD, even thou only.

α.37.21 Neit Isaiah wunnaumonuh Amoz ann8team8, en Hezechiahut, n8wau yeu wussin Jehvovah um-Manitt8m8oh Israel, paantamauwean ayeuuhkonittue Senacherib, Assyriae ketass8t.
E.37.21 Then Isaiah the son of Amoz sent unto Hezekiah, saying, Thus saith the LORD God of Israel, Whereas thou hast prayed to me against Sennacherib king of Assyria:

α.37.22 Yeu ukkutt8onk Jehovah ne an8wop papaume nagum: peénomp, wuttaunoh Zion kutjishanumuk, kah momontauae kutahan8wehtunk, wuttaunoh Jerusalem, kenónokuhquaehtunk.
E.37.22 This is the word which the LORD hath spoken concerning him; The virgin, the daughter of Zion, hath despised thee, and laughed thee to scorn; the daughter of Jerusalem hath shaken her head at thee.

α.37.23 Howan kuhkékom, kupblasphemon? kah howan ayeuuhkonittue kummishont8wánumau, kah kukqun[ú]hque táhshinum kuskesukquash, ayeuuhkonittue 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
E.37.23 Whom hast thou reproached and blasphemed? and against whom hast thou exalted thy voice, and lifted up thine eyes on high? even against the Holy One of Israel.

α.37.24 Nashpe kittinneumog kukkehkom Jehovah, kah kussip, nashp[é] mataánukish nutchariotsumash, nukkuhkuhquem en kudohkôag wadchuuhkontu, sussippoeu Lebanon, kah nuttumehtah quanunkqussitcheg chikuppog, kah pepenamwe k8wâog, kah pish nuppetutteam kodukóag wussissipôiyeumut, kah uk-Carmelle touohkomuk.
E.37.24 By thy servants hast thou reproached the Lord, and hast said, By the multitude of my chariots am I come up to the height of the mountains, to the sides of Lebanon; and I will cut down the tall cedars thereof, and the choice fir trees thereof: and I will enter into the height of his border, and the forest of his Carmel.

α.37.25 N8wonuhkontamup kah n8tatumup nippe, kah nashpe nusseet nukôhkonéhteap wame wusseppum8ash neg wéenuhkauógkutcheg.
E.37.25 I have digged, and drunk water; and with the sole of my feet have I dried up all the rivers of the besieged places.

α.37.26 Sunnummatta n8adt ken8tam8mus uttoh ánteau, kah n8adt nukkuhkenauéhtinneap? yeuyeu nukkezteauun, onk woh ken kummahchumwehteauuneat pummeneutausue keitotanash wep8to8ut.
E.37.26 Hast thou not heard long ago, how I have done it; and of ancient times, that I have formed it? now have I brought it to pass, that thou shouldest be to lay waste defenced cities into ruinous heaps.

α.37.27 Newaj neg na wadohkitcheg n8chumwesuog, kah chepshanaog kah naswaiyeuog, tatuppeyeu8og ohteuhkone moskehtuut, kah ohchippogqut, kah, woskeche weetuome moskehtuut, kah pissagquodtinnit weachiminneash.
E.37.27 Therefore their inhabitants were of small power, they were dismayed and confounded: they were as the grass of the field, and as the green herb, as the grass on the housetops, and as corn blasted before it be grown up.

α.37.28 Qut n8wahteoh kutayeuonk, kah kussohham8onk kah kuppetukonat, kah kummusquanummuonk.
E.37.28 But I know thy abode, and thy going out, and thy coming in, and thy rage against me.

α.37.29 Newutche kummusquanummuonk, kah k8wogkoue[ó]nk kuhkuhquem8 en nuhtauogkut: newaj ponum n8hquon kutchónit, kah nup-bridlum ut kussisset8nit, kah kukkushquenush en mayut ne wâman.
E.37.29 Because thy rage against me, and thy tumult, is come up into mine ears, therefore will I put my hook in thy nose, and my bridle in thy lips, and I will turn thee back by the way by which thou camest.

α.37.30 Kah yeu pish kukkehkinneasuonk yeu kodtum8k pish kummeechumw8, ne nehenwonchekik: kah nahohtóeu kodtumuk, ne nan noh wadchegit: kah nishwe kodtum8k ohkehteagk, kah kepenum8k, kah weenominneohketeagk, kah meech8k ne meechu[m]muonk.
E.37.30 And this shall be a sign unto thee, Ye shall eat this year such as groweth of itself; and the second year that which springeth of the same: and in the third year sow ye, and reap, and plant vineyards, and eat the fruit thereof.

α.37.31 Kah sekqshoncheg ut wekit Judah neg pohquohhogig, nág pish ohkeayeu unuhchabukaog, kah wohkummiyeu unummeechummuog.
E.37.31 And the remnant that is escaped of the house of Judah shall again take root downward, and bear fruit upward:

α.37.32 Newutche ashqushoncheg pish sohhamwog wutch Jerusalem, kah neg wutch pohquohhogig wadchuut Zion: wuszealum Jehovah ayeuteaunit yeu pish wutussen.
E.37.32 For out of Jerusalem shall go forth a remnant, and they that escape out of mount Zion: the zeal of the LORD of hosts shall do this.

α.37.33 Newaj yeu n8wadt Jehovah papaume wutássyriae ketass8t, matta pish petutteaou pummeyeu keihtotanat kah matta pish nawuttit in kouhquodt kah matta pish naṣhpe peyoou ogqunegash, & matta pish wutayeuuhkonittue kutaham8un.
E.37.33 Therefore thus saith the LORD concerning the king of Assyria, He shall not come into this city, nor shoot an arrow there, nor come before it with shields, nor cast a bank against it.

α.37.34 Ne may wagkup, ne pish wonk wuttin qushken kah matta pish yeu petuttutteaun keihtotan n8wau Jehovah[-]
E.37.34 By the way that he came, by the same shall he return, and shall not come into this city, saith the LORD.

α.37.35 Newutche yeu n8wadchumun keihtotan, wadchanumunat wutche nen nehenwonche, kah wutche nuttinneum David.
E.37.35 For I will defend this city to save it for mine own sake, and for my servant David's sake.

α.37.36 Neit wut-Angelumoh Jehovah sohhamwoh, kah nushau ut wuttuppukkussinn8wongan8wout Assyriansog, nequt pasuk8e, kah shwosuk tahshinchage, kah napanna tahshe muttanonganogkussuog: kah nompoaeu omohkehettit kusseh nag wame nupwog.
E.37.36 Then the angel of the LORD went forth, and smote in the camp of the Assyrians a hundred and fourscore and five thousand: and when they arose early in the morning, behold, they were all dead corpses.

α.37.37 Neit Senacherib wut-Assyriae ketass8t amaeu kah monchu kah qushku, kah ayeu Ninive.
E.37.37 So Sennacherib king of Assyria departed, and went and returned, and dwelt at Nineveh.

α.37.38 Kah nniyeup wó[u]ssumont weekit Nishroch ummanitt8m, Hidramelech kah Sharezer wunnaumonuh, wuttogkomukquoh ohkeit, kah Esarhaddon wunnaumonuh wunnompe nanawunnuwómukquoh.
E.37.38 And it came to pass, as he was worshipping in the house of Nisroch his god, that Adrammelech and Sharezer his sons smote him with the sword; and they escaped into the land of Armenia: and Esarhaddon his son reigned in his stead.

α.38.1 YEush ut kesukodtash Hezekiah mahchinau en nuppunat, kah Isaiah quoshodtumwaen wunnaumonuh Amoz peyaonukquoh, kah wuttugquoh, yeu wussin Jehovah, wunohtoush kek, newutche pish kenup, kah matta kuppomantamóh.
E.38.1 In those days was Hezekiah sick unto death. And Isaiah the prophet the son of Amoz came unto him, and said unto him, Thus saith the LORD, Set thine house in order: for thou shalt die, and not live.

α.38.2 Neit Hezechiah quinnippinnum wuskesuk en sussipponkomuk, kah péantamauau Jehovah.
E.38.2 Then Hezekiah turned his face toward the wall, and prayed unto the LORD,

α.38.3 Kah n8wau, mehquontash yeuyeu woi Jehovah k8wehquetumoush, uttoh an pomusháomp ut anaquabean wunnamuhkutée, káh pañuppeteaháeu kah nummahche ussem né wanekik ut anaquabean, kah Hezechiah muttauhpâsu.
E.38.3 And said, Remember now, O LORD, I beseech thee, how I have walked before thee in truth and with a perfect heart, and have done that which is good in thy sight. And Hezekiah wept sore.

α.38.4 Neit wuttinn8waonk Jehovah peyaonuk Isayah n8wau,
E.38.4 Then came the word of the LORD to Isaiah, saying,

α.38.5 Monchish us Hezechiah, yeu wussin Jehovah, um-Manitt8moh David k8sh: nunn8tam kuppeantamoonk, nunnaum kussippegwash: kusseh, nukk8tn[e]hteoh kukkesukodtumash nabo napanna tahshe kodtumwae.
E.38.5 Go, and say to Hezekiah, Thus saith the LORD, the God of David thy father, I have heard thy prayer, I have seen thy tears: behold, I will add unto thy days fifteen years.

α.38.6 Kah pish kuppohquohwhunush kah yeu keitotan, wutch wunnutcheganit Ass[y]iae ketass8t: kah n8wadchanum yeu otán.
E.38.6 And I will deliver thee and this city out of the hand of the king of Assyria: and I will defend this city.

α.38.7 Kah yeu pish kuhkinneasuonk wutch Jehovahut, woh wutussen Jehovah ne an8wadt.
E.38.7 And this shall be a sign unto thee from the LORD, that the LORD will do this thing that he hath spoken;

α.38.8 Kusseh, nutomponcheáhtoh dialle onkauohteau ne womussúm8uk ut Ahaze wussun-dialumut, ompo[h]ch[é]eu piogquonéhtuonk neit nepauz piogquonehtuongane qushkeu, nish mahche pamuhkogkish.
E.38.8 Behold, I will bring again the shadow of the degrees, which is gone down in the sun dial of Ahaz, ten degrees backward. So the sun returned ten degrees, by which degrees it was gone down.

α.38.9 OOsukuhwhesuonk Hezechiah Judae ketass8t, mahchinadt, kah keteóp wutch ummahchinónat.
E.38.9 The writing of Hezekiah king of Judah, when he had been sick, and was recovered of his sickness:

α.38.10 Nussip tâmussumuk nukkesukodtumash, pish nuttom weenohkée squontamut: sequnnumukish nukkodtum8mash nutamaunumonteanash.
E.38.10 I said in the cutting off of my days, I shall go to the gates of the grave: I am deprived of the residue of my years.

α.38.11 Nussip matta pish nunnau Jehovah, Jehovah ut pomantamoe ohkeit: matta pish wonk nunnauoh wosketomp, weeche wadohkitcheg muttaohkit.
E.38.11 I said, I shall not see the LORD, even the LORD, in the land of the living: I shall behold man no more with the inhabitants of the world.

α.38.12 Nukkechisuonk nutontoht[ò]nteau onatuh nanaushepsaen wekit: nuttummussum nukketeaonk onatuh monakinehteáenin: pish nuttummussuk nashpé mohchim8e mahchinnaonguh: w[u]tch kesukodtut pajeh wunnonk8ut, pish kummahcheh.
E.38.12 Mine age is departed, and is removed from me as a shepherd's tent: I have cut off like a weaver my life: he will cut me off with pining sickness: from day even to night wilt thou make an end of me.

α.38.13 Nutogketomup pajeh mohtompanúut, onatuh qunnonouut pish pokshadto wame nuskonash, wutch kesukodtut pajeh wunnonk8ut k8wohkukquohsumeh.
E.38.13 I reckoned till morning, that, as a lion, so will he break all my bones: from day even to night wilt thou make an end of me.

α.38.14 Onatuh sassadt asuh mameesashquis, ne nuttinn8won, nutogque mauop wuskuhwhunanâut: nuskesukquash sauunum88ash spadtauwompinneat: woi Jehovah, nussinukkuhhuk, nontumah.
E.38.14 Like a crane or a swallow, so did I chatter: I did mourn as a dove: mine eyes fail with looking upward: O LORD, I am oppressed; undertake for me.

α.38.15 Toh pish nussim? naneeswe nuttukqunáh, kah nagum wutussen: pish nukkemwusham ut wame nukkodtum8mut, n8wésogke keteahogkôunit.
E.38.15 What shall I say? he hath both spoken unto me, and himself hath done it: I shall go softly all my years in the bitterness of my soul.

α.38.16 Woi Lord nashpe yeush pomantamwog wosk[e]tompaog: kah ut wame yeush nunnashauongane pomantamoonk ohteau, neit kukketeáheh kah kuppomantamwaheh
E.38.16 O LORD, by these things men live, and in all these things is the life of my spirit: so wilt thou recover me, and make me to live.

α.38.17 Kusseh, wutche wunohteaonk nutáhtop mishe weesogkunóonk, qut k8womonomp nukketeahogkou, kah kuppohquohwhun wutch aninn8e pissohtheganit; newutch kuttinnôhteap wame nummatcheseongash kuppusquanit.
