E.38.17 Behold, for peace I had great bitterness: but thou hast in love to my soul delivered it from the pit of corruption: for thou hast cast all my sins behind thy back.

α.38.18 Newutche weenohk[é] mattá woh k8wóweenomuk8h, nupp8onk matta kummishanumuko[u], neg womussitcheg en passahtheganit, matta woh annoontamóog k8namuhkutéayeum.
E.38.18 For the grave cannot praise thee, death can not celebrate thee: they that go down into the pit cannot hope for thy truth.

α.38.19 Pâmontog, pâmontog noh pish k8woweenomuk, ne ásee yeu kesukok, wut8shimau pish wahteauwahuah k8namuhkutéyeum en mukkiesut.
E.38.19 The living, the living, he shall praise thee, as I do this day: the father to the children shall make known thy truth.

α.38.20 Jehovah nukkenuppe wadchanuk, newaj pish unn8homóog nukket8homaongash nashpe pemunneohtone puhpegk, tosohke pomontamog ut wekit Jehovah.
E.38.20 The LORD was ready to save me: therefore we will sing my songs to the stringed instruments all the days of our life in the house of the LORD.

α.38.21 Newutche Isaiah n8wop, neemunumohettich figse puttukqutchéi, kah ponaskéhtuáhettich mogquenit, kah pish keteau.
E.38.21 For Isaiah had said, Let them take a lump of figs, and lay it for a plaister upon the boil, and he shall recover.

α.38.22 Hezekiah wonk n8wop, teagwe kuhkinneasuonk onk woh nukkuhkuhquem en weekit Jehovah.
E.38.22 Hezekiah also had said, What is the sign that I shall go up to the house of the LORD?

α.39.1 NA ahquompak Merod[a]ch-Baladan wunnaumonuh Baladan Babylone ketass8t, negonshúau wussukwhongash noh en, kah mag8onk en Hezechiahut, newutche n8tam mahchinap, kah keteau.
E.39.1 At that time Merodachbaladan, the son of Baladan, king of Babylon, sent letters and a present to Hezekiah: for he had heard that he had been sick, and was recovered.

α.39.2 Kah Hezechiah nah 8weekontam8ónuh, kah wunnohtinuh wunnompak8unikkomuk, silver, kah gold, kah spicesash, kah mishôadtue sussequeáeu pummeeash, kah wame ukkenauwamée week, káh wame ne ohtag ut weekit, kah ut wame wutass8tom8onganit, ne Hezechiah matta nohtinnunk.
E.39.2 And Hezekiah was glad of them, and shewed them the house of his precious things, the silver, and the gold, and the spices, and the precious ointment, and all the house of his armour, and all that was found in his treasures: there was nothing in his house, nor in all his dominion, that Hezekiah shewed them not.

α.39.3 Neit Isaiah quoshodtumwáen peyaonau Hezechiah ketass8toh, kah wuttinuh, toh n8waog yeug wosketompaog? kah tohnoh 8mwog en kuhhogkat, kah Hezechiah n8wop, neg nuppeyaonukquog wutch nôadtit wutohtimoneat, wutch Babylon.
E.39.3 Then came Isaiah the prophet unto king Hezekiah, and said unto him, What said these men? and from whence came they unto thee? And Hezekiah said, They are come from a far country unto me, even from Babylon.

α.39.4 Neit n8wop, teagwa naumwog ut kékit? k[á]h Hezekiah namp8ham, naumwog wame ne neekit ohtag, matta ne teag ut nunnompag8unnekomukqut, ne matta nóhtinóog.
E.39.4 Then said he, What have they seen in thine house? And Hezekiah answered, All that is in mine house have they seen: there is nothing among my treasures that I have not shewed them.

α.39.5 Neit Isaiah unnau, Hezechiahoh, n8tash ukkutt8onk Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
E.39.5 Then said Isaiah to Hezekiah, Hear the word of the LORD of hosts:

α.39.6 Kusseh, kesukodtash peyom8ash, ne wame kekit ohtag, kah nish k8shog wadchanummóhetteupash pajeh yeu kesukok, pish uss8wuttauunash Babylon, matta pish teag ushqunnum8un wussin Jehovah.
E.39.6 Behold, the days come, that all that is in thine house, and that which thy fathers have laid up in store until this day, shall be carried to Babylon: nothing shall be left, saith the LORD.

α.39.7 Kah neg pish monchanaog kenaumonuh, neg sohhogig wutch kohhogkat, neg pish wânamoniéaneg, kah nag pish wuttinneumunneunk wekit Babylone ketass8t.
E.39.7 And of thy sons that shall issue from thee, which thou shalt beget, shall they take away; and they shall be eunuchs in the palace of the king of Babylon.

α.39.8 Neit Hezechiah unnau Isaiahoh, wunnegen ukkutt8onk Jehovah ne an8wáan: kah wonk n8wop, newutche wunohteaonk kah wanumuhkuteyeuuk ohteau ut nukkesukodtumut.
E.39.8 Then said Hezekiah to Isaiah, Good is the word of the LORD which thou hast spoken. He said moreover, For there shall be peace and truth in my days.

α.40.1 TAphéninongqutch, taphéninongqutch nummissinninneumog, n8wau kum-Manitt8m.
E.40.1 Comfort ye, comfort ye my people, saith your God.

α.40.2 Tapheáe ken8nók Jerusalem, kah mishont8wánumók, ummattompagum wohkukquashin, ummatcheseonk ahquontamun: newutche attumunum wutch Jehovah wunnutcheganit, pápskeu wutch wame ummatcheseongash.
E.40.2 Speak ye comfortably to Jerusalem, and cry unto her, that her warfare is accomplished, that her iniquity is pardoned: for she hath received of the LORD's hand double for all her sins.

α.40.3 OOwadtauatonkqussuonk noh mashont8adt ut touohkomuk; quagquoshwehtam8k ummay Jehovah, sampwehteó8k ut touohkomuk ummay num-Manitt8mun.
E.40.3 The voice of him that crieth in the wilderness, Prepare ye the way of the LORD, make straight in the desert a highway for our God.

α.40.4 Nishnoh 8nóuhkôi pish qunóhqutteauun, kah nishnoh wadchu, kah wadchuemes pish tiuhquohquttauunash, kah woonkagk pish sampweteauunash, kah machipsquehtuash pish m8siyeuash.
E.40.4 Every valley shall be exalted, and every mountain and hill shall be made low: and the crooked shall be made straight, and the rough places plain:

α.40.5 Kah wussohsumoonk Jehovah pish náhtúhkon, kah wame weyaus pish wunnaumuneau moayeu: newutche wutt8n Jehovah wussinnin.
E.40.5 And the glory of the LORD shall be revealed, and all flesh shall see it together: for the mouth of the LORD hath spoken it.

α.40.6 Wadtauatonkqussuonk n8wop, Mishont8wash, Kah n8wau, Teagwe woh mishont8wai, wame weyaus moskehtu8, kah wame na$ut wanegik tatuppeyeu8 ohteuhkone uppeshaónut.
E.40.6 The voice said, Cry. And he said, What shall I cry? All flesh is grass, and all the goodliness thereof is as the flower of the field:

α.40.7 Maskeht ahp8hteau, uppeshau penusheau, newutche wunnashontamun Jehovah, wunnamuhkut missinninnúog moskehtu8og.
E.40.7 The grass withereth, the flower fadeth: because the spirit of the LORD bloweth upon it: surely the people is grass.

α.40.8 Moskeht ahp8hteau, uppeshau penusheau: qut wuttinn8waonk num-Manitt8mun pish michemohteau.
E.40.8 The grass withereth, the flower fadeth: but the word of our God shall stand for ever.

α.40.9 Woi Zion, noh wanonchimudt, kuhkuhquish en kussôhkôiyeue wadchuut: woi Jerusalem ken wanonchimwean, menuhke mishont8wash, mishont8wash, wabesehkon: utash Judáe keitotanash, moninneok kum-Manitt8mw8.
E.40.9 O Zion, that bringest good tidings, get thee up into the high mountain; O Jerusalem, that bringest good tidings, lift up thy voice with strength; lift it up, be not afraid; say unto the cities of Judah, Behold your God!

α.40.10 Kusseh, Lord Manit menuhku peyau, kah wuhpit nanawunnumwanshau: kusseh, wutonkquatunk weechayeumuk, kah wutanakausuonk ohteau anaquabit.
E.40.10 Behold, the Lord GOD will come with strong hand, and his arm shall rule for him: behold, his reward is with him, and his work before him.

α.40.11 Pish sohkom8uneau uf-flockum onatuh nanaushepsaenin: noh pish mouneau lambsoh ut wuhpittenit, kah pish ukkeninuh ut upp8chenauónut, kah pish manunne sagkompanau wompeqúaunitcheh.
E.40.11 He shall feed his flock like a shepherd: he shall gather the lambs with his arm, and carry them in his bosom, and shall gently lead those that are with young.

α.40.12 Howan quaquadh8k nippeash ut wunnutcheganit? kah quadompskinuk kesukquash nashpe wunnutcheg, kah miahtunk ohkee puppissai, ut quttuhhonganit, kah quadh8k wadchuash ut qutompagh8teganit, kah wadchuemesash quttompagh8teganit.
E.40.12 Who hath measured the waters in the hollow of his hand, and meted out heaven with the span, and comprehended the dust of the earth in a measure, and weighed the mountains in scales, and the hills in a balance?

α.40.13 Howan kogáhtimont wunnashauanitt8moh Jehovah, asuh kogáhqutteamweneumwit ukkuhk8tomauuh.
E.40.13 Who hath directed the Spirit of the LORD, or being his counsellor hath taught him?

α.40.14 Howaneh k8n8náhetteup, howan ukkuhk8tomauoh, kah ukkuhk8tomauoh wussittumóe may? kah ukkuhk8tomauoh wahteauonk kah wunnahtinuh wohwohtamwe may.
E.40.14 With whom took he counsel, and who instructed him, and taught him in the path of judgment, and taught him knowledge, and shewed to him the way of understanding?

α.40.15 Kusseh, wutohtimoneash tatuppeyeu8ash pápenuppáshunk p8thonchuut, ogquanu[m]ukquss8og puppissiyeuwésit ut qutompagh8teganit: kusseh, nemunum ogquidnash onatuh ne teag peyasik.
E.40.15 Behold, the nations are as a drop of a bucket, and are counted as the small dust of the balance: behold, he taketh up the isles as a very little thing.

α.40.16 Kah Lebanon matta wamuttinn8 chikohsumunat, kah puppinashimwog na apitcheg matta womattinn8 wutche chikohtae mag8onk.
E.40.16 And Lebanon is not sufficient to burn, nor the beasts thereof sufficient for a burnt offering.

α.40.17 Wáme wutohtimoneash ut anaquabit, onatuh matteagwuninu8g, kah náh wutogquanumoh anue peyasik onk ne mo teag, kah t[á]hn8che.
E.40.17 All nations before him are as nothing; and they are counted to him less than nothing, and vanity.

α.40.18 Neit Howan ogquanumôg Godut? asuh teagwe ogqueneunkqussuonk kutogqunneauau.
E.40.18 To whom then will ye liken God? or what likeness will ye compare unto him?

α.40.19 Anakausuen sabaswau nunneukontunkoh, kah Golde-Smith sepagenumauoh upputtoguhwaeu gold, kah wunnupasahdtoh silvere chainsash.
E.40.19 The workman melteth a graven image, and the goldsmith spreadeth it over with gold, and casteth silver chains.

α.40.20 Noh machekit noh mat teag woh mag8k, pepenam mehtug, ne woh mo anittinn8g: natinnewhau nehtoou anakausuenuñeu ukquoshauehtauonat nunneukontungoh, ne matta woh ontapegk.
E.40.20 He that is so impoverished that he hath no oblation chooseth a tree that will not rot; he seeketh unto him a cunning workman to prepare a graven image, that shall not be moved.

α.40.21 Sunnummatta k8wahteauomw8? sunnummatta ken8tam8m8? sunnummatta kuttitteaunaous, waj kutchissik? sunnummatta k8wohtamm8unnaous wutch quenohtagish muttaok?
E.40.21 Have ye not known? have ye not heard? hath it not been told you from the beginning? have ye not understood from the foundations of the earth?

α.40.22 Noh quenapit petukqui ohkeit, kah neg na wadohkitcheg tatuppeyeu8og chansompsit, noh agque sepagunuk kesuk onkwheganit, kah wutogque sepagunumunash weetu ne weetimuk.
E.40.22 It is he that sitteth upon the circle of the earth, and the inhabitants thereof are as grasshoppers; that stretcheth out the heavens as a curtain, and spreadeth them out as a tent to dwell in:

α.40.23 Noh mat toh antuppehheunk sontimosoh: tahn8cheáheau ohkee wussittum8eneuh.
E.40.23 That bringeth the princes to nothing; he maketh the judges of the earth as vanity.

α.40.24 Nux nag pish matta ohkéhteaununk, nux matta pish seahwhoog, nux 8weepuhtugk8 matta pish wadchabukkinn8 ut ohkeit, kah noh pish wonk upp8tomuh, kah nag pish upp8suog, kah pemsquoh pish wutogque amaunuh sequkkepaneganit.
E.40.24 Yea, they shall not be planted; yea, they shall not be sown: yea, their stock shall not take root in the earth: and he shall also blow upon them, and they shall wither, and the whirlwind shall take them away as stubble.

α.40.25 Neit hówan tatupanumeóg, asuh neanèyeue n8wau wunneetupantamwéyeuit?
E.40.25 To whom then will ye liken me, or shall I be equal? saith the Holy One.

α.40.26 Tahshinum8k qunuhqueu kuskesuk88ash, kah kuhkinneam8k howan noh yeush kahkénauwéhteunk, noh kuhkénaue sohh8wunont wutayeuwehteomoh: wame 8wesuongane missahwhoh, nashpe mohsag ummenuhkesuonk, newutche noh menuhkesu, matta pasuk quenauwadtinn8.
E.40.26 Lift up your eyes on high, and behold who hath created these things, that bringeth out their host by number: he calleth them all by names by the greatness of his might, for that he is strong in power; not one faileth.

α.40.27 Tohwutch n8waan, woi Jakob, kah missohhaman, woi Israel, nummay adtahtôsu wutch Lordut, kah n8sumitteáonk paumushóm8 wutch num-Manitt8mut?
E.40.27 Why sayest thou, O Jacob, and speakest, O Israel, My way is hid from the LORD, and my judgment is passed over from my God?

α.40.28 Sun matta k8wahteo8h, sun matta ken8tam8mus machemappue Manit Jehovah noh kezteunk weekqshinne ohke, matta kodtinneó8 asuh sauunnum8? matta howan woh wohkuhquónam8 noh 8wohwohtam8onk.
E.40.28 Hast thou not known? hast thou not heard, that the everlasting God, the LORD, the Creator of the ends of the earth, fainteth not, neither is weary? there is no searching of his understanding.

α.40.29 Noh ummenuhkesuáheau kôdtinneánitcheh, kah neh mat mánuhkesénitcheh nano ummenuhkeheuh.
E.40.29 He giveth power to the faint; and to them that have no might he increaseth strength.

α.40.30 Wuskenúog pish kodtinneaog kah sauunumwog, kah nunkompaog pish pápukquanne penushaog.
E.40.30 Even the youths shall faint and be weary, and the young men shall utterly fall:

α.40.31 Qut neg pahtussuóunoncheg Jehovah pish wuskehteauog ummenuhkesuongan8: pish ogque ushpushaog wompussikukquaut nashpe wunnuppuhwhunoh; nag pish quogqueog kah matta sauunum8og, nag pish pomushaog, kah mat kodtinneau8og.
E.40.31 But they that wait upon the LORD shall renew their strength; they shall mount up with wings as eagles; they shall run, and not be weary; and they shall walk, and not faint.

α.41.1 CHequnapek ut anaquabeh, woi munóhhanog, kah missinninnúog wuskehteauwehettich ummenuhkesuongan8: pas8tsháhettich kah ket8káhettich: moae peyontuh ut wussittum8onganit.
E.41.1 Keep silence before me, O islands; and let the people renew their strength: let them come near; then let them speak: let us come near together to judgment.

α.41.2 Howan omohkinont sampweusseaénúh wutch wutchepwóiyeu, weekomont en wusseetut, áninnumauont wutohtimoneash ut anaquabenit, kah nanawunnumwáheont ta[h]s8tamwoh? wutogque áninnumauoh wuttogkodteg puppissiyuut, kah wutohtompeh onatuh t8annóhhanne sequkkepaneg.
E.41.2 Who raised up the righteous man from the east, called him to his foot, gave the nations before him, and made him rule over kings? he gave them as the dust to his sword, and as driven stubble to his bow.

α.41.3 Nah wunn8swuttahwhóh, wunohteae paumwushau en may$ut ne matta wusseetue paumushog.
E.41.3 He pursued them, and passed safely; even by the way that he had not gone with his feet.

α.41.4 Howan ne ásit kah kezteunk, wehquetuk pometeongash wutch waj kutchissik? nen Jehovah, negonne, kah weeche maumachish, nen n$noh.
E.41.4 Who hath wrought and done it, calling the generations from the beginning? I the LORD, the first, and with the last; I am he.

α.41.5 Munnohhanash wunnaumuneau, kah wabesuog, wekqshinne ohkeash wabesum8ash, pas8tsháog, kah peyaog.
E.41.5 The isles saw it, and feared; the ends of the earth were afraid, drew near, and came.

α.41.6 Nishnoh pasuk [à]ninnumauau weetatteamungoh, kah nishnoh pasuk unnau weematoh wunne wutt8antash.
E.41.6 They helped every one his neighbour; and every one said to his brother, Be of good courage.

α.41.7 Neit wunnágittôhôsuénin wutt8anatamheau gold-smithoh, kah noh m8sitteunk nashpe hammer, kah noh togkodtog anvil, n8waog, pakodche kesompskutteau, kah ukkeneepunun nashpe kenontugwhegash, onk woh matta ontohtano.
E.41.7 So the carpenter encouraged the goldsmith, and he that smootheth with the hammer him that smote the anvil, saying, It is ready for the sodering: and he fastened it with nails, that it should not be moved.

α.41.8 Qut ken Israel, ken nuttinninneum, Jakob noh pepenauog, 8skannem Abram netomp.
E.41.8 But thou, Israel, art my servant, Jacob whom I have chosen, the seed of Abraham my friend.

α.41.9 Ken noh pepenauog wutch wehshik ohke, kah k8wehkomush wutch kenugke mogkouwáut, kah kuttinnunup, ken nuttinninneum, kuppepenaush, kah mattà kuppogkénun8h.
E.41.9 Thou whom I have taken from the ends of the earth, and called thee from the chief men thereof, and said unto thee, Thou art my servant; I have chosen thee, and not cast thee away.

α.41.10 Wabesehkon, newutche k8wetomsh, chepshuhkon, newutche nen kum-Manitt8m: kummenuhkehesh: nux kutáninnumoush, n[ù]x nashpe nussampwée nuttinnuhkounne sampweusseonk kukkogkôunush.
E.41.10 Fear thou not; for I am with thee: be not dismayed; for I am thy God: I will strengthen thee; yea, I will help thee; yea, I will uphold thee with the right hand of my righteousness.

α.41.11 Kusseh, wame nag m8m8qhikqueáneg pish akodchuog kah chepshaog, pish monteagk88og, kah neg mekonukqueaneg pish onkapunaog.
E.41.11 Behold, all they that were incensed against thee shall be ashamed and confounded: they shall be as nothing; and they that strive with thee shall perish.

α.41.12 Nag pish kénátinneahwhòog, & matta pish kenamheoog, neg mekônukqueaneg, neg mátompaguhkónukqueaneg, pish monteagk88og, kah mat tohhentuppayeu8og.
E.41.12 Thou shalt seek them, and shalt not find them, even them that contended with thee: they that war against thee shall be as nothing, and as a thing of nought.

α.41.13 Newutche nen Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, nukkinninum kuttinohkôu, kuttinnush, wabesehkon, kutanninnumoush.
E.41.13 For I the LORD thy God will hold thy right hand, saying unto thee, Fear not; I will help thee.

α.41.14 Wabesehkon ken ask8kse J[o]kob, kah kenaau Israelle wosketomp[a]og kuttanninnumoush, n8wau Jehovah, kah kuppohquohwussuaéneum, OOneetupanatam8moh Israel.
E.41.14 Fear not, thou worm Jacob, and ye men of Israel; I will help thee, saith the LORD, and thy redeemer, the Holy One of Israel.

α.41.15 Kusseh kuttayimoush wuske pogguhham8e weepittum8e auwohteaonk: pish k[u]ppogham wadchuash, kah kussukquttahhamunash, kah pish kuttogqueteoh wadchuash wussadteamunit:
E.41.15 Behold, I will make thee a new sharp threshing instrument having teeth: thou shalt thresh the mountains, and beat them small, and shalt make the hills as chaff.

α.41.16 Pish kuppáuanóntamunash, kah waban pish ummonchadtauunash, kah pemsquoh pish wusseáhhamunash: kah ken pish k8woweenoam ut 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
E.41.16 Thou shalt fan them, and the wind shall carry them away, and the whirlwind shall scatter them: and thou shalt rejoice in the LORD, and shalt glory in the Holy One of Israel.

α.41.17 Mach[ee]k[u] kah qu[é]nahukquit natinnehog nippe, kah na monteagwuninno, kah weenan8 kohkutt8n8e sauunum8m8, nen Lord pish nag nunn8tauoog nen um-Manitt8moh Israel matta nunnukonóog.
E.41.17 When the poor and needy seek water, and there is none, and their tongue faileth for thirst, I the LORD will hear them, I the God of Israel will not forsake them.

α.41.18 N8wôshwunum sepuash ut qunuhqui ayeuonganit, kah tohkekomm[ú]ash ut nôeu 8nóuhkôiyeuut, nupseeu nuppéhteau touohkomuk, kah nu[n]bobohteai nuttohkekomuúhteam.
E.41.18 I will open rivers in high places, and fountains in the midst of the valleys: I will make the wilderness a pool of water, and the dry land springs of water.

α.41.19 Nutohketeam chikkuppog ut touohkomukqut, Shittahuhtug, kah Mirtluhtug, kah pummeeuhtug, kah ut touushinne ohkeit nutohketeam firruhtug, kah pineuhtug, kah boxuhtug moeu.
E.41.19 I will plant in the wilderness the cedar, the shittah tree, and the myrtle, and the oil tree; I will set in the desert the fir tree, and the pine, and the box tree together:

α.41.20 Onk woh nag naumwog, kah wahteauog kah natwontamwog, kah wohtamwog moaeu, wunnutcheg Jehovah yue ussem8, kah 8neetupanatam8moh Israel ukkezteauun.
E.41.20 That they may see, and know, and consider, and understand together, that the hand of the LORD hath done this, and the Holy One of Israel hath created it.

α.41.21 Pas8che paduto8k kuppissaumatuonk n8wau Lord, s8h8wuttau8k kummenuhke unnaumaiyeum8ash, n8wau ukketass8tam8moh Jakob.
E.41.21 Produce your cause, saith the LORD; bring forth your strong reasons, saith the King of Jacob.

α.41.22 Sohh8wuttauwéhettich, kah nahtinnukqutteuh toh pish ônagk: natitteahettich mahche nnagish, uttoh ônagk, onk woh nunnatwontamunánonash, kah woh n8wahteomun adt wohkukquoshik, asuh wahteauwahinnean toh pish ônagk.
E.41.22 Let them bring them forth, and shew us what shall happen: let them shew the former things, what they be, that we may consider them, and know the latter end of them; or declare us things for to come.

α.41.23 Nahtitteagk nish pish ompetak ônagish, onk woh n8wahteomun, kum-Manitt88mw8: nux wunnesek ash matchesek onk woh nutchepshomun, kah woh moéu naumunan.
E.41.23 Shew the things that are to come hereafter, that we may know that ye are gods: yea, do good, or do evil, that we may be dismayed, and behold it together.

α.41.24 Kusseh, matta toh kuttin tuppéayeu8mw8, kah kutanakausuongan8 matteagwunninn8: noh jishánumukqussu noh pepenunkqueóg.
E.41.24 Behold, ye are of nothing, and your work of nought: an abomination is he that chooseth you.

α.41.25 Nutomuhkin pasuk wutch nanumaiyeu, kah noh pish peyau: waj pashpishont pish wehquetum n8wesuonk, kah pish ogque nuhkuhkauau sontimoh, man8nskut, onatuh ahkuhqutteaenin tahtashkuhkauont man8nskoh.
E.41.25 I have raised up one from the north, and he shall come: from the rising of the sun shall he call upon my name: and he shall come upon princes as upon morter, and as the potter treadeth clay.

α.41.26 Howan wahteauwáhu[a]dt waj kutchissik, onk woh n8wahteauunan? kah nish asquam ahquompan8g; onk woh nussimun noh sampweusseaenú8? qut matta howan wunnahtitteauunash, qut matta howan 8wahteauwahuwáunash, nux matta howan n8tam8 kukkutt8wongan88ash.
E.41.26 Who hath declared from the beginning, that we may know? and beforetime, that we may say, He is righteous? yea, there is none that sheweth, yea, there is none that declareth, yea, there is none that heareth your words.

α.41.27 Negonnu pish unnau Zion, kusseh, nag naau, kah nuttinninnumau Jerusalem neh wanaunchumwunutcheh.
E.41.27 The first shall say to Zion, Behold, behold them: and I will give to Jerusalem one that bringeth good tidings.

α.41.28 Newutch nummoninneam, kah na matta wosketompaun8, ut kenugke nagoh, kah na matta kogohqutteamwenuunn8, noh woh namp8hamiit pasuk kutt8onk, nat8tomauog.
E.41.28 For I beheld, and there was no man; even among them, and there was no counsellor, that, when I asked of them, could answer a word.

α.41.29 Kusseh nag wame tahn8cheyeu8og, wutanakausuongan88ash matteagwunun8ash: nag wussabassumwe nunnekontunkan8oh waban[n]u8oh, kah naswaiyeu8oh:
E.41.29 Behold, they are all vanity; their works are nothing: their molten images are wind and confusion.

α.42.1 Nók nuttinneum noh kónunog, noh pepenauog, nukketeahogkou womononcheh, nupponamau nunnashauanitt8moh, noh pish sohh8wuttauau wussittumoonk Gentilsuh.
E.42.1 Behold my servant, whom I uphold; mine elect, in whom my soul delighteth; I have put my spirit upon him: he shall bring forth judgment to the Gentiles.

α.42.2 Matta pish mishont8woou, asuh tháhshinnum8 asuh n8tamwahuwoou 8wadtauatonkqussuonk ut maikontu.
E.42.2 He shall not cry, nor lift up, nor cause his voice to be heard in the street.

α.42.3 Sukqutchoshae wekinasq mâtta uppohquanum8un k[á]h pukuttae hashábpoh matta wutontahwhoh, pish sohh8wuttáu wussittum8onk en wunnamuhkuteyeuut.
E.42.3 A bruised reed shall he not break, and the smoking flax shall he not quench: he shall bring forth judgment unto truth.

α.42.4 Matta pish sauunum8, asuh paunompasu noh pajeh upponamunat wussittumoonk ut ohkeit, kah munnohhanash pish pahtsuwontamog wuttinnaumatuonk.
E.42.4 He shall not fail nor be discouraged, till he have set judgment in the earth: and the isles shall wait for his law.

α.42.5 Yeu wussin Manit Jehovah, noh kahkenauwehteunk kesukquash, & noh sepaginuk, noh mashegskehteunk ohke, kah ne noh waj sohham8m88k, noh nashauwaheont missinninnuh na$ut, kah nashauanitt8heont neh ne paumushanitcheh.
E.42.5 Thus saith God the LORD, he that created the heavens, and stretched them out; he that spread forth the earth, and that which cometh out of it; he that giveth breath unto the people upon it, and spirit to them that walk therein:

α.42.6 Nen Jehovah k8wehkomush ut sampweusseonganit, kah pish nukkenunnum kenutcheg, kah pish kenananunush, kah pish kuttinninnumoush wutche 8n8waongan8 missinninnuog, wutche 8wequaiyeum8 gentilsog.
E.42.6 I the LORD have called thee in righteousness, and will hold thine hand, and will keep thee, and give thee for a covenant of the people, for a light of the Gentiles;

α.42.7 Woshwunnumunat pogkenumwae muskesukquash sohh8wunonat kobshagkinitcheg wutch kubshagkinnittuonganit, kah neg apitcheg pohkenaiyeuut, wutch kuppishagkinnittuae kommukqut.
E.42.7 To open the blind eyes, to bring out the prisoners from the prison, and them that sit in darkness out of the prison house.

α.42.8 Nen Jehovah, ne n8wesuonk, kah nussohsumoonk matta nuttinnumauoun onkatuk, kah matta n8woweenomuwaonk nunneukontunganog.
E.42.8 I am the LORD: that is my name: and my glory will I not give to another, neither my praise to graven images.

α.42.9 Kusseh, negonae ônagish nnihyeuash, kah wuske teagwasinish n8wahteauwáhuwam; asquam sasonkunun8gkup, kuttinunnanaôash.
E.42.9 Behold, the former things are come to pass, and new things do I declare: before they spring forth I tell you of them.

α.42.10 Unn8hamok Jehovah wuske unn8homáonk; kah woweenomaonk wutch wehqshik ohke, kenaau w8mséogish en kehtahhanit, kah wame ne noh ohtag, munnohkanash, kah neg na wadohkitcheg.
E.42.10 Sing unto the LORD a new song, and his praise from the end of the earth, ye that go down to the sea, and all that is therein; the isles, and the inhabitants thereof.

α.42.11 Touohkomuk kah 8tanash naut, mishont8wáhettich, otanamesash nish Kedar wadohkitchish: wadohkitcheg qussukquanit ket8hamahettich, mishont8wahettich wutch kussôhkôiyeue wadchuut.
E.42.11 Let the wilderness and the cities thereof lift up their voice, the villages that Kedar doth inhabit: let the inhabitants of the rock sing, let them shout from the top of the mountains.

α.42.12 Sohsumm8wounáhettich Jehovah, kah wahteauwaheáhettich waweenomaonk munnáhhunoh.
E.42.12 Let them give glory unto the LORD, and declare his praise in the islands.

α.42.13 Jehovah pish ogque sohham menuhkesuenûut, pish wogkowunum m8sitteam8onk, onatuh mattompagwehteaénin: pish mishont8wau, nux onkquont8wau, pish sohkauau ummatwomoh.
E.42.13 The LORD shall go forth as a mighty man, he shall stir up jealousy like a man of war: he shall cry, yea, roar; he shall prevail against his enemies.

α.42.14 Nussepe chequnap, nummanunap, nukquihtin nuhhog: eyeu nutogque mishont8wam neechae mittamwussissut, pish nuppagwohteam nummishashquinneunk pasukqut.
E.42.14 I have long time holden my peace; I have been still, and refrained myself: now will I cry like a travailing woman; I will destroy and devour at once.

α.42.15 Nummáhchumwéhtoh wadchuash kah wadchuemesash, kah nunnunassum wame weherbsum8ash, kah sepuash nummenúhhann8team, kah nunnunassum nuppissepagwash.
E.42.15 I will make waste mountains and hills, and dry up all their herbs; and I will make the rivers islands, and I will dry up the pools.

α.42.16 Kah pogkenumwog nuppas8 mayut ne matta wahteauhetteg, nutuss8unóog maikontu ne matta wahteauhetteg: pohkenai n8wequaiyeuhteam ut nag anaquabhettit, kah woonkagish nussampweteauunash, yeush nuttinheonaoash, kah matta nutohquanumóog.
E.42.16 And I will bring the blind by a way that they knew not; I will lead them in paths that they have not known: I will make darkness light before them, and crooked things straight. These things will I do unto them, and not forsake them.

α.42.17 Nag pish qushkeog, pish mishe akodchuog, pabuhtanumoncheg nunneukontunkoh, neg anoncheg sabassume nunneukontunkoh kenaau num-Manitt8munónog.
E.42.17 They shall be turned back, they shall be greatly ashamed, that trust in graven images, that say to the molten images, Ye are our gods.

α.42.18 N8tam8k kenaau kôkobsóogish, kah natauwompek kenaau pogkenumógish, onk woh kenaumw8.
E.42.18 Hear, ye deaf; and look, ye blind, that ye may see.

α.42.19 Howan pogkenuk webe nuttinninneum? asuh kôkohsont qut nutann8naeneum noh an8nog? howan pogkenuk neane noh pannuppeyeuit, kah pogkenuk neane wuttinneumoh Jehovah?
E.42.19 Who is blind, but my servant? or deaf, as my messenger that I sent?  who is blind as he that is perfect, and blind as the LORD's servant?

α.42.20 Nauman monatash qut matta kukkehkinneasséinash: wôhshinnuman mehtauogash, qut matta n8tam8.
E.42.20 Seeing many things, but thou observest not; opening the ears, but he heareth not.

α.42.21 Lord tapeneam wutche 8nomwausseonk, pish mishehteau naumatuonk, kah ukquhtiánittamutteauun.
E.42.21 The LORD is well pleased for his righteousness' sake; he will magnify the law, and make it honourable.

α.42.22 Qut yeug missinninnuog mukk8kinaog kah matcheheóog, wame puttahwh[ô]og ut wonogquehtu, kah adtashôog ut kuppishaginnitteae kommukqut: nag másompanitcheg, kah matta howan uppohquohwhunoh nag mukk8kinôog, kah wanne howan n8wau ompontin8k.
E.42.22 But this is a people robbed and spoiled; they are all of them snared in holes, and they are hid in prison houses: they are for a prey, and none delivereth; for a spoil, and none saith, Restore.

α.42.23 Howan ut kenugke kenaau, yeu n8tog? howan ahchuwussittog kah n8tog wutche ompetak?
E.42.23 Who among you will give ear to this? who will hearken and hear for the time to come?

α.42.24 Howan anumauont Jakoboh wutche matchehtóonk, kah Israeloh chechequnnuaenúh? sun matta Lord, noh matcheneheogkut? newutche nag cheketamwog pomushonat ummayut, kah matta noswehtamwog wuttinnaumatuonk.
E.42.24 Who gave Jacob for a spoil, and Israel to the robbers? did not the LORD, he against whom we have sinned? for they would not walk in his ways, neither were they obedient unto his law.

α.42.25 Newaj sokenumauont ummishe musquantam8onk, kah menuhkesue ayeuwuttuonk: kah wéenohtauoh n8teau, qut onch matta wahteauun, kah wutchikoswoh, qut matta upponam8un ut wuttahhut.
E.42.25 Therefore he hath poured upon him the fury of his anger, and the strength of battle: and it hath set him on fire round about, yet he knew not; and it burned him, yet he laid it not to heart.

α.43.1 QUt yeuyeu, yeu wussin Jehovah noh kezhikquean, woi Jakob, kah noh kakénauáhikquean, woi Israel, wabesehkon: newutche kummanóuwhush, k8wesuongane missohwhush, ken nuttaihe.
E.43.1 But now thus saith the LORD that created thee, O Jacob, and he that formed thee, O Israel, Fear not: for I have redeemed thee, I have called thee by thy name; thou art mine.

α.43.2 Pannupwusháan nippéash, k8weetomsh, kah qushkodteaan sepuash nish matta pish kenehtipánuk8unash: pannupwushaan n8teau, matta pish kutchikkussu, kah n8n8uneau matta pish kenashqussuk8un.
E.43.2 When thou passest through the waters, I will be with thee; and through the rivers, they shall not overflow thee: when thou walkest through the fire, thou shalt not be burned; neither shall the flame kindle upon thee.

α.43.3 Newutche nen Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, 8neetupanatam8moh Israel kuppohquohwussuaéneum: nummagup Egypt wutch kumman8whun8onk, Ethiopia kah Sheba wutche ken.
E.43.3 For I am the LORD thy God, the Holy One of Israel, thy Saviour: I gave Egypt for thy ransom, Ethiopia and Seba for thee.

α.43.4 Nádteoh máshoadtean ut anaquabeh, kukquhtiánumukqus[si]p, kah k8womonsh, newaj mag8 wosketompaog wutche ken, kah missinninnuog wutche kuppomantam8onk.
E.43.4 Since thou wast precious in my sight, thou hast been honourable, and I have loved thee: therefore will I give men for thee, and people for thy life.

α.43.5 Wabesehkon, newutche k8weetomsh: pish nuppas8 k8skannemunneog wutch wutchepwôou, kah kummohmóunush wutch wutcheksuiyeu.
E.43.5 Fear not: for I am with thee: I will bring thy seed from the east, and gather thee from the west;

α.43.6 Pish nuttin nanumit, magush, kah sowanish assaéhkon, pas8k nunnaumonunk wutch noadtit, kah nuttaunog wutch wehqshik ohke.
E.43.6 I will say to the north, Give up; and to the south, Keep not back: bring my sons from far, and my daughters from the ends of the earth;

α.43.7 Nish$noh pasuk noh as8wesit n8wesuonk: newutche nukkezeh wutche nussohsumóonk, nukkehkenauéhheop, nukkezheop.
E.43.7 Even every one that is called by my name: for I have created him for my glory, I have formed him; yea, I have made him.

α.43.8 Sohh8wunok pôgkenukeg missinninnuog wuskesukqutcheg, kah k[ó]kobsonch$eg wohtauogkutcheg.
E.43.8 Bring forth the blind people that have eyes, and the deaf that have ears.

α.43.9 Wame wutohtimoneash miyaém8utch, kah missinninnuog móappéhettich: howan kenugke nagoh woh yeu wahteauwáhuadt, kah nahtinukqueog negonne anágkupash? sohh8wunáhettich 8wauwáeneum8oh, onk woh sampweógquanumóog, kah n8tamohettich, kah n8wahettich, wunnamuhkuteyeu8.
E.43.9 Let all the nations be gathered together, and let the people be assembled: who among them can declare this, and shew us former things? let them bring forth their witnesses, that they may be justified: or let them hear, and say, It is truth.

α.43.10 Kenaau n8wauwaeneumog wussin Jehovah, kah nuttinninneum noh pepenauog: onk woh k8wahteomw8 kah woh k8namptiimw8, kah woh k8wohtamumw8, noh nen: negonne onk nen matta Manittoun8, kah matta pish wonk asuhkaue onk nen.
E.43.10 Ye are my witnesses, saith the LORD, and my servant whom I have chosen: that ye may know and believe me, and understand that I am he: before me there was no God formed, neither shall there be after me.

α.43.11 Nen, nen Jehovah, kah matta wonk howan wadchanuwaenu8, webe nen.
E.43.11 I, even I, am the LORD; and beside me there is no saviour.

α.43.12 N8wahteauwahuap, kah wadchanuap, kah nunnáhtitteap na matta penowe manitt8un8g ut kenugke kenaau: newutche kenaau n8wauwaeneumog n8wau Jehovah, nen Manitto.
E.43.12 I have declared, and have saved, and I have shewed, when there was no strange god among you: therefore ye are my witnesses, saith the LORD, that I am God.

α.43.13 Nux, asquam kesukodtin8g, nen n$noh, kah matta woh howan pohquohwussuóou wutch nunnutcheganit: pish nutanakaus, kah howan woh 8tamehtauun?
E.43.13 Yea, before the day was I am he; and there is none that can deliver out of my hand: I will work, and who shall let it?

α.43.14 Yeu wussin Jehovah kum$Mano[u]huwaeneum8, 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, wutche kenaau, nutann8hteam en Babilon, kah nuttiuhkongqueh wame wussontimom8uh, kah Caldeansog, neg ummauongan8 ohtag kuht8nugquehtu.
E.43.14 Thus saith the LORD, your redeemer, the Holy One of Israel; For your sake I have sent to Babylon, and have brought down all their nobles, and the Chaldeans, whose cry is in the ships.

α.43.15 Nen Jehovah k8neetupanatam8m8, kezkukqutche Israel, kukketass8tam8m8.
E.43.15 I am the LORD, your Holy One, the creator of Israel, your King.

α.43.16 Yeu wussin Jehovah, noh ayik may ut kehtahhannit, kah may mishe nippekontu.
E.43.16 Thus saith the LORD, which maketh a way in the sea, and a path in the mighty waters;

α.43.17 Sohh8wuttunk charit kah horse, kah menuhkesue kenauwameonk: nag pish mo[á]e sepsinwog, nag matta pish omohkeog: nag ontohwhoog, ogque wuhkohshanoog hashabput.
E.43.17 Which bringeth forth the chariot and horse, the army and the power; they shall lie down together, they shall not rise: they are extinct, they are quenched as tow.

α.43.18 Méhquontam8hteok negonne anagkupush, kah natwontam8hteok noadt anagkupash.
E.43.18 Remember ye not the former things, neither consider the things of old.

α.43.19 Kusseh, n8skeu ussem: eyeu pish sonkun, sun matta pish k8wahte[u]uneau? nummayehteam touóhkomukqut, kah nussepuehteam touushinne ohkeit.
E.43.19 Behold, I will do a new thing; now it shall spring forth; shall ye not know it? I will even make a way in the wilderness, and rivers in the desert.

α.43.20 Ohteuhkônee puppinashimwog pish nukquehtianumukquog, Dragonsog, kah kuhk8khosog, newutche nummag nippe ut touohkomukqut, kah sepuash ut touushinne ohkéit, n8tattamheonat nummissinninnuog pepenauogig.
E.43.20 The beast of the field shall honour me, the dragons and the owls: because I give waters in the wilderness, and rivers in the desert, to give drink to my people, my chosen.

α.43.21 Yeug missinninnuog nukkuhkenauehteauonuh nuhhog, nag pish nahtitteaóg n8woweenomitteaonk.
E.43.21 This people have I formed for myself; they shall shew forth my praise.

α.43.22 Qut matta k8wehquetumiyeuh woi Jakob, qut kussauanumeh woi Israel.
E.43.22 But thou hast not called upon me, O Jacob; but thou hast been weary of me, O Israel.

α.43.23 Chiko[h]tae kummag8e puppinashimwog matta kuppaudtiyeuh, kah matta kenashpe quttiánumyeuh kussephausuongash: matta k8tinninneumuhkônuwahiñ8 nashpe mag8onk, kah matta kussauanunóh nashpe incense.
E.43.23 Thou hast not brought me the small cattle of thy burnt offerings; neither hast thou honoured me with thy sacrifices. I have not caused thee to serve with an offering, nor wearied thee with incense.

α.43.24 Matta kutteagwu kuttaphumwanshu weetemungque wekinask, kah matta k8wamepwuhheuh k8nogk8e sephausuongash, qut k8tinninneumuhkausuwáheh nashpe kummatcheseongash, kussau[u]neh nashpe kummatcheseongash.
E.43.24 Thou hast bought me no sweet cane with money, neither hast thou filled me with the fat of thy sacrifices: but thou hast made me to serve with thy sins, thou hast wearied me with thine iniquities.

α.43.25 Nen, nen noh jishkhog kuppanneseseongash wutche nen nehenwon[c]he, kah matta nummehquontam8h kummatcheseongash.
E.43.25 I, even I, am he that blotteth out thy transgressions for mine own sake, and will not remember thy sins.

α.43.26 Mehquontamwaheh, ken8tamwanshittitteuh: wahteauwahuash, onk woh kussampweogquanumit.
E.43.26 Put me in remembrance: let us plead together: declare thou, that thou mayest be justified.

α.43.27 Negonne k8sh matcheseup: & kukkuhk8tomwehtamog nuppannesehtunkquog.
E.43.27 Thy first father hath sinned, and thy teachers have transgressed against me.

α.43.28 Newaj matchetupanatamwaheog peantamwaekomukque sontimóog, kah nummag Jakob én matánumónat, kah Israel en kekontinneat.
E.43.28 Therefore I have profaned the princes of the sanctuary, and have given Jacob to the curse, and Israel to reproaches.

α.44.1 QUt onch yeuyeu n8tash woi Jakob, nuttinninneum, kah ISrael noh pepenauog.
E.44.1 Yet now hear, O Jacob my servant; and Israel, whom I have chosen:

α.44.2 Yeu wussin Jehoah noh kezhukquean, kah kahkenauwéhikquean wutch ôontomukqut, noh aninnumunkquean: wabesehkon woi Jakob nuttinninneum: kah ken Jesurun noh pepenauogkup.
E.44.2 Thus saith the LORD that made thee, and formed thee from the womb, which will help thee; Fear not, O Jacob, my servant; and thou, Jesurun, whom I have chosen.

α.44.3 Newutch nussokanumau nippe noh kohkutt8g, kah tomogkonash ut nobohteaiyeuut: nussokun nunnashauanitt8m k8skannemunit, kah n8nanitteaonk ut kutontseonganit.
E.44.3 For I will pour water upon him that is thirsty, and floods upon the dry ground: I will pour my spirit upon thy seed, and my blessing upon thine offspring:

α.44.4 Kah nag pish ogque sontuog ut kenugke moskehtekontu, onatuh anumwussukuppeit ut kishke nippekontu.
E.44.4 And they shall spring up as among the grass, as willows by the water courses.

α.44.5 Pasuk pish n8wau n8chi Jehovah, kah onkatuk pish ussowenau wuhhogkuh 8wesuonk Jakob: kah onkatog pish wussukwhosuohtu nashpe wunnutcheg en Jehovahut, kah nahohtoeu 8wesuonganeh[e]au Israeloh.
E.44.5 One shall say, I am the LORD's; and another shall call himself by the name of Jacob; and another shall subscribe with his hand unto the LORD, and surname himself by the name of Israel.

α.44.6 Yeu wussin Jehovah Israelle ketass8t, kah ummanouhuaeneumoh, Jehovah ayeuteaunit, Nen negonáe, k[á]h nen maumachish, kah chonchippe nen wanne Manitt8un8.
E.44.6 Thus saith the LORD the King of Israel, and his redeemer the LORD of hosts; I am the first, and I am the last; and beside me there is no God.

α.44.7 Kah howan neane nen, pish wehqutteamwit, kah pish 8wahteauwahuon, kah pish n8nohtonkqun, náiteuh kahtimog nukkône missinninnuog? kah nish paóm8gish, kah pish peyom8ash? nah nohtin[á]hettich.
E.44.7 And who, as I, shall call, and shall declare it, and set it in order for me, since I appointed the ancient people? and the things that are coming, and shall come, let them shew unto them.

α.44.8 Wabesehteok kah chepshonteog, sunnummatta kuttinn8n[á]s nâ wutch ahquompag, kah n8wahteauwahuwon[á]h? kenaau n8wauwaeneumog, sun wonk Manitto8 chonchippe nen? nux na matta Manitt8un8, matta pasuk n8waheoh.
E.44.8 Fear ye not, neither be afraid: have not I told thee from that time, and have declared it? ye are even my witnesses. Is there a God beside me? yea, there is no God; I know not any.

α.44.9 Neg ayeuoncheg nunneukontungoh, wame neg tahn8cheyeu8og, kah ukkodtantamukóm8ash matta pish 8chienáoash, kah nag nehenwonche 8wauwóm8oh, nag mat naumóog, kah matta wahteáu8og, onk woh akodchuog.
E.44.9 They that make a graven image are all of them vanity; and their delectable things shall not profit; and they are their own witnesses; they see not, nor know; that they may be ashamed.

α.44.10 Howan káhkenauweheont manitto, kah sabaswont nunneukontunkoh, ne matta tohhentupán8g?
E.44.10 Who hath formed a god, or molten a graven image that is profitable for nothing?

α.44.11 Kusseh wame weetomukqutcheh pish akodchuoh: kah anakausuenuog, neg wosketompo8og, wame miyaehettich, kah neepauwehettich: nag pish wabesuog, pish moeu akodchuog.
E.44.11 Behold, all his fellows shall be ashamed: and the workmen, they are of men: let them all be gathered together, let them stand up; yet they shall fear, and they shall be ashamed together.

α.44.12 Smith nashpe wuttongsumash naneeswe, wutayimun nashpe mohkohsaash, kah kehkenauwehtin nashpe hamer, kah nashpe wuhpitte[n]ue menuhkesuonk wutayimun: nux kodtupp8, kah sa[u]unum, matta wuttattam8 nippe kah sauunum.
E.44.12 The smith with the tongs both worketh in the coals, and fashioneth it with hammers, and worketh it with the strength of his arms: yea, he is hungry, and his strength faileth: he drinketh no water, and is faint.

α.44.13 Wunnagkittuhhausuenin sampwompanum ukkehkinneasuonk ukkuhkhamun nashpe pemuneat: 8nteouun nashpe upplainsumash kah ukkuhkhamun nashpe ukompasash, kah wutogquehteauun wosketompaut, neaunak wosketompae wunneetuonk, onk woh ohteau wetuomut.
E.44.13 The carpenter stretcheth out his rule; he marketh it out with a line; he fitteth it with planes, and he marketh it out with the compass, and maketh it after the figure of a man, according to the beauty of a man; that it may remain in the house.

α.44.14 Wannagittahwau chikkupoh, kah nemunnum cypressuhtug, kah n8timis, ne sampwuttahhamont, ut kenugke touohkomukque metugquekontu, ohkehteau monunkqsoh, kah sokanon wunnekheuh.
E.44.14 He heweth him down cedars, and taketh the cypress and the oak, which he strengtheneth for himself among the trees of the forest: he planteth an ash, and the rain doth nourish it.

α.44.15 Neit pish ponamon: newutche na 8tinnumun, kah pish auwossu, nux wunnashqunánumun, kah apwau petukqunneg, nux, ayeuau manitto kah wowussumoh: ayeuau nunneukontunkoh, kah wunnauwaéhtauoh.
E.44.15 Then shall it be for a man to burn: for he will take thereof, and warm himself; yea, he kindleth it, and baketh bread; yea, he maketh a god, and worshippeth it; he maketh it a graven image, and falleth down thereto.

α.44.16 Nawhutche chikohsum n8taut, nashpe nawhutche meechu weyaus: app8sue app8su, kah wamep8h, nux, ouwassu, kah n8wau, kah nutáuwas, nunnaum n8teau.
E.44.16 He burneth part thereof in the fire; with part thereof he eateth flesh; he roasteth roast, and is satisfied: yea, he warmeth himself, and saith, Aha, I am warm, I have seen the fire:

α.44.17 Kah nawhutche um-manitt8hkon, wuttinneuhkontunkoh[;] wunnauwaéhtauoh, kah 8wowussumoh; peantamauoh kah n8wau, pohquohwusseh, newutche ken num-manitt8m.
E.44.17 And the residue thereof he maketh a god, even his graven image: he falleth down unto it, and worshippeth it, and prayeth unto it, and saith, Deliver me; for thou art my god.

α.44.18 Matta wahteau8og asuh wohtamwog: newutch yânunum wuskesukquash, nag matta woh naumoog, kah wuttah8oash, matta woh wohtam8mun8ash.
E.44.18 They have not known nor understood: for he hath shut their eyes, that they cannot see; and their hearts, that they cannot understand.

α.44.19 Kah mtta howan natwontam8 ut wuttahhut, kah matta wohwohtamóonk asuh wahteauonk ohteau n8wonat, nawhutche nutchikohsumun n8taut, nux wonk nuttittanapwon petukquinunk ut mukossáhtu, nutapwam weyaus kah nummechin, kah nawhutche woh nutayimun onkquontam8onk? sun woh nunnauwaéhtam mehtug.
E.44.19 And none considereth in his heart, neither is there knowledge nor understanding to say, I have burned part of it in the fire; yea, also I have baked bread upon the coals thereof; I have roasted flesh, and eaten it: and shall I make the residue thereof an abomination? shall I fall down to the stock of a tree?

α.44.20 Mechu pukquee: as8kekodteamwe metah wutamaunukqun, matta woh pohquohwhunóou ukketeahogkôunoh, asuh n8wóou, sunnummatta pann8waonganinn8 nuttinohkôunit?
E.44.20 He feedeth on ashes: a deceived heart hath turned him aside, that he cannot deliver his soul, nor say, Is there not a lie in my right hand?

α.44.21 Yeush mehquontash, (woi Jakob kah Israel) newutche ken nuttinninneum: kukkuhkenauwéhinup: ken nutinninneum, woi Israel, matta pish k8wanánumun8h.
E.44.21 Remember these, O Jacob and Israel; for thou art my servant: I have formed thee; thou art my servant: O Israel, thou shalt not be forgotten of me.

α.44.22 Nutjiskham kummatcheseongash onátuh kuhpogki matokqsit, kah onatuh ongquohqut kuppanneseongásh, qushkek en nuhhogkat, newutche kuppohquohwhunush.
E.44.22 I have blotted out, as a thick cloud, thy transgressions, and, as a cloud, thy sins: return unto me; for I have redeemed thee.

α.44.23 Ket8ham8k, woi kesukquog, newutche Jehovah ummahche ussen: mishont8wagk agwe ohkekontu: kuss8homunk, woi wadchuash, woi touohkomuk, kah nishnoh metug na ohtag, newutche Jehovah pohquohwhunau Jakoboh, kah sohsumwaheau wuhhogkuh ut Israelut.
E.44.23 Sing, O ye heavens; for the LORD hath done it: shout, ye lower parts of the earth: break forth into singing, ye mountains, O forest, and every tree therein: for the LORD hath redeemed Jacob, and glorified himself in Israel.

α.44.24 Yeu wussin Jehovah kummanouhuwaéneum, kah noh kahkenauwéhikquean wutch ôontomukqut, nen Jehovah noh ayik wame teanteaquassinish, noh nahse sepákinuk kesuk noh sepagenuk ohke, nusse[u]:
E.44.24 Thus saith the LORD, thy redeemer, and he that formed thee from the womb, I am the LORD that maketh all things; that stretcheth forth the heavens alone; that spreadeth abroad the earth by myself;

α.44.25 Noh mat toh ken tuppehteo8k ukkehkinneasuongan8 pann8waenuog: kah kogkeaheont pauwauwoh, noh quoshkeaheont waantamwoh, kah mattammagwutteunk 8wahteauongan8.
E.44.25 That frustrateth the tokens of the liars, and maketh diviners mad; that turneth wise men backward, and maketh their knowledge foolish;

α.44.26 Nóh manuhkehteunk wuttinn8waonk wuttinnúmoh, kah asit ukkuhqutteam8ongan8 wutann8naéneumoh, noh anont Jerusalem, ken pish wutohtuonk Judae keitotanash pish kutayeuwutteamw8, kah nuttahshinum mahchum8e ayeuongash.
E.44.26 That confirmeth the word of his servant, and performeth the counsel of his messengers; that saith to Jerusalem, Thou shalt be inhabited; and to the cities of Judah, Ye shall be built, and I will raise up the decayed places thereof:

α.44.27 Noh anont m8naiyeuoh, nunnappesish kah pish nunnunassum kussepeumash.
E.44.27 That saith to the deep, Be dry, and I will dry up thy rivers:

α.44.28 Noh anont papaume Cyrus, noh nunnanau shepsueneum kah pish pakodche ussen, wame nukkodtantamoonk, anont Jerusalem pish kutayeuit, kah Templeut, kukquenohtagom pish wunnushitteáuun.
E.44.28 That saith of Cyrus, He is my shepherd, and shall perform all my pleasure: even saying to Jerusalem, Thou shalt be built; and to the temple, Thy foundation shall be laid.

α.45.1 YEu wuttinnon Jehovah Cyruṣoh sasequnoncheh; wuttinohkou nuttinnumau sohkomunat wutohtimoneash ut anaquabit: kah nutompinim wussegan8ash tahs8tamwog, wohshinumunat ut anaquabit neesikkuphouune squontamash, kah sqúontamash matta pish kuphôsin8ash.
E.45.1 Thus saith the LORD to his anointed, to Cyrus, whose right hand I have holden, to subdue nations before him; and I will loose the loins of kings, to open before him the two leaved gates; and the gates shall not be shut;

α.45.2 Kenegonuhkouush, kah nussámpweteoh woonki ayeuongash, nussohquetahham wompohshogque squontamash, kàh nuppohshittahham moúhshogque pummetunkqshitteungash.
E.45.2 I will go before thee, and make the crooked places straight: I will break in pieces the gates of brass, and cut in sunder the bars of iron:

α.45.3 Káh kuttinnumoush pohkenae nompak8unash, kah adtahtoe w[é]nauwetuongash assampámukquehtu, onk woh k8wahteoh, nen Jehovah ne as8wenimuk, nen um-Manitt8moh Israel.
E.45.3 And I will give thee the treasures of darkness, and hidden riches of secret places, that thou mayest know that I, the LORD, which call thee by thy name, am the God of Israel.

α.45.4 Newutche Jakob nuttinneum kah Israel pepenauog, kuttehenush: kuttohtoe wesuonganuhkoush, tohkonogque matta k8wahein.
E.45.4 For Jacob my servant's sake, and Israel mine elect, I have even called thee by thy name: I have surnamed thee, though thou hast not known me.

α.45.5 Nen Jehovah kah matta onkatog, matta Manitt8un8h webe nen: kupputtugquabinuh tohkonogque mo k8wahein.
E.45.5 I am the LORD, and there is none else, there is no God beside me: I girded thee, though thou hast not known me:

α.45.6 Onk wutch wutchepwoiyeu kah wutcheksuiyeu woh wahteauog, matta onkatog qut webe nen, nen Jehovah kah matta onkatok.
E.45.6 That they may know from the rising of the sun, and from the west, that there is none beside me. I am the LORD, and there is none else.

α.45.7 Nukkuhkenauwehteop wequai kah nukkezteop pohkenai: n8nohteahuam, kah matchit nukkezteoh: nen Jehovah wame yeush nutussenash.
E.45.7 I form the light, and create darkness: I make peace, and create evil: I the LORD do all these things.

α.45.8 Padtippashunk, kenaau kesukquog wutch waabe, kah kesukquash sokenumohettich sampweusseonk: ohke wóhshwem8utch, kah paudtauehettich wadchanittuonk kah sampweusseonk moae sonkitch: nen Jehovah nukkezteauunah.
E.45.8 Drop down, ye heavens, from above, and let the skies pour down righteousness: let the earth open, and let them bring forth salvation, and let righteousness spring up together; I the LORD have created it.

α.45.9 Missi wutonkapunaonk noh mekonont kezhikqutcheh: kodchuhkishq mekontaj ohkee kodchuhkishq: sun woh man8nsk unnau neh kahkenauehhikqutcheh, teag kutayim? asuh kutanakausuonk, matta wunnutcheeu?
E.45.9 Woe unto him that striveth with his Maker! Let the potsherd strive with the potsherds of the earth. Shall the clay say to him that fashioneth it, What makest thou? or thy work, He hath no hands?

α.45.10 Missi wutonkapunaonk noh anont 8shoh teaguas k8naumoni? asuh mittamwussissoh, teaguas keneecham:
E.45.10 Woe unto him that saith unto his father, What begettest thou? or to the woman, What hast thou brought forth?

α.45.11 Yeu wussin Jeh[ó]vah 8neetupan[a]tam8moh Israel, kah kezhukqutch[é]h, nat8tomah papaume nish pish anagish, papaume nunnaumonuh, kah papaume nunnutchegane ánakausuonk, ann8negk.
E.45.11 Thus saith the LORD, the Holy One of Israel, and his Maker, Ask me of things to come concerning my sons, and concerning the work of my hands command ye me.

α.45.12 Nutayimup ohke, kah nukkezheap wosketomp na$ut: nen nunnutcheg sepagunumup kesukquash kah wame ne kenauwameonk nutann8tamun.
E.45.12 I have made the earth, and created man upon it: I, even my hands, have stretched out the heavens, and all their host have I commanded.

α.45.13 Nutomohkinumauup ut wunnomwausseonganit, kah nussampweteoh wame ummayásh: noh pish ayim nukkeitotan, kah noh pish moncheaheau nummissinomon, matta unnoadtuut asuh onkquatunkanit, n8wau Jehovah ayeuteaunit.
E.45.13 I have raised him up in righteousness, and I will direct all his ways: he shall build my city, and he shall let go my captives, not for price nor reward, saith the LORD of hosts.

α.45.14 Yeu wussin Jehovah, wutanakausuonk Egypté wutan[á]qushaongash Ethiopia kah Sabeansog, qunuhqussuenuog pish kuppeyaonukquog, kah kuttaiheog, nag pish kutassuhkungquog, kah nashpe chainsash, nag pish quṣhkodteaog: kah nag pish kenauwaehtunkquog, pish k8wehquetumunkquog, n8waog wunnamuhkut God kutapehtunk, kah matta onkatog, matta Manitt8[un]8.
E.45.14 Thus saith the LORD, The labour of Egypt, and merchandise of Ethiopia and of the Sabeans, men of stature, shall come over unto thee, and they shall be thine: they shall come after thee; in chains they shall come over, and they shall fall down unto thee, they shall make supplication unto thee, saying, Surely God is in thee; and there is none else, there is no God.

α.45.15 Wunnamuhkut ken Manit padtogquean, woi Israelle Manit, wadchanuwaenin.
E.45.15 Verily thou art a God that hidest thyself, O God of Israel, the Saviour.

α.45.16 Nag pish akodchuog, kah nag wame wonk pish quehquenauanumoog, nag pish moaeu naswaiyeuog neg ayeuoncheg nunneukontunkoh.
E.45.16 They shall be ashamed, and also confounded, all of them: they shall go to confusion together that are makers of idols.

α.45.17 Qut Israel pish wadchanau ut Jehovahut nashpe michemohtae wadchanittuonk, matta pish kutakodchu, asuh kukkuhquenauanum8h yeoyatche.
E.45.17 But Israel shall be saved in the LORD with an everlasting salvation: ye shall not be ashamed nor confounded world without end.

α.45.18 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah noh kezteunk kesukquash, God nagum nehenwonche noh kuhkenauwehteunkup ohke, kah kezteunkup, ummenuhkehteáuun, matta táhn8che ukkezteaúouun, wuttinuk|kezteauun wutohkineat, nen Jehovah kah matta onkatok.
E.45.18 For thus saith the LORD that created the heavens; God himself that formed the earth and made it; he hath established it, he created it not in vain, he formed it to be inhabited: I am the LORD; and there is none else.

α.45.19 Matta nukkeme eyin, ut pohkenaiyeue ayeuonkanit ohkéit: matta nuttinnoh 8skannemuneoh Jakob, tahn8che natinneahwhegk: nen Jehovah sampweusseonk nussim, n8wahteauwahuwam nish sampwagish.
E.45.19 I have not spoken in secret, in a dark place of the earth: I said not unto the seed of Jacob, Seek ye me in vain: I the LORD speak righteousness, I declare things that are right.

α.45.20 Miyaek, kah peyunk moae pas8tshagk, kenau pohquohhamogish ut [vv]utohtimoneat nag matta wahteauunganaeog, neg wanohtunkig nunneukontungane mehtug, kah wowussumaog Manitto neh woh mo wadchanuwanegeh.
E.45.20 Assemble yourselves and come; draw near together, ye that are escaped of the nations: they have no knowledge that set up the wood of their graven image, and pray unto a god that cannot save.

α.45.21 Unnok pas8tshan8k, nux miyae kogahq[ú]ttehettich: howan yeu wahteauwahuwon wutch n8wadt? sunnummatta nen Jehovah? kah na matta Manitt8un8 webe nen sampwu Manit, kah wadchanuwaenin, matta onkatuk webe nen.
E.45.21 Tell ye, and bring them near; yea, let them take counsel together: who hath declared this from ancient time? who hath told it from that time?  have not I the LORD? and there is no God else beside me; a just God and a Saviour; there is none beside me.

α.45.22 Monunnéiegk, kah wadchanitteagk, wame kenaau wehqshit ohke, newutch[é] nen God, kah matta wonk howan.
E.45.22 Look unto me, and be ye saved, all the ends of the earth: for I am God, and there is none else.

α.45.23 Nutchad[c]h[e]keyeuwop nashpe nen, nuttinn8waonk sohham8m8 wutch nutt8nut ut sampweyeuong[a]nit kah matta pish qushkemun8ash, onk woh nish$noh mukkuttuk nunnauwaehtunk, kah nish$noh meenan pish nutchadchekeimuk.
E.45.23 I have sworn by myself, the word is gone out of my mouth in righteousness, and shall not return, That unto me every knee shall bow, every tongue shall swear.

α.45.24 Pish pásuk n8wau wunnamuhkut, ut Jehova[ú]t n8nomwausseonk, k[á]h nummenuhkesuonk ohteau: noh$ut pish wosketompáog peyoneau, k[a]h wame neg musq[ú]anumonch[e]g pish akod[c]huog.
E.45.24 Surely, shall one say, in the LORD have I righteousness and strength: even to him shall men come; and all that are incensed against him shall be ashamed.

α.45.25 Ut Jehovah$ut wame Israelle wuskannem pish sampweogquanittamun, kah pish waeenowaog.
E.45.25 In the LORD shall all the seed of Israel be justified, and shall glory.

α.46.1 BEL nauwaeu, Nebo nauwôsu, wuttinn[é]ukontunk[a]nouh woskeche puppinashimwut, ka[h] nee[t]asuut: k8weanunn8ash tuhkekomeechummuash, neg tuhkequane weanun sauunum8e puppinashimwut.
E.46.1 Bel boweth down, Nebo stoopeth, their idols were upon the beasts, and upon the cattle: your carriages were heavy loaden; they are a burden to the weary beast.

α.46.2 Nauwoseog, nauwaeog moaeu, matta pohquohwuttauoog weanun, qut nag nehenwonche missinohkonunk.
E.46.2 They stoop, they bow down together; they could not deliver the burden, but themselves are gone into captivity.

α.46.3 N8tiek woi Jakob week, k[à]h wame sequttahwhutcheg wekit Israel, neg konunutcheg wutch munnogkussit, kah tahshinutcheg wutch ôontomukqut.
E.46.3 Hearken unto me, O house of Jacob, and all the remnant of the house of Israel, which are borne by me from the belly, which are carried from the womb:

α.46.4 Kah pajeh kukkehchiyeuunneaout, nen nnoh, kah pajeh wompoquonat kukkinnunnumw8: nukkezteop, kah kutashinnumw8 kah kukkinnunumw8, kah kuppohquohwhununumw8.
E.46.4 And even to your old age I am he; and even to hoar hairs will I carry you: I have made, and I will bear; even I will carry, and will deliver you.

α.46.5 Howan kuttatupanumimw8, kah keananumimw8, kah kuttatupinomw8, onk woh nutogqueneunkqussin?
E.46.5 To whom will ye liken me, and make me equal, and compare me, that we may be like?

α.46.6 Mahtshadtoog Gold wutch munn8tadt kah quttompagh8teog silver ut quthompak8teganit, kah ann8naog gold$smithoh, kah um-Manitt8hkou, neg penushaog, kah wowussummuwaog.
E.46.6 They lavish gold out of the bag, and weigh silver in the balance, and hire a goldsmith; and he maketh it a god: they fall down, yea, they worship.

α.46.7 Wuttahshinouh ut wuttugkeout, ukkenunnouh, upponouh ut wutayeuonganit, kah neepau: wutch wutayeuonganit matta pish ontappu: nux pasuk pish ummauunnitteauoh, qut matta woh wunnamp8hamunk8oh, kah matta 8wadchanuk8oh wutch 8tamehpunnaonganit.
E.46.7 They bear him upon the shoulder, they carry him, and set him in his place, and he standeth; from his place shall he not remove: yea, one shall cry unto him, yet can he not answer, nor save him out of his trouble.

α.46.8 Yeu mehquontam8k, kah nahtitteagk k8skeetompoongan8: wonk mehquontamwahuwagk, woi kenaau panneusséógish.
E.46.8 Remember this, and shew yourselves men: bring it again to mind, O ye transgressors.

α.46.9 Mehquontam8k nish n8adt anagkupash, newutche nen God, kah matta onkatog, nen God, kah matta howan nean[é]yeuw8.
E.46.9 Remember the former things of old: for I am God, and there is none else; I am God, and there is none like me,

α.46.10 Wahteauwahuwáan wohkukquoshik waj kutchishik, kah wutch n8wadt, nish asquam anán8gish, an8waon, nukkogahk8waonk pish menuhkohteau, kah pish nutussen wame nean tapeneam.
E.46.10 Declaring the end from the beginning, and from ancient times the things that are not yet done, saying, My counsel shall stand, and I will do all my pleasure:

α.46.11 N8wehkom mahchipp8áe psukses wutch wutchepwoiyeu, wosketomp noh kezteunk ne pakodtantam, wutch noadtit wutohtimóneat: nux nussinneap, kah wonk pish n[u]tussen, nuppogkodtantamunap, kah wonk nutussen.
E.46.11 Calling a ravenous bird from the east, the man that executeth my counsel from a far country: yea, I have spoken it, I will also bring it to pass; I have purposed it, I will also do it.

α.46.12 N8tiek manuhkitteahô[ó]gish, nô8sukómógish wunn[o]mw[a]usseonk.
E.46.12 Hearken unto me, ye stouthearted, that are far from righteousness:

α.46.13 Nuppas8chewuttoh n8nomwausseonk: matta pish nôadtit ahtano, kah n8wadchanuwaonk matta pish pahtsúmun8, kah n8nohto wadchanittuonk ut Zion wutche Israel nussohsumoonk.
E.46.13 I bring near my righteousness; it shall not be far off, and my salvation shall not tarry: and I will place salvation in Zion for Israel my glory.

α.47.1 NOOkish kah apsh puppissiyeuut: woi penomp Babilone wuttaunin, apsh ohkeit: wanne t[a]hs8tamoe appuonganinno woi Caldeanse wuttaunin: newutche matta pish wonk kuttéhennitteoh kehkéchumwit kah mam[a]ttanumwit.
E.47.1 Come down, and sit in the dust, O virgin daughter of Babylon, sit on the ground: there is no throne, O daughter of the Chaldeans: for thou shalt no more be called tender and delicate.

α.47.2 Nemunush toguhwóngan[ó]mp[u]sk, kah n8khikanehteaush, wohshinush kummeesunk, poskis kuhkont, poskinush kehquau, qushkodteash seipu[a]sh.
E.47.2 Take the millstones, and grind meal: uncover thy locks, make bare the leg, uncover the thigh, pass over the rivers.

α.47.3 Kukkôussuonk pish wohshwohteau, nux kutakodchuonk pish naumun, kuttann8toush, matta kutogque nogkuṣhauun8 wosketompaut.
E.47.3 Thy nakedness shall be uncovered, yea, thy shame shall be seen: I will take vengeance, and I will not meet thee as a man.

α.47.4 Numman8whunnuaéneum, Jehovah ut ayeuteaunit, ne 8wesuonk, 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
E.47.4 As for our redeemer, the LORD of hosts is his name, the Holy One of Israel.

α.47.5 Chequnapsh, âush pohkenaiyeuut, woi Caldeanse wutta[u]nin: newutche matta pish wonk kutehennitteoh, ass8tam8e sonksq
E.47.5 Sit thou silent, and get thee into darkness, O daughter of the Chaldeans: for thou shalt no more be called, The lady of kingdoms.

α.47.6 Numm8squanum nummissinninnúmog? nunnishketeoh nutohtoonk, kah neg nummagununk en kenutcheganit: matta kummonanumoog, ut kutchisetu tuhkéque yoak kuppon.
E.47.6 I was wroth with my people, I have polluted mine inheritance, and given them into thine hand: thou didst shew them no mercy; upon the ancient hast thou very heavily laid thy yoke.

α.47.7 Kah kussip, pish nummicheme sonksquau: newaj matta yeush ponam8an kuttahhut, kah matta kummehquontamoh ogkomáe ônag.
E.47.7 And thou saidst, I shall be a lady for ever: so that thou didst not lay these things to thy heart, neither didst remember the latter end of it.

α.47.8 Newutche yeu n8tash n8sukog weekontam8ongash, kah mat toh hentupánatamwée ayig: kussim ut kuttahhut, nen, kah matta howan w[e]be nen, matta pish nussekousquaappu, kah matta pish n8wahteo8h wannehteaonk mukkiesog.
E.47.8 Therefore hear now this, thou that art given to pleasures, that dwellest carelessly, that sayest in thine heart, I am, and none else beside me; I shall not sit as a widow, neither shall I know the loss of children:

α.47.9 Qut yeush nesinash pish kénuppe kuppeyogqunash, pasuk kesukod: wanneheaonk mukkiog, kah sekousquaonk: nish pish papannuppe kenuhkuhkongqunash, wutche mataanukish kuppauwauongash, kah wutche kumm8cheke moneetue usseongash.
E.47.9 But these two things shall come to thee in a moment in one day, the loss of children, and widowhood: they shall come upon thee in their perfection for the multitude of thy sorceries, and for the great abundance of thine enchantments.

α.47.10 Newutche kuppabuhtantam kummatcheseonk, kussip, matta howan nunnogk8, k8waantam8onk kah k8wahteauonk k8wounkhik, kah kussip, ut kuttahhut, nen, kah matt[a] onkatuk webe nen.
E.47.10 For thou hast trusted in thy wickedness: thou hast said, None seeth me. Thy wisdom and thy knowledge, it hath perverted thee; and thou hast said in thine heart, I am, and none else beside me.

α.47.11 Newaj machuk nuhkuhkongquean, mata pish k8wahteoh uttoh waj tahsheem8uk: kah woskeetuonk pish kenuhkuhkunk, kah matta pish kuttapenum8un kutamaunumunat: kah touushin tean[ú]k pish kenuhkuhkunk, ne matta pish wahteauouan,
E.47.11 Therefore shall evil come upon thee; thou shalt not know from whence it riseth: and mischief shall fall upon thee; thou shalt not be able to put it off: and desolation shall come upon thee suddenly, which thou shalt not know.

α.47.12 Eyeu nepaush nashpe kuppauwa[u]ongash, kah mataane[k] kummonetuonk, uttoh adt anakausean wutch k8ske[m]unneat, tapenuman kah so[h]koman.
E.47.12 Stand now with thine enchantments, and with the multitude of thy sorceries, wherein thou hast laboured from thy youth; if so be thou shalt be able to profit, if so be thou mayest prevail.

α.47.13 Kussauunum nashpe mataanukish kukkog[a]hquttuongash: Astrologersog, wauwacheg ut anogqsut, kah nepauzsae mashogig, neepauwehettich, kah nag wadchanuk8k wutch yeush pish nuhkuhkongqueogish.
E.47.13 Thou art wearied in the multitude of thy counsels. Let now the astrologers, the stargazers, the monthly prognosticators, stand up, and save thee from these things that shall come upon thee.

α.47.14 Kusseh, neg pish tatuppeyeu8og sequekepuneganit: n8teau pish nah wutchikohsoh, nag matta pish pohquohwhunau8og wuhhogkauh wutch menuhke n8n8naut: na matta mohkussaun8 kutauwossinneat, asuh n8tau apinneat anaquohtag.
E.47.14 Behold, they shall be as stubble; the fire shall burn them; they shall not deliver themselves from the power of the flame: there shall not be a coal to warm at, nor fire to sit before it.

α.47.15 Yeu pish wuttatuppeyeuunneau, neg weetanakausumacheg, kutanaqu[s]haeneumog wutch k8skenuuneat, nag pish nanwiyeuog nish$noh pasuk ut wutayeuonganit, matta howan pish k8wadchanuk8h.
E.47.15 Thus shall they be unto thee with whom thou hast laboured, even thy merchants, from thy youth: they shall wander every one to his quarter; none shall save thee.

α.48.1 YEU n8tam8k woi Jakob wek, neg ahenutcheg 8wesuonk Israel, kah neg wutch sohhogig Judae nippekontu, neg chadchekeyeuwacheg nashpe 8wesuonk Jehovah, kah mâs[a]whoncheg 8wesuonk um-Manitt8moh Israel, qut matta wunnamuhkuteyeuut asuh sampwesuonganit.
E.48.1 Hear ye this, O house of Jacob, which are called by the name of Israel, and are come forth out of the waters of Judah, which swear by the name of the LORD, and make mention of the God of Israel, but not in truth, nor in righteousness.

α.48.2 Newutche nag hennaog wuhhogkauh wutch wunnetupanatamwe otanat, kah quensinwog um-Manitt8moh Israel, Jehovah ayeuteanit ne 8wesuonk.
E.48.2 For they call themselves of the holy city, and stay themselves upon the God of Israel; The LORD of hosts is his name.

α.48.3 N8wahteauwahuwam négonne ânagish wutch waj|kutchissik, kah yeush sohham8m8ash wutch nutt8nut, kah nish nunnahtukonash: nukkenuppe ussenash, kah n$niyeupash.
E.48.3 I have declared the former things from the beginning; and they went forth out of my mouth, and I shewed them; I did them suddenly, and they came to pass.

α.48.4 Newutche n8wahteop kussiogkus, kah kussittipuk moohshog kutchoht, kah kushkodtuk wompohshag.
E.48.4 Because I knew that thou art obstinate, and thy neck is an iron sinew, and thy brow brass;

α.48.5 Waj kutchissik k8wahteauwahunun, asquam anan8g, kenahtinununah: ishkont woh kussim, nuttinneukontunk yeu wutussen, kah nukkogkoksumwe kah sabassumwe nunnúkontunk, nah wutann8nuh
E.48.5 I have even from the beginning declared it to thee; before it came to pass I shewed it thee: lest thou shouldest say, Mine idol hath done them, and my graven image, and my molten image, hath commanded them.

α.48.6 Ken8tamup, wame yeu, naish, kah sunnummatta k8wahteauwahuaneau? kenahtinush wuske teagwahsinish yeu$wutch, adtuhtosikish kah matta k8wahteau8unapash.
E.48.6 Thou hast heard, see all this; and will not ye declare it? I have shewed thee new things from this time, even hidden things, and thou didst not know them.

α.48.7 Nish yeuyeu kezteauunash, qut matta waj kutchissik negonae kesukod asquam n8tam8an ishkont woh kussim, kusseh nish n8wahteauunash,
E.48.7 They are created now, and not from the beginning; even before the day when thou heardest them not; lest thou shouldest say, Behold, I knew them.

α.48.8 Nux, matta ken8tam8, nux, matta k8wahteou, nux wutch na ahquompag kehtauog matta wohshinum8muk: newutch n8wahteoh, woh ahche k8nass8muwae ussem, & kuttehenit panneseaenin wutch ôontomukqut.
E.48.8 Yea, thou heardest not; yea, thou knewest not; yea, from that time that thine ear was not opened: for I knew that thou wouldest deal very treacherously, and wast called a transgressor from the womb.

α.48.9 Wutche n8wesuonk nutassanumun nummusquantamoonk: kah wutch n8woweenomitteaonk, kummukk8naush, ishkont kuttummeswush.
E.48.9 For my name's sake will I defer mine anger, and for my praise will I refrain for thee, that I cut thee not off.

α.48.10 Kusseh, kuppahkhesh, qut matt[a] nashpe silver, kuppepe[n]aush ut sabassumwe onkapunnaonganit.
E.48.10 Behold, I have refined thee, but not with silver; I have chosen thee in the furnace of affliction.

α.48.11 Wutche nen nehenwonche, nux wutche nen nehenwonche pish nutussen: newutche u[t]toh woh n8wesuonk nishketeauun? kah m[á]tta howan nuttinnumauoh nussohsumoonk.
E.48.11 For mine own sake, even for mine own sake, will I do it: for how should my name be polluted? and I will not give my glory unto another.

α.48.12 N8tah woi Jakob, kah Israel n8wehkumog: nen n$noh nen negonne, nen wonk maumachish.
E.48.12 Hearken unto me, O Jacob and Israel, my called; I am he; I am the first, I also am the last.

α.48.13 Nunnutcheg wonk wunohtau quenohtag ohke, kah nuttinnohkou qutomskinnau kesukquash; nag wehkumog moae neepoog
E.48.13 Mine hand also hath laid the foundation of the earth, and my right hand hath spanned the heavens: when I call unto them, they stand up together.

α.48.14 Wame kenaau moegk kah n8tam8k, howan kenugke nagoh yeush wahteauwáhuwachish? Jehovah 8womonuh: pish ussu wuttenantam8onk ut Babilon, kah wuhpit pish nuhkuhkauau Caldeansoh.
E.48.14 All ye, assemble yourselves, and hear; which among them hath declared these things? The LORD hath loved him: he will do his pleasure on Babylon, and his arm shall be on the Chaldeans.

α.48.15 Nen nen Nussin, nux n8wehkom: nuppas8, kah pish wutchayeuhteau ummay.
E.48.15 I, even I, have spoken; yea, I have called him: I have brought him, and he shall make his way prosperous.

α.48.16 Pas8sukiek, yeu n8tam8k, matta nukkeme eyin wutch waj|kutchissik, wutch na ahquompak ne ânag, na nen, kah eyeu Lord Jehovah, kah wunnashauanitt8moh nutann8nuk.
E.48.16 Come ye near unto me, hear ye this; I have not spoken in secret from the beginning; from the time that it was, there am I: and now the Lord GOD, and his Spirit, hath sent me.

α.48.17 Yeu wussin Jehovah kummanouhuwaeneum, 8neetupanatam8moh Isra[a]l, nen Jehovah kum$Manitt8m, noh kohk8tomungquean k8chiinneat, noh sagkompagunukquean en mayut ut$toh woh aóan.
E.48.17 Thus saith the LORD, thy Redeemer, the Holy One of Israel; I am the LORD thy God which teacheth thee to profit, which leadeth thee by the way that thou shouldest go.

α.48.18 Woi n8tamas nutann8team8ongash! neit k8nohteaonk woh tatuppeyeu8 sepuut, kah k8nomwausseonk onatuh ketahhanne tukk8ut.
E.48.18 O that thou hadst hearkened to my commandments! then had thy peace been as a river, and thy righteousness as the waves of the sea:

α.48.19 K8skannemuneunk wonk woh tatuppeyeu8og naguntu; kah k8nogkusseeu ontseonk onatuhyeu8 mamossompsquehtu: 8wesuonk woh matta tummussum8un, asuh pagwotoouun wutch anaquabeh.
E.48.19 Thy seed also had been as the sand, and the offspring of thy bowels like the gravel thereof; his name should not have been cut off nor destroyed from before me.

α.48.20 Sohham8k Babilon: wussem8k wutch Caldeansog nashpe ket8homae wadtautaonkqussuonk, wahteauwahuwak, yeu n8wak, unn8wak adt wehqshit ohken8wagk Jehovah man8whau wuttinnumoh Jakoboh.
E.48.20 Go ye forth of Babylon, flee ye from the Chaldeans, with a voice of singing declare ye, tell this, utter it even to the end of the earth; say ye, The LORD hath redeemed his servant Jacob.

α.48.21 Kah nag matta kuhkutt8n8og pamuwunont touohkomukquash: wussohwhutchuw[a]nehkauoh nippe wutch qussukquanit, pasehtham wonk qussuk, kah nippe sohwhutchuan.
E.48.21 And they thirsted not when he led them through the deserts: he caused the waters to flow out of the rock for them: he clave the rock also, and the waters gushed out.

α.48.22 Na matta wunohteaonganinn8, n8wau Jehovah, matcheetunutcheh.
E.48.22 There is no peace, saith the LORD, unto the wicked.

α.49.1 KUhkehtiegk woi munnáhannog, kah n8tiek woi missinninnuog wutch n8adtut, Jehovah n8wehkomuk wutch ôontomukqut, wutch wunnogkussit nokas missohham n8wesuonk.
E.49.1 Listen, O isles, unto me; and hearken, ye people, from far; The LORD hath called me from the womb; from the bowels of my mother hath he made mention of my name.

α.49.2 Kah ogquehteau nutt8n kenu togkodteg, ut wunnuppawhunne onkóohtómut nutadtahshik, kah nutayimunk kussenausue kôuhquod: ut uppetauwónut nutadtahshik.
E.49.2 And he hath made my mouth like a sharp sword; in the shadow of his hand hath he hid me, and made me a polished shaft; in his quiver hath he hid me;

α.49.3 Kah nuttinuk, ken nuttinninneum woi Israel, ut kuhhogkat sohsumm8w[ô]nit.
E.49.3 And said unto me, Thou art my servant, O Israel, in whom I will be glorified.

α.49.4 Neit nussip, tahn8tanakausip, nummohtshadtoh nummenuhkesuonk wutche monteag, kah tahn8che, wunnamuhkut n8sumitteaonk ohteau ut Jehovah, kah nutanakausuonk weechayeumukqun num-Manitt8m.
E.49.4 Then I said, I have laboured in vain, I have spent my strength for nought, and in vain: yet surely my judgment is with the LORD, and my work with my God.

α.49.5 Kah eyeu, n8wau Jehovah noh kahkénauwéhit wutch ôontomukqut 8tinninnúmuneat, wonk uppaudtauónat Jakoboh: tókónogque Israel matta môunnôun, qut onch pish nussohsum ut wuskesukqut Jehovah, kah num-Manitt8m pish n8menuhkesuonkanin.
E.49.5 And now, saith the LORD that formed me from the womb to be his servant, to bring Jacob again to him, Though Israel be not gathered, yet shall I be glorious in the eyes of the LORD, and my God shall be my strength.

α.49.6 
E.49.6 And he said, It is a light thing that thou shouldest be my servant to raise up the tribes of Jacob, and to restore the preserved of Israel: I will also give thee for a light to the Gentiles, that thou mayest be my salvation unto the end of the earth.

α.49.7 
E.49.7 Thus saith the LORD, the Redeemer of Israel, and his Holy One, to him whom man despiseth, to him whom the nation abhorreth, to a servant of rulers, Kings shall see and arise, princes also shall worship, because of the LORD that is faithful, and the Holy One of Israel, and he shall choose thee.

α.49.8 
E.49.8 Thus saith the LORD, In an acceptable time have I heard thee, and in a day of salvation have I helped thee: and I will preserve thee, and give thee for a covenant of the people, to establish the earth, to cause to inherit the desolate heritages;

α.49.9 
E.49.9 That thou mayest say to the prisoners, Go forth; to them that are in darkness, Shew yourselves. They shall feed in the ways, and their pastures shall be in all high places.

α.49.10 
E.49.10 They shall not hunger nor thirst; neither shall the heat nor sun smite them: for he that hath mercy on them shall lead them, even by the springs of water shall he guide them.

α.49.11 
E.49.11 And I will make all my mountains a way, and my highways shall be exalted.

α.49.12 
E.49.12 Behold, these shall come from far: and, lo, these from the north and from the west; and these from the land of Sinim.

α.49.13 
E.49.13 Sing, O heavens; and be joyful, O earth; and break forth into singing, O mountains: for the LORD hath comforted his people, and will have mercy upon his afflicted.

α.49.14 
E.49.14 But Zion said, The LORD hath forsaken me, and my Lord hath forgotten me.

α.49.15 
E.49.15 Can a woman forget her sucking child, that she should not have compassion on the son of her womb? yea, they may forget, yet will I not forget thee.

α.49.16 
E.49.16 Behold, I have graven thee upon the palms of my hands; thy walls are continually before me.

α.49.17 
E.49.17 Thy children shall make haste; thy destroyers and they that made thee waste shall go forth of thee.

α.49.18 
E.49.18 Lift up thine eyes round about, and behold: all these gather themselves together, and come to thee. As I live, saith the LORD, thou shalt surely clothe thee with them all, as with an ornament, and bind them on thee, as a bride doeth.

α.49.19 
E.49.19 For thy waste and thy desolate places, and the land of thy destruction, shall even now be too narrow by reason of the inhabitants, and they that swallowed thee up shall be far away.

α.49.20 
E.49.20 The children which thou shalt have, after thou hast lost the other, shall say again in thine ears, The place is too strait for me: give place to me that I may dwell.

α.49.21 
E.49.21 Then shalt thou say in thine heart, Who hath begotten me these, seeing I have lost my children, and am desolate, a captive, and removing to and fro? and who hath brought up these? Behold, I was left alone; these, where had they been?

α.49.22 
E.49.22 Thus saith the Lord GOD, Behold, I will lift up mine hand to the Gentiles, and set up my standard to the people: and they shall bring thy sons in their arms, and thy daughters shall be carried upon their shoulders.

α.49.23 
E.49.23 And kings shall be thy nursing fathers, and their queens thy nursing mothers: they shall bow down to thee with their face toward the earth, and lick up the dust of thy feet; and thou shalt know that I am the LORD: for they shall not be ashamed that wait for me.

α.49.24 
E.49.24 Shall the prey be taken from the mighty, or the lawful captive delivered?

α.49.25 
E.49.25 But thus saith the LORD, Even the captives of the mighty shall be taken away, and the prey of the terrible shall be delivered: for I will contend with him that contendeth with thee, and I will save thy children.

α.49.26 
E.49.26 And I will feed them that oppress thee with their own flesh; and they shall be drunken with their own blood, as with sweet wine: and all flesh shall know that I the LORD am thy Saviour and thy Redeemer, the mighty One of Jacob.

α.50.1 
E.50.1 Thus saith the LORD, Where is the bill of your mother's divorcement, whom I have put away? or which of my creditors is it to whom I have sold you?  Behold, for your iniquities have ye sold yourselves, and for your transgressions is your mother put away.

α.50.2 
E.50.2 Wherefore, when I came, was there no man? when I called, was there none to answer? Is my hand shortened at all, that it cannot redeem? or have I no power to deliver? behold, at my rebuke I dry up the sea, I make the rivers a wilderness: their fish stinketh, because there is no water, and dieth for thirst.

α.50.3 
E.50.3 I clothe the heavens with blackness, and I make sackcloth their covering.

α.50.4 
E.50.4 The Lord GOD hath given me the tongue of the learned, that I should know how to speak a word in season to him that is weary: he wakeneth morning by morning, he wakeneth mine ear to hear as the learned.

α.50.5 
E.50.5 The Lord GOD hath opened mine ear, and I was not rebellious, neither turned away back.

α.50.6 
E.50.6 I gave my back to the smiters, and my cheeks to them that plucked off the hair: I hid not my face from shame and spitting.

α.50.7 
E.50.7 For the Lord GOD will help me; therefore shall I not be confounded: therefore have I set my face like a flint, and I know that I shall not be ashamed.

α.50.8 
E.50.8 He is near that justifieth me; who will contend with me? let us stand together: who is mine adversary? let him come near to me.

α.50.9 
E.50.9 Behold, the Lord GOD will help me; who is he that shall condemn me?  lo, they all shall wax old as a garment; the moth shall eat them up.

α.50.10 
E.50.10 Who is among you that feareth the LORD, that obeyeth the voice of his servant, that walketh in darkness, and hath no light? let him trust in the name of the LORD, and stay upon his God.

α.50.11
