E.50.11 Behold, all ye that kindle a fire, that compass yourselves about with sparks: walk in the light of your fire, and in the sparks that ye have kindled. This shall ye have of mine hand; ye shall lie down in sorrow.

α.51.1 
E.51.1 Hearken to me, ye that follow after righteousness, ye that seek the LORD: look unto the rock whence ye are hewn, and to the hole of the pit whence ye are digged.

α.51.2 
E.51.2 Look unto Abraham your father, and unto Sarah that bare you: for I called him alone, and blessed him, and increased him.

α.51.3 
E.51.3 For the LORD shall comfort Zion: he will comfort all her waste places; and he will make her wilderness like Eden, and her desert like the garden of the LORD; joy and gladness shall be found therein, thanksgiving, and the voice of melody.

α.51.4 
E.51.4 Hearken unto me, my people; and give ear unto me, O my nation: for a law shall proceed from me, and I will make my judgment to rest for a light of the people.

α.51.5 
E.51.5 My righteousness is near; my salvation is gone forth, and mine arms shall judge the people; the isles shall wait upon me, and on mine arm shall they trust.

α.51.6 
E.51.6 Lift up your eyes to the heavens, and look upon the earth beneath: for the heavens shall vanish away like smoke, and the earth shall wax old like a garment, and they that dwell therein shall die in like manner: but my salvation shall be for ever, and my righteousness shall not be abolished.

α.51.7 
E.51.7 Hearken unto me, ye that know righteousness, the people in whose heart is my law; fear ye not the reproach of men, neither be ye afraid of their revilings.

α.51.8 
E.51.8 For the moth shall eat them up like a garment, and the worm shall eat them like wool: but my righteousness shall be for ever, and my salvation from generation to generation.

α.51.9 
E.51.9 Awake, awake, put on strength, O arm of the LORD; awake, as in the ancient days, in the generations of old. Art thou not it that hath cut Rahab, and wounded the dragon?

α.51.10 
E.51.10 Art thou not it which hath dried the sea, the waters of the great deep; that hath made the depths of the sea a way for the ransomed to pass over?

α.51.11 
E.51.11 Therefore the redeemed of the LORD shall return, and come with singing unto Zion; and everlasting joy shall be upon their head: they shall obtain gladness and joy; and sorrow and mourning shall flee away.

α.51.12 
E.51.12 I, even I, am he that comforteth you: who art thou, that thou shouldest be afraid of a man that shall die, and of the son of man which shall be made as grass;

α.51.13 
E.51.13 And forgettest the LORD thy maker, that hath stretched forth the heavens, and laid the foundations of the earth; and hast feared continually every day because of the fury of the oppressor, as if he were ready to destroy? and where is the fury of the oppressor?

α.51.14 
E.51.14 The captive exile hasteneth that he may be loosed, and that he should not die in the pit, nor that his bread should fail.

α.51.15 
E.51.15 But I am the LORD thy God, that divided the sea, whose waves roared: The LORD of hosts is his name.

α.51.16 
E.51.16 And I have put my words in thy mouth, and I have covered thee in the shadow of mine hand, that I may plant the heavens, and lay the foundations of the earth, and say unto Zion, Thou art my people.

α.51.17 
E.51.17 Awake, awake, stand up, O Jerusalem, which hast drunk at the hand of the LORD the cup of his fury; thou hast drunken the dregs of the cup of trembling, and wrung them out.

α.51.18 
E.51.18 There is none to guide her among all the sons whom she hath brought forth; neither is there any that taketh her by the hand of all the sons that she hath brought up.

α.51.19 
E.51.19 These two things are come unto thee; who shall be sorry for thee?  desolation, and destruction, and the famine, and the sword: by whom shall I comfort thee?

α.51.20 
E.51.20 Thy sons have fainted, they lie at the head of all the streets, as a wild bull in a net: they are full of the fury of the LORD, the rebuke of thy God.

α.51.21 
E.51.21 Therefore hear now this, thou afflicted, and drunken, but not with wine:

α.51.22 
E.51.22 Thus saith thy Lord the LORD, and thy God that pleadeth the cause of his people, Behold, I have taken out of thine hand the cup of trembling, even the dregs of the cup of my fury; thou shalt no more drink it again:

α.51.23 
E.51.23 But I will put it into the hand of them that afflict thee; which have said to thy soul, Bow down, that we may go over: and thou hast laid thy body as the ground, and as the street, to them that went over.

α.52.1 
E.52.1 Awake, awake; put on thy strength, O Zion; put on thy beautiful garments, O Jerusalem, the holy city: for henceforth there shall no more come into thee the uncircumcised and the unclean.

α.52.2 
E.52.2 Shake thyself from the dust; arise, and sit down, O Jerusalem: loose thyself from the bands of thy neck, O captive daughter of Zion.

α.52.3 
E.52.3 For thus saith the LORD, Ye have sold yourselves for nought; and ye shall be redeemed without money.

α.52.4 
E.52.4 For thus saith the Lord GOD, My people went down aforetime into Egypt to sojourn there; and the Assyrian oppressed them without cause.

α.52.5 
E.52.5 Now therefore, what have I here, saith the LORD, that my people is taken away for nought? they that rule over them make them to howl, saith the LORD; and my name continually every day is blasphemed.

α.52.6 
E.52.6 Therefore my people shall know my name: therefore they shall know in that day that I am he that doth speak: behold, it is I.

α.52.7 
E.52.7 How beautiful upon the mountains are the feet of him that bringeth good tidings, that publisheth peace; that bringeth good tidings of good, that publisheth salvation; that saith unto Zion, Thy God reigneth!

α.52.8 
E.52.8 Thy watchmen shall lift up the voice; with the voice together shall they sing: for they shall see eye to eye, when the LORD shall bring again Zion.

α.52.9 
E.52.9 Break forth into joy, sing together, ye waste places of Jerusalem: for the LORD hath comforted his people, he hath redeemed Jerusalem.

α.52.10 
E.52.10 The LORD hath made bare his holy arm in the eyes of all the nations; and all the ends of the earth shall see the salvation of our God.

α.52.11 
E.52.11 Depart ye, depart ye, go ye out from thence, touch no unclean thing; go ye out of the midst of her; be ye clean, that bear the vessels of the LORD.

α.52.12 
E.52.12 For ye shall not go out with haste, nor go by flight: for the LORD will go before you; and the God of Israel will be your rereward.

α.52.13 
E.52.13 Behold, my servant shall deal prudently, he shall be exalted and extolled, and be very high.

α.52.14 
E.52.14 As many were astonied at thee; his visage was so marred more than any man, and his form more than the sons of men:

α.52.15 
E.52.15 So shall he sprinkle many nations; the kings shall shut their mouths at him: for that which had not been told them shall they see; and that which they had not heard shall they consider.

α.53.1 
E.53.1 Who hath believed our report? and to whom is the arm of the LORD revealed?

α.53.2 
E.53.2 For he shall grow up before him as a tender plant, and as a root out of a dry ground: he hath no form nor comeliness; and when we shall see him, there is no beauty that we should desire him.

α.53.3 
E.53.3 He is despised and rejected of men; a man of sorrows, and acquainted with grief: and we hid as it were our faces from him; he was despised, and we esteemed him not.

α.53.4 
E.53.4 Surely he hath borne our griefs, and carried our sorrows: yet we did esteem him stricken, smitten of God, and afflicted.

α.53.5 
E.53.5 But he was wounded for our transgressions, he was bruised for our iniquities: the chastisement of our peace was upon him; and with his stripes we are healed.

α.53.6 
E.53.6 All we like sheep have gone astray; we have turned every one to his own way; and the LORD hath laid on him the iniquity of us all.

α.53.7 
E.53.7 He was oppressed, and he was afflicted, yet he opened not his mouth: he is brought as a lamb to the slaughter, and as a sheep before her shearers is dumb, so he openeth not his mouth.

α.53.8 
E.53.8 He was taken from prison and from judgment: and who shall declare his generation? for he was cut off out of the land of the living: for the transgression of my people was he stricken.

α.53.9 
E.53.9 And he made his grave with the wicked, and with the rich in his death; because he had done no violence, neither was any deceit in his mouth.

α.53.10 
E.53.10 Yet it pleased the LORD to bruise him; he hath put him to grief: when thou shalt make his soul an offering for sin, he shall see his seed, he shall prolong his days, and the pleasure of the LORD shall prosper in his hand.

α.53.11 
E.53.11 He shall see of the travail of his soul, and shall be satisfied: by his knowledge shall my righteous servant justify many; for he shall bear their iniquities.

α.53.12 
E.53.12 Therefore will I divide him a portion with the great, and he shall divide the spoil with the strong; because he hath poured out his soul unto death: and he was numbered with the transgressors; and he bare the sin of many, and made intercession for the transgressors.

α.54.1 
E.54.1 Sing, O barren, thou that didst not bear; break forth into singing, and cry aloud, thou that didst not travail with child: for more are the children of the desolate than the children of the married wife, saith the LORD.

α.54.2 
E.54.2 Enlarge the place of thy tent, and let them stretch forth the curtains of thine habitations: spare not, lengthen thy cords, and strengthen thy stakes;

α.54.3 
E.54.3 For thou shalt break forth on the right hand and on the left; and thy seed shall inherit the Gentiles, and make the desolate cities to be inhabited.

α.54.4 
E.54.4 Fear not; for thou shalt not be ashamed: neither be thou confounded; for thou shalt not be put to shame: for thou shalt forget the shame of thy youth, and shalt not remember the reproach of thy widowhood any more.

α.54.5 
E.54.5 For thy Maker is thine husband; the LORD of hosts is his name; and thy Redeemer the Holy One of Israel; The God of the whole earth shall he be called.

α.54.6 
E.54.6 For the LORD hath called thee as a woman forsaken and grieved in spirit, and a wife of youth, when thou wast refused, saith thy God.

α.54.7 
E.54.7 For a small moment have I forsaken thee; but with great mercies will I gather thee.

α.54.8 
E.54.8 In a little wrath I hid my face from thee for a moment; but with everlasting kindness will I have mercy on thee, saith the LORD thy Redeemer.

α.54.9 
E.54.9 For this is as the waters of Noah unto me: for as I have sworn that the waters of Noah should no more go over the earth; so have I sworn that I would not be wroth with thee, nor rebuke thee.

α.54.10 
E.54.10 For the mountains shall depart, and the hills be removed; but my kindness shall not depart from thee, neither shall the covenant of my peace be removed, saith the LORD that hath mercy on thee.

α.54.11 
E.54.11 O thou afflicted, tossed with tempest, and not comforted, behold, I will lay thy stones with fair colours, and lay thy foundations with sapphires.

α.54.12 
E.54.12 And I will make thy windows of agates, and thy gates of carbuncles, and all thy borders of pleasant stones.

α.54.13 
E.54.13 And all thy children shall be taught of the LORD; and great shall be the peace of thy children.

α.54.14 
E.54.14 In righteousness shalt thou be established: thou shalt be far from oppression; for thou shalt not fear: and from terror; for it shall not come near thee.

α.54.15 
E.54.15 Behold, they shall surely gather together, but not by me: whosoever shall gather together against thee shall fall for thy sake.

α.54.16 
E.54.16 Behold, I have created the smith that bloweth the coals in the fire, and that bringeth forth an instrument for his work; and I have created the waster to destroy.

α.54.17 
E.54.17 No weapon that is formed against thee shall prosper; and every tongue that shall rise against thee in judgment thou shalt condemn. This is the heritage of the servants of the LORD, and their righteousness is of me, saith the LORD.

α.55.1 EHoh nish$noh pasuk noh kuhkutt8g, peyonch nippekontu, kah noh mátta ohto8g teaguas: peyonk, adtôagk, kah meets[e]k, nux peyonk, adtóagk wine kah sogkodtunk matta wutch teaguas, kah matta noadtue.
E.55.1 Ho, every one that thirsteth, come ye to the waters, and he that hath no money; come ye, buy, and eat; yea, come, buy wine and milk without money and without price.

α.55.2 Tohwutch mag8og teagwash ne matta pâdtukqunnunganun8g? kah kutanakausuongan8, wutche ne matta taphuomun8? menuhke n8tiegk, kah meech8k ne wanegik, kah kukketeahogkoun8 weekontaj ut wunogquneat.
E.55.2 Wherefore do ye spend money for that which is not bread? and your labour for that which satisfieth not? hearken diligently unto me, and eat ye that which is good, and let your soul delight itself in fatness.

α.55.3 Ahch8suttah, kah peyaauseh n8tam8k, kah kutteahogkoun8 pish pomantam; kah kutayimauonumw8 m[â]chemohtag wunn8waonk, papane monanumaongash David.
E.55.3 Incline your ear, and come unto me: hear, and your soul shall live; and I will make an everlasting covenant with you, even the sure mercies of David.

α.55.4 Kusseh, nuttinninnumau missinninnuh 8wauwonat, sagkompaginnuen, kah ann8nuwaenin en missinninnuut.
E.55.4 Behold, I have given him for a witness to the people, a leader and commander to the people.

α.55.5 Kusseh, pish k8wehkom wutohtimoin ne matta wahteauo[n]an, kah wutohtimoneash nish matta wahik8unish, pish kukquentunkqunash, wutche Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, k[a]h wutch 8neetupanatam8moh Israel: newutche noh kussohsum8wahik.
E.55.5 Behold, thou shalt call a nation that thou knowest not, and nations that knew not thee shall run unto thee because of the LORD thy God, and for the Holy One of Israel; for he hath glorified thee.

α.55.6 Natinneah8k Jehovah woh ash namhit: wehkomash pas8tappit.
E.55.6 Seek ye the LORD while he may be found, call ye upon him while he is near:

α.55.7 Matchetou nukkotutch ummay, kah matsampweusseaenin wuttenantam8ongash, kah qushkeitch en Jehovah$ut, kah pish ummonanumuh, kah en num-Manitt8mut newutche noh pish m8cheke ahquontam.
E.55.7 Let the wicked forsake his way, and the unrighteous man his thoughts: and let him return unto the LORD, and he will have mercy upon him; and to our God, for he will abundantly pardon.

α.55.8 Newutche nuttenantam8ongash matta k8tenantamuonkaneinash, kah kummayash matta nummayash n8wau Jehovah.
E.55.8 For my thoughts are not your thoughts, neither are your ways my ways, saith the LORD.

α.55.9 Newutche neane kesukquash anue qunuhquotash onk ne ohke, netatuppe nummayash qunuhquodtash anue onk kummayash kah nuttenantam8ongash, onk kuttenattam8ongash.
E.55.9 For as the heavens are higher than the earth, so are my ways higher than your ways, and my thoughts than your thoughts.

α.55.10 Newutche neane n8kem8[u]k sokanon kah k8n wutch kesukqut, kah matta qushkeog, qut nippehkontamwog ohke, kah ummechumuhkon, kah 8nt8nohquamuhkon, onk, onk woh 8skannemunneuhkauonat ahketeanutcheh, kah petukqununk wutch noh meetsit.
E.55.10 For as the rain cometh down, and the snow from heaven, and returneth not thither, but watereth the earth, and maketh it bring forth and bud, that it may give seed to the sower, and bread to the eater:

α.55.11 Ne pish nneu nuttinn8waonk ne sohham8m8ug wutch nutt8nut: matta pish mahchiyeue qushkemun8 en nuhhogkat, qut pish kézteau8m8 nê tapeneam, kah pish wunayeum8 uttôh áne ann8tam.
E.55.11 So shall my word be that goeth forth out of my mouth: it shall not return unto me void, but it shall accomplish that which I please, and it shall prosper in the thing whereto I sent it.

α.55.12 Newutche pish k8wekontamwe sohham8m8, kah pish k8nohteae monchanitteamw8: wadchuash kah wadchuemesash pish mishont8a8hamóm8ash ut anaquabeog, kah wame ohteakon8e mehtugquash pish pohponkinitchahhuog.
E.55.12 For ye shall go out with joy, and be led forth with peace: the mountains and the hills shall break forth before you into singing, and all the trees of the field shall clap their hands.

α.55.13 Nonompu asinnekô[á]s pish wutch sonkin firuhtug, kah nonompu kôus pish wutchegin myrtlúhtug: kah ne pish wutch wesuonk Jehovahut, kah wutch machemohtag kuhkinneasuonk, ne matta pish támuttahham8muk.
E.55.13 Instead of the thorn shall come up the fir tree, and instead of the brier shall come up the myrtle tree: and it shall be to the LORD for a name, for an everlasting sign that shall not be cut off.

α.56.1 YEu wussin Lord, nanawehteau8k wussittumóonk, kah s[a]mpweussek, newutche n8wadchanuwaonk pas8che peyom8: kah nussampweusseonk wahteauwahuwon.
E.56.1 Thus saith the LORD, Keep ye judgment, and do justice: for my salvation is near to come, and my righteousness to be revealed.

α.56.2 Wunánumau wosketomp noh yeu asit, kah wunnaumonuh wosketomp noh másunuk, noh nanawehteunk sabath wutch matta wunnishketeau8unat, kah noh nanawehteunk wunnutcheg wutch matchesenat.
E.56.2 Blessed is the man that doeth this, and the son of man that layeth hold on it; that keepeth the sabbath from polluting it, and keepeth his hand from doing any evil.

α.56.3 Kah wunnaumonuh penuot noh weetashunt wuhhogkuh Lordut, ahque n8waj, n8wonat, Jehovah papaquanne nutchippunuk wutch ummissinninnúmut: kah eunuchsog n8wahettékitch, kusseh, nen nunohtae mehtug.
E.56.3 Neither let the son of the stranger, that hath joined himself to the LORD, speak, saying, The LORD hath utterly separated me from his people: neither let the eunuch say, Behold, I am a dry tree.

α.56.4 Newutche wuttinnon Lord eunuchsoh, neg nanawehteunkig nussabbat8mash, káh neg pepenogig nish woh wohsikkitteahikqueanish, kah neg manúhkenukig n8n8waonk.
E.56.4 For thus saith the LORD unto the eunuchs that keep my sabbaths, and choose the things that please me, and take hold of my covenant;

α.56.5 Nuttinnumauóog ut neekit, kah anóme nuppummenutonganit, ayeuonk kah wesuonk, anue wunnegen onk 8wesuongan8 wunnaumoniitcheg kah wuttaunitcheg: nuttinnumauóog machemohtag wesuonk, ne matta pish támatahham8muk.
E.56.5 Even unto them will I give in mine house and within my walls a place and a name better than of sons and of daughters: I will give them an everlasting name, that shall not be cut off.

α.56.6 Kah wonk wunnaumonuh pen8wot neg agwappéhtauáhettit Jehovah, wowussumónat, kah womantamunat 8wesuonk Jehovah, 8tinninneumuneat, nishnoh pasuk noh nanawehteunk Sabbath matta niṣhketeau8unat, kah noh kônunuk n8n8waonk.
E.56.6 Also the sons of the stranger, that join themselves to the LORD, to serve him, and to love the name of the LORD, to be his servants, every one that keepeth the sabbath from polluting it, and taketh hold of my covenant;

α.56.7 Neg nuppas8oog n8neetupanatamwe wadchúmut, kah n8weekontamwaheóog, ut nuppeantamwáe kommukqut, wutchikohtae mag8ongan8oash, kah wussephausuongan8oash, nish pish tapeneamunash ut nut[-]altarumut; newutche nek pish hettamun peantamwae kommuk wutch wame nummissinninneumog.
E.56.7 Even them will I bring to my holy mountain, and make them joyful in my house of prayer: their burnt offerings and their sacrifices shall be accepted upon mine altar; for mine house shall be called an house of prayer for all people.

α.56.8 Jehovah Manit, noh móunont pakenitcheh nummissinninneumoh, n8wau, nano nummóunúmau, chabesitcheg neh m[o]etunkqutcheh.
E.56.8 The Lord GOD, which gathereth the outcasts of Israel saith, Yet will I gather others to him, beside those that are gathered unto him.

α.56.9 Wame kenaaú ohteakóne puppinashimwog peyunk mahchipwunneat, wame kenaau touohkomukque puppinashimwog,
E.56.9 All ye beasts of the field, come to devour, yea, all ye beasts in the forest.

α.56.10 Wutaskwhôsuéneumoh pogkenumwoh: nag wame as8tuog, nag wame mokákutt8e anumwog, matta wohwóhteau8og: kouéog, sepsinwog, wekontamwog kogkouequon.
E.56.10 His watchmen are blind: they are all ignorant, they are all dumb dogs, they cannot bark; sleeping, lying down, loving to slumber.

α.56.11 Nux, nag nehnehteáp8e anumwog, neg woh mo wamep8gig, kah nag nanaushepsaenuog matta wohwohtamóog: nag wame moninneamwog nehenwonche ummayyeu, nishnoh pasuk wutch wutonts8nam8onk, wutch wutchippaiyeumut.
E.56.11 Yea, they are greedy dogs which can never have enough, and they are shepherds that cannot understand: they all look to their own way, every one for his gain, from his quarter.

α.56.12 Peyunk, n8waog, nunneemskom wine, kah nunnumwohtauómun nuhhogkanonog onkuppe, kah saup pish neyane yeuyeu kesukok, kah m8cheke muttae.
E.56.12 Come ye, say they, I will fetch wine, and we will fill ourselves with strong drink; and to morrow shall be as this day, and much more abundant.

α.57.1 SAmpweusseaen nup, kah matta howan upponam8un wuttahhut: kah monaneteaénuog amaunóog, matta howàn wunnatwontam8un, sampweusseaenin am[à]unau wutch machuk ne paóm8ug.
E.57.1 The righteous perisheth, and no man layeth it to heart: and merciful men are taken away, none considering that the righteous is taken away from the evil to come.

α.57.2 Noh pish petutteau wunohteaonganit, nag pish anwôsinwog ut wutapinneaóut, nish$noh pasuk paumwushadt ut wussampweusseonganit.
E.57.2 He shall enter into peace: they shall rest in their beds, each one walking in his uprightness.

α.57.3 Qut pas8tshagk, kenaau wunnaumonauh pauwásq, 8skannem mamussuaenin, kah nanwun8dsquâsuen.
E.57.3 But draw near hither, ye sons of the sorceress, the seed of the adulterer and the whore.

α.57.4 Howan ayeuuhkonittue chétwhók kuhhogkaóog? howan ayeuuhkonittue mashe kushkutt8naéhtauóg, kah sonkhénanúwaéhtauóg? sunnummatta kenaau panneseae wunneechaninneunk? pann8wae wuskannem?
E.57.4 Against whom do ye sport yourselves? against whom make ye a wide mouth, and draw out the tongue? are ye not children of transgression, a seed of falsehood.

α.57.5 Kukkussináheomw8 kuhhogkaóog nashpe nunneukontunkkanog, ut agwe nish$noh askuh[n]kq nushonat mukkiesog 8nôuhkôiyeutu, ut agwe pass[o]mpsk[o]déhtu.
E.57.5 Enflaming yourselves with idols under every green tree, slaying the children in the valleys under the clifts of the rocks?

α.57.6 Ut kenugke kussitchuáne m8sompsquéhtu, ne kutchippiyeum: nish, nish kutittanohtôadtuonk: kussókanumau[ô]og nag wuttattam8e sephausuonk, kummag meetsue mag8onk, sun woh nutattumunum taphettuonk yeush ut?
E.57.6 Among the smooth stones of the stream is thy portion; they, they are thy lot: even to them hast thou poured a drink offering, thou hast offered a meat offering. Should I receive comfort in these?

α.57.7 Ut qunuhqui kodohk[ó]ag na kupponamun kutappin: na kuttinne kuhkuhquen kumm[à]gunat sephausuongash.
E.57.7 Upon a lofty and high mountain hast thou set thy bed: even thither wentest thou up to offer sacrifice.

α.57.8 Onkauùssquont wonk, kah pogkomukquongash ne kupponamun kummequantam8onk: newutche kuposkehtau onkatok onk nen, kah kukkuhkuhquem: kummisheu kuskéhteop kutappin, kah nag k8n8wón[a]óog, k8womontam wutappinneau ut$toh ut nauman.
E.57.8 Behind the doors also and the posts hast thou set up thy remembrance: for thou hast discovered thyself to another than me, and art gone up; thou hast enlarged thy bed, and made thee a covenant with them; thou lovedst their bed where thou sawest it.

α.57.9 Kah kutóm ketass8tamwut nashpe pummee, kah nano kummishteo k8weetemunkquot8mash, kah kutann8n kutann8naeneumog wutch n8adtut, kah kuttiahquonkqueh kuhhog wehque chepiohkomuk.
E.57.9 And thou wentest to the king with ointment, and didst increase thy perfumes, and didst send thy messengers far off, and didst debase thyself even unto hell.

α.57.10 Kussauunuk kumishe mayuk8m, qut onch matta kussú, matt[a] annoôsuonganinno: kummishkom kenutchegane pomantam8onk, newajeh matta n8henn8muk.
E.57.10 Thou art wearied in the greatness of thy way; yet saidst thou not, There is no hope: thou hast found the life of thine hand; therefore thou wast not grieved.

α.57.11 Howan wabesuônadt kah quoshadt, waj pann8wáan, kah matta kummequanumu, asuh kupponam8un kuttahhut? sunnummatta nutchepappu wutch n8adt, kah matta kukqushéu?
E.57.11 And of whom hast thou been afraid or feared, that thou hast lied, and hast not remembered me, nor laid it to thy heart? have not I held my peace even of old, and thou fearest me not?

α.57.12 N8wahteauwáhuam kussampweusseonk, kah kutanakausuongash: newutche nish matta pish n8chiéinash.
E.57.12 I will declare thy righteousness, and thy works; for they shall not profit thee.

α.57.13 Máuan, weechógquéaneg pohquohwhunukqush: qut waban pish 8wame monchanuh: tan8cheéyeuuk pish wunneemunuh; qut noh pabahtanumit, pish ohtau ohke, kah pish ahtou n8neetupanatamwe wadchúm.
E.57.13 When thou criest, let thy companies deliver thee; but the wind shall carry them all away; vanity shall take them: but he that putteth his trust in me shall possess the land, and shall inherit my holy mountain;

α.57.14 Kah pish n8waog, kuhkuhquonteagk, kuhkuhquonteagk quoshauwehtam8k may, amaunum8k togkussittassunóonk wutch ummayeuont nummissinninnúmog.
E.57.14 And shall say, Cast ye up, cast ye up, prepare the way, take up the stumblingblock out of the way of my people.

α.57.15 Newutche yeu wussin noh quanunkqussit kah masugkenuk noh áyit machemóhtagit, noh as8wésit wanetupanatamweyeuit: nuttai qunuhqui kah wunneetupanatamwe ayeuonganit: n8weetom wonk, pohquehteáheont, kah ahohpateáhont, quaquakqheónat ahhohpanitcheh, kah quaquakqheonat pohqueteahónitcheh.
E.57.15 For thus saith the high and lofty One that inhabiteth eternity, whose name is Holy; I dwell in the high and holy place, with him also that is of a contrite and humble spirit, to revive the spirit of the humble, and to revive the heart of the contrite ones.

α.57.16 Newutche matta nummicheme mekónteóh, kah matta nagwutteae pish nummusquanittam8: newutche wunnashaongan8 woh sauunum8m8 ut anaquabeh, kah keteahogkôunog neg kezheógig.
E.57.16 For I will not contend for ever, neither will I be always wroth: for the spirit should fail before me, and the souls which I have made.

α.57.17 Wutche wutiahchewont[à]m8e matcheséonk, nummusquantamup, kah nuttogkomop; nupputtogquep, kah nummusquantamop, kah pittuanumwu kutchitáushóp ut wuttahh8wáe mayut.
E.57.17 For the iniquity of his covetousness was I wroth, and smote him: I hid me, and was wroth, and he went on frowardly in the way of his heart.

α.57.18 Nunnaumup ummayash, kah nunneetke[h] nussagkompagun wonk, kah nunnompinnumau taphettuonk, kah ummauunnitteaéneumoh.
E.57.18 I have seen his ways, and will heal him: I will lead him also, and restore comforts unto him and to his mourners.

α.57.19 Nukkezteóh ummeechummúonk mussissitt8n, wunohteaonk, wunohteaj noh nóapit, kah noh pas8tappit, n8wau Lord, kah nunneetskeh.
E.57.19 I create the fruit of the lips; Peace, peace to him that is far off, and to him that is near, saith the LORD; and I will heal him.

α.57.20 Qut matchetukeg tatuppeyeu8og mishontuk8e kehtahhanit, matta ch[é]pohtan8g, noh nippe sohwanúhtog pissag, kah nishkeneunkquok.
E.57.20 But the wicked are like the troubled sea, when it cannot rest, whose waters cast up mire and dirt.

α.57.21 Matta 8nohteaonganúmu matcheetou n8wau num-Manitt8m.
E.57.21 There is no peace, saith my God, to the wicked.

α.58.1 MIshont8ash, wohquontogan, ogque mishont8ash monuhpuhpequonut kah náhtus nummissinninnúmog uppanneseongan8oash, kah wek Jakob ummatcheseongan8oash.
E.58.1 Cry aloud, spare not, lift up thy voice like a trumpet, and shew my people their transgression, and the house of Jacob their sins.

α.58.2 Qut onch nag natinneáhikquog asekesukokish, kah weekontamwog wahteauun nummayash, onatuh sampweusseae wutohtimóin, kah matta ahquontamoe ukkuhk8waongash um-Manitt8m8uh: nunnat8tamunkquog sampweusseae kuhk8waongash: weekontamup pas8sukauunat God
E.58.2 Yet they seek me daily, and delight to know my ways, as a nation that did righteousness, and forsook not the ordinance of their God: they ask of me the ordinances of justice; they take delight in approaching to God.

α.58.3 Tohwutch mat meetseog, kah matta kenaum8un? tohwutch onkapunnanogkut nukketeahogkôunoh, kah matta kukkehkinneaséin? kusseh, matmeetsue kesukkodtut kutohtóm8 weekontamóonk, kah chekée usséhuwom8 wame kutanakausuongánooash.
E.58.3 Wherefore have we fasted, say they, and thou seest not? wherefore have we afflicted our soul, and thou takest no knowledge? Behold, in the day of your fast ye find pleasure, and exact all your labours.

α.58.4 Kusseh, mekonittue, kah penuánittue matkummeetsúmw8, tattéohtinat machetoe menutcheg: matta pish matkummeetsumw8, neáseóg yeu kesukok kukqunúhque n8tunkqunuhkônaóut k8wadtauatonkqussuongan8.
E.58.4 Behold, ye fast for strife and debate, and to smite with the fist of wickedness: ye shall not fast as ye do this day, to make your voice to be heard on high.

α.58.5 Sun nein matmeetsuonk ne pepenam? kesuk neadt wosketomp uhquanumwéheunt ukketeahogkounoh? sun ne wunnauánumunat uppuhkuk onatuh bulrush, kah ogque upponamunat man8tiónak kah pukquee? sun yeu kuttéhettamun matmeetsuonk, kah 8sekitteae kesukodt8m Jehovah?
E.58.5 Is it such a fast that I have chosen? a day for a man to afflict his soul? is it to bow down his head as a bulrush, and to spread sackcloth and ashes under him? wilt thou call this a fast, and an acceptable day to the LORD?

α.58.6 Sunnummatta yeu matmeetsuonk ne pepenam? ompinimunat matcheetowongane kishpissuongash, ompenimunat tuhkequanne weanunash, kah sânukahwhut wutchippinnúinneat, kah pokshanónat nishnoh yoak?
E.58.6 Is not this the fast that I have chosen? to loose the bands of wickedness, to undo the heavy burdens, and to let the oppressed go free, and that ye break every yoke?

α.58.7 Sunnummatta ne kuttinnumauónat kuppetukqunnunk kodtupwutcheg, kah kuppasuonat kekit, matcheku noh sohwohteamuk: nauadt poskissu, kutonk8h, & matta kutadtahsh[o]h kuhhog wutch nehenwonche keyaus.
E.58.7 Is it not to deal thy bread to the hungry, and that thou bring the poor that are cast out to thy house? when thou seest the naked, that thou cover him; and that thou hide not thyself from thine own flesh?

α.58.8 Neit k8wequáiyeum pish ogque sonkqsúm8 mahtompanut, kah k8niyeuonk pish kenuppe sonksum8: kah kussampweusseonk pish kenegonuhkunk, wussohsumóonk Jehovah, noh pish kuppisquane nanauhik.
E.58.8 Then shall thy light break forth as the morning, and thine health shall spring forth speedily: and thy righteousness shall go before thee; the glory of the LORD shall be thy rereward.

α.58.9 Neit pish k8wehquetum, kah Jehovah pish kenamp8hamunk, pish kummauunnitteau, kah noh pish n8wau, nen yeu: amaunadt yoak wutch kenashómut, kenutcheg sontikquanuwóm8ut, kah tahn8che keket8kaonk.
E.58.9 Then shalt thou call, and the LORD shall answer; thou shalt cry, and he shall say, Here I am. If thou take away from the midst of thee the yoke, the putting forth of the finger, and speaking vanity;

α.58.10 Kôdtunadt kukketeahogkou en noh kodtupwit, kah wampwehe[à]dt unkuppunáe keteahogkou, neit k8wequaiyeum pish waapem8 ut pohkenaouut, kah kuppohkenaiyeum pish tatuppeyeu8 pohshaquadt.
E.58.10 And if thou draw out thy soul to the hungry, and satisfy the afflicted soul; then shall thy light rise in obscurity, and thy darkness be as the noon day:

α.58.11 Kah Jehovah pish nagwutteae kussamp8wunuk, kah pish wamepwéheau kukketeahogkounoh, kunkohteadtag, kah wunogquehteau koskonash: kah pish kuttatuppeyeu wuttadtippadtaueu tanohketeaonganit, kah tohkekomuut, noh wunnippe matta ahquohtán8g.
E.58.11 And the LORD shall guide thee continually, and satisfy thy soul in drought, and make fat thy bones: and thou shalt be like a watered garden, and like a spring of water, whose waters fail not.

α.58.12 Kah nag wágig kuhhogkat, pish ayimwog nukkonne ayeuongash nish matchteomukish: pish kuttashinum monaash pometeongash quenohtagish: kah pish kuttehenit, onchteunk pokqshunk, kah nompenuk ayeuongane mayash.
E.58.12 And they that shall be of thee shall build the old waste places: thou shalt raise up the foundations of many generations; and thou shalt be called, The repairer of the breach, The restorer of paths to dwell in.

α.58.13 Qushkinnuman kusseet wutch sabbath$dayut, matta kutusseinat nehenwonche k8wekontam8onk, ut n8eetupantamwe kesukodtumut, kah hettaman sabbath n8wekontam8onk, 8neetupanatam8m Jehovah, quohtianumukquok, kah noh quttianumadt, matta ussean nehenwonche kummayash asuh mat kenemunnum8unat nehenwonche wekontam8onk, kah matta kusseinat nehenwonceh kukk8ttwongash.
E.58.13 If thou turn away thy foot from the sabbath, from doing thy pleasure on my holy day; and call the sabbath a delight, the holy of the LORD, honourable; and shalt honour him, not doing thine own ways, nor finding thine own pleasure, nor speaking thine own words:

α.58.14 Neit pish k8wekontamwah kuhhog Jehovahut, kah kenayeúmukqu[éb]esh ut qunuhqui ayeuonganéhtu ut ohkeit, & pish kussohkom8nsh nashpe wutohtoonk Jacob k8sh, newutche wutt8n Jehovah ukkutt8kontamun.
E.58.14 Then shalt thou delight thyself in the LORD; and I will cause thee to ride upon the high places of the earth, and feed thee with the heritage of Jacob thy father: for the mouth of the LORD hath spoken it.

α.59.1 KUsseh, wunnutcheg Jehovah tiohqutteauóuun, onk ne woh mo adchanuómun8, kah wehtauog matta tuhkequanun8 woh moh wunn8tam8unat.
E.59.1 Behold, the LORD's hand is not shortened, that it cannot save; neither his ear heavy, that it cannot hear:

α.59.2 Qut kummatcheseongash chippemoash ut nashaue kenaau, kah kum-Manitt8m8óut, kah kummatcheseongash adtahtau wuskesuk wutch kenaau, woh mo n8tam8unat.
E.59.2 But your iniquities have separated between you and your God, and your sins have hid his face from you, that he will not hear.

α.59.3 Newutche kenutcheoash wunnishketeauunash musqueheonk, kah kuttinwhunutchegash nashpe matcheseonk, kah kussissitt8n8ash pann8wom8ash, keenan woonki m8m8sk8womo.
E.59.3 For your hands are defiled with blood, and your fingers with iniquity; your lips have spoken lies, your tongue hath muttered perverseness.

α.59.4 Wanne howan wehqueteum8 sámpweusseonk, kah matta howan ket8konshittam8 wanamuhkuteyeuuk: nag pabahtantamwog tahn8cheyeuuk, káh pann8waog, wompequo8og woskehuwaonk, kah neechaog panneusseonk.
E.59.4 None calleth for justice, nor any pleadeth for truth: they trust in vanity, and speak lies; they conceive mischief, and bring forth iniquity.

α.59.5 Ahtinnasinwog 8woanash cokatrice, kah monakeneheaog manunapit wuthashabpoh: noh meechik nag 8woano8ash nup, kah ne sanukehthamuk, ⟦sohwutchuanu viper.⟧
E.59.5 They hatch cockatrice' eggs, and weave the spider's web: he that eateth of their eggs dieth, and that which is crushed breaketh out into a viper.

α.59.6 Ummonakenehteaongan8 matta pish onkwhooog wuhhogkauh nashpe wutanakausuongash: wutanakausuongan8oash matcheseae anakausuongash, kah chekee usseonk ohteau wunnutcheganit.
E.59.6 Their webs shall not become garments, neither shall they cover themselves with their works: their works are works of iniquity, and the act of violence is in their hands.

α.59.7 Wusseetoash u[h]shom8ash matchitut, & kenupshaaog sokohkonat mat woskehuwae musqueheonk: wuttenantam8ongan8oash matcheseae unnantam8ongash, mahchumwehtoonk kah paguanuonk ut ummayeuout.
E.59.7 Their feet run to evil, and they make haste to shed innocent blood: their thoughts are thoughts of iniquity; wasting and destruction are in their paths.

α.59.8 Wunohteae may matta wahteau8og, kah na matta wussittum8onganun8 ut ummoncheongan8out: neg ayimauaog woonki mayash wuttinniin howan na aont, matta pish wunohteaonk.
E.59.8 The way of peace they know not; and there is no judgment in their goings: they have made them crooked paths: whosoever goeth therein shall not know peace.

α.59.9 Newaj na8sukongqueog wussittumoonk, kah sampweusseonk matta kumatanuk8unan: nuppahtómun wequai kah kusseh pohkenai: wompag, qut nuppomushomun pohkenáhtu.
E.59.9 Therefore is judgment far from us, neither doth justice overtake us: we wait for light, but behold obscurity; for brightness, but we walk in darkness.

α.59.10 Nunn8sweemun qussukquaneuntunk onatuh pohp[ôg]kenumuk, kah nuppopogkénumunun, onatuh mat wuskesuk8og: nuttogkussittássunumun pohshequaeu, onatuh nohkog, touishinne ayeuonganehtu onatuh nápumuk.
E.59.10 We grope for the wall like the blind, and we grope as if we had no eyes: we stumble at noon day as in the night; we are in desolate places as dead men.

α.59.11 Nutogquont8wómun mosqut, kah nutogque mishe maumun wuskuhwunanáut: nunnátauwompattamumun wussittumoonk, qut na matta ohtano, wadchanittuonk qut nô óhteau.
E.59.11 We roar all like bears, and mourn sore like doves: we look for judgment, but there is none; for salvation, but it is far off from us.

α.59.12 Newutche nuppaneseonganónash muttaánutash ut anaquabean, kah nummatcheseonganunonash nutayeuuhkônittue wauwaónukqunánonash: newutche nuppanneseonganunonash n8weetómukqunánonash, kah nummatcheseonganunonash n8wahteauunánonash.
E.59.12 For our transgressions are multiplied before thee, and our sins testify against us: for our transgressions are with us; and as for our iniquities, we know them;

α.59.13 Panneséog kah ayeuuhkonittue pann8waheogkut Jehovah, kah amaéog wutch num-Manitt8munónut, an8wáogish sunukkôwhuttuonk kah ontogquéhtam8onk, ananatamog, kah metass8wae kodt8kôog pann8waongash.
E.59.13 In transgressing and lying against the LORD, and departing away from our God, speaking oppression and revolt, conceiving and uttering from the heart words of falsehood.

α.59.14 Kah wussittum8onk qushkem8: kah sampweusseonk nôadtit neepattau: newutche wanamuhkutéyeuuk pógkishin maikontu, kah tatuppenéhettuonk matta petutteamun8.
E.59.14 And judgment is turned away backward, and justice standeth afar off: for truth is fallen in the street, and equity cannot enter.

α.59.15 Nux, wunnamuhkutéyeuuk panushean, kah noh nôkodtuk machuk, muk8kinnuwaheau wuhh[h]ogkuh, kah Jehovah wunnaumun, kah matta 8sekitteáhik8un newutche matta wussittum8wonganinn8.
E.59.15 Yea, truth faileth; and he that departeth from evil maketh himself a prey: and the LORD saw it, and it displeased him that there was no judgment.

α.59.16 Kah naum na matta wosketompaunn8, kah monchanatam matta howan ukken8tamwanshuh, newaj 8hpit paudtauont wadchanittuonk, kah wussampweusseonk ukqukquninukqun.
E.59.16 And he saw that there was no man, and wondered that there was no intercessor: therefore his arm brought salvation unto him; and his righteousness, it sustained him.

α.59.17 Newutche ogque hogk8 sampweusseonk mohpanáganit ahhohtag, kah wadchanittue uppuhkukqut ahhohtag uppuhkukqut? kah hogk8 ann8tôadtue hogk8unash wutche wuthogk8onk, kah hogk8 zeale onatuh petashqusháonk.
E.59.17 For he put on righteousness as a breastplate, and an helmet of salvation upon his head; and he put on the garments of vengeance for clothing, and was clad with zeal as a cloak.

α.59.18 Neaunak wutusseongan8oash, ne wuttinonkquttauun ayeuuhkonukqutcheh musquanittam8onk, kah onkquatunk en ummatwomut, pish onkquttauau munóhhanoh onkquatunk.
E.59.18 According to their deeds, accordingly he will repay, fury to his adversaries, recompence to his enemies; to the islands he will repay recompence.

α.59.19 Neit pish wabesuontamwog 8wesuonk Jehovah wutch wutcheksuiyeu, kah wussohsumóonk waj pashpishont: matwau ogque petutteadt tomogkanit, wunnashauanitt8moh Jehovah pish wutáyeuuhkonittue tahshinnumauoh muttaagk.
E.59.19 So shall they fear the name of the LORD from the west, and his glory from the rising of the sun. When the enemy shall come in like a flood, the Spirit of the LORD shall lift up a standard against him.

α.59.20 Kah man8hhuwaenin pish peyau Zion, kah en nahoh ámaécheg wutch pannesénut ut Jakob, wussin Jehovah.
E.59.20 And the Redeemer shall come to Zion, and unto them that turn from transgression in Jacob, saith the LORD.

α.59.21 Qut nen, yeu n8n8waonganun nagoh wussin Jehovah, nunnashauanitt8m noh apehtunkquean, kah nukkutt8wongash nish ponamunish kutt8nit, nish matta pish amaémunoash wutch kutt8nut, kah matta wutch wutt8n8óut k8skannemuneog, asuh matta wutch wutt8n8wout k8skannemuneog 8skannémun8óut, wussin Lord, yeu wutche kah micheme.
E.59.21 As for me, this is my covenant with them, saith the LORD; My spirit that is upon thee, and my words which I have put in thy mouth, shall not depart out of thy mouth, nor out of the mouth of thy seed, nor out of the mouth of thy seed's seed, saith the LORD, from henceforth and for ever.

α.60.1 TOOkish, wôhsish, newutche k8wequa8m peyom8, kah wussohsum8onk Lord k8waabéhtunkqun.
E.60.1 Arise, shine; for thy light is come, and the glory of the LORD is risen upon thee.

α.60.2 Newutche kusseh, pohkenái pish nuhkuhkom ohke, kah kuhpogke pohkenái ut missinninnutu: qut Jehovah pish kuppashpishaónuk, kah wussohsumóonk pish kenaumontean.
E.60.2 For, behold, the darkness shall cover the earth, and gross darkness the people: but the LORD shall arise upon thee, and his glory shall be seen upon thee.

α.60.3 Kah Gentilsog pish peyaog k8wequaiyeumut, kah ketass8tamwog ut kussohsumóe omohkeonganit.
E.60.3 And the Gentiles shall come to thy light, and kings to the brightness of thy rising.

α.60.4 Spadtauomps waéenu, kah naish, nag wame miyaéog, kuppeyaônukquog, kenaumonunk pish nóadtit 8mwog, kah kuttaunog pish nanukkehéoog ut kishke ken.
E.60.4 Lift up thine eyes round about, and see: all they gather themselves together, they come to thee: thy sons shall come from far, and thy daughters shall be nursed at thy side.

α.60.5 Neit pish kenaum, kah kummoáeu tomogkem, kah kuttah pish wabesu, kah pish misheheau; newutche kehtahhanne monacheg pish qunnuppekompauog en kuhhogkat, ummenuhkesuongan8 Gentilsog pish kuppeyaónukqunash.
E.60.5 Then thou shalt see, and flow together, and thine heart shall fear, and be enlarged; because the abundance of the sea shall be converted unto thee, the forces of the Gentiles shall come unto thee.

α.60.6 Mataánukeg Camelsog pish kenuhkuhkunk, Midiane kah Ephahe dromedarisog: wame neg apitcheg Sheba pish peyaog, neg pish paudtoog gold, kah weetemungquok, kah nag pish wahteauwahuwáog waeenomaongash Jehovah.
E.60.6 The multitude of camels shall cover thee, the dromedaries of Midian and Ephah; all they from Sheba shall come: they shall bring gold and incense; and they shall shew forth the praises of the LORD.

α.60.7 Wame Kedare floksog pish miyaéog en kuhhogkat: Nebajothe ramsog pish k8wowussehitteaonganog: nag pish tapenumoe kuhkuhqueog en nut-altarumut, kah nussohsum8wahteoh sohsumóe nek.
E.60.7 All the flocks of Kedar shall be gathered together unto thee, the rams of Nebaioth shall minister unto thee: they shall come up with acceptance on mine altar, and I will glorify the house of my glory.

α.60.8 Howanig yeug agque pt8écheg matokqsit, kah onatuh wsk[uh]whunanáout en 8wadshaoont?
E.60.8 Who are these that fly as a cloud, and as the doves to their windows?

α.60.9 Wunnamuhkut munnáhanash pish nuppahtsuónukqunash, kah Tarshishe kuht8nogquash negonne, pas8ónat kenaumonunk wutch nôadtit, pas8ónat kenaumonunk wutch nôadtit, wus$silverum8, kah uk-goldum8 weeche nagoh; en 8wesuonganit Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, kah en 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, newutche kussohsum8ónuk
E.60.9 Surely the isles shall wait for me, and the ships of Tarshish first, to bring thy sons from far, their silver and their gold with them, unto the name of the LORD thy God, and to the Holy One of Israel, because he hath glorified thee.

α.60.10 Kah wunnaumonaoh pen8wohteaog pish ayimwog kuthassunninneutungash, kah ukketass8tam[o]m8uh pish kutannumunkquog: newutche musquantamon kuttagkomunup, qut kodtumonteánitteon kummonánumunup.
E.60.10 And the sons of strangers shall build up thy walls, and their kings shall minister unto thee: for in my wrath I smote thee, but in my favour have I had mercy on thee.

α.60.11 Newaj pish kutishquontamash nagwutteáe wôshwohtag, nish matta pish kuppuhhaúsin8ash kesukodaeu asuh nukkonáeu, onk woh wosketompaog kuppaudtunkquog 8weenauweetuongan8 Gentilsog, kah ukketass8tam8m8uh woh paudtauonauh.
E.60.11 Therefore thy gates shall be open continually; they shall not be shut day nor night; that men may bring unto thee the forces of the Gentiles, and that their kings may be brought.

α.60.12 Newutche wutohtimoin kah ass8tamóonk ne matta wadtinninneumuhkonk8an, neg pish unkquanumôog, nux yeush wutohtimoneash pish papaquáne mohchimoash.
E.60.12 For the nation and kingdom that will not serve thee shall perish; yea, those nations shall be utterly wasted.

α.60.13 Wussohsumóonk Lebanon pish kenuhkuhkunk, firuhtug, pineuhtug, kah boxuhtug moeu, wunnehteauunat nus-sanctuarie ayeuonk, kah nussohsumwáhto nusseetoe ayeuonk.
E.60.13 The glory of Lebanon shall come unto thee, the fir tree, the pine tree, and the box together, to beautify the place of my sanctuary; and I will make the place of my feet glorious.

α.60.14 Wunnaumonáuh wonk neg unkquanumwehikqueaneg, nag pish nauwaée kuppéyogquog kah wame neg jishanumukqueaneg, nag pish nauwaeog ut agwe kusseetut, kah pish kuttéhenukquog ukkeitotan Jehovah wus-Zion8m 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
E.60.14 The sons also of them that afflicted thee shall come bending unto thee; and all they that despised thee shall bow themselves down at the soles of thy feet; and they shall call thee; The city of the LORD, The Zion of the Holy One of Israel.

α.60.15 Uttôhadt, ohquanumunumukup káh jishanumunumukup, newaj matta wosketomp pannuppuhkongk8an; kutáyimáush michemohtae wunneetuonk, 8wekontam8ongan8 monaash pometeaonganash.
E.60.15 Whereas thou has been forsaken and hated, so that no man went through thee, I will make thee an eternal excellency, a joy of many generations.

α.60.16 Ken8n wonk pish wussogkodtunkan8 gentilsog: kah pish ken8nontam wohpanágun8 ketass8tamoh, kah pish k8wahteoh nen Jehovah k8wadchanuaeneum, kah kummanouhuwaeneum, ummissugkeneumoh Jakob.
E.60.16 Thou shalt also suck the milk of the Gentiles, and shalt suck the breast of kings: and thou shalt know that I the LORD am thy Saviour and thy Redeemer, the mighty One of Jacob.

α.60.17 Nompéeu brasse nuppaudtoh gold, kah nompéeu m8óhsh nuppaudtoh silver, kah nompeeu wudtuk brasse: kah nompe qussukquanash m8óhshag; kah n8nohteahéog kutannohsuénúmog, kah koshkomunukeg nussampweusseaenúheoog.
E.60.17 For brass I will bring gold, and for iron I will bring silver, and for wood brass, and for stones iron: I will also make thy officers peace, and thine exactors righteousness.

α.60.18 Chekeayeu8k matta pish wonk n8tam8un ut kutohkit, mohchumoonk asuh pagwanuonk ut kussissippóiyeumut: qut pish ku[téh]ettam kuthassunninnútungash, wadchanittuonk, kah k8squontamash waeenomaonk.
E.60.18 Violence shall no more be heard in thy land, wasting nor destruction within thy borders; but thou shalt call thy walls Salvation, and thy gates Praise.

α.60.19 Nepauz matta pish wonk k8wôhsumungk8 kesukodae kah wutche wôhsittae nanepâuhshad matta pish k8wôhsumunk8. qut Jehovah pish noh kummicheme weequaiy8m, kah kum-Manitt8m noh pish kussohsum8onk.
E.60.19 The sun shall be no more thy light by day; neither for brightness shall the moon give light unto thee: but the LORD shall be unto thee an everlasting light, and thy God thy glory.

α.60.20 Kenepauz8m màtta pish wonk wayau8, & kenanepauhshadt matta pish monchu, newutche Jehovah pish kummicheme ohtae wequai8m, kah kummauongane kesukodtash pish wohkukquoshinash.
E.60.20 Thy sun shall no more go down; neither shall thy moon withdraw itself: for the LORD shall be thine everlasting light, and the days of thy mourning shall be ended.

α.60.21 Kummissinninnumog wonk wame pish sampweusseaenúog; pish ohtoog ohke micheme, 8tuhqunnum ne ahketeaomp, nunnutchegane anakausuonk, onk woh nussohsum8ónit.
E.60.21 Thy people also shall be all righteous: they shall inherit the land for ever, the branch of my planting, the work of my hands, that I may be glorified.

α.60.22 Noh peississit pish muttannonganeyeu8, noh n8chumwesit pish menuhki wutohtimóin, nen Lord nukkenuppe ussen ut wutaquompiyeum8ut.
E.60.22 A little one shall become a thousand, and a small one a strong nation: I the LORD will hasten it in his time.

α.61.1 WUnnashauanitt8moh Lord Jehovah nutapéhtunk, newutche Jehovah nussusséqunuk kuhk8tomauonat manunnissitcheg wunaunchem8kaonk, nutann8[n]uk aseepinónat pohqutteahhoncheg, wahteauwaheonat chippinnú8onk en missinôut, kah wôshinnumauónat kuppishagkinnittuonk neg kashpissitcheg.
E.61.1 The Spirit of the Lord GOD is upon me; because the LORD hath anointed me to preach good tidings unto the meek; he hath sent me to bind up the brokenhearted, to proclaim liberty to the captives, and the opening of the prison to them that are bound;

α.61.2 Wahteauwahuónat 8weekontamwae kodtum8m Jehovah, kah wutann8t8wae ukkesukkodtum num-Manitt8mun, tapheonat wame neg mógig.
E.61.2 To proclaim the acceptable year of the LORD, and the day of vengeance of our God; to comfort all that mourn;

α.61.3 Kehtimónaóont neg mogig ut Zion, aninnumauonát, wunn[é]tuonk nompee onk ne pukquee, weekontamoe pummee nompee mauonk, tabuttantamoe hogk8onk nompee tohkéqunoe nashauonk, onk woh neg hennóog sampweusseae mehtugquash, wutohketeaonk Jehovah, onk woh sohsum8waheau.
E.61.3 To appoint unto them that mourn in Zion, to give unto them beauty for ashes, the oil of joy for mourning, the garment of praise for the spirit of heaviness; that they might be called trees of righteousness, the planting of the LORD, that he might be glorified.

α.61.4 Kah nag pish ayimwog nukkône mohchum8e ayeuongash pish tahshinumwog negonáe touushinneash, kah pish onchehteóog mohchim8e keitotanash, nish tauuhshikish m8cheke pometuongash.
E.61.4 And they shall build the old wastes, they shall raise up the former desolations, and they shall repair the waste cities, the desolations of many generations.

α.61.5 Kah penuohteaog pish neepóog, kah pish assamóog kuf-flocksum8uh, kah wunnaumonáuh penuwoht neg pish kutanaskúhhamwaenúm8óog, kah neg wánteunkeg k8weenominneohtekonash.
E.61.5 And strangers shall stand and feed your flocks, and the sons of the alien shall be your plowmen and your vinedressers.

α.61.6 Qut pish kuttiss8wésimw8 wussephàusuéneumoh Jehovah: wosketompaog pish kuttéhenukkumw8 wuñohtompeantog8moh num-Manitt8mun: pish kummeechimw8 8wenauwetuongan8 Gentilsog, kah ut wussohsum8ongan8wout pish k8woweenauómw8.
E.61.6 But ye shall be named the Priests of the LORD: men shall call you the Ministers of our God: ye shall eat the riches of the Gentiles, and in their glory shall ye boast yourselves.

α.61.7 Nompeeu kutakodchuongan8, pish keneese tahshe attumumunumw8: kah nompeeu naswáiyeuonk pish weekontamwog ut wutchippiyeum8óut: newaj ut wutuhkeout, pish neese pishkeu wutohteauuneau: machemohtag wekontamóonk pish apehtunkquog.
E.61.7 For your shame ye shall have double; and for confusion they shall rejoice in their portion: therefore in their land they shall possess the double: everlasting joy shall be unto them.

α.61.8 Newutche nen Jehovah n8womontam wussittumóonk, nusskeneam mukk8kinnuáonk wutche chikohtáe mag8ongash, kah nussampwehte[ó]h wutanakausuongan8 ut wanummuhkutéyeuuk, kah nag nutayimauóog machemohtag wunn8waonk.
E.61.8 For I the LORD love judgment, I hate robbery for burnt offering; and I will direct their work in truth, and I will make an everlasting covenant with them.

α.61.9 Kah 8skannemun8 pish wahteauun ut kenugke Gentilsut, kah wutontseongan8 ut kenug[h]e missinninnuut: wame neg nauoncheg pish samp8áog, neg wuskannemuneog neh Jehov[á]h wunnanumoncheh.
E.61.9 And their seed shall be known among the Gentiles, and their offspring among the people: all that see them shall acknowledge them, that they are the seed which the LORD hath blessed.

α.61.10 Pish nummishe wekontamut Jehovahut, nukketeahogkou pish wekontam ut num-Manitt8mut, newutche noh nuthogkquanuk wadchanittue hogk8unash, nutunkqwhuk sampweusseae petashqushaonk, onatuh wussentamwaen agwheont wuhhogkuh wu[n]hogk8ongash, kah onatuh weetauadteáenúnt hogqunn[ú]mont nompakouunash.
E.61.10 I will greatly rejoice in the LORD, my soul shall be joyful in my God; for he hath clothed me with the garments of salvation, he hath covered me with the robe of righteousness, as a bridegroom decketh himself with ornaments, and as a bride adorneth herself with her jewels.

α.61.11 Newutche onatuh ohke sonketeunk wunnéht8nunk, kah neane tanohketeaonk, so[h]kenuwáhtunk nish ne adt tanohketeamukish: ne ne Lord Jehovah sonketeauwáhteauun sampwuss[é]onk kah woweenomaonk ut anaquohtag wame wutohtimóneash.
E.61.11 For as the earth bringeth forth her bud, and as the garden causeth the things that are sown in it to spring forth; so the Lord GOD will cause righteousness and praise to spring forth before all the nations.

α.62.1 WUtche Zion matta nutchequnappu, kah wutche Jerusalem matta nutannósin8, nô pajeh wussampweusseonk ogquesohham8m8ut wôhsittag, kah 8wadchanuáonk onatuh lamp châgkossit.
E.62.1 For Zion's sake will I not hold my peace, and for Jerusalem's sake I will not rest, until the righteousness thereof go forth as brightness, and the salvation thereof as a lamp that burneth.

α.62.2 Kah Gentilsog pish naumwog kussampweusseonk, kah wame ketass8tamwog kuss[ó]hsum8onk: kah pish kuttéhenit wuske wesuonl, ne wutt8n Jehovah pish waésuonganehteunk.
E.62.2 And the Gentiles shall see thy righteousness, and all kings thy glory: and thou shalt be called by a new name, which the mouth of the LORD shall name.

α.62.3 Kah wonk pish sohsum8ongane kutchetuhquabéyeu ut wunnutcheganit Jehovah; kah tahs8tamoe chetuhquab ut wunnutcheganit kum-Manitt8m.
E.62.3 Thou shalt also be a crown of glory in the hand of the LORD, and a royal diadem in the hand of thy God.

α.62.4 Matta pish wonk kuttéhennitteóh, ohquánumit, kah kutohke matta pish wonk hettam8un tawushik: qut pish kuttéhennit Hephzibah, kah kutohke Beulah: newutche Jehovah kuttapeneúnk, kah kutohke pish weetauadteom8.
E.62.4 Thou shalt no more be termed Forsaken; neither shall thy land any more be termed Desolate: but thou shalt be called Hephzibah, and thy land Beulah: for the LORD delighteth in thee, and thy land shall be married.

α.62.5 Newutche neane wusken weetauomont peenompoh, kenaumonuk pish k8weetauómunk: k[a]h neane wessentamwaen weekontam8ônont weetauadteánutcheh, ne ne pish kum-Manitt8m k8weekontam8ónuk.
E.62.5 For as a young man marrieth a virgin, so shall thy sons marry thee: and as the bridegroom rejoiceth over the bride, so shall thy God rejoice over thee.

α.62.6 Nuppon askuhwhosuenuog ut kukqussukquaneutonganit, woi Jerusalem, neg matta pish chequnapékeg kesukodtae kah nukkonáe: ken[à]au masuhwhógish Jehovah chequn[á]péhteok.
E.62.6 I have set watchmen upon thy walls, O Jerusalem, which shall never hold their peace day nor night: ye that make mention of the LORD, keep not silence,

α.62.7 Kah anwôhsumûhteogk nô pajeh menehkhit, kah nô pajeh woweenomwáheónat Jerusalemoh ut ohkeit.
E.62.7 And give him no rest, till he establish, and till he make Jerusalem a praise in the earth.

α.62.8 Jehovah chadchekeyeuau nashpwe wuttinuhkou, kah nashpe menuhke wuhpit, wunnamuhkut, matta wonk nummagou k8weatchimineash kummatwom8óog 8meechuminneaóont, kah wunnaumonáuh penuohte[a]og matta pish wuttattam8og k8winum, ne anakausuontaman.
E.62.8 The LORD hath sworn by his right hand, and by the arm of his strength, Surely I will no more give thy corn to be meat for thine enemies; and the sons of the stranger shall not drink thy wine, for the which thou hast laboured:

α.62.9 Qut nag magunukeg pish ummeechineau kah pish wowussumaog Jehovah, kah neg mom[ó]unukeg, pish 8tattamuneau ut n8neetupanatamwe chippinneutunkanit.
E.62.9 But they that have gathered it shall eat it, and praise the LORD; and they that have brought it together shall drink it in the courts of my holiness.

α.62.10 Pannupwushak, pannupwushak squontamash, quashauwéhtam8k ummay8m missinninnuog: pogkétimómukquag, pogketimomuhquag may mukkinnumok qussukquanash, tahshinum8k muttoagk wutche missinninnúog.
E.62.10 Go through, go through the gates; prepare ye the way of the people; cast up, cast up the highway; gather out the stones; lift up a standard for the people.

α.62.11 Kusseh, Jehovah wahteauwáhuwau en wéhqshik muttaok, unnók wuttaunoh Zion, kusseh, k8wadchanitteaonk peyom8: kusseh, wutonkquatunk nashpeu, kah wutanakausuonk ohteau anaquabit.
E.62.11 Behold, the LORD hath proclaimed unto the end of the world, Say ye to the daughter of Zion, Behold, thy salvation cometh; behold, his reward is with him, and his work before him.

α.62.12 Kah pish wuttehenóuh, wunneetupanatamwe missinninnuog, man8whoncheh Jehovah: kah pish kuttehenit, nátinneáwhut, matta ahquontamoe keitotan.
E.62.12 And they shall call them, The holy people, The redeemed of the LORD: and thou shalt be called, Sought out, A city not forsaken.

α.63.1 HOwan yeuoh wag Edom, wag Bozrah, nashpe adtissohs8e hogk8unash? noh wanegik wuthogk8onk, noh paumushadt ut mishe ummenuhkesuonganit? nen an8wi ut sampwesuonganit, menuhkesue n8wadchánuam.
E.63.1 Who is this that cometh from Edom, with dyed garments from Bozrah?  this that is glorious in his apparel, travelling in the greatness of his strength? I that speak in righteousness, mighty to save.

α.63.2 Toh waj musquag kuthogk8onk, kah kuth[ó]gk8ongash onatuh noh tahtahtushkog wine wisq?
E.63.2 Wherefore art thou red in thine apparel, and thy garments like him that treadeth in the winefat?

α.63.3 Nunnusse tahtaskom wine-presse, kah matta howae missinninnuog n8weetomuk8: newutche nag nuttahtaskuskauóog ut nummusquanittam8onganit, kah nussissequohkauóog musquantamon, kah wusqueheonk pish séahôsu ut nuthogk8onganit, kah nunnishketeóh wame nuthogk8unash.
E.63.3 I have trodden the winepress alone; and of the people there was none with me: for I will tread them in mine anger, and trample them in my fury; and their blood shall be sprinkled upon my garments, and I will stain all my raiment.

α.63.4 Newutche ann8tóadtue kesukod nuttahhut ohteau, kah ukkodtum8m8 man8hogig peyom8.
E.63.4 For the day of vengeance is in mine heart, and the year of my redeemed is come.

α.63.5 Kah nunnatauwompip, kah na matta howan aninnohsu: kah nummonchanatamup na matta howan wuttit tahshinnuwáun: newaj nehenwonche nuhpit paudtunkquée wadchanittuonk, kah nummusquantamóonk nuttahshinukqun.
E.63.5 And I looked, and there was none to help; and I wondered that there was none to uphold: therefore mine own arm brought salvation unto me; and my fury, it upheld me.

α.63.6 Kah nuttahtashkuhkáu missinninnuog ut nummusquantam8onganit, kah nukkogkeissippamwuhheog ut nummusquantam8onganit, kah nuppaudto ummenuhkesuongan8 ohkeit.
E.63.6 And I will tread down the people in mine anger, and make them drunk in my fury, and I will bring down their strength to the earth.

α.63.7 Nummisham 8womoausuongash Jehovah, kah woweenomaonk Lord, neaunak wame ne Jehovah aninnumunkqueog: kah mohsag 8netuonk nogque en wekit Israel, ne a[n]inn[u]mauont, neaunak ummo[n]anitteuonk, kah neaun[á]k mataanukish 8w[ó]moauwuongash.
E.63.7 I will mention the lovingkindnesses of the LORD, and the praises of the LORD, according to all that the LORD hath bestowed on us, and the great goodness toward the house of Israel, which he hath bestowed on them according to his mercies, and according to the multitude of his lovingkindnesses.

α.63.8 Newutche n8wop, wunnamuhkut nag nummissinninnúmog, matta pann8w[à]e mukkiesog: neit nag 8wad[c]hanuaenum8uh.
E.63.8 For he said, Surely they are my people, children that will not lie: so he was their Saviour.

α.63.9 Ut wame 8tamehpunaongan8out noh wuttamehpunóp, kah wutanaquabee angelumoh nah 8wadchanuh: ut womoausuonganit, kah ut ukkitteamonteanitteaonganit nah umman8whuh, kah wuttahshinuh, kah ukké[n]unuh ut wame nôadte kesukodtut.
E.63.9 In all their affliction he was afflicted, and the angel of his presence saved them: in his love and in his pity he redeemed them; and he bare them, and carried them all the days of old.

α.63.10 Qut nag wutcheketauóuh, kah m8m8sqheáog 8neetupanatamwe nashauonk: n[é]waj quinnuppeit nag 8matwóminneaóut, kah nah wutayeuuhkonuh.
E.63.10 But they rebelled, and vexed his holy Spirit: therefore he was turned to be their enemy, and he fought against them.

α.63.11 Neit mehquontam nukóne kesukodtash Moses kah ummissinninnúmoh, n8wau, ut$toh wutappin noh pas8omp wutch ketahhannit, weeche uf$flocksumoe nanáshi[p]seaneumoh? uttoh wutapin noh ponamauont 8neetupanat[a]mwe nashauonganoh?
E.63.11 Then he remembered the days of old, Moses, and his people, saying, Where is he that brought them up out of the sea with the shepherd of his flock? where is he that put his holy Spirit within him?

α.63.12 Noh sagkompanomp ut wuttinohkôunit Moses, nashpe wussohsumoe wuhpit, pohshinuk nippe ut anaquabenit, ummicheme wesuonganúhkau[ó]nat wuhhogkuh?
E.63.12 That led them by the right hand of Moses with his glorious arm, dividing the water before them, to make himself an everlasting name?

α.63.13 Noh sagkompanomp papannuppe m8noiyeuut, onatuh horse ut touo[h]komukqut, onk woh nag matta togkussittassun8og?
E.63.13 That led them through the deep, as an horse in the wilderness, that they should not stumble?

α.63.14 Onatuh puppinashim 8mussit ut 8nôuhkoiyeuut, wunnashauanitt8moh Jehovah wutanw[ô]hsum8wáheuh: ne kuttinne sagkompanánuh kummissinninnumog kutáyimauwonat sohsumoe wesuonk.
E.63.14 As a beast goeth down into the valley, the Spirit of the LORD caused him to rest: so didst thou lead thy people, to make thyself a glorious name.

α.63.15 Womómpsh wutch kesukqut, kah naish wutch k8neetupanatamwe kah kussohsumoe ayeuonganit: uttiyeu kus-zealum kah kummenuhkesuonk, mishont8wae kenogkus, kah kummonánummuongash? sun kohkôunôsuash?
E.63.15 Look down from heaven, and behold from the habitation of thy holiness and of thy glory: where is thy zeal and thy strength, the sounding of thy bowels and of thy mercies toward me? are they restrained?

α.63.16 Wunnamuhkut ken n8shun, tohkônogque Abraham matta k8wahikk8unan, kah Israel matta k8wahik8un: ken woi Jehovah, n8shun numman8huwaeneumun, k8wesuonk wutch machemohtag.
E.63.16 Doubtless thou art our father, though Abraham be ignorant of us, and Israel acknowledge us not: thou, O LORD, art our father, our redeemer; thy name is from everlasting.

α.63.17 Woi Jehovah tohwutch panneseáheog wutch kummayut? kah menehketeaháheog wutch kukqushitteaonganit? qushkish wutche [h]itti[n]ninnumog, kutohtoongane chippan8ongash
E.63.17 O LORD, why hast thou made us to err from thy ways, and hardened our heart from thy fear? Return for thy servants' sake, the tribes of thine inheritance.

α.63.18 K8neetupanatamwe missinninnuog wutogguhse ohtauuneau: ayeúqueagig neg tahtashkuhkauóog ut k8neetupanatamwe ayeuonganit.
E.63.18 The people of thy holiness have possessed it but a little while: our adversaries have trodden down thy sanctuary.

α.63.19 Nenawun kuttaiheog, nag matta kenánaánawunóog, nag matta hennóog k8wesuonk.
E.63.19 We are thine: thou never barest rule over them; they were not called by thy name.

α.64.1 WOI napehnont nehnekikoman kesukquash onk woh ken8kem, onk woh wadchuash n8konóhanash ut anaquabean.
E.64.1 Oh that thou wouldest rend the heavens, that thou wouldest come down, that the mountains might flow down at thy presence,

α.64.2 Netatupe sabasumwae n8tau chagohtag, n8teau quô[qu]ônche[k]o[m]euteau nippe: wahteauwahuonat, k8wesuonk ayeuqueaneg, onk woh wutohtimoneash nunnukshaash ut anaquabean.
E.64.2 As when the melting fire burneth, the fire causeth the waters to boil, to make thy name known to thine adversaries, that the nations may tremble at thy presence!

α.64.3 Ase[à]n uhqueneunkquokish nish matta anantam8ágish, k8w8msip, wadchuash [n]8konóhanupash ut anaquabean.
E.64.3 When thou didst terrible things which we looked not for, thou camest down, the mountains flowed down at thy presence.

α.64.4 Newutche nadteoh kádshi[k] muttaok, wosketompaog matta n8tam8og, asuh matta mehtauoge nunnáuhtam8og, asuh matta muskesukque naumoog, woi God, webe ken, uttoh an quoshauwehtauont neh pahtsuónukqutcheh.
E.64.4 For since the beginning of the world men have not heard, nor perceived by the ear, neither hath the eye seen, O God, beside thee, what he hath prepared for him that waiteth for him.

α.64.5 Nog kenogskau weekontog, kah asit sampweusseonk, yeug mequanumukqueaneg ut kummayut: kusseh, ken kummusquantam, newutche nummatchesemun: yeush ut ohteau matchemohtag, kah pish k8wadchanitteamun.
E.64.5 Thou meetest him that rejoiceth and worketh righteousness, those that remember thee in thy ways: behold, thou art wroth; for we have sinned: in those is continuance, and we shall be saved.

α.64.6 Qut nenawun wame onátuh nishkeneunkquok, kah wame nussampweseonganonash tatuppeyeu8ash nishkeneungque monakenissit, kah nenawun wame nummass8pussimun onatuh wunnepogqut: kah nummatcheseonganonash, onatuh wabanit nutamaunukqun.
E.64.6 But we are all as an unclean thing, and all our righteousnesses are as filthy rags; and we all do fade as a leaf; and our iniquities, like the wind, have taken us away.

α.64.7 Kah matta howan wequttum8un k8wesuonk, noh wogkouunuk wuhhog kuttohqunukqunat: newutche kutunkhumaimun kuskesuk, kah kummahchukkussukqun newutche nuppanneseongash.
E.64.7 And there is none that calleth upon thy name, that stirreth up himself to take hold of thee: for thou hast hid thy face from us, and hast consumed us, because of our iniquities.

α.64.8 Qut [e]yeu, woi Jehovah, ken n8shun: nenawun man8nsk, ken nutohkuhquéhteaeneumun, kah nenawun wame kenutchegane anakausuonk.
E.64.8 But now, O LORD, thou art our father; we are the clay, and thou our potter; and we all are the work of thy hand.

α.64.9 Mishe musquanittogkon, woi Jehovah, mehquantogkon matcheseonk micheme, kuhkinneash, naish k8wehquetumauunumun, nenawun wame kummissinninneumog.
E.64.9 Be not wroth very sore, O LORD, neither remember iniquity for ever: behold, see, we beseech thee, we are all thy people.

α.64.10 K8neetupanatamwe keitotanash touohkomukqueyeu8ash: Zion touohkomukk88: Jerusalem touwushin.
E.64.10 Thy holy cities are a wilderness, Zion is a wilderness, Jerusalem a desolation.

α.64.11 N8neetupanatamwe kah n8neetue wetuómun, uttoh n8shunónog adt, wowussumukqueap, ne mahchekutteau wutche n8teau, kah wame n8ne teagwasinnumunónash mohtuppashinash.
E.64.11 Our holy and our beautiful house, where our fathers praised thee, is burned up with fire: and all our pleasant things are laid waste.

α.64.12 Sun woh kutchequnapeh kuhhog yeush wutche, woi Jehovah? sun woh kummanunap, kah kumm8cheke onkuppunasimun?
E.64.12 Wilt thou refrain thyself for these things, O LORD? wilt thou hold thy peace, and afflict us very sore?

α.65.1 NAg nunnatinneóhikquog, neg matta nat8mukqueaneg: nag nunnamhikquog matta natinneawh[e]gig: nussip, mónunneaiek monunneaiek, nuttinnomp wutohtimóin, ne matta ahettam8muk n8wesuonk.
E.65.1 I am sought of them that asked not for me; I am found of them that sought me not: I said, Behold me, behold me, unto a nation that was not called by my name.

α.65.2 Nussepagenum nunnutchegash, qunnikesuk, en cheketamwe missinninnúut, neg aóncheg may ne matta wanegeninn8g, neaunak nehenwonche wuttenantam8ongan8.
E.65.2 I have spread out my hands all the day unto a rebellious people, which walketh in a way that was not good, after their own thoughts;

α.65.3 Missinninnúog m8m8sqh[ú]kqutche nagwutte[à]eu, neg sephausitcheg ut tanohketeaonganéhtu, kah chogkositcheg weetemungquok ut brikse Altarsut.
E.65.3 A people that provoketh me to anger continually to my face; that sacrificeth in gardens, and burneth incense upon altars of brick;

α.65.4 Neg apitcheg weenohkekontu, kah kaecheg wadchuuhkontu, neg mechikeg swinese weyaus, kah sabahheg ne ayimuk wutch nishkeneunkquokish, ohteau 8wishquóut:
E.65.4 Which remain among the graves, and lodge in the monuments, which eat swine's flesh, and broth of abominable things is in their vessels;

α.65.5 Neg án8wacheg, nussikkompau, pas8suksuhkon, newutche n8neetupanatamweyeu anue onk ken: yeug ogqueyeu8og pukut ut nutchânut, n8teau ne náhteagun[a]g.
E.65.5 Which say, Stand by thyself, come not near to me; for I am holier than thou. These are a smoke in my nose, a fire that burneth all the day.

α.65.6 Kusseh wussukwhosu anaquabean: matta nutchequnappu, qut nutonkquodtauoog, nutonkquodtauoog ut upp8chenauóun8out.
E.65.6 Behold, it is written before me: I will not keep silence, but will recompense, even recompense into their bosom,

α.65.7 Kummatcheseonganooash, kah ummatcheseonganooash k8sh8oog moaeu (wussin Jeh[h]vah) neg châgossitcheg weetemungquok ut wadchuuhkontu, kah nup-blasphemónukquog wadchuésukontu: newaj pish quttuhhum nôadte wutanakausuongan8 ut upp8chenauón8óut.
E.65.7 Your iniquities, and the iniquities of your fathers together, saith the LORD, which have burned incense upon the mountains, and blasphemed me upon the hills: therefore will I measure their former work into their bosom.

α.65.8 Yeu wussin Jehovah, neane wuske wine naméhteómuk ut nequttachéiyeuut, kah howan n8wau, nehtóhkon newutche wunanitteaonk ohteau: ne nutussen newutche nuttinneum, onk woh mat nuppagwanoog wame.
E.65.8 Thus saith the LORD, As the new wine is found in the cluster, and one saith, Destroy it not; for a blessing is in it: so will I do for my servants' sakes, that I may not destroy them all.

α.65.9 Kah pish nussohh8wutto wuskannem wutch Jakob, kah wutche Judah noh ohtunk n8wadchumash kah pepenauogig pish wutahtauuneau kah nuttinneumog na pish 8tohkinneau.
E.65.9 And I will bring forth a seed out of Jacob, and out of Judah an inheritor of my mountains: and mine elect shall inherit it, and my servants shall dwell there.

α.65.10 Kah Sharon pish flokse chippinneutunkanu8 kah Achoré 8nouhkoi, ne herdse sepsinóe ayeuunk, wutche nummissinninneumog neg natinneóhikqueaneg.
E.65.10 And Sharon shall be a fold of flocks, and the valley of Achor a place for the herds to lie down in, for my people that have sought me.

α.65.11 Qut kenaau ahquanumoncheg Jehovah, neg wananatogeg n8neetupanatamwe wadchum, neg quoshauwéhtogig table wutche chipwushaog, kah quoshwéhtogig wuttattamoe mag8onk, ut neg adtasúkeg.
E.65.11 But ye are they that forsake the LORD, that forget my holy mountain, that prepare a table for that troop, and that furnish the drink offering unto that number.

α.65.12 Newaj pish ogkémunóg wutch togkodteg, kah pish wame kenauwaemw8 en pagwanittinneat: newutche wehqutteamweon matta kenamp8ham8mw8, ket8kôon, matta ken8tam8m8, qut kummatcheussemw8 ut anaquohtag nuskesukquash, kah kuppepenamumw8 ne matta tapeneám8:
E.65.12 Therefore will I number you to the sword, and ye shall all bow down to the slaughter: because when I called, ye did not answer; when I spake, ye did not hear; but did evil before mine eyes, and did choose that wherein I delighted not.

α.65.13 Newaj yeu n8wadt Lord Jehovah, kusseh nuttinneumog pish meetsuog, qut pish kenaau kukkodtuppumw8, kusseh nuttinneumog pish wuttattamwog, qut pish kenaau kukkuhkutt8numw8, kusseh nuttinneumog pish muskouantamwog, qut pish kutakodchimw8.
E.65.13 Therefore thus saith the Lord GOD, Behold, my servants shall eat, but ye shall be hungry: behold, my servants shall drink, but ye shall be thirsty: behold, my servants shall rejoice, but ye shall be ashamed:

α.65.14 Kusseh nuttinninneumog pish weekontamwutte[a]hae ket8hamoog, qut kenaau pish ken[e]uántamwutteahaeu kummaumw8, kah pish pohquetteahaeu kutt8numw8.
E.65.14 Behold, my servants shall sing for joy of heart, but ye shall cry for sorrow of heart, and shall howl for vexation of spirit.

α.65.15 Kah pish kenukkodtumumw8 k8wesuonkan8 wutch matánumáonk pepenauog: newutche Lord Jehovah pish kenushh[ú]k, kah pish penoweseonganeheau wuttinninneumoh.
E.65.15 And ye shall leave your name for a curse unto my chosen: for the Lord GOD shall slay thee, and call his servants by another name:

α.65.16 Noh wunánumont wuhhogkuh ut ohkeit, noh pish wun[à]numau wuhhogkuh ut wunnamuhkut[e]é Manitt8ut: kah noh chadchekeyeuadt ut ohkit, pish nashpe chadchekeyeuau wunnamuhkuttee Manitto, newutche negonáeu wuttamehpunaongash wunanittamunash, kah newutche nish adtahtásuash wutch nuskesukqut
E.65.16 That he who blesseth himself in the earth shall bless himself in the God of truth; and he that sweareth in the earth shall swear by the God of truth; because the former troubles are forgotten, and because they are hid from mine eyes.

α.65.17 Newutche kusseh nukkesteoh wuske kesukquash & wuske ohke: kah negoneyeuit matta pish mequontam8un, asuh 8waantam8un.
E.65.17 For, behold, I create new heavens and a new earth: and the former shall not be remembered, nor come into mind.

α.65.18 Qut kenaau wekontam8k kah micheme muskouanatam8k ut ne kestéau: newutche kusseh nukkesteau Jerusalem, wekontamoonk, kah ummissinninumoh wutch wekontam8onk.
E.65.18 But be ye glad and rejoice for ever in that which I create: for, behold, I create Jerusalem a rejoicing, and her people a joy.

α.65.19 Kah pish nummuskouantam ut Jerusalem, kah pish n8wekontam ut nummissinninnúut, kah wussippég8e wuttauatonkqussuonk matta pish wonk n8tam8un naut, asuh wadtaúatonkqussue mauonk.
E.65.19 And I will rejoice in Jerusalem, and joy in my people: and the voice of weeping shall be no more heard in her, nor the voice of crying.

α.65.20 Na pish matta wonk wutch wusketuun8, asuh kehchis, noh matta nómwohto8g ukkesukodtumash: newutche mukkies pish nup nequt pasuk8ekodtumwohkog; qut matcheseaen nequt pasuk8 kodtumwohkog pish mattanum[a]u.
E.65.20 There shall be no more thence an infant of days, nor an old man that hath not filled his days: for the child shall die an hundred years old; but the sinner being an hundred years old shall be accursed.

α.65.21 Kah nag pish ayimwog wetuomash, kah wutáyinaoash[:] pish weenominneohketeaog kah pish ummechineau meechummuonk.
E.65.21 And they shall build houses, and inhabit them; and they shall plant vineyards, and eat the fruit of them.

α.65.22 Nag matta pish wekittea8og kah onkatog 8wekin: nag matta pish ohkehteauouog kah onkatog ummeechin: newutche neane nékuk mehtug ne wuttinnékinneau nummissinninneumog, kah pepenauogeg pish sepohtóog wunnetchegane anakausuonk.
E.65.22 They shall not build, and another inhabit; they shall not plant, and another eat: for as the days of a tree are the days of my people, and mine elect shall long enjoy the work of their hands.

α.65.23 Nag matta pish tahn8tanakauseog, asuh nechauóog wutch wuttamehpunáonk: newutche neh 8skannemun8ch wunnánumoncheh Jehovah, kah wutontseongan8 nag weeche.
E.65.23 They shall not labour in vain, nor bring forth for trouble; for they are the seed of the blessed of the LORD, and their offspring with them.

α.65.24 Kah pish n$nih, ash waeequttumhettékup, nunnamp8hamauóog, kah ashp[à]me keket8kahettit, pish nunn8tauóog.
E.65.24 And it shall come to pass, that before they call, I will answer; and while they are yet speaking, I will hear.

α.65.25 Mukquoshim kah lambe pish weetatupp8t[u]og, kah qunnonou pish ogque meech sekuppoghegash oxinut: kah puppissi pish meechuog ask8og. Nag matta pish woskehuwowog, asuh pagwohteauóog ut wame n8neetupanatamwe wadchúmut, wussin Jehovah.
E.65.25 The wolf and the lamb shall feed together, and the lion shall eat straw like the bullock: and dust shall be the serpent's meat. They shall not hurt nor destroy in all my holy mountain, saith the LORD.

α.66.1 YEu wussin Jehovah, kesuk nutappuonk, kah ohke nukquenannéhtuonk: uttiyeu weetu ne áyimaiye[o]g? kah uttiyeu nutann8sin8e ayeuonk?
E.66.1 Thus saith the LORD, The heaven is my throne, and the earth is my footstool: where is the house that ye build unto me? and where is the place of my rest?

α.66.2 Newutche wame yeush ukkesteauunash nunnutcheg, kah wame yeush nniyeupash, wussin Jehovah: qut nogque in yeuoh wosketomp nummónunneau, noh matchekit, kah pohqueteáhont, kah nanukshontog nuttinn8waonk.
E.66.2 For all those things hath mine hand made, and all those things have been, saith the LORD: but to this man will I look, even to him that is poor and of a contrite spirit, and trembleth at my word.

α.66.3 Noh nashont oxinoh, onatuh nashont wosketompuh, noh sephausit lamboh, ontauh támehtahhog anum wussittipuk; noh maguk mag8onk, onatuh maguk pigse wusqueheunk: noh chogkussik weetemungquok, onatuh noh wunánumont nunneukontunkan: nux nag pepenamwog nehenwonche ummay[y]euóash, kah ukketeahogk8un8oh wekontamwoh wunnishkeneunkquodt8m8ash.
E.66.3 He that killeth an ox is as if he slew a man; he that sacrificeth a lamb, as if he cut off a dog's neck; he that offereth an oblation, as if he offered swine's blood; he that burneth incense, as if he blessed an idol. Yea, they have chosen their own ways, and their soul delighteth in their abominations.

α.66.4 Nen wonk nuppepenam pohch8wunukquéhetticheh, kah nunnuhkuhkauwaheóog 8wabesuongash, newutche weehqutteamweon matta howan namp8hamunk8, kôdt8hk[ò]on nag matta n8tam8og, qut nag matcheseog ut anaquabeh, kah pepenamwog ne matta wekontam8h.
E.66.4 I also will choose their delusions, and will bring their fears upon them; because when I called, none did answer; when I spake, they did not hear: but they did evil before mine eyes, and chose that in which I delighted not.

α.66.5 N8tam8k wuttinn8waonk Jehovah, kenaau nanukushántamógish wuttinn8waonk: keematt8oog neg pagkénukqueógig wutche n8wesuonk, n8waog, Jehovah sohsumwáhunaj, qut noh pish nogqussu, wutche k8wekontam8wongan8, kah nag pish akodchuog.
E.66.5 Hear the word of the LORD, ye that tremble at his word; Your brethren that hated you, that cast you out for my name's sake, said, Let the LORD be glorified: but he shall appear to your joy, and they shall be ashamed.

α.66.6 Mishont8wae wadtauatonkqussuonk wutch keitotanat, wadtauatonkqussuonk wutch templeut, 8wâdtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah, noh onkquodtauont ummatwomoh.
E.66.6 A voice of noise from the city, a voice from the temple, a voice of the LORD that rendereth recompence to his enemies.

α.66.7 Ahquam kodtauweekheunk, neechau, ash aonkquommam8kup, neechau mukkutchuksoh.
E.66.7 Before she travailed, she brought forth; before her pain came, she was delivered of a man child.

α.66.8 Howan n8tog neahunig? howan nag* neaûnagish? sun woh ohke neechahtauun pasuk kesukod, asuh woh wutohtimoin pasukqut neekin: newutche queenau Zion kodtauweekheont neechau wunneechanoh.
E.66.8 Who hath heard such a thing? who hath seen such things? Shall the earth be made to bring forth in one day? or shall a nation be born at once?  for as soon as Zion travailed, she brought forth her children.

α.66.9 Sun woh n8wompikquáhuwam, kah sun woh matta nunneechahuóh, wussin Jehovah? woh nunneechahuwan, kah sun woh nukkuppoh wussin kum-Manitt8m?
E.66.9 Shall I bring to the birth, and not cause to bring forth? saith the LORD: shall I cause to bring forth, and shut the womb? saith thy God.

α.66.10 Weekontam8k weeche Jerusalem, kah weeche muskouanatam8[é]nuk, kenaau wame womonógish, muskouanatamwe weekontamok noh weeche, kenaau wame mauunuitteauwánshógish.
E.66.10 Rejoice ye with Jerusalem, and be glad with her, all ye that love her: rejoice for joy with her, all ye that mourn for her:

α.66.11 Onk woh ken8numw8, kah woh kuttaphetteamw8 nashpe wekontamwe wussogkodtunk, onk woh kussesenamuneau, onk woh k8wekontam8wontamumw8 madta$áneuk wussohsumóonk.
E.66.11 That ye may suck, and be satisfied with the breasts of her consolations; that ye may milk out, and be delighted with the abundance of her glory.

α.66.12 Newutche yeu wussin Jehovah, kusseh, nukqunteau wunohteaonk onatuh sepuut, kah wussohsum8ongan8 Gentilsog, onatuh kussitchuáne sep: neit pish ken8numw8, pish kukkinuk8, kah pish kuppumukahh8[n]uk8 ut ukkuttukqut.
E.66.12 For thus saith the LORD, Behold, I will extend peace to her like a river, and the glory of the Gentiles like a flowing stream: then shall ye suck, ye shall be borne upon her sides, and be dandled upon her knees.

α.66.13 Onatuh nah ohkasoh taphikquit ne pish kuttinne taphenineau: kah pish kuttaphetteamw8 ut Jerusalemut.
