E.66.13 As one whom his mother comforteth, so will I comfort you; and ye shall be comforted in Jerusalem.

α.66.14 Kah yeu naumog, kuttahhou pish weekontamòm8, kah kuskonn8 pish ogque neekin mosketuut, kah wunnutcheg Jehovah pish wahteauun in nogque wuttinneumit, kah ummusquantamoonk nogque in ummatwomut.
E.66.14 And when ye see this, your heart shall rejoice, and your bones shall flourish like an herb: and the hand of the LORD shall be known toward his servants, and his indignation toward his enemies.

α.66.15 Newutche kusseh, Jehovah pish nashpe peyau n8teau, kah nashpe wutchariotsumash onatuh pemsquoh: chekee onkquttauunat ummusquantam8onk, kah wutáuskomuongash nashpe n8n8unáe n8taash.
E.66.15 For, behold, the LORD will come with fire, and with his chariots like a whirlwind, to render his anger with fury, and his rebuke with flames of fire.

α.66.16 Newutche nashpe n8teau kah nashpe wuttogkodteg, Jehovah pish keket8kontam wame weyaus, kah nashoncheh Jehovah pish monaoh.
E.66.16 For by fire and by his sword will the LORD plead with all flesh: and the slain of the LORD shall be many.

α.66.17 Nag waneetupanatamwaheoncheg wuhhogkauh, kah pahkheoncheg wuhhogkauh, ut tanohketeaonganehtu, ut onkauwonkq, ut nashauwe, meechhettit pigse weyaus, kah nishkeneunkquok, kah mishabohques, pish moaeu mohtupaeog wussin Jéhovah.
E.66.17 They that sanctify themselves, and purify themselves in the gardens behind one tree in the midst, eating swine's flesh, and the abomination, and the mouse, shall be consumed together, saith the LORD.

α.66.18 Newutche n8wahteoh wutanakausuonganooash, kah wuttenantam8onganooash: pish peyaum8, pish nummukkinnumunat wame wutohtimoneash, kah unnont8waongash, kah nag pish peyaog, kah pish naumwog nussohsumoonk.
E.66.18 For I know their works and their thoughts: it shall come, that I will gather all nations and tongues; and they shall come, and see my glory.

α.66.19 Kah nupponum kuhkinneasuonk ut kenugke nagoh, kah nutann8noog en wutohtimoinneat, neg pohquohhokig, en Tarshish, Pul, kah Lud, neg p8tonkinoncheg ahtompeh, en Tubal, kah Javan, en noadtit munnohannehtu, neg matta n8tamógig n8woweenomitteaonk, kah matta naum8og nussohsumoonk, kah nag pish wahteauwahuwaog nussohsumoonk ut kenugke Gentilsut.
E.66.19 And I will set a sign among them, and I will send those that escape of them unto the nations, to Tarshish, Pul, and Lud, that draw the bow, to Tubal, and Javan, to the isles afar off, that have not heard my fame, neither have seen my glory; and they shall declare my glory among the Gentiles.

α.66.20 Kah nag pish paudtauaog wame kemat8oh, wutch mag8onk en Jehovahut, wutch wame wutohtimoinneat, ut horsesut chariotsut, kah littersut, kah ut mulsut, kah ut kogkinupshae puppinashimwut, ut n8neetupanatamwe wadchúmut, ut Jerusalem, wussin Jehovah, onatuh wuneechanoh Israel paudtaúunit mag8onk, ut pohkishqúadt, ut wekit Jehovah.
E.66.20 And they shall bring all your brethren for an offering unto the LORD out of all nations upon horses, and in chariots, and in litters, and upon mules, and upon swift beasts, to my holy mountain Jerusalem, saith the LORD, as the children of Israel bring an offering in a clean vessel into the house of the LORD.

α.66.21 Kah wonk nag nawhutch nunneemunoog wutche sephausuenuog kah Levitsog wussin Jehovah..
E.66.21 And I will also take of them for priests and for Levites, saith the LORD.

α.66.22 Newutche neane wuske kesukquash kah wuske ohke, nish pish ayimonish, 
E.66.22 For as the new heavens and the new earth, which I will make, shall remain before me, saith the LORD, so shall your seed and your name remain.

α.66.23 Kah pish nnih, wutch pasuk wuske nepauzsaut en onkatoganit, & wutch pasuk saboth en onkatoganit, wame weyaus pish peyaog wowussitteamuneat ut anaquabeh wussin Jehovah.
E.66.23 And it shall come to pass, that from one new moon to another, and from one sabbath to another, shall all flesh come to worship before me, saith the LORD.

α.66.24 Kah nag pish sohhamwog, kah pish moninneauwáog nupp8e wuhhogkau[h], wosketompaog neg ayeuuhkonittue panneussehtaitcheg, newutche wutask8kin8uh matta pish nupp8oh, kah wunn8tomw8 matta pish onthamm8un, kah nag pish unkquanumukqussuog ut wame weyausut.
E.66.24 And they shall go forth, and look upon the carcases of the men that have transgressed against me: for their worm shall not die, neither shall their fire be quenched; and they shall be an abhorring unto all flesh.
